 GauravaVilasaharibhaktivilāsaḥprathamo vilāsaḥatha maṅgalācaraṇamcaitanyadevaṃ bhagavantam āśrayeśrīvaiṣṇavānāṃ pramudeñjasā likhan āvaśyakaṃ karma vicārya sādhubhiḥsārdhaṃ samāhṛtya samastaśāstrataḥ  Hbhv bhakter vilāsāṃś cinute prabodhānandasya śiṣyo bhagavatpriyasya gopālabhaṭṭo raghunāthadāsaṃsantoṣayan rūpasanātanau ca  Hbhv mathurānāthapādābjapremabhaktivilāsataḥ jātaṃ bhaktivilāsākhyaṃ tadbhaktāḥ śīlayantv imam  Hbhv jīyāsur ātyantikabhaktiniṣṭhāḥ śrīvaiṣṇavā māthuramaṇḍaletra kāśīśvaraḥ kṛṣṇavane cakāstu śrīkṛṣṇadāsaś ca salokanāthaḥ  Hbhv tatra lekhyapratijñāādau sakāraṇaṃ lekhyaṃ śrīgurvāśrayaṇaṃ tataḥ guruḥ śiṣyaḥ parīkṣādir bhagavān manavo sya ca  Hbhv mantrādhikārī siddhyādiśodhanaṃ mantrasaṃskriyāḥ dīkṣā nityaṃ brāhmakāle śubhotthānaṃ pavitratā prātaḥ smṛtyādi kṛṣṇasya vādyādaiś ca prabodhanam  Hbhv nirmālyottāraṇādyādau maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ maitrādikṛtyaṃ śaucācamanaṃ dantasya dhāvanam  Hbhv snānaṃ tāntrikasandhyādi devasadmādisaṃskriyā  Hbhv tulasyādyāhṛtir gehasnānam uṣṇodakādikam vastraṃ pīṭhaṃ cordhvapuṇḍraṃ śrīgopīcandanādikam  Hbhv cakrādimudrā mālā ca gṛhasandhyārcanaṃ guroḥ māhātmyaṃ cātha kṛṣṇasya dvāraveśmāntarārcanam  Hbhv pūjārthāsanam arghyādisthāpanaṃ vighnavāraṇam śrīgurvādinatir bhūtaśuddhiḥ prāṇaviśodhanam  Hbhv nyāsamudrāpañcakaṃ ca kṛṣṇadhyānāntarārcane pūjā padāni śrīmūrtiśālagrāmaśilās tathā  Hbhv dvārakodbhavacakrāṇi śuddhayaḥ pīṭhapūjanam āvāhanādi tanmudrā āsanādisamarpaṇam  Hbhv snapanaṃ śaṅkhaghaṇṭādivādyaṃ nāmasahasrakam purāṇapāṭho vasanam upavītaṃ vibhūṣaṇam  Hbhv gandhaḥ śrītulasīkāṣṭhacandanaṃ kusumāni ca patrāṇi tulasī cāṅgopāṅgāvaraṇapūjanam  Hbhv dhūpo dīpaś ca naivedyaṃ pānaṃ homo balikriyā avagaṇḍūṣādyāsyavāso divyagandhādikaṃ punaḥ  Hbhv rājopacārā gītādi mahānīrājanaṃ tathā śaṅkhādivādanaṃ sāmbuśaṅkhanīrājanaṃ stutiḥ  Hbhv natiḥ pradakṣiṇā karmādyarpaṇaṃ japa yācane āgaḥkṣamāpaṇaṃ nānāgāṃsi nirmālyadhāraṇam  Hbhv śaṅkhāmbutīrthaṃ tulasīpūjā tanmṛttikādi ca dhātrīsnānaniṣedhasya kālo vṛtter upārjanam  Hbhv madhyāhne vaiśadevādiśrāddhaṃ cānarpyam acyute vinārcām aśane doṣās tathānarpitabhojane  Hbhv naivedyabhakṣaṇaṃ santaḥ satsaṅgo sadasaṅgatiḥ asadgatir vaiṣṇavopahāsanindādiduṣphalam  Hbhv satāṃ bhaktir viṣṇuśāstraṃ śrīmadbhāgavataṃ tathā līlākathā ca bhagavaddharmāḥ sāyaṃ nijakriyāḥ  Hbhv karmapātaparīhāras trikālārcā viśeṣataḥ naktaṃ kṛtyānyatho pūjāphalasiddhyādidarśanam  Hbhv viṣṇvarthadānaṃ vividhopacārā nyūnapūraṇam śayanaṃ mahimārcāyāḥ śrīmannāmnas tathādbhutaḥ  Hbhv nāmāparādhā bhaktiś ca premāthāśrayaṇādayaḥ pakṣeṣv ekādaśī sāṅgā śrīdvādaśyaṣṭakaṃ mahat  Hbhv kṛtyāni mārgaśīrṣādimāseṣu dvādśeṣv api puraścaraṇakṛtyāni mantraṃ siddhasya lakṣaṇam  Hbhv mūrtyāvirbhāvanaṃ mūrtipratiṣṭhā kṛṣṇamandiram jīrṇoddhṛtiḥ śrītulasīvivāho nanyakarma ca  Hbhv tatra śrīgurūpasattikāraṇamkṛpayā kṛṣṇadevasya tadbhaktajanasaṅgataḥ bhakter māhātmyam ākarṇya tām icchan sadguruṃ bhajet  Hbhv atrānubhūyate nityaṃ duḥkhaśreṇī paratra ca duḥsahā śrūyate śāstrāt titīrṣed api tāṃ sudhīḥ  Hbhv tathā coktam ekādaśaskandhe BhP labdhvā sudurlabham idaṃ bahusambhavāntemānuṣyam arthadam anityam apīha dhīraḥ tūrṇaṃ yateta na pated anumṛtyu yāvanniḥśreyasāya viṣayaḥ khalu sarvataḥ syāt  Hbhv svayaṃ śrībhagavatā ca BhP nṛdeham ādyaṃ sulabhaṃ sudurlabhaṃplavaṃ sukalpaṃ gurukarṇadhāram mayānukūlena nabhasvateritaṃpumān bhavābdhiṃ na taret sa ātmahā  Hbhv atha śrīgurūpasattiḥtatraiva śrīprabuddhayogeśvaroktau BhP tasmād guruṃ prapadyeta jijñāsuḥ śreya uttamam śābde pare ca niṣṇātaṃ brahmaṇy upaśamāśrayam  Hbhv svayaṃ śrībhagavaduktau BhP madabhijñaṃ guruṃ śāntam upāsīta madātmakam  Hbhv kramadīpikāyāṃ  ca vipraṃ pradhvastakāmaprabhṛtiripughaṭaṃ nirmalāṅgaṃ gariṣṭhāṃbhaktiṃ kṛṣṇāṅghripaṅkeruhayugalarajorāgiṇīm udvahantam vettāraṃ vedaśāstāgamavimalapathāṃ sammataṃ satsu dāntaṃvidyāṃ yaḥ saṃvivitsuḥ pravaṇatanumanā deśikaṃ saṃśrayeta  Hbhv śrutāv api MuṇḍU  ChāU  tadvijñānārthaṃ sa gurum evābhigacchet samitpāṇiḥ śrotriyaṃ brahmaniṣṭham ācāryavān puruṣo veda  Hbhv atha gurūpasattinityatāśrībhāgavate daśamaskandhe śrutistutau BhP vijitahṛṣīkavāyubhir adāntamanas turagaṃya iha yatanti yantum atilolam upāyakhidaḥ vyasanaśatānvitāḥ samavahāya guroś caraṇaṃvaṇija ivāja santy akṛtakarṇadharā jaladhau  Hbhv śrutau ca KaṭhU naiṣā tarkeṇa matir āpaneyāproktānyenaiva sujñānāya preṣṭha  Hbhv atha viśeṣataḥ śrīguror lakṣaṇānimantramuktāvalyām avadātānvayaḥ śuddhaḥ svocitācāratatparaḥ āśramī krodharahito vedavit sarvaśāstravit  Hbhv śraddhāvān anasūyaś ca priyavāk priyadarśanaḥ śuciḥ suveśas taruṇaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  Hbhv dhīmān anuddhatamatiḥ pūrṇo hantā vimarśakaḥ saguṇo rcāsu kṛtadhīḥ kṛtajñaḥ śiṣyavatsalaḥ  Hbhv nigrahānugrahe śakto homamantraparāyaṇaḥ ūhāpohaprakārajñaḥ śuddhātmā yaḥ kṛpālayaḥ ity ādilakṣaṇair yukto guruḥ syād garimānidhiḥ  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ ca devatopāsakaḥ śānto viṣayeṣv api niḥspṛhaḥ adhyātmavid brahmavādī vedaśāstrārthakovidaḥ  Hbhv uddhartuṃ caiva saṃhartuṃ samartho brāhmaṇottamaḥ tattvajño yantramantrāṇāṃ marmabhettā rahasyavit  Hbhv puraścaraṇakṛd dhomamantrasiddhaḥ prayogavit tapasvī satyavādī ca gṛhastho gurur ucyate  Hbhv viṣṇusmṛtau paricaryāyaśolābhalipsuḥ śiṣyād gurur nahi kṛpāsindhuḥ susampūrṇaḥ sarvasattvopakārakaḥ  Hbhv niḥspṛhaḥ sarvataḥ siddhaḥ sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ sarvasaṃśayasaṃchettā nālaso gurur āhṛtaḥ  Hbhv śrīnāradapañcarātre śrībhagavannāradasaṃvāde brāhmaṇaḥ sarvakālajñaḥ kuryāt sarveṣv anugraham tadabhāvād dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ śāntātmā bhagavanmayaḥ  Hbhv bhāvitātmā ca sarvajñaḥ śāstrajñaḥ satkriyāparaḥ siddhitrayam āyukta ācāryatvebhiṣecitaḥ  Hbhv kṣatraviṭśūdrajātīnāṃ kṣatriyo nugrahe kṣamaḥ kṣatriyasyāpi ca guror bhāvād īdṛśo yadi  Hbhv vaiśyaḥ syāt tena kāryaś ca dvaye nityam anugrahaḥ sajātīyena śūdreṇa tādṛśena mahāmate anugrahābhiṣekau ca kāryau śūdrasya sarvadā  Hbhv kiṃ ca varṇottamtha ca gurau sati yā viśrutepi ca svadeśato that vānyatra nedaṃ kāryaṃ śubhārthinā  Hbhv vidyamāne tu yaḥ kuryāt yatra tatra viparyayam tasyehāmutra nāśaḥ syāt tasmāc chāstroktam ācaret kṣatraviṭśūdrajātīyaḥ prātilomyaṃ na dīkṣayet  Hbhv pādme ca PadmaP mahābhāgavataḥ śreṣṭho brāhmaṇo vai gurur nṛṇām sarveṣām eva lokānām asau pūjyo yathā hariḥ  Hbhv mahākūlaprasūto pi sarvayajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ sahasraśākhādhyāyī ca na guruḥ syād avaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv  itigṛhītaviṣṇudīkṣāko viṣṇupūjāparo naraḥ vaiṣṇavo bhihito bhijñair itaro smād avaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv tattvasāgarebahvāśī dīrghasūtrī ca viṣayādiṣu lolupaḥ hetuvādarato duṣṭo vāgvādī guṇanindakaḥ  Hbhv aromā bahuromā ca ninditāśramasevakaḥ kāladanto sitauṣṭhaś ca durgandhiśvāsavāhakaḥ  Hbhv duṣṭalakṣaṇasampanno yadyapi svayam īśvaraḥ bahupratigrhāsakta ācāryaḥ śrīkṣayāvahaḥ  Hbhv atha śiṣyalakṣaṇānimantramuktāvalyāmśiṣyaḥ śuddhānvayaḥ śrīmān vinītaḥ priyadarśanaḥ satyavāk puṇyacarito dabhradhīr dambhavarjitaḥ  Hbhv kāmakrodhaparityāgī bhaktaś ca gurupādayoḥ devatāpravaṇaḥ kāyamanovāgbhir divāniśam  Hbhv nīrujo nirjitāśeṣapātakaḥ śraddhyānvitaḥ dvijadevapitṝṇāṃ ca nityam arcāparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv yuvā viniyatāśeṣakaraṇaḥ karuṇālayaḥ ity ādilakṣaṇair yuktaḥ śiṣyo dīkṣādhikāravān  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe ca BhP  amāny amatsaro dakṣo nirmamo dṛṭhasauhṛdaḥ asatvaro rthajijñāsur anasūyur amoghavāk  Hbhv athāpekṣyāḥagastyasaṃhitāyāmalasā malināḥ kliṣṭā dāmbhikāḥ kṛpaṇās tathā daridrā rogiṇo ruṣṭā rāgiṇo bhogalālasāḥ  Hbhv asūyāmatsaragrastāḥ śaṭhāḥ paruṣavādinaḥ anyāyopārjitadhanāḥ paradāraratāś ca ye  Hbhv viduṣāṃ vairiṇaś caiva ajñāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ bhraṣṭavratāś ca ye kaṣṭavṛttayaḥ piśunāḥ khalāḥ  Hbhv bahvāśinaḥ krūraceṣṭā durātmanaś ca nindita ity evam ādayo py anye pāpiṣṭhāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ  Hbhv akṛtyebhyo nivāryāś ca guruśikṣāsahiṣṇavaḥ evambhūtāḥ parityājyāḥ śiṣyatve nopakalpitāḥ  Hbhv yady ete hy upakalperan devatākrośabhājanāḥ bhavantīha dardrās te putradāravivarjitāḥ  Hbhv nārakāś caiva dehānte tiryañcaḥ prabhavanti te  Hbhv hayaśīrṣapañcarātrejaiminiḥ sugataś caiva nāstiko nagna eva ca kapilaś cākṣapādaś ca ṣaḍ ete hetuvādinaḥ  Hbhv etanmatānusāreṇa vartante ye narādhamāḥ te hetuvādinaḥ proktās tebhyas tantraṃ na dāpayet  Hbhv  ititayoḥ parīkṣā cānyo nyam ekābdaṃ sahavāsataḥ vyavahārasvabhāvānubhavenaivābhijāyate  Hbhv atha parīkṣaṇammantramuktāvalyāṃtayor vatsaravāsena jñātānyonyasvabhāvayoḥ gurutā śiṣyatā ceti nānyathaiveti niścayaḥ  Hbhv śrutiś canāsaṃvatsaravāsine deyāt  Hbhv sārasaṅgrahepisadguruḥ svāśritaṃ śiṣyaṃ varṣm ekaṃ parīkṣayet  Hbhv rājñi cāmātyajā doṣāḥ patnīpāpaṃ svabhartari tathā śiṣyārjitaṃ pāpaṃ guruḥ prāpnoti niścitam  Hbhv kramadīpikāyāṃ tu  santoṣayed akuṭilādretarāntarātmātaṃ svair dhanaiś ca vapuṣāpy anukūlavāṇyā abdatrayaṅkamalanābhadhiyātidhīrastuṣṭe vivakṣatu gurāv atha mantradīkṣām  Hbhv atha viśeṣataḥ śrīgurusevāvidhiḥkaurme śrīvyāsagītāyāmudakumbhaṃ kuśān puṣpaṃ samidho syāharet sadā mārjanaṃ lepanaṃ nityam aṅgānāṃ vāsasāṃ caret  Hbhv nāsya nirmālyaśayanaṃ pādukopāsanahāv api ākrāmed āsanaṃ chyāyām āsandīṃ vā kadācana  Hbhv sādhayed dantakāṣṭhādīn kṛtyaṃ cāsmai nivedayeet  Hbhv anāpṛcchya na gantavyaṃ bhavet priyahite rasaḥ na pādau sārayed asya sannidhāne kadācana  Hbhv jṛmbhāhāsyādikaṃ caiva kaṇṭhaprāvaraṇaṃ tathā varjayet sannidhau nityam athāsphoṭanam eva ca  Hbhv kiṃ caśreyas tu guruvad vṛttir nityam eva samācaret guruputreṣu dāreṣu guroś caiva svabandhuṣu  Hbhv utsādanaṃ vai gātrāṇāṃ snāpanocchiṣṭabhojane na kuryād guruputrasya pādayoḥ śaucam eva ca  Hbhv guruvat paripūjyāś ca savarṇā guruyoṣitaḥ asavarṇās tu sampūjyāḥ pratyutthānābhivādanaiḥ  Hbhv abhyañjanaṃ snāpanaṃ ca gātrotsādanam eva ca gurupatnyā ca kāryāṇi keśānāṃ ca prasādhanam  Hbhv devyāgame śrīśivoktauguruśayyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pāduke pādapīṭhakam snānodakaṃ tathā chāyāṃ laṅghayen na kadācana  Hbhv guror agre pṛthakpūjām advaitaṃ ca parityajet dīkṣāṃ vyākhyāṃ prabhutvaṃ ca guror agre vivarjayet  Hbhv śrīnāradoktauyatra yatra guruṃ paśyet tatra tatra kṛtāñjali praṇamet daṇḍavad bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥ  Hbhv guror vākyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pādukopānahau tathā vastraṃ chāyāṃ tathā śiṣyo laṅghayen na kadācana  Hbhv śrīmanusmṛtau not foundnodāhared guror nāma parokṣam api kevalam na caivāsyānukurvīta gatibhāṣaṇaceṣṭitam  Hbhv guror gurau sannihite guruvad dhṛtim ācaret na cāvisṛṣṭo guruṇā svān gurūn abhivādayet  Hbhv śrīnāradapañcarātreyathā tathā yatra tatra na gṛhṇīyāc ca kevalam abhaktyā na guror nāma gṛhṇīyāc ca yatātmavān  Hbhv praṇavaḥ śrīs tato nāma viṣṇuśabdād anantaram pādaśabdasametaṃ ca natamūrdhāñjalīyutaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ cana tam ājñāpayen mohāt tasyājñāṃ na ca laṅghayet nānivedya guroḥ kiñcid bhoktavyaṃ vā guros tathā  Hbhv anyatra caāyāntam agrato gacched gacchantaṃ tam anuvrajet āsane śayane vāpi na tiṣṭhed agrato guroḥ  Hbhv yat kiñcid annapānādi priyaṃ dravyaṃ manoramam samarpya gurave paścāt svayaṃ bhuñjīta pratyaham  Hbhv śrīviṣṇusmṛtauna guror apriyaṃ kuryāt tāḍitaḥ pīḍito pi vā nāvamanyeta tadvākyaṃ nāpriyaṃ hi samācaret  Hbhv ācāryasya priyaṃ kuryāt prāṇair api dhanair api karmaṇā manasā vācā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv śrīnāradapañcarātre yo vakti nyāyarahitam anyāyena śṛṇoti yaḥ tāv ubhau narakaṃ ghoraṃ vrajataḥ kālam akṣayam  Hbhv vaiṣṇavatantre trāyasva bho jagannātha guro saṃsāravahninā dagdhaṃ māṃ kāladaṣṭaṃ ca tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Hbhv  ititatra śrīvāsudevasya sarvadevaśiromaṇeḥ pādāmbujaikabhāg eva dīkṣā grāhyā manīṣibhiḥ  Hbhv prathamaskandhe BhP  sattvaṃ rajas tama iti prakṛter guṇās tairyuktaḥ paramapuruṣa eka ihāsya dhatte sthityādaye hariviriñcihareti saṃjñāḥśreyāṃsi tatra khalu sattvatanor nṝṇāṃ syuḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  athāpi yatpādanakhāvasṛṣṭaṃjagad viriñcopahṛtārhaṇāmbhaḥ seśaṃ punāty anyatamo mukundātko nāma loke bhagavatpadārthaḥ  Hbhv śrīdaśamaskandhe BhP  tan niśamyātha munayo vismitā muktasaṃśayāḥ bhūyāṃsaṃ śraddadhur viṣṇuṃ yataḥ śāntir yato bhayam  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde PadmaP  vyāmohāya carācarasya jagatas te te purāṇāgamāstāṃ tām eva hi devatāṃ paramikāṃ jalpantu kalpāvadhi siddhānte punar eka eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ samastāgamavyāpāreṣu vivecanavyatikaraṃ nīteṣu niścīyate  Hbhv nārasiṃhe satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyam utkṣipya bhujam ucyate vedāc chāstraṃ paraṃ nāsti na devaḥ keśavāt paraḥ  Hbhv yataḥ pādme arir mitraṃ viṣṃ pathyam adharmo dharmatāṃ vrajet suprasanne hṛṣīkeśe viparīte viparyayaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrībhagavadvākyammannimittaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpam api dharmāya kalpate mām anādṛtya dharmo pi pāpaṃ syān matprabhāvataḥ  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo nyaṃ devam upāsate svamātaraṃ parityajya śvapacīṃ vandate hi saḥ  Hbhv tatraivānyatra vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo nyaṃ devam upāsate tyaktvāmṛtaṃ sa mūḍhātmā bhuṅkte halāhalaṃ viṣam  Hbhv mahābhārate yas tu viṣṇuṃ parityajya mohād anyam upāsate sa hemarāśim utsṛjya pāṃśurāśiṃ jighṛkṣati  Hbhv anādṛtya tu yo viṣṇum anyadevaṃ samāśrayet gaṅgāmbhasaḥ sa tṛṣṇārto mṛgatṛṣṇāṃ pradhāvati  Hbhv pañcarātre yo mohād viṣṇum anyena hīnadevena durmatiḥ sādhāraṇaṃ sakṛd brūte so ntyajo nāntyajo ntyajaḥ  Hbhv vaiṣṇavatantre na labheyuḥ punar bhaktiṃ harer aikāntikīṃ jaṅāḥ ekāgramanasaś cāpi viṣṇusāmānyadarśinaḥ  Hbhv anyatra ca yas tu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ brahmarudrādidaivataiḥ samatvenaiva vīkṣeta sa pāṣaṇḍī bhaved dhruvam  Hbhv  itisahasranāmastotrādau ślokaughāḥ santi cedṛśāḥ viśeṣataḥ sattvaniṣṭhaiḥ sevoy viṣṇur na cāparaḥ  Hbhv tathā ca śrīharivaṃśe śivavākyam harir eva sadārādhyo bhavadbhiḥ sattvasaṃsthitaiḥ viṣṇumantraṃ sadā viprāḥ paṭhadhvaṃ dhyāta keśavam  Hbhv  itiīdṛṅmāhātmyavākyeṣu saṅgṛhīteṣu sarvataḥ granthabāhulyadoṣaḥ syāl likhyantepekṣitāni tat  Hbhv atha na nivartante yoginaḥ tad etad ṛcābhyuktam tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ divīva cakṣur ātatam tad viprāso vipanyavo jāgṛvāṃsaḥ samindhate viṣṇor yat paramaṃ padam  Hbhv atha vyarthatvād api likhyate  Hbhv śrīmadgopāladevasya sarvaiśvaryapradarśinaḥ tādṛkśaktiṣu mantreṣu nahi kiñcid vicāryate  Hbhv tathā ca kramadīpikāyām sarveṣu varṇeṣu tathāśrameṣunārīṣu nānāhvayajanmabheṣudātā phalānām abhivāñchitānāṃdrāg eva gopālakamantra eṣaḥ  Hbhv trailokyasaṃmohanatantre caaṣṭādaśākṣaramantram adhikṛtya śrīśivenoktam na cātra śātravā doṣā narṇasvādivicāraṇā ṛkṣarāśivicāro vā na kartavyo manau priye  Hbhv kecic chinnāś ca ruddhāś ca kecin madasamuddhatāḥ malināḥ stambhitāḥ kecit kīlitā dūṣitā api etair doṣair yuto nāyaṃ yatas tribhunottamaḥ  Hbhv  itisāmānyataś ca yathā bṛhadgautamīye atha kṛṣṇamanūn vakṣye dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalapradān yān vai vijñāya munayo lebhire muktim añjasā  Hbhv gṛhasthā vanagāś caiva yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ striyaḥ śūdrādayaś caiva sarve yatrādhikāriṇaḥ  Hbhv nātra cintyo riśuddhyādir nārimitrādilakṣaṇam na vā prayāsabāhulyaṃ sādhane na pariśramaḥ  Hbhv ajñānatūlarāśeś ca analaḥ kṣaṇamātrataḥ siddhasādhyasusiddhārirūpā nātra vicāraṇā  Hbhv sarveṣāṃ siddhamantrāṇāṃ yato brahmākṣaro manuḥ prajāpatir avāpāgryaṃ devarājyaṃ śacīpatiḥ avāpus tridaśāḥ svargaṃ vāgīśatvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ  Hbhv ity āditatraivāntare viṣṇubhaktyā viśeṣeṇa kiṃ na sidhyati bhūtale kīṭādibrahmaparyantaṃ govindānugrahān mune  Hbhv sarvasampattinilayāḥ sarvatrāpy akutobhayāḥ ity ādi kathitaṃ kiñcin māhātmyaṃ vo munīśvarāḥ  Hbhv ākāśe tārakā yadvat sindhoḥ saikatasṛṣṭivat etadvijñānamātreṇa labhen muktiṃ caturvidhām  Hbhv etadanyeṣu mantreṣu doṣāḥ santi pare ca ye tadarthaṃ mantrasaṃskārā lipyante tantrato daśa  Hbhv saradātilake jananaṃ jīvanaṃ ceti tāḍanaṃ rodhanaṃ tathā athābhiṣeko vimalīkaraṇāpyāyane punaḥ tarpaṇaṃ dīpanaṃ guptir daśaitā mantrasaṃskriyāḥ  Hbhv mantrāṇāṃ mātṛkāmadhyād uddhāro jananaṃ smṛtam praṇavāntaritān kṛtvā mantravarṇān japet sudhīḥ  Hbhv etaj jīvanam ity āhur mantratantraviśāradāḥ manor varṇān samālikhya tāḍayec candanāmbhasā  Hbhv pratyekaṃ vāyunā mantrī tāḍanaṃ tad udāhṛtam vilikhya mantraṃ taṃ mantrī prasūnaiḥ karavīrajaiḥ  Hbhv tanmantrākṣarasaṅkhyātair hanyād yat tena rodhanam svatantroktavidhānena mantrī mantrārṇasaṅkhyayā  Hbhv aśvatthapallavair mantram abhiṣiñced viśuddhaye saṃcintya manasā mantraṃ yotir mantreṇa nirdahet  Hbhv mantre mūlatrayaṃ mantrī vimalīkaraṇaṃ tv idam tāravyomāgnimanuyugadaṇḍī jyotir manur mataḥ kuśodakena japtena pratyarṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ manoḥ  Hbhv tena mantreṇa vidhivad etad āpyāyanaṃ smṛtam mantreṇa vāriṇā yantre tarpaṇaṃ tarpaṇaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv tāramāyāramāyogo manor dīpanam ucyate japyamānasya mantrasya gopanaṃ tv aprakāśanam  Hbhv balitvāt kṛṣṇamantrāṇāṃ saṃskārāpekṣaṇaṃ nahi sāmānyoddeśamātreṇa tathāpy etad udīritam  Hbhv iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāsegauravo nāma prathamo vilāsaḥ  DaiksikaVilasadvitīyo vilāsaḥdaikṣikaḥtaṃ śrīmatkṛṣṇacaitanyaṃ vande jagadgurum yasyānukampayā śvāpi mahābdhiṃ santaret sukham  Hbhv atha dīkṣāvidhiḥdīkṣāvidhir likhyatetrānusṛtya kramadīpikām vinā dīkṣāṃ hi pūjāyāṃ nādhikāro sti karhicit  Hbhv āgame dvijānām anupetānāṃ svakarmādhyayanādiṣu yathādhikāro nāstīha syāc copanayanād anu  Hbhv tathātrādīkṣitānāṃ tu mantradevārcanādiṣu nādhikāro sty ataḥ kuryād ātmānaṃ śivasaṃstutam  Hbhv skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde te narāḥ paśavo loke kiṃ teṣāṃ jīvane phalam yair na labdhā harer dīkṣā nārcito vā janārdanaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrīrukmāṅgadamohinīsaṃvādeviṣṇuyāmale ca adikṣitasya vāmoru kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ nirarthakam paśuyonim avāpnoti dīkṣāvirahito janaḥ  Hbhv viśeṣato viṣṇuyāmale snehād vā lobhato vāpi yo gṛhṇīyād adīkṣayā tasmin gurau saśiṣye tu devatāśāpa āpatet  Hbhv viṣṇurahasye ca avijñāya vidhānoktaṃ haripūjāvidhikriyām kurvan bhaktyā samāpnoti śatabhāgaṃ vidhānataḥ  Hbhv divyaṃ jñānaṃ yato dadyāt kuryāt pāpasya saṅkṣayam tasmād dīkṣeti sā proktā deśikais tattvakovidaiḥ  Hbhv ato guruṃ praṇamyaivaṃ sarvasvaṃ vinivedya ca gṛhṇīyād vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ dīkṣāpūrvaṃ vidhānataḥ  Hbhv skānde tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde tapasvinaḥ karmaniṣṭhāḥ śreṣṭhās te vai narā bhuvi prāptā yais tu harer dīkṣā sarvaduḥkhavimocinī  Hbhv tantrasāgare ca yathā kāñcanatāṃ yāti kāṃsyaṃ rasavidhānataḥ tathā dīkṣāvidhānena dvijatvaṃ jāyate nṛṇām  Hbhv atha dīkṣākālaḥ  tatra māsaśuddhiḥāgame mantrasvīkaraṇaṃ caitre bahuduḥhaphalapradam vaiśākhe ratnalābhaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv āṣāḍhe bandhunāśāya śrāvaṇe tu bhayāvaham prajāhānir bhādrapade sarvatra śubham āśvine  Hbhv kārttike dhanavṛddhiḥ syān mārgaśīrṣe śubhapradam pauṣe tu jñānahāniḥ syān māghe medhāvivardhanam phālgune sarvavaśyatvam ācāryaiḥ parikīrtitam  Hbhv kvacic ca samṛddhiḥ śrāvaṇe nūnaṃ jñānaṃ syāt kārttike tathā phālgunepi samṛddhiḥ syān malamāsaṃ parityajet  Hbhv gautamīyemantrārambhas tu caitre syāt samastapuruṣārthadaḥ vaiśākhe ratnalābhaḥ syāt jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv āṣāḍhe bandhunāśaḥ syāt pūrṇāyuḥ śrāvaṇe bhavet prajānāśo bhaved bhādre āśvine ratnasañcayaḥ  Hbhv kārttike mantrasiddhiḥ syāt mārgaśīrṣe tathā bhavet pauṣe tu śatrupīḍā syāt māghe medhāvivardhanam phālgune sarvakāmāḥ syur malamāsaṃ parityajet  Hbhv skānde tatraiva śrīrukmāṅgadamohinīsaṃvādekārttike tu kṛtā dīkṣā nṝṇāṃ janmanikṛntanī tasmāt sarvaprayatnena dīkṣāṃ kurvīta kārttike  Hbhv śrīmadgopālamantrāṇāṃ dīkṣāyāṃ tu na duṣyati caitramāse yad uktā tad dīkṣā tatraiva deśikaiḥ  Hbhv atha bāraśuddhiḥravau gurau tathā some kartavyaṃ budhaśukrayoḥ  Hbhv atha nakṣatraśuddhiḥnāradatantrerohiṇī śravaṇārdrā ca dhaniṣṭhā cottarātrayaḥ puṣyaṃ śatabhiṣaś caiva dīkṣānakṣatram ucyate  Hbhv kvacic caaśvinīrohiṇīsvātiviśākhāhastabheṣu ca jyeṣṭhottarātrayeṣv eva kuryān mantrābhiṣecanam  Hbhv atha tithiśuddhiḥsārasaṅgrahedvitīyā pañcamī caiva ṣaṣṭhī caiva viśeṣataḥ dvādaśyām api kartavyaṃ trayodaśyām athāpi ca  Hbhv kvacic capūrṇimā pañcamī caiva dvitīyā saptamī tathā trayodaśī ca daśamī praśastā sarvakāmadā  Hbhv  iti evaṃ śuddhe dine śuklapakṣe śukragurūdaye sallagne candratārānukūle dīkṣā praśasyate  Hbhv athātrāpavādaḥ viśeṣavidhiḥrudrayāmalesattīrtherkavidhugrāse tantudāmanaparvaṇoḥ mantradīkṣāṃ prakurvīta māsarkṣādi na śodhayet  Hbhv sulagnacandratārādibalam atra sadaiva hi labdho tra mantor dīrghāyuḥsampatsantativardhanaḥ  Hbhv sūryagrahaṇakālena samāno nāsti kaścana yatra yad yat kṛtaṃ sarvam anantaphaladaṃ bhavet na māsatithivārādiśodhanaṃ sūryaparvaṇi  Hbhv tattvasāgare cadurlabhe sadgurūṇāṃ ca sakṛt saṅga upasthite tadanujñā yadā labdhā sa dīkṣāvasaro mahān  Hbhv grāme vā yadi vāraṇye kṣetre vā divase niśi āgacchati gurur daivād yadā dīkṣā tadājñayā  Hbhv yadaivecchā tadā dīkṣā guror ājñānurūpataḥ na tīrthaṃ na vrataṃ homo na snānaṃ na japakriyā dīkṣāyāḥ karaṇaṃ kintu svecchāprāpte tu sadgurau  Hbhv atha maṇḍapanirmāṇavidhiḥkriyāvatyādibhedena bhaved dīkṣā caturvidhā tatra kriyāvatī dīkṣā saṅkṣepeṇaiva likhyate  Hbhv bhūmiṃ saṃskṛtya tasyāṅ cārcayitvā vāstudevatāḥ saptahastamitaṃ kuryān maṇḍapaṃ ramyavedikam  Hbhv aṣṭadhvajaṃ caturdhāraṃ kṣīrapādapatoraṇam triguṇīkṛtasūtrāḍhyaṃ kuśamālābhiveṣṭitam  Hbhv atha kuṇḍanirmāṇavidhiḥtasmiṃś ca diśi kauveryāṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ trimekhalam kuṇḍe kuryāc caturviṃśatyaṅgulipramitaṃ budhah  Hbhv khātaṃ trimekhalocchrāyasahitaṃ tāvad ācaret tasmāt khātād bahiḥ kuryāt kaṇṭham ekāṅgulaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv tatrādymekhalocchrāyavistārau caturaṅgulau tryaṅgulau tau dvitīyāyās tṛtīyāyā yugāṅgulau  Hbhv yoniṃ ca paścime bhāge mekhalātritayopari ṣaḍaṅgulāṃ ca vistāre dairghye ca dvādaśāṅgulām  Hbhv ekāṅgulāṃ tathocchrāye madhye chidrasamanvitām gadādharākṛtiṃ kuryād vidhivan mekhalānvitām  Hbhv śatārdhahome kuṇḍaṃ syād ūrdhvamuṣṭikaronmitam  Hbhv śatahomeratnimātram sahasre pāṇinā mitam lakṣe caturbhir hastaiś ca koṭau tair aṣṭabhir mitam caturasraṃ kuṇḍakhātaṃ kurvītādhaś ca tādṛśam  Hbhv homas tv adhikasaṅkhākaḥ kuṇḍe vai nyūnasaṅkhyayā kṛte kāryo na c anyūnasaṅkhyākaḥ saṅkhayādhike  Hbhv yathāvidhy eva kartavyaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatnena dhīmatā anyathā bahavo doṣā bhaveyur bahuduḥkhadāḥ  Hbhv tad uktaṃ tāntrikaiḥevaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ kuṇḍam iṣṭaphalapradam anekadoṣadaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatra nyūnādhikām bhavet  Hbhv tasmāt samyak parīkṣyaiva kartavyaṃ śubham icchatā hastamātraṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vā saṃkṣipte homakarmaṇi  Hbhv hārītenāpi vistārādhikyahīnatve alpāyur jāyate dhruvam khātādhikye bhaved yogī hīne tu dhanasaṃkṣayaḥ kuṇḍe vakre ca santāpo maraṇaṃ chinnamekhale  Hbhv śokas tu mekhalonatve tadādhikye paśukṣayaḥ bhāryānāśo yonihīne kaṇṭhahīne śubhakṣayaḥ  Hbhv aṅguliparimāṇaṃ coktamtiryagyavodarāṇyaṣṭāv ūrdhvā vā brīhayas trayaḥ jñeyam aṅgulimānaṃ tu madhyamā madhyaparvaṇā  Hbhv  iti viśeṣo pekṣito nyatra sraksruvaprakriyādikaḥ jñeyo granthāntarāt so trādhikyabhītyā na likhyate  Hbhv atha dīkṣāmaṇḍalavidhiḥathokṣite pañcagavyair gandhāmbhobhiś ca maṇḍape yathāvidhi likhed dīkṣāmaṇḍalaṃ vedikopari  Hbhv tanmadhye cāṣṭapatrābjaṃ bahir vṛttatrayaṃ tataḥ tato rāśīṃs tataḥ pīṭhaṃ catuṣpādasamanvitam  Hbhv tasmād bahiś caturdikṣu likhed vīthīcatuṣṭayam śobhāpaśobhākoṇāḍhyaṃ tato dvāracatuṣṭayam  Hbhv atha dīkṣāṅgapūjāprātaḥkṛtyaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā yathāsthānaṃ nyaset tataḥ śaṅkhaṃ pūjopacārāṃś ca purolekhyaprakārataḥ  Hbhv tatrādau kumbhasthāpanavidhiḥgurūn gaṇeśaṃ cābhyarcya pīṭhapūjāṃ vidhāya ca padmamadhye nyaset śālīṃs taṇḍulāṃś ca kuśāṃs tathā  Hbhv vahner daśakalā yādivarṇādyāś ca kuśopari nyasyābhyarcya japaṃs tāraṃ nyaset kumbhaṃ yathoditam  Hbhv tāś coktāḥdhūmrārcir uṣmā jvalanī jvālinī visphuliṅinī suśrīḥ surūpā kapilā havyakavyavahe api  Hbhv  iti kādyaṣṭhāntair yutā bhādyair ḍāntaiś cārṇair vilomagaiḥ sūryasya ca kalāḥ kumbhe dvādaśa nyasya pūjayet  Hbhv adhunā tasmin kuṇḍe sūryakalānāṃ nyāsādikaṃ likhatikādyair iti kakārādyaiṣ ṭhakārāntair arṇair varṇair yutā dvādaśāpi kalāḥ cakāraḥ samuccaye bhakārādyair ḍakārāntair varṇair api yutāḥ nanu bhakārādīnāṃ dvādaśavarṇānāṃ ḍakārāntatā kathaṃ syāt krameṇa kṣakārāntatāprāptes tatrāhavilomagaiḥ vyutkramaprāptaiḥ  ayam arthaḥanulomapaṭhitakakārādyaikaikam akṣaraṃ pratilomapaṭhitabhakārādyekaikākṣareṇa sahitam ādau sūryakalāsu saṃyojya nyāsādikaṃ  kuryād iti  prayogaś ca kaṃ bhaṃ tapanyai nama ity ādi  Hbhv tāś coktāḥtapanī tāpanī dhūmrā bhrāmarī jvālinī ruciḥ suṣumṇā bhogadā viśvā bodhinī dhāriṇī kṣamā  Hbhv  iti kubmhāntar nikṣipen mūlamantreṇa kusumaṃ sitam sākṣataṃ sasitaṃ svarṇaṃ saratnaṃ ca kuśāṃs tathā  Hbhv tataś coktaprakāreṇādhārarūpam agniṃ kumbharūpaṃ sūryaṃ ca vicintya kumbhasya tasya antar madhye śuklakusumādikaṃ kṣipet sasitaṃ saśarkaram  tad uktamprottolayitvā tanmadhye śuklapuṣpaṃ sitāyutam svarṇaṃ ratnaṃ ca kūrcaṃ ca mūlenaiva vinikṣipet  iti yac ca mūlagranthārthād adhikaṃ kiṃcil likhatetat pūrvagatasya yathoditam ity asyānuvartanād iti jñeyam  Hbhv kumbhaṃ ca vidhinā tīrthāmbunā śuddhena pūrayet jale cendukulā nyasya sasvarāḥ ṣoḍaśārcayet  Hbhv tāś coktāḥamṛtā mānadā pūṣā tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭī ratir dhṛtiḥ śaśinī candrikā kāntir jyotsnā śrīḥ prītir aṅgadā pūrṇā pūrṇāmṛtā ca  Hbhv  iti śuddhāmbupūrite śaṅkhe kṣiptvā gandhāṣṭakaṃ kalāḥ āvāhya sarvās tāḥ prāṇapratiṣṭhām ācaret kramāt  Hbhv gandhāṣṭakaṃ coktamuśīraṃ kuṅkumaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bālakaṃ cāgurur murā jaṭāmāṃsī candanaṃ cetīṣṭaṃ gandhāṣṭakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv  iti kaiścic candanakarpūrāgurukuṅkumarocanāḥ kakkolakapimāṃsyaś ca gandhāṣṭakam idaṃ matam  Hbhv tathaivākārajā varṇaiḥ kādibhir daśabhir daśa ukārajāṣṭakārādyaiḥ pakārādyair makārajāḥ  Hbhv catasro bindujāḥ ṣādyaiś caturbhir nādajāḥ kalāḥ svaraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhir yuktā nyasec chaṅkhe ca ṣoḍaśa  Hbhv tāś coktāḥsṛṣṭir ṛddhiḥ smṛtir medhā kāntir lakṣmīr dhṛitḥ sthirā sthitiḥ siddhir akārotthāḥ kalā daśa samīritaḥ  Hbhv jarā ca pālinī śāntir aiśvarī ratikāmike varadā hlādinī prītir dīrghā cokārajāḥ kalāḥ  Hbhv tīkṣṇā raudrā bhayā nidrā tantīr kṣut krodhanī kriyā utkārī caiva mṛtyuś ca makārākṣarajāḥ kalāḥ  Hbhv nivṛttiś ca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntis tathaiva ca indhikā dīpikā caiva recikā mocikā parā  Hbhv sūkṣmā sūkṣmāmṛtā jñānājñānā cāpy āyanī tathā vyāpinī vyomarūpā ca anantā nādasambhavāḥ  Hbhv  iti nyāsaṃ kalānāṃ sarvāsāṃ kuryād ekaikaśaḥ kramāt nāmoccārya caturthāntaṃ tattadvarṇair namo ntakam  Hbhv pūrvaṃ prāṇapratiṣṭhāyās tāsām āvāhanāt param ṛcaḥ pañca yathāsthānaṃ paṭhet tāś cārcayet kalāḥ  Hbhv haṃśaḥ śuciṣad ity ādau pratad viṣṇus tataḥ param tryambakaṃ tat savitur viṣṇur yonim iti kramāt  Hbhv tac ca śaṅkhodakaṃ kumbhe mūlamantreṇa nikṣipet pidadhyāt tan mukhaṃ śakravallīcūtādipallavaiḥ  Hbhv śarāVenātha puṣpādiyuktenācchādya tat punaḥ saṃveṣṭya vastrayugmena tataḥ kumbhaṃ ca maṇḍayet  Hbhv atha kumbhe śrībhagavatpūjāvidhiḥtasminn āvāhya kalase paraṃ tejo yathāvidhi sakalīkṛtya cācāryaḥ pūjayed āsanādibhiḥ  Hbhv sakalīkaraṇaṃ coktamdevatāṅge ṣaḍaṅgānāṃ nyāsaḥ syāt sakalīkṛtiḥ  Hbhv kecic cāhuḥ karanyāsau vinākhilaiḥ nyāsais tattejasaḥ sāṅgīkaraṇaṃ sakalīkṛtaḥ  Hbhv evaṃ ca kumbhe taṃ sāṅgopāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ prabhum agrato lekhyavidhinārcayed bhojyārpaṇāvadhi  Hbhv naivedyārpaṇataḥ paścān maṇḍalasya ca sarvataḥ sadīpān paiṣṭikān nyasyet sabījāṅkurabhājanāt  Hbhv atha dīkṣāhomavidhiḥtato dīkṣāṅgahomārthaṃ kuṇḍalasya ca sarvataḥ saṃmārjya darbhamārjanyā yathāvidhy upalepayet  Hbhv vikīrya sarṣapāṃs tatra gavyaiḥ samprokṣya pañcabhiḥ madhye sampūjayed vāstupuruṣaṃ dikṣu tatpatīn  Hbhv śoṣaṇādīni kuṇḍasya kṛtvā prokṣya kuśāmbubhiḥ ullikhya cāsmin yonyādisahitaṃ maṇḍalaṃ likhet  Hbhv śrībījaṃ madhyayonau ca vilikhyābhukṣya pūjayet nidhāya tatra puṣpādiviṣṭaraṃ sādhu kalpayet  Hbhv tatra lakṣmīmṛtyusnānāṃ viṣṇuṃ cāvāhya pūjayet tāmrādipātreṇānīyāgrato gniṃ sthāpayec chubhram  Hbhv gandhādināgnim abhyarcya viṣṇoḥ sakrīḍataḥ śriyā athāṅgadevatāḥsahasrārciḥ svastipūrṇa uttiṣṭhapuruṣas tathā dhūmavyāpī saptajihvo dhanurdhara iti smṛtaḥ  Hbhv aṣṭamūrtayaś cajātavedāḥ saptajihvo havyavāhana eva ca aśvodarajasaṃjñaś ca tathā vaiśvānaro paraḥ kaumāratejāś ca tathā viśvadevamukhāhvayau  Hbhv  iti tato vahniṃ paristīrya saṃskṛtājyaṃ yathāvidhi hutvā ca vyāhṛtīḥ paścāt trīn vārān juhuyāt punaḥ  Hbhv tato sya garbhadhānādīn vivhāntān yathākramam saṃskārān ācared uktamantreṇāṣṭāhutais tathā  Hbhv itthaṃ hi saṃskṛte vahnau pīṭham abhyarcya tatra ca devam āvāhya gandhādidīpāntavidhinārcayet  Hbhv taṃ cāgniṃ devarasanāṃ saṃkalpyāṣṭottaraṃ budhaḥ sahasraṃ juhuyāt sarpiḥśarkarāpāyasair yutaiḥ  Hbhv hutvājyenātha mahatīvyāhṛtīr vidhinā kṛtī graharkṣakaraṇādibhyo baliṃ dadyād yathoditam  Hbhv atha homadravyādiparimāṇamkarṣamātraṃ ghṛtaṃ home śuktimātraṃ payaḥ smṛtam uktāni pañcagavyāni tatsamāni manīṣibhiḥ  Hbhv tatsamaṃ madhudugdhānnam akṣamātram udāhṛtam dadhi prasṛtimātraṃ syāt lājāḥ syuḥ muṣṭisaṃmitāḥ  Hbhv  ity ādi atha natvāmbupānārthaṃ pradāyācamanāni ca ātmārpaṇāntam abhyarcya lekhyena vidhinācaret  Hbhv atha guruśiṣyaniyamādiḥvratasthaṃ vāgyataṃ śiṣyaṃ praveśyātha yathāvidhi taddehe mātṛkāṃ sāṅgāṃ nyasyāthopadiśec ca tām  Hbhv devaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ kumbhagataṃ cānusmaran guruḥ japtvāṣṭottarasāhasraṃ śayīta prāśya kiṃcana  Hbhv darbhoparyajine tvaiṇe niviṣṭo mātṛkāṃ smaran guruṃ ca śiṣyo nidrāṇaṃ tāṃ śayīta japan vratī  Hbhv iti pūrvadinakṛtyam atha taddinakṛtyāniprātaḥkṛtyaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā kumbhaṃ cābhyarcya pūrvavat hutvā dattvā baliṃ karmānyat kuryāt svārpaṇāvadhi  Hbhv saṃhāramudrayā kṛṣṇe saṃyojyāvṛttidevatāḥ tam cāmṛtamayaṃ dhyātvā svasmiṃś cāgniṃ vilāpayet  Hbhv dhvajatoraṇadikkumbhamaṇḍapādyadhidevatāḥ sarvā vibhāvya cidrūpāḥ kumbhe saṃyojya pūjayet  Hbhv ato guruṃ ca bhagavaddṛṣṭyā parikramya praṇamya ca dattvoktāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ tasmai svaśarīraṃ samarpayet  Hbhv atha dīkṣāṅgapūjātathā ca daśamaskandhe BhP  iyad eva hi sacchiṣyaiḥ kartavyaṃ guruniṣkṛtam yad vai viśuddhabhāvena sarvārthātmārpaṇaṃ gurau  Hbhv athābhiṣecanavidhiḥyāgālayād uttarasyām āśāyāṃ snānamaṇḍape pīṭhe niveśya taṃ śiṣyaṃ kārayec choṣaṇādikam  Hbhv pīṭhanyāsāntam akhilaṃ mātṛkānyāsapūrvakam nyāsaṃ śiṣyatanau kṛtvā pīṭhamantreṇa pūjayet  Hbhv sadūrvākṣatapuṣpāṃ ca mūrdhni śiṣyasya rocanām nidhāya kalasaṃ tasyāntike vādyādinā nayet  Hbhv śrīkṛṣṇam atha samprārthya guruḥ kumbhasya vāsasā nīrājya śiṣyaṃ tanmūrdhni nyaset tatpallavādikam  Hbhv tad uktamvidhivat kumbham uddhṛtya tanmukhasthān suradrumān śiśoḥ śirasi vinyasya mātṛkāṃ manasā japet  Hbhv tataḥ kumbhāmbhasā śiṣyaṃ prokṣya trir mūlamantrataḥ viprāśīr maṅgalodghoṣair abhiṣiñcen manūn paṭhan  Hbhv athābhiṣekamantrāḥvaśiṣṭhasaṃhitāyāmsurās tvām abhiṣiñcyaṃ tu brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ vāsudevo jagannāthas tathā saṅkarṣaṇo vibhuḥ  Hbhv pradyumnaś cāniruddhaś ca bhavantu vibhavāya te ākhaṇḍalo gnir bhagavān yamo vai nirṛtis tathā  Hbhv varuṇaḥ pavanaś caiva dhanādhyakṣas tathā śivaḥ brahmaṇā sahitā hy ete dikpālāḥ pāntu vaḥ sadā  Hbhv kīrtir lakṣmīr dhṛtir medhā puṣṭiḥ śraddhā kriyā gatiḥ buddhir lajjā vapuḥ śāntir māyā nidrā ca bhāvanā  Hbhv etās tvām abhiṣiñcantu rāhuḥ ketuś ca pūjitāḥ devadānavagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ  Hbhv ṛṣayo munayo gāvo devamātara eva ca devapatnyo dhruvā nāgā daityā apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ  Hbhv astrāṇi sarvaśastrāṇi rājāno vāhanāni ca auṣadhāni ca ratnāni kālasyāvayavāś ca ye  Hbhv saritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailās tīrthāni jaladā nadāḥ ete tvām abhiṣiñcantu dharmakāmārthasiddhaye  Hbhv atha mantrakathanavidhiḥparidhāyāṃśuke śiṣya ācānto yāgamaṇḍape gatvā bhaktyā guruṃ natvā guror āsīta dakṣiṇe  Hbhv guruḥ samarpya gandhādīn puruṣāhārasaṃmitam nivedya pāyasaṃ kṛṣṇe kuryāt puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ  Hbhv sāmpradāyikamudrādibhūṣitaṃ taṃ kṛtāñjalim pañcāṅgapramukhair nyāsaiḥ kuryāt śrīkṛṣṇasācchiśum  Hbhv nyasya pāṇitalaṃ mūrdhni tasya karṇe ca dakṣiṇe ṛṣyādiyuktaṃ vidhavan mantraṃ vāratrayaṃ vadet  Hbhv dīrghamantraṃ ca śiṣyasya yāvad āgrahaṇaṃ paṭhet ca gavāśvatthāgnimadhyagam bhāvayed daivataṃ viṣṇuṃ guruvipraśarīragam  Hbhv yatra yatra parivādo mātsaryāc chrūyate guroḥ tatra tatra na vastavyaṃ niryāyāt saṃsmaran harim  Hbhv yaiḥ kṛtā ca guror nindā vibhoḥ śāstrasya nārada nāpi taiḥ saha vastavyaṃ vaktavyaṃ vā kathañcana  Hbhv pradakṣiṇe prayāṇe ca pradāne ca viśeṣataḥ prabhāte ca pravāse ca svamantraṃ bahuśaḥ smaret  Hbhv svapne Hbhv kāṃsyapātre na bhuñjīta na plakṣabaṭapatrayoḥ devāgāre na niṣṭhīvet kṣutaṃ cātra vivarjayet na sopānatkacaraṇaḥ praviśed antaraṃ kvacit  Hbhv ekādaśyāṃ na cāśnīyāt pakṣayor ubhayor api jāgaraṃ vidhṛtiś caraṇāmṛtasevanam tulasīmaṇimālādibhūṣādhāraṇam anvaham  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilāpūjā pratimāsu ca bhaktitaḥ nirmālyatulasībhakṣas tulasyavacayo vidheḥ  Hbhv vidhinā tāntrikī sandhyā śikhābandho hi karmaṇi viṣṇupādodakenaiva pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇakriyā mahārājopacāraiś ca śaktyāṃ sampūjanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv viṣṇubhaktyavirodhena nityanaimittikī kriyā bhūtaśuddhyādikaraṇaṃ nyāsāḥ sarve yathāvidhi  Hbhv navīnaphalapuṣpāder bhaktitaḥ saṃnivedanam tulasīpūjanaṃ nityaṃ śrībhāgavatapūjanam  Hbhv trikālaṃ viṣṇupūjā ca purāṇaśrutir anvaham viṣṇor niveditānāṃ vai vastrādīnāṃ ca dhāraṇam  Hbhv sarveṣāṃ śayanādyupacāraś ca rāmādīnāṃ ca cintanam  Hbhv sandhyayoḥ śayanaṃ naiva na śaucaṃ mṛttikāṃ vinā tiṣṭhatācamanaṃ naiva tathā gurvāsanāsanam  Hbhv gurvagre pādavistāracchāyāyā laṅghanaṃ guroḥ śaktau caikādaśīdine  Hbhv dvādaśyāṃ ca divāsvāpas tulasyāvacayas tathā tatra viṣṇor divāsnānaṃ śrāddhaṃ haryaniveditaiḥ  Hbhv vṛddhāv atulasīśrāddhaṃ tathā śrāddham avaiṣṇavam caraṇāmṛtapānepi Hbhv prasādāgrahaṇaṃ viṣṇor varjayed vaiṣṇavaḥ sadā catuḥśataṃ vidhīn etān niṣedhān śrāvayed guruḥ  Hbhv aṅgīkāre kṛte bāḍhaṃ tannīrājanapūrvakam devapūjāṃ kārayitvā dakṣakarṇe mantraṃ japet  Hbhv Hbhv atha varāhapurāṇoktadīkṣāvidhiḥidānīṃ śṛṇu me devi pañcapātakanāśanam yajanaṃ devadevasya viṣṇoḥ putravasupradam  Hbhv iha janmani dāridryavyādhikuṣṭhādipīḍitaḥ alakṣmīvān aputras tu yo bhavet puruṣo bhuvi tasya sadyo bhavel lakṣmīr āyur vittaṃ sutāḥ sukham  Hbhv dṛṣṭvā tu maṇḍale devi devaṃ devyā samanvitam nārāyaṇaṃ paraṃ devaṃ yaḥ paśyati vidhānataḥ  Hbhv pūjitaṃ navanābhe tu ṣoḍaśābjadale tathā ācāryadarśitaṃ devaṃ mantramūrtim ayonijam  Hbhv kārttike māsi śuddhāyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ sarvāsu ca yajed devaṃ dvādaśīṣu vidhānataḥ  Hbhv saṅkrāntau ca mahābhāge candrasūryagrahepi vā yaḥ paśyati hariṃ devaṃ pūjitaṃ guruṇā śubhe tasya sadyo bhavet tuṣṭiḥ pāpadhvaṃso py aśeṣataḥ  Hbhv sa sāmānyo hi devānāṃ bhavatīti na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca parīkṣaṇam saṃvatsaraṃ guruḥ kuryāj jātiśaucakriyādibhiḥ  Hbhv upasannāṃs tato jñātvā hṛdayenāvadhārayet tepi bhaktimato jñātvā ātmanaḥ parameśvaram saṃvatsaraṃ guror bhaktiṃ kuryur viṣṇāv ivācalām  Hbhv saṃvatsaraṃ tataḥ pūrṇe guruṃ caiva prasādayet  Hbhv bhagavaṃs tvatprasādena saṃsārārṇavatāraṇam icchāmas tv aihikīṃ lakṣmīṃ viśeṣeṇa tapodhana  Hbhv evam abhyarthya medhāvī guruṃ viṣṇum ivāgrataḥ abhyarcya tadanujñāto daśamyāṃ kārttikasya tu  Hbhv kṣīravṛkṣasamudbhūtaṃ mantritaṃ parameṣṭhinā bhakṣayitvā śayītorvyāṃ devadevasya sannidhau  Hbhv svapnān dṛṣṭvā guror agre śrāvayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ tataḥ śubhāśubhaṃ tadvad ālapet paramo guruḥ ekādaśyām upoṣyātha snātvā devālayaṃ vrajet  Hbhv guruś ca maṇḍalaṃ bhūmau kalptāyāṃ tu vartayet lakṣaṇair vividhair bhūmiṃ lakṣayitvā praveśayet  Hbhv navanābhaṃ yadā kuryān maṇḍalaṃ varṇakair budhaḥ tadānīṃ pūrvato devam indram aindryāṃ tu pūjayet  Hbhv lokapālam athāgneyyām agniṃ sampūjayed dvijaḥ yamaṃ tad anu yāmyāyāṃ nairṛtyāṃ nirṛtiṃ nyaset vāruṇyāṃ varuṇaṃ caiva vāyavyāṃ pavanaṃ yajet  Hbhv dhanadaṃ cottare nyasya rudram aiśānagocare sampūjyaivaṃ vidhānena dikpatreṣu viśeṣataḥ adhaḥpatre tathā viṣṇum arcayet parameśvaram  Hbhv pūrvapatre balaṃ pūjya pradyumnaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā aniruddhaṃ tathā pūjya paścime cottare tathā pūjayed vāsudevaṃ tu sarvapātakaśāntidam  Hbhv aiśānyāṃ vinyasec chaṅkham āgneyyāṃ cakram eva ca saumyāyāṃ tu gadā pūjyā vāyavyāṃ padmam eva ca  Hbhv nairṛtyāṃ muṣalaṃ pūjyaṃ dakṣiṇe garuḍaṃ tathā vāmato vinyasel lakṣmīṃ devadevasya buddhimān  Hbhv dhanuś caiva ca khaḍgaṃ ca devasya purato nyaset śrīvatsaṃ kaustubhaṃ caiva devasya purato rcayet  Hbhv evaṃ pūjya yathānyāyaṃ devadevaṃ janārdanam diṅmaṇḍale ca vinyasya cāṣṭau kumbhān vidhānataḥ vaiṣṇavaṃ kalasaṃ caiva navamaṃ tatra kalpayet  Hbhv snāpayen muktikāmāṃs tu vaiṣṇavena ghaṭena tu śrīkāmān snāpayet tadvad aindreṇātha ghaṭena tu  Hbhv jayapratāpakāmāṃs tu āgneyenābhiṣecayet mṛtyuñjayavidhānena yāmyena snāpanaṃ tathā  Hbhv duṣṭapradhvaṃsnāyālaṃ nairṛtena vidhīyate śāntaye vāruṇyenātha pāpanāśāya vāyavam  Hbhv dravyasampattikāmasya kauvareṇa vidhīyate raudreṇa jñānahetus tu lokapālaghaṭās tv ime  Hbhv ekaikena naraḥ snātaḥ sarvapāpavarjitaḥ bhaved avyāhatajñānaḥ śrīmāṃś ca puruṣaḥ sadā  Hbhv kiṃ punar navabhiḥ snāto naraḥ pātakavarjitaḥ jāyate viṣṇusadṛśaḥ sadyo rājāthavā punaḥ  Hbhv athavā dikṣu sarvāsu yathāsaṅkhyena lokapān pūjayet svasvanāmnā tu ṣaḍbhinnena vidhānataḥ  Hbhv evaṃ sampūjya devāṃs tu lokapālān prasannadhīḥ paścāt parīkṣitān śiṣyān baddhanetrān praveśayet  Hbhv āgneyadhāraṇādagdhān vāyunā vidhūtāṃs tataḥ somenāpy āyitān paścāc chrāvayen niyamān budhaḥ  Hbhv na ninded abrāhmaṇān devān viṣṇuṃ brāhmaṇam eva ca rudram ādiyam agniṃ ca lokapālān grahāṃs tathā vandeta vaiṣṇavaṃ cāpi puruṣaṃ pūrvadīkṣitam  Hbhv evaṃ tu samayān śrāvya paścād dhomaṃ tu kārayet tattvāni śiṣyadeheṣu vinyasya ca viśodhayet  Hbhv oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarvarūpiṇe huṃ svāhā  Hbhv ṣoḍaśākṣaramantreṇa homayej jvalitānalaḥ garbhādhānādikāś caiva kriyāḥ sarvāś ca kārayet  Hbhv tribhis tribhir āhutibhir devadevasya sannidhau tato panīya dṛgbandhaṃ puraḥ śiṣyaṃ niveśya ca prāyaḥ pūrvoktavidhinā mantraṃ tasmai gurur diśet  Hbhv homānte dīkṣitaḥ paścād dāpayed gurudakṣiṇām hastyaśvaratnakaṭakaṃ hemagrāmādikaṃ nṛpaḥ  Hbhv dāpayed gurave prājño madhyamo madhyamāṃ tathā dāpayed itaro yugmaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ yathāvidhi  Hbhv evaṃ kṛte tu yat puṇyaṃ māhātmyaṃ jāyate dhare tad aśakyaṃ tu gaditum api varṣaśatair api  Hbhv dīkṣitātmā guror bhūtvā vārāhaṃ śṛṇuyād yadi tena vedāḥ purāṇāni sarve mantrāḥ susaṅgrahāḥ  Hbhv japtāḥ syuḥ puṣkare tīrthe prayāge sindhusāgare devahūte kurukṣetre vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv graheṇa viṣuve caiva yat phalaṃ japatāṃ bhavet tat phalaṃ dviguṇaṃ tasya dīkṣito yaḥ śṛṇoti ca  Hbhv devā api tapaḥ kṛtvā dhyāyanti ca vadanti ca kadā me bhārate varṣe janma syād bhūtadhāriṇi  Hbhv dīkṣitāś ca bhaviṣyāmo vārāhaṃ śṛṇumaḥ kadā vārāhaṃ ṣoḍaśātmānaṃ yuktā dehe kadācana paśyāmaḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ yad gatvā na punar bhavet  Hbhv evaṃ jalpanti vibudhā manasā cintayanti ca vārāhayāgaṃ kārttikyāṃ kadā drakṣyāmahe dhare  Hbhv eṣa te vidhir uddiṣṭo mayā te bhūtadhāriṇi devagandharvayakṣāṇāṃ sarvathā durlabho hy asau  Hbhv evaṃ yo vetti tattvena yaś ca paśyati maṇḍalam yaś cemaṃ śṛṇuyād devi sarve muktā iti śrutiḥ  Hbhv atha saṅkṣiptadīkṣāsaṅkṣiptaś cātha dīkṣāyā vidhir eṣa vilikhyate mukhyakalpe hy aśaktasya janasya syād dhitāya ca  Hbhv sumuhūrtetha samprāpte sarvatobhadramaṇḍale nūtanaṃ gandhapuṣpādimaṇḍitaṃ kalasaṃ nyaset  Hbhv vastrāvṛtaṃ payaḥ pūrṇaṃ pañcapallavasaṃyutam sarvauṣadhipañcaratnamṛtsnāsaptakagarbhitam  Hbhv mṛttikāś ca saptoktāḥaśvasthānād gajasthānād valmīkāc ca catuṣpathāt rājadvārāc ca goṣṭhāc ca nadyāḥ kūlān mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ  Hbhv  iti kṛṣṇam abhyarcya taṃ kumbhaṃ kuśakūrcena deśikaḥ deyamantreṇa sāṣṭaṃ tu sahasram abhimantrayet  Hbhv tadadbhiḥ pūrvavac chiṣyam abhiṣicya diśen manum śiṣyo rcayed guruṃ bhaktyā yathāśakti dvijān api  Hbhv athopadeśas tattvasāgareatrāpy aśaktaḥ kaścic ced abjam abhyarcya sākṣatam tadambhasābhiṣicyāṣṭa vārān mūlena ke karam  Hbhv nidhāyāmuṃ japet karṇe upadeśeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ candrasūryagrahe tīrthe siddhakṣetre śivālaye mantramātraprakathanam upadeśaḥ sa ucyate  Hbhv tatra tatraiva viśeṣaḥ śrīnāradapañcarātre vittalobhād vimuktasya svalpavittasya dehinaḥ saṃsārabhayabhītasya viṣṇubhaktasya tattvataḥ  Hbhv agnāv ājyānvite bījaiḥ salilaiḥ kevalaiś ca vā dravyahīnasya kurvīta vacasānugrahaṃ guruḥ  Hbhv yaḥ samaḥ sarvabhūteṣu virāgo vītamatsaraḥ jitendriyaḥ śucir dakṣaḥ sarvāṅgāvayavānvitaḥ  Hbhv karmaṇā manasā vācā bhīte cābhayadaḥ sadā samabuddhipadaṃ prāptas tatrāpi bhagavanmayaḥ  Hbhv pañcakālaparaś caiva pañcarātrārthavit tathā viṣṇutattvaṃ parijñāya ekaṃ cānekabhedagam vīkṣayen medinīṃ sarvāṃ kiṃ punaś copasannatān  Hbhv atha mantradānamāhātmyamskānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde iha kīrtiṃ vadānyatvaṃ prajāvṛddhiṃ dhanaṃ sukham vidyādānena labhate sāttviko nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv yathā surāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ paramaḥ parameśvaraḥ tathaiva sarvadānānāṃ vidyādānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam  Hbhv yāvac ca pātakaṃ tena kṛtaṃ janmaśatair api tat sarvaṃ nāśam āpnoti vidyādānena dehinām  Hbhv vidyādānāt paraṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati yena dattena cāpnoti śivaṃ paramakāraṇam  Hbhv iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāsedaikṣiko nāma dvitīyo vilāsaḥ   SauciyaVilasatṛtīyavilāsaḥśaucīyaḥvandenantādbhutaiśvaryaṃ śrīcaitanyaṃ mahāprabhum nīco pi yatprasādāt syāt sadācārapravartakaḥ  Hbhv puṃso gṛhītadīkṣasya śrīkṛṣṇaṃ pūjayiṣyataḥ ācāro likhyate kṛtyaṃ śrutismṛtyanusārataḥ  Hbhv atha dīkṣitasya pūjāyā nityatālabdhvā mantraṃ tu yo nityaṃ nārcayen mantradevatām sarvakarmaphalaṃ tasyāniṣṭaṃ yacchati devatā  Hbhv atha sadācāraḥna kiñcit kasyacit sidhyet sadācāraṃ vinā yataḥ tasmād avaśyaṃ sarvatra sadācāro hy apekṣyate  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe ViP  vaṛṇāśramācaravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyat tattoṣakāraṇam  Hbhv atha sadācārasya nityatāmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe śrīmadālasālarkasaṃvādegṛhasthena sadā kāryam ācāraparipālanam na hy ācāravihīnasya sukham atra paratra ca  Hbhv yajñadānatapāṃsīha puruṣasya na bhūtaye bhavanti yaḥ sadācāraṃ samullaṅghya pravartate  Hbhv bhaviṣyottare ca śrīkṛṣṇayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvādeācārahīnaṃ na punanti vedāḥyadyapy adhītāḥ saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥ chandāṃsy enaṃ mṛtyukāle tyajantinīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jātapakṣāḥ  Hbhv kapālasthaṃ yathā toyaṃ śvadṛtau vā yathā payaḥ duṣṭaṃ syāt sthānadoṣeṇa vṛttahīne tathāśubham ācārarahito rājan neha nāmutra nindati  Hbhv  iti lekhyena smaraṇādīnāṃ nityatvenaiva setsyati smaraṇādyātmakasyāpi sadācārasya nityatā  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe  tatraiva gṛhidharmaprasaṅge sadācāravatā puṃsā jitau lokāv ubhāv api  Hbhv sādhavaḥ kṣīṇadoṣās tu sacchabdaḥ sādhuvācakaḥ teṣām ācaraṇaṃ yat tu sadācāraḥ sa ucyate  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍe skandāgastyasaṃvādeanadhyayanaśīlaṃ ca sadācāravilaṅghinam sālasyaṃ ca durannādaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ bādhatentakaḥ  Hbhv tato bhyaset prayatnena sadācāraṃ sadā dvijaḥ tīrthāny apy abhilaṣyanti sadācārasamāgamam  Hbhv bhaviṣyottare ca tatraivaācāraprabhavo dharmaḥ santaś cācāralakṣaṇāḥ sādhūnāṃ ca yathā vṛttaṃ sa sadācāra iṣyate  Hbhv tasmāt kuryāt sadācāraṃ ya icched gatim ātmanaḥ sarvalakṣaṇahīno pi samucācāravān nṛpa śraddadhāno nasūyaś ca sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv kiṃ caācāra eva dharmasya mūlaṃ rājan kulasya ca ācārād vicyuto jantur na kulīno na dhārmikaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ caācāro bhūtijanana ācāraḥ kīrtivardhanaḥ ācārād vardhate hy āyur ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam  Hbhv ācāra eva nṛpapuṅgava sevyamānodharmārthakāmaphalado bhaviteha puṃsām tasmāt sadaiva viduṣāvahitena rājanśāstrodito hy anudinaṃ paripālanīyaḥ  Hbhv atha tatra nityakṛtyānibrāhme muhūrta utthāya kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kīrtayan prakṣālya pāṇipādau ca dantadhāvanam ācaret  Hbhv ācamya vasanaṃ rātres tyaktvānyat paridhāya ca punar ācamane kuryāl lekhyena vidhināgrataḥ  Hbhv athecchan paramāṃ śuddhiṃ mūrdhni dhyātvā guroḥ padau stutvā ca kīrtayan kṛṣṇaṃ smaraṃś caitad udīrayet  Hbhv atha prātaḥsmaraṇakīrtanejayati jananivāso devakījanmavādoyaduvarapariṣat svair dorbhir asyann adharmam sthiracaravṛjinaghnaḥ susmita śrīmukhenavrajapuravanitānāṃ vardhayan kāmadevam  Hbhv BhP smṛte sakalakalyāṇabhājanaṃ yatra jāyate puruṣas tam ajaṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim  Hbhv vidagdhagopālavilāsinīnāṃsambhogacihnāṅkitasarvagātram pavitram āmnāyagirām agamyaṃbrahma prapadye navanītacauram  Hbhv daśamaskandhe BhP  udgāyatīnām aravindalocanaṃvrajāṅganānāṃ divam aspṛśad dhvaniḥ dadhnaś ca nirmanthanaśabdamiśritonirasyate yena diśām amaṅgalam  Hbhv  iti paṭhet punaś ca sādhūnāṃ sampradāyānusārataḥ catuḥślokīm imāṃ sarvadoṣaśāntyai śubhāptaye  Hbhv prātaḥ smarāmi bhavabhītimahārtiśāntyainārāyaṇaṃ garuḍavāhanam abjanābham grāhābhibhūtavaravārivāraṇamuktihetuṃcakrāyudhaṃ taruṇavārijapatranetram  Hbhv prātar namāmi manasā vacasā ca mūrdhnāpādāravindayugalaṃ paramasya puṃsaḥ nārāyaṇasya narakārṇavatāraṇasyapārāyaṇapravaṇavipraparāyaṇasya  Hbhv prātar bhajāmi bhajatām abhayaṅkaraṃ taṃprāk sarvajanmakṛtapāpabhayāvahatyai yo grāhavaktrapatitāṅghrigajendraghoraśokapraṇāśam akarod dhṛtaśaṅkhacakraḥ  Hbhv ślokatrayam idaṃ puṇyaṃ prātaḥ prātaḥ paṭhet tu yaḥ lokatrayagurus tasmai dadyād ātmapadaṃ hariḥ  Hbhv  iti tad etal likhitaṃ kutra kutracid vyavahārataḥ kintu svābhīṣṭarūpādi śrīkṛṣṇasya vicintayet  Hbhv itthaṃ vidadhyād bhagavatkīrtanasmaraṇādikam sarvatīrthābhiṣekaṃ vai bahir antarviśodhanam  Hbhv tathā ca skānde skandaṃ prati śrīśivoktausakṛn nārāyaṇaety uktvā pumān kalpaśatatrayam gaṅgādisarvatīrtheṣu snāto bhavati putraka  Hbhv anyatra caśayanād utthito yas tu kīrtayen madhusūdanam kīrtanāt tasya pāpasya nāśam āyāty aśeṣataḥ  Hbhv  iti māhātmyaṃ kīrtanasyāgre lekhyaṃ mukhyaprasaṅgataḥ smaraṇasya tu māhātmyam adhunā likhyate kiyat  Hbhv tatrādau tasya nityatāpādme bṛhatsahasranāmni stotre smartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit sarve vidhiniṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ  Hbhv skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrīmadagastyoktausā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sa mohaḥ sa ca vibhramaḥ yanmuhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīdhruvacariteiyam eva parā hānir upasargo yam eva ca abhāgyaṃ paramaṃ caitad vāsudevaṃ na yat smaret  Hbhv ye muhūrtāḥ kṣaṇā ye ca yāḥ kāṣṭhā ye nimeṣakāḥ ṛte viṣṇusmṛter yātās teṣu muṣṭo yamena saḥ  Hbhv  iti nityatvepy asya māhātmyaṃ vicitraphaladānataḥ jñeyaṃ śāstroditaṃ darśapūrṇamāsādivad budhaiḥ  Hbhv atha smaraṇamāhātmyamtatra sarvatīrthasnānādhikatvamuktaṃ ca smārtair apimāntraṃ pārthivam āgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyam eva ca vāruṇaṃ mānasaṃ ceti snānaṃ saptavidhaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv śaṃ na āpas tu vai māntraṃ mṛdālambhaṃ tu pārthivam bhasmanā snānam āgneyaṃ snānaṃ gorajasānilam  Hbhv ātape sati yā vṛṣṭir divyaṃ snānaṃ tad ucyate bahir nadyādiṣu snānaṃ vāruṇaṃ procyate budhaiḥ dhyānaṃ yan manasā viṣṇor mānasaṃ tat prakīrtanam  Hbhv kiṃ caasāmarthyena kāyasya kāladeśādyapekṣayā tulyaphalāni sarvāṇi syur ity āha parāśaraḥ  Hbhv snānānāṃ mānasaṃ snānaṃ manvādyaiḥ paramaṃ smṛtam kṛtena yena mucyante gṛhasthā api vai dvijāḥ  Hbhv paramaśodhaktavamgāruḍe śrīnāradoktauviṣṇudharme ca pulasytyoktau apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthāṃ gato pi vā yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ  Hbhv yadyapy upahataḥ pāpair manasāyantadustaraiḥ tathāpi saṃsmaran viṣṇuṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ  Hbhv śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  prāyaścittāny aśeṣāṇi tapaḥ karmātmakāni vai yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇāṃ kṛṣṇānusmaraṇaṃ param  Hbhv kṛte pāpenutāpo vai yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate prāyaścittaṃ tu tasyaikaṃ harisaṃsmaraṇaṃ param  Hbhv kiṃ ca ViP  kalikalmaṣam atyugraṃ narakārtipradaṃ nṝṇām prayāti vilayaṃ sadyaḥ sakṛd yatrānusaṃsmṛte  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye ṇārP  śukrabalisaṃvāde harir harati pāpāni duṣṭacittair api smṛtaḥ anicchayāpi saṃspṛṣṭo dahaty eva hi pāvakaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva ṇārP  prāyaścittaprasaṅgāntemahāpātakayukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ sa vai vimucyate sadyo yasya viṣṇuparaṃ manaḥ  Hbhv brahmavaivarte karmaṇā manasā vācā yaḥ kṛtaḥ pāpasañcayaḥ so py aśeṣaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti smṛtvā kṛṣṇāṅghrapaṅkajam  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrīparāśareṇa yamamārgaṃ mahāghoraṃ narakāṃś ca yamaṃ tathā svapnepi na naraḥ paśyed yaḥ smared garuḍadhvajam  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  śrīśukena sakṛn manaḥ kṛṣṇapadāravindayorniveśitaṃ tadguṇarāgi yair iha na te yamaṃ pāśabhṛtaś ca tadbhaṭānsvapne pi paśyanti hi cīrṇaniṣkṛtāḥ  Hbhv sarvāpadvimocakatvamśrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  śrīprahlādoktau dantā gajānāṃ kulśāgraniṣṭhurāḥśīrṇā yad ete na balaṃ mamaitat mahāvipatpātavināśano yaṃjanārdanānusmaraṇānubhāvaḥ  Hbhv vāmanapurāṇe ca viṣṭayo vyatipātāś ca yenye durnītisambhavāḥ te sarve smaraṇād viṣṇor nāśam āyānty upadravāḥ  Hbhv pādme māghamāhātmye devadyutistutau yasya smaraṇamātreṇa na moho na ca durgatiḥ na rogo na ca duḥkhāni tam anantaṃ namāmy aham  Hbhv durvāsanonmūlanatvamdvādaśaskandhe BhP  yathā hemni sthito vahnir durvarṇaṃ hanti dhātujam evam ātmagato viṣṇur yoginām aśubhāśayam  Hbhv sarvamaṅgalakāritvampāṇḍavagītāyāmlābhas teṣāṃ jayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ yeṣām indīvaraśyāmo hṛdayasthajanārdanaḥ  Hbhv sarvasatkarmaphaladatvamskānde kārttikaprasaṅgegastyoktaudeveṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu caivadāneṣu tīrtheṣu vrateṣu caiva iṣṭeṣu pūrteṣu ca yat pradiṣṭaṃnṝṇāṃ smṛte tatphalam acyute ca  Hbhv karmasādguṇyakāritvambṛhannāradīye ṇārP nyūnātiriktatā siddhā kalau vedoktakarmaṇām harisaṃsmaraṇam evātra sampūrṇaphaladāyakam  Hbhv smṛtau capramādāt kurvatāṃ karma pracyavetādhvareṣu yat smaraṇād eva tad viṣṇoḥ sampūrṇaṃ syād iti śrutiḥ  Hbhv sarvakarmādhikatvambṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge ṇārP tulāpuruṣadānānāṃ rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ phalaṃ viṣṇoḥ smṛtisamaṃ na jātu dvijasattama  Hbhv dvādaśaskandhe BhP vidyātapaḥprāṇanirodhamaitrītīrthābhiṣekavratadānajapyaiḥ nātyantaśuddhiṃ labhate ntarātmāyathā hṛdisthe bhagavaty anante  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe ViP  hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prati śrīprahlādoktau bhayaṃ bhayānām apahāriṇi sthitemanasy anante mama kutra tiṣṭhati yasmin smṛte janmajarodbhavānibhayāni sarvāṇy apayānti tāta  Hbhv tatraivānyatra ViP  viṣṇusaṃsmaraṇāt kṣīṇasamastakleśasaṃcayaḥ muktiṃ prayāti svargāptis tasya vighno numīyate  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye ṇārP  varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ purāṇaṃnijaprabhābhāvitasarvalokam saṅkalpitārthapradam ādidevaṃsmṛtvā vrajen muktipadaṃ manuṣyaḥ  Hbhv skāndeyasya smaraṇamātreṇa janmasaṃsārabandhanāt vimucyate namas tasmai viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave  Hbhv tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge śrīparāśaroktautadaiva puruṣo mukto janmaduḥkhajarādibhiḥ bhaktyā tu parayā nūnaṃ yadaiva smarate harim  Hbhv bhagavatprasādanambṛhannāradīye ṇārP  yena kenāpy upāyena smṛto nārāyaṇo vyayaḥ api pātakayuktasya prasannaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv śrīvaikuṇṭhalokaprāpakatvamvāmanapurāṇeanādyanantam ajarāmaraṃ hariṃye saṃsmaranty aharahar niyataṃ narā bhuvi tat sarvagaṃ brahma paraṃ purāṇaṃte yānti vaiṣṇavapadaṃ dhurvam avyayaṃ ca  Hbhv pādme  devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde yamasya dūtānuśāsanesmaranti ye sakṛd bhūtāḥ prasaṅgenāpi keśavam te vidhvastākhilāghaughā yanti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  Hbhv brahmapurāṇe viṣṇurahasye śāṭhyenāpi narā nityaṃ ye smaranti janārdanam te pi yānti tanuṃ tyaktvā viṣṇulokam anāmayam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarenirāśīr nirmamo yas tu viṣṇor dhyānaparo bhavet tatpadaṃ samavāpnoti yatra gatvā na śocati  Hbhv sārūpyaprāpaṇamkāśīkhaṇḍe śrībindumādhavaprasaṅge agnibindustutauye tvāṃ trivikrama sadā hṛdi śīlayantikādambinīrucir arociṣam ambujākṣa saudāminīvilasitāṃśukavītamūrtetepi spṛśanti tava kāntim acintyarūpām  Hbhv śrībhagavadgītāsu ṅītā  antakāle ca mām eva smaran muktvā kalevaram yaḥ prayāti sa madbhāvaṃ yāti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv daśamaskandhe BhP  pṛthukopākhyāne smarataḥ pādakamalam ātmānam api yacchati kiṃ nv arthakāmān bhajato nātyabhīṣṭān jagadguruḥ  Hbhv vaiṣṇavevāsudeve mano yasya japahomārcanādiṣu tasyāntarāyo maitreya devendratvādi satphalam  Hbhv gāruḍemahatas tapaso mūlaṃ prasavaḥ puṇyasantateḥ jīvitasya phalaṃ svādu niyataṃ smaraṇaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv dvitīyaskandhe BhP  etāvān sāṅkhyayogābhyāṃ svadharmapariniṣṭhayā janmalābhaḥ paraḥ puṃsām ante nārāyaṇasmṛtiḥ  Hbhv ataeva jarāsandhaniruddhanṛpavargaiḥ prārthitaṃ daśamaskandhe BhP  taṃ naḥ samādiśopāyaṃ yena te caraṇābjayoḥ smṛtir yathā na viramed api saṃsaratām iha  Hbhv śrīnāradenāpi BhP  dṛṣṭaṃ tavāṅghriyugalaṃ janatāpavargaṃbrahmādibhir hṛdi vicintyam agādhabodhaiḥ saṃsārakūpapatitottaraṇāvalambaṃdhyāyaṃś carāmy anugṛhāṇa yathā smṛtiḥ syāt  Hbhv  iti kṛṣṇasmaraṇamāhātmyamahābdhir dustaro dhiyā yo yiyāsati tatpāraṃ sa hi caitanyavañcitaḥ  Hbhv tataḥ pādodakaṃ kiñcit prāk pītvā tulasīdalaiḥ gṛhītenācaret tena svamūrdhany abhiṣecanam  Hbhv athādau śrīguruṃ natvā śrīkṛṣṇasya padābjayoḥ kiñcid vijñāpayan sarvasvakṛtyāny arpayen namet  Hbhv atha prātaḥ praṇāmaḥvāmanapurāṇe sarvamaṅgalamaṅgalyaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ śivam nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya sarvakarmāṇi kārayet  Hbhv atha vijñāpanamviṣṇudharmottare yadutsavādikaṃ karma tat tvayā prerito hare kariṣyāmi tvayā jñeyam iti vijñāpanaṃ mama  Hbhv prātaḥ prabodhito viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśena yat tvayā yad yat kārayasīśāna tat karomi tavājñayā  Hbhv trailokyacaitanyamayādidevaśrīnātha viṣṇo bhavadājñayaiva prātaḥ samutthāya tava priyārthaṃsaṃsārayātrām anuvartayiṣye  Hbhv saṃsārayātrām anuvartamānaṃtvadājñayā śrīnṛharentarātman spardhātiraskārakalipramādabhayāni mā mābhibhavantu bhūman  Hbhv jānāmi dharmaṃ na ca me pravṛttirjānāmy adharmaṃ na ca me nivṛttiḥ tvayā hṛṣīkeśa hṛdi sthitenayathā niyukto smi tathā karomi  Hbhv atha praṇāmavākyānimahābhārate namo brahmaṇyadevāya gobrāhmaṇahitāya ca jagaddhitāya kṛṣṇāya govindāya namo namaḥ  Hbhv garuḍapurāṇeasuravibudhasiddhair jñāyate yasya nāntaḥsakalamunibhir antaś cintyate yo viśuddhaḥ nikhilahṛdi niviṣṭo vetti yaḥ sarvasākṣītam ajam amṛtam īśaṃ vāsudevaṃ nato smi  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe ViP yajñibhir yajñapuruṣo vāsudevaś ca sātvataḥ vedāntavedibhir viṣṇuḥ procyate yo nato smi tam  Hbhv evaṃ vijñāpayan dhyāyan kīrtayaṃś ca yathāvidhi praṇāmānācarec chaktyā catuḥsaṅkhyāvarān budhaḥ  Hbhv śrīgopīcandanenordhvapuṇḍraṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi āsīta prāṅmukho bhūtvā śuddhasthāne śubhāsane  Hbhv tathā ca nāradīyapañcarātrenirgatyācamya vidhivat praviśya ca punaḥ sudhīḥ āsane prāṅmukho bhūtvā vihite copaviśya vai  Hbhv sampradāyānusāreṇa bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāya ca prāṇāyāmāṃś ca vidhivat kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyet yathoditam  Hbhv tathā coktamupapātakeṣu sarveṣu pātakeṣu mahatsu ca praviśya rajanīpādaṃ viṣṇudhyānaṃ samācaret  Hbhv vaihāyasapañcarātre catathaiva rātriśeṣaṃ tu kālaṃ sūryodayāvadhi kartavyaṃ sajapaṃ dhyānaṃ nityam ārādhakena vai  Hbhv vibhajya pañcadhā rātriṃ śeṣe devārcanādikam japaṃ homaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ nityaṃ kurvīta sādhakaḥ  Hbhv ataeva viṣṇusmṛtaurātres tu paścime yāme muhūrtau brāhmya ucyate  Hbhv  iti pādodapānādīnāṃ ca sa vidhir mahimāgrataḥ lekhyo dhunā tu dhyānasya sa saṅkṣepeṇa likhyate  Hbhv tāpanīyaśrutiṣu ṅṭū  satpuṇḍarīkanayanaṃ meghābhaṃ vaidyutāmbaram dvibhujaṃ jñānamudrāḍhyaṃ vanamālinam īśvaram  Hbhv gopagopīgavāvītaṃ suradrumatalāśritam dviyālaṅkaraṇopetaṃ ratnapaṅkajamadhyagam  Hbhv kālindījalakallolasaṅgimārutasevitam cintayaṃś cetasā kṛṣṇaṃ mukto bhavati saṃsṛteḥ  Hbhv mṛtyuñjayasaṃhitānusāroditasāradātilake ca smared vṛndāvane ramye mohayantam anāratam govindaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ gopakanyāḥ sahasraśaḥ  Hbhv ātmano vadanāmbhojapreritākṣimadhuvratāḥ kāmabāṇena vivaśāś ciram āśleṣeṇotsukāḥ  Hbhv muktāhāralasatpīnottuṅgastanabharānatāḥ srastadhammillavasanā madaskhalitabhāṣaṇāḥ  Hbhv dantapaṅktiprabhodbhāsispandamānādharāñcitāḥ vilobhayantīr vividhair vibhramair bhāvagarbhitaiḥ  Hbhv phullendīvarakāntim induvadanaṃ barhāvataṃsapriyaṃśrīvatsāṅkam udārakaustubhadharaṃ pītāmbaraṃ sundaram gopīnāṃ nayanotpalārcitatanuṃ gogopasaṅghāvṛtaṃgovindaṃ kalaveṇuvādanaparaṃ divyāṅgabhūṣaṃ bhaje  Hbhv  iti śrīgautamīyatantrādau taddhyānaṃ prathitaṃ param agrato trāpi saṃlekhyaṃ yad iṣṭaṃ tatra tad bhajet  Hbhv bṛhatśātātāpasmṛtaupakṣopavāsād yat pāpaṃ puruṣasya praṇaśyati prāṇāyāmaśatenaiva yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām  Hbhv prāṇāyāmasahasreṇa yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām kṣaṇamātreṇa tat pāpaṃ harer dhyānāt praṇaśyati  Hbhv viṣṇudharmesarvapāpaprasakto pi dhyāyan nimiṣam acyutam bhūtas tapasvī bhavati paṅktipāvanapāvanaḥ  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe  cadhyāyen nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānādiṣu ca karmasu prāyaścittaṃ hi sarvasya duṣkṛtasyeti niścitam  Hbhv kalidoṣaharatvambṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge ṇārP  samastajagadādhāraṃ paramārthasvarūpiṇam ghore kaliyuge prāpte viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati  Hbhv sarvadharmādhikāritvamskānde kārttikamāhātmye agastyoktaukintv asya bahubhis tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tasya bahubhir vrataiḥ yo nityaṃ dhyāyate devaṃ nārāyaṇam ananyadhīḥ  Hbhv mokṣapradatvambṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge ṇārP  ye mānavā vigatarāgaparāvarajñānārāyaṇaṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ smaranti dhyānena tena hata kilbiṣacetanās temātuḥ payodhararasaṃ na punaḥ pibanti  Hbhv śrīvaikuṇṭhaprāpakatvamskānde śrībrahmoktaumuhūrtam api yo dhyāyen nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ so pi sadgatim āpnoti kiṃ punas tatparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde PadmaP dhyāyanti puruṣaṃ divyam acyutaṃ ye smaranti ca labhante tecyutasthānaṃ śrutir eṣā purātanī  Hbhv sārūpyaprāpaṇamekādaśaskandhe BhP  vaireṇa yaṃ nṛpatayaḥ śiśupālapauṇḍraśālvādayo gativilāsavilokanādyaiḥ dhyāyanta ākṛtadhiyaḥ śayanāsanādautatsāmyam āpur anuraktadhiyāṃ punaḥ kim  Hbhv svataḥ paramaphalatvamcaturthaskandhe BhP  śrīpṛthūktau bhajanty atha tvām ata eva sādhavovyudastamāyāguṇavibhramodayam bhavatpadānusmaraṇād ṛte satāṃnimittam anyad bhagavan na vidmahe  Hbhv skandapurāṇe brahmoktau ca āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ idame eva suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ hāyaśīrṣapañcarātre nārāyaṇavyūhastave ye tyaktalokadharmārthā viṣṇubhaktivaśaṃ gatāḥ dhyāyanti paramātmānaṃ tebhyo pīha namo namaḥ  Hbhv  iti smaraṇe yat tan māhātmyaṃ taddhyānepy akhilaṃ viduḥ bhedaḥ kalpyeta sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ tayoḥ kiyān  Hbhv atha śrībhagavatprabodhanamtato devālaye gatvā ghaṇṭādyudghoṣapūrvakam prabodhya stutibhiḥ kṛṣṇaṃ nīrājyaṃ prārthayed idam  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  so sāv adabhrakaruṇo bhagavān vivṛddhapremasmitena nayanāmburuhaṃ vijṛmbhan utthāya viśvavijayāya ca no viṣādaṃmādhvyā girāpanayatāt puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ  Hbhv devaprapannārtihara prasādaṃ kuru keśava avalokanadānena bhūyo māṃ pārayācyuta  Hbhv  iti devālayaṃ praviśyātha stotrāṇīṣṭāni kīrtayan kṛṣṇasya tulasīvarjaṃ nirmālyam apasārayet  Hbhv atha nirmālyottāraṇamatrismṛtauprātaḥkāle sadā kuryān nirmālyottāraṇaṃ budhaḥ tṛṣitāḥ paśavo baddhāḥ kanyakā ca rajasvalā devatā ca sanirmālyā hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv nārasiṃhe śrīyamoktaudevamālyāpanayanaṃ devāgāre samūhanam snāpanaṃ sarvadevānāṃ gopradānasamaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv nāradapañcarātreyaḥ prātar utthāya vidhāya nityaṃnirmālyam īśasya nirākaroti na tasya duḥkhaṃ na daridratā canākālamṛtyur na ca rogamātram  Hbhv aruṇodayavelāyāṃ nirmālyaṃ śalyatāṃ vrajet prātas tu syān mahāśalyaṃ ghaṭikāmātrayogataḥ  Hbhv atiśalyaṃ vijānīyāt tato vajraprahāravat aruṇodayavelāyāṃ śalyaṃ tat kṣamate hariḥ  Hbhv ghaṭikāyām atikrāntau kṣudraṃ pātakam āvahet muhūrte samatikrānte pūrṇaṃ pātakam ucyate  Hbhv atipātakam ev syāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye muhūrtatritaye pūrṇe mahāpātakam ucyate  Hbhv tataḥ paraṃ brahmavadho mahāpātakapañcakam prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte prāyaścittaṃ tato na hi  Hbhv nirmālyasya vilambe tu prāyaścittam athocyate atikrānte muhūrtārdhe sahasraṃ japam ācaret  Hbhv pūrṇe muhūrte sañjāte sahasraṃ sārdham ucyate sahasradvitīyaṃ kuryāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye  Hbhv muhūrtatritayetīte ayutaṃ japam ācaret prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte puraścaraṇam ucyate prahare samatikrānte prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate  Hbhv atha śrīmukhaprakṣālanamśrīhastāṅghrimukhāmbhojakṣālanāya ca tadgṛhe gaṇḍūṣāṇi jalair dattvā dantakāṣṭhaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā pāduke śuddhamṛttikām salilaṃ ca punar dadyād vāso pi mukhamārjanam  Hbhv tataḥ śrītulasīṃ puṇyām arpayet bhagavatpriyām tanmāhātmyaṃ ca tanmukhyaprasaṅge lekhyam agrataḥ  Hbhv atha dantakāṣṭhārpaṇamāhātmyamviṣṇudharmottaredantakāṣṭhapradānena dantasaubhāgyam ṛcchati jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā virogas tv abhijāyate  Hbhv pādukāyāḥ pradānena gatim iṣṭām avāpnuyāt mṛdbhāgadānād devasya bhūmim āpnoty anuttamām  Hbhv atha maṅgalanīrājanampaṭhitvātha priyān ślokān mahāvāditranisvanaiḥ prabhor nīrājanaṃ kuryān maṅgalākhyaṃ jagaddhitam  Hbhv nīrājanaṃ tv idaṃ sarvaiḥ kartavyaṃ śucivigrahaiḥ paramaśraddhayotthāya draṣṭavyaṃ ca sadā naraiḥ  Hbhv strīṇāṃ puṃsāṃ ca sarveṣām etat sarveṣṭapūrakam samastadainyadāridryaduritādyupaśāntikṛt  Hbhv atha prātaḥsnānārthodyamaḥtato ruṇodayasyānte snānārthaṃ niḥsared bahiḥ kīrtayan kṛṣṇanāmāni tīrthaṃ gacched anantaram  Hbhv tathā ca śukrasmṛtaubrāhme muhūrte cotthāya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ svastikādyāsanaṃ baddhvā dhyātvā kṛṣṇapādāmbujam  Hbhv tato nirgatya nilayānnāmānīmāni kīrtayet śrīvāsudevāniruddhapradyumnādhokṣajācyuta śrīkṛṣṇānanta govinda saṅkarṣaṇa namo stu te  Hbhv gatvā tīrthādikaṃ tatra nikṣipya snānasādhanam vidhinācarya maitryādikṛtyaṃ śaucaṃ vidhāya ca ācamya khāni saṃmārjya snānaṃ kuryāt yathocitam  Hbhv atha maitryādikṛtyavidhiḥśrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  aurvasagarasaṃvāde gṛhidharmakathanetataḥ kalye samutthāya kuryān mūtraṃ nareśvara nairṛtyām iṣuvikṣepam atītyādhikaṃ gṛhāt  Hbhv dūrādāvasathān mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca samutsṛjet pādāv asecanocchiṣṭe prakṣipen na gṛhāṅgaṇe  Hbhv ātmacchāyāṃ taroś chāyāṃ gosūryāgnyanilāṃs tathā guruṃ dvijādīṃś ca budho na meheta kadācana  Hbhv na kṛṣṭe śasyamadhye vā govraje janasaṃsadi na vartmani na nadyāditīrtheṣu puruṣarṣabha  Hbhv nāpsu naivāmbhasas tīre na śmaśāne samācaret utsargaṃ vai purīṣasya mūtrasya ca visarjanam  Hbhv udaṅmukho divotsargaṃ viparītamukho niśi kurvītānāpadi prājño mūtrotsargaṃ ca pārthiva  Hbhv tṛṇair ācchādya vasudhāṃ vastraprāvṛtamastakaḥ tiṣṭhen nāticiraṃ tatra naiva kiñcid udīrayet  Hbhv tathā kaurme vyāsagītāyāmnidhāya dakṣiṇe karṇe brahmasūtram udaṅmukhaḥ antardhāpya mahīṃ kāṣṭhaiḥ patrair loṣṭrais tṛṇena vā  Hbhv prāvṛtya tu śiraḥ kuryād vinmūtrasya visarjanam na caivābhimukhaḥ strīṇāṃ gurubrāhmaṇayor gavām na devadevālayor nāpām api kadācana  Hbhv nadīṃ jyotīṃṣi vīkṣitvā na vāyvagnimukho pi vā prayādityaṃ pratyanalaṃ pratisomaṃ tathaiva ca  Hbhv kāśīkāṇḍe śrīskandāgastyasaṃvādetataś cāvaśyakaṃ kartuṃ nairṛtīṃ diśam āśrayet grāmād dhanuḥśataṃ gacchen nagarāc ca caturguṇam  Hbhv karṇopavītyudagvaktro divase sandhyayor api vinmūtre visṛjen maunī niśāyāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  Hbhv nālokayed diśo bhāgān jyotiś cakraṃ nabho malam vāmena pāṇinā śiśnaṃ dhṛtvottiṣṭhet prayatnavān  Hbhv tatraivāgrena mūtraṃ govraje kuryān na valmīke na bhasmani na garteṣu sasattveṣu na tiṣṭhan na vrajann api  Hbhv yathāsukhamukho rātrau divā chāyāndhakārayoḥ bhītiṣu prāṇabādhāyāṃ kuryān malavisarjanam  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe BhP  tatraivavalmīkamūṣikotkhātāṃ mṛdaṃ nāntarjalāt tathā śaucāvaśiṣṭāṃ gehāc ca na dadyāl lepasambhavām  Hbhv antaḥprāṇyavapannāṃ ca halotkhātāṃ ca pārthiva parityajen mṛdaś caitāḥ sakalāḥ śaucasādhane  Hbhv ekā liṅge gude tisras daśa vāmakare nṛpa hastadvaye saptānyā mṛdaḥ śaucopapādikāḥ  Hbhv yamasmṛtautisras tu pādayor deyāḥ śuddhikāmena nityaśaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ catisras tu mṛttikā deyāḥ kṛtvā tu nakhaśodhanam  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍe ca tatraivaguhye dadyān mṛdaṃ caikāṃ pāyau pañcāmbusāntarāḥ daśa vāmakare cāpi sapta pāṇidvaye mṛdaḥ  Hbhv ekaikāṃ pādayor dadyāt tisraḥ pāṇyor mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ itthaṃ śaucaṃ gṛhī kuryād gandhalepakṣayāvadhi  Hbhv kramād dviguṇam etat tu brahmacaryādiṣu triṣu divā śaṅkhasmṛtaumṛttikā tu samuddiṣṭā triparvī pūryate yayā  Hbhv dakṣasmṛtauardhaprasṛtimātrā tu prathamā mṛttikā smṛtā dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā ca tadardhaṃ parikīrtitā  Hbhv atha kevalamūtrotsargedakṣaḥekā dantadhāvanavidhiḥtatra kātyāyanaḥutthāya netraṃ prakṣālya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ parijapya ca mantreṇa bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam  Hbhv mantraś cāyamāyur balaṃ yaśo varcaḥ prajā paśuvasūni ca brahma dahaty āsaptamaṃ kulam  Hbhv vṛddhavaśiṣṭhaḥupavāse tathā śrāddhena khāded dantadhāvanam dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo hanti saptakulāni vai  Hbhv anyatra capratipaddaraṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyekādaśīravau dantānāṃ vyāsaḥpratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ dantadhāvanam parṇair anyatra kāṣṭhaiś ca jīvollekhhaḥ sadaiva hi  Hbhv paiṭhīnasiḥalābhe ca niṣedhe vā kāṣṭhānāṃ dantadhāvanam parṇādinā viśuddhena jihvollekhaḥ sadaiva hi  Hbhv atha tatraivāpavādaḥkāṣṭhaiḥ pratipadādau yan niṣiddhaṃ dantadhāvanam tṛṇaparṇais tu tat kuryād amām ekādaśīṃ vinā  Hbhv ata eva vyāsasya vacanāntaramalābhe dantakāṣṭhānāṃ niṣiddhāyāṃ tathā tithau apāṃ dvādaśagaṇḍūṣair vidadhyād dantadhāvanam  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍe tatraivamukhe paryuṣite yasmād bhaved aśucibhāg naraḥ tataḥ kuryāt prayatnena śuddhyarthaṃ dantadhāvanam  Hbhv upavāsepi no śuddhānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ viśāṃ vara  Hbhv atrismṛtausnāne manaḥprasādaḥ syād devā abhimukhāḥ sadā saubhāgyaṃ śrīḥ sukhaṃ puṣṭiḥ puṇyaṃ vidyā yaśo dhṛtiḥ  Hbhv mahāpāpāny alakṣmīṃ ca duritaṃ durvicintitam PadmaP  śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde evam uccārya tattīrthe pādau prakṣālya vāg yataḥ smaran nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānaṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ  Hbhv tīrthaṃ prakalpayed dhīmān mūlamantram imaṃ paṭhan auṃ namo āmantrya tu vidhānataḥ  Hbhv aśvakrānte rathakrānte viṣṇukrānte vasundhare mṛttike hara me pāpaṃ yan mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam  Hbhv uddhṛtāsi varāheṇa viṣṇunā śatabāhunā namas te sarvalokānāṃ prabhavāraṇi  Hbhv tad uktaṃ gautamīyatantreśālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ tulasīgandhamiśritam kṛtvā śaṅkhe bhrāmayaṃs triḥ prakṣipen nijamūrdhani  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilātoyam apītvā yas tu mastake prekṣepaṇaṃ prakurvīta brahmahā sa nigadyate  Hbhv viṣṇupādodakān pūrvaṃ viprapādodakaṃ pibet viruddham ācaran mohād brahmahā sa nigadyate  Hbhv śrīcaraṇāmṛtadhāraṇamantraḥakālamṛtyuharaṇaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam viṣṇoḥ pādodakaṃ pītvā śirasā dhārayāmy aham  Hbhv  iti lekhyo grye kṛṣṇapādābjatīrthadhāraṇapānayoḥ mahimātra tu tattīrthenābhiṣekasya likhyate  Hbhv atha śrīcaraṇodakābhiṣekamāhātmyampadmapurāṇe  sa snātaḥ sarvatīrtheṣu sarvayajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ śālagrāmaśilātoyair yo bhiṣekaṃ samācaret  Hbhv gaṅgā godāvarī revā nadyo muktipradās tu yāḥ nivasanti satīrthās tāḥ śālagrāmaśilājale  Hbhv koṭitīrthasahasrais tu sevitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam tīrthaṃ yadi bhavet puṇyaṃ śālagrāmaśilodbhavam  Hbhv tatraiva śrīgautamāmbarīṣasaṃvādeyeṣāṃ dhautāni gātrāṇi hareḥ pādodakena vai ambarīṣa kule teṣāṃ dāso smi vaśagaḥ sadā  Hbhv rājante tāni tāvac ca tīrthāni bhuvanatraye yāvan na prāpyate toyaṃ śālagrāmābhiṣekajam  Hbhv skānde kārttikamāhātmyegṛhepi vasatas tasya gaṅgāsnānaṃ dine dine śālagrāmaśilātoyair yo biṣiñcati mānavaḥ  Hbhv tatraivānyatra cayāni kāni ca tīrthāni brahmādyā devatās tathā viṣṇupādodakasyaite kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  Hbhv śālagrāmodbhvao devo devo dvāravatībhavaḥ ubhayoḥ snānatoyena brahmahatyā nivartate  Hbhv kiṃ casa vai cāvabhṛtasnātaḥ sa ca gaṅgājalāplutaḥ viṣṇupādodakaṃ kṛtvā śaṅkheyaḥ snāti mānavaḥ  Hbhv śrīnṛsiṃhapurāṇegaṅgāprayāgagayanaimiṣapuṣkarāṇipuṇyāni yāni kurujāṅgalayāmunāni kālena tīrthasalilāni punanti pāpaṃpādodakaṃ bhagavataḥ prapunāti sadyaḥ  Hbhv smṛtau catrirātriphaladā nadyo yāḥ kāścid asamudragāḥ samudragāś ca pakṣasya māsasya saritāṃ patiḥ  Hbhv ṣaṇmāsaphaladā godā vatsarasya tu jāhnavī pādodakaṃ bhagavato dvādaśābdaphalapradam  Hbhv tannityatāgaruḍapurāṇejalaṃ ca yeṣāṃ tulasīvimiśritaṃpādodakaṃ cakraśilāsamudbhavam nityaṃ trisandhyaṃ plavate na gātraṃkhagendra te dharmabahiṣkṛtā narāḥ  Hbhv  iti tato jalāñjalīn kṣiptvā mūrdhni trīn kumbhamudrayā mūlenāthāviśeṣeṇa kuryād devāditarpaṇam  Hbhv atha sāmānyato devāditarpaṇamtac ca vaidikeṣu prasiddham evabrahmādayo ye devās tān devān tarpayāmi bhūrdevāṃs tarpayāmi bhuvardevāṃs tarpayāmi svardevāṃs tarpayāmi bhūrbhuvaḥsvardevāṃs tarpayāmi  Hbhv  ity ādi ācāmyāṅgāni saṃmārjya snānavastrāṇyavāsasā paridhāyāṃśuke śukle niviśyācamanaṃ caret  Hbhv vidhivat tilakaṃ kṛtvā punaś cācamya vaiṣṇavaḥ vidhāya vaidikīṃ sandhyām athopāsīta tāntrikīm  Hbhv atha vaidikī sandhyākaurme tatraivaprākkuleṣu tataḥ sthitvā darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyet sandhyām iti śrutiḥ  Hbhv manusmṛtau brāhmaṇāḥ śāktikāḥ sarve na śaivā na ca vaiṣṇavāḥ yata upāsate devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram  Hbhv yā ca sandhyā jagatsūtir māyātītā hi niṣkalā aiśvarī kevalā śaktis tattvatrayasamudbhavā  Hbhv dhyātvārkamaṇḍalagatāṃ sāvitrīṃ tāṃ japed budhaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ satataṃ vipraḥ sandhyopāsanam ācaret  Hbhv kiṃ casahasraparamāṃ nityaṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām sāvitrīṃ vai japed vidvān prāṅmukhaḥ prayataḥ sthitaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ casandhyāhīno śucir nityam anarhaḥ sarvakarmasu yad anyat kurute kiñcin na tasya phalam apnuyāt  Hbhv yo nyatra kurute yatnaṃ dharmakārye dvijottamaḥ vihāya sandhyāpraṇatiṃ sa yāti narakāyutam  Hbhv ananyacetasaḥ śāntā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ upāsya vidhivat sandhyāṃ prāptāḥ pūrve parāṃ gatim  Hbhv atha tāntrikī sandhyātataḥ sampūjya salile nijāṃ śrīmantradevatām tarpayed vidhinā tasya tathivāvaraṇāni ca  Hbhv tathā ca bodhāyanasmṛtauhaviṣāgnau jale kāmagāyatrīśrīsanatkumārakalpeādau manmatham uddhṛtya kāmadevapadaṃ vadet āyānte vidmahe puṣpabāṇāyeti padaṃ vadet dhīmahīti tathoktvātha tan no naṅgaḥ pracodayāt  Hbhv  iti athārkamaṇḍale kṛṣṇaṃ matāntaratāntrikasandhyāvidhiḥādau dakṣiṇahastena gṛhṇīyād vāri vaiṣṇavaḥ tato hṛdayamantreṇa vāmapāṇitalerpayet  Hbhv tadaṅgulīviniryātāmbhaḥkaṇair dakṣapāṇinā mastake netramantreṇa kuryāt tataḥ param tan naḥ kṛṣṇa iti prānte prapūrvaṃ codayād iti  Hbhv mūrdhni nyaset tadaṅgāni lalāṭe netrayor dvayoḥ bhujayoḥ pādayoś caiva sarvāṅgeṣu tathā kramāt  Hbhv tāni coktānipañcabhiś ca tirbhiś caiva pañcabhiś ca tribhiḥ punaḥ caturbhiś ca caturbhiś ca kuryād aṅgāni varṇakiḥ  Hbhv  iti rāsakrīḍārataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dhyātvā cādityamaṇḍale tatsammukhotkṣiptabhujo gāyatrīṃ tāṃ japet kṣaṇam  Hbhv atha tatra jale śrībhagavatpūjāvidhiḥaṅganyāsaṃ svamantreṇa kṛtvāthābjaṃ jalāntare sañcintya pīṭhamantreṇa tarpayec ca sakṛt sakṛt  Hbhv tasmiṃś ca kṛṣṇam āvāhya sakalīkṛtya mānasān pañcopacārāt dattvāpsu dhenumudrāṃ pradarśayet  Hbhv tajjalaṃ cāmṛtaṃ dhyātvā svamantreṇābhimantrya ca aṣṭottaraśataṃ kṛṣṇottamāṅge tarpayet kṛtī  Hbhv tataś ca mūlamantreṇa vārān vai pañcaviṃśatim abhijaptenodakenācamanaṃ vidhinā caret  Hbhv atha viśeṣato devāditarpaṇampādme  tatraivabrahmāṇaṃ tarpayet pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ prajāpatīn devā yakṣās tathā nāgā gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ  Hbhv krūrāḥ sarpāḥ suparṇāś ca taravo jambhakādayaḥ vidyādharā jaladharās tathaivākāśagāminaḥ  Hbhv nirādhārāś ca ye jīvā pāpadharmaratāś ca ye teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā  Hbhv kṛtopavīto devebhyo nivītī ca bhavet tataḥ manuṣyāṃs tarpayed bhaktyā ṛṣiputrān ṛṣīṃs tathā  Hbhv sanakaś ca sanandaś ca tṛtīyaś ca sanātanaḥ kapilaś cāsuriś caiva voḍhuḥ pañcaśikhas tathā sarve te tṛptim āyāntu maddattenāmbunā sadā  Hbhv marīcim atryaṅgirasau pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ nāradam eva ca devabrahmaṛṣīn sarvāṃs tarpayet sākṣatodakaiḥ  Hbhv apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvāsavyaṃ jānu ca bhūtale agniṣv āttās tathā saumyā bahiṣmantas tathoṣmapāḥ  Hbhv kavyānalau barhiṣadas tathā caivājyapāḥ punaḥ tarpayet pitṛbhaktyā ca satilokdakacandanaiḥ  Hbhv yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtākṣayāya ca  Hbhv auḍumbarāya dadhnāya nīlāya parameṣṭhine vṛkodarāya citrāya citraguptāya vai namaḥ  Hbhv darbhapāṇiḥ suprayataḥ pitṝn svān tarpayet tataḥ  Hbhv pitrādīn nāmagotreṇa tathā mātāmahān api santarpya vidhinā sarvān imaṃ mantram udīrayet  Hbhv yebāndhavā bāndhavā vā yenyajanmani bāndhavāḥ te tṛptim akhilāṃ yāntu ye cāsmattoyakāṅkṣiṇaḥ  Hbhv  iti sandhyopāsanataḥ pūrvaṃ tatas tu tarpaṇaṃ kuryāt trailokyāpyāyanāya vai  Hbhv ata eva śrīrāmārcanacandrikāyāmniṣpīḍayitvā vastraṃ tu paścāt sandhyāṃ samācaret anyathā kurute yas tu snānaṃ tasyāphalaṃ bhavet  Hbhv kiṃ cavastraṃ triguṇitaṃ yas tu niṣpīḍayati mūḍhadhīḥ vṛthā snānaṃ bhavet tasya niṣpīḍayati cāmbuni  Hbhv kāśīkāṇḍeapi sarvanadītoyair mṛtkūṭaiś cātha gorasaiḥ āpātam ācarec chaucaṃ bhāvaduṣṭo na śuddhibhāk  Hbhv naktaṃ dinaṃ nimajjyāpsu kaivartāḥ kim u pāvanāḥ śataśo pi tathā snātā na śuddhā bhāvadūṣitāḥ  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye  śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvādepuṇyena gāṅgena jalena kāledeśepi āpnoti phalaṃ na cānyat  Hbhv ataeva bhaviṣyottareyasya hastau ca pādau ca vāṅ manaś ca susaṃyatam vidyātapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrthaphalam āpnuyāt  Hbhv aśraddadhānaḥ pāpātmā nāstiko cchinnasaṃśayaḥ hetuniṣṭhaś ca pañcaite na tīrthaphalabhāginaḥ  Hbhv iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāseśaucīyo nāma tṛtīyo vilāsaḥ   VaisnavalamkaraVilasacaturtho vilāsaḥśrīvaiṣṇavālaṅkāraḥsnātvā
