sarvapātakaiḥ  Hbhv āropitaṃ dhvajaṃ dṛṣṭvā yebhinandanti dhārmikāḥ tepi sarve pramucyante mahāpātakakoṭibhiḥ  Hbhv itievaṃ bṛhannāradīye khyātaṃ yac cānyad adbhutam dhvajāropaṇamāhātmyaṃ tad draṣṭavyam ihākhilam  Hbhv atha patādāropaṇamāhātmyamdvārakāmāhātmyekṛṣṇālayaṃ yaḥ kurute patākābhiś ca śobhitam sadaiva tasya loke tu vāsas tasya na cānyataḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarepatākāṃ ca śubhāṃ dattvā tathā keśavaveśmani vāyulokam avāpnoti bahūn abdagaṇān dvijaḥ  Hbhv dodhūyate yathā sā tu vāyunā keśavālaye tathā tasyāpi sakalaṃ dehāt pāpaṃ vidhūyate  Hbhv atha vandanamālākadalīstambhāropaṇamāhātmyamdvārakāmāhātmye tatraivabhūpa vandanamālāṃ tu kurute kṛṣṇaveśmani devakanyāvṛtair lakṣaiḥ sevyate suranāyakaiḥ  Hbhv yaḥ kuryāt kṛṣṇabhavanaṃ kadalīstambhaśobhitam nandate cāpsaroyuktaḥ svāgataṃ tasya devarāṭ  Hbhv atha pīṭhapātravastrādisaṃskāraḥtatra tāmrādipātraṃ yat prabhor vastrādikaṃ ca yat pīṭhādikaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ yathoktaṃ ca viśodhayet  Hbhv tatra pīṭhasya saṃskāraḥnārasiṃhepādapīṭhaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya bilvapatreṇa dharṣayet uṣṇāmbunā ca prakṣālya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv atha taijasādipātrāṇāṃ saṃskāraḥmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeuḍumbarāṇām amlena kṣāreṇa trapusīsayoḥ bhasmāmbubhiś ca kāmsyānāṃ śuddhiḥ plāvo dravasya ca  Hbhv vāyupurāṇe camaṇivajrapravālānāṃ muktāśaṅkhopalasya ca siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena tilakalkena vā punaḥ  Hbhv brāhmesuvarṇarūpyaśaṅkhāśmaśuktiratnamayāni ca kāṃsyāyastāmraraityāni trapusīsamayāni ca  Hbhv nirlepāni tu śudhyanti kevalenodakena tu śūdrocchiṣṭhāni śodhyāni tridhā kṣārāmlavāribhiḥ  Hbhv itiatiduṣṭaṃ tu pātrādi viśodhyātithyakarmaṇe yuñjyāt tatparivartāya prabhukarmāntarāya vā  Hbhv etasya parivartena prabhavenyat samarpayet ity ayaṃ sarvato loke sadācāro virājate  Hbhv manuḥ tāmrāyaḥkāṃsyaraityānāṃ trapuṇaḥ sīsakasya ca śaucaṃ yathārhaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣārāmlodakavāribhiḥ  Hbhv śaṅkhaḥamlodakena tāmrasya sīsasya trapuṇas tathā kṣāreṇa śuddhiṃ kāṃsyasya lauhasya ca vinirdiśet  Hbhv kiṃ casūtikocchiṣṭhabhāṇḍasya surādyupahatasya ca triḥsaptamārjanāc chuddhir na tu kāṃsyasya tāpanam  Hbhv anyatra catāmram amlena śudhyena na cedāmiṣalepanam āmiṣeṇa tu yal liptaṃ punar dāhena śudhyanti  Hbhv brāhmesūtikāśavaviṇmūtrarajaḥsvalahatāni ca prakṣeptavyāni tāny agnau yac ca yāvat sahed api  Hbhv ata eva devalaḥlohānāṃ dahanāc chuddhir bhasmanā gomayena vā dahanāt khananād vāpi śailānām ambhasāpi vā  Hbhv kāṣṭhānāṃ takṣaṇāc chuddhir mṛdgomayajalair api mṛṇmayānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ dahanāc chuddhir iṣyate  Hbhv manuḥ madyair mūtraiḥ purīṣair vā ṣṭhīvanaih pūyaśoṇitaiḥ saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śuddhyeta punaḥpākena mṛnmayam  Hbhv vṛddhaśātātapaḥsaṃhatānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ yad ekam upahanyate tasyaivaṃ śodhanaṃ proktaṃ sāmānyadravyaśuddhikṛt  Hbhv atha vastrādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥtatra śaṅkhaḥtāntavaṃ malinaṃ pūrvam adbhiḥ kṣāraiś ca śodhayet aṃśubhiḥ śoṣayitvā vā vāyunā vā samāharet  Hbhv ūrṇāpaṭṭāṃśukakṣaumadukūlāvikacarmaṇām alpāśauce bhavec chuddhiḥ śoṣaṇaprokṣaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv tāny evāmedhyaliptāni nenijyād gaurasarṣapaiḥ dhānyakalkaiḥ parṇakalkaiḥ rasaiś ca phalabalkalaiḥ  Hbhv tulikādyupadhānāni puṣparatnāmbarāṇi ca śodhayitvātape kiṃcit karair unmārjayen muhuḥ  Hbhv paścāc ca vāriṇā prokṣya śucīty evam udāharet tāny apy atimalāktāni yathāvat pariśodhayet  Hbhv śātātapaḥkusumbhakuṅkumāraktās tathā lākṣārasena ca prakṣālanena śudhyanti caṇḍālasparśane tathā  Hbhv yamaḥkṛṣṇājinānāṃ vātaiś ca bālānāṃ mṛdbhir ambhasā gomūtreṇāsthidantānāṃ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ  Hbhv śaṅkhaḥsiddhārthakānāṃ kalkena dantaśṛṅgamayasya ca gobālaiḥ phalapātrāṇām asthnāṃ syāc chṛṅgavat tathā  Hbhv kiṃ caniryāsānāṃ guḍānāṃ ca lavaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca kusumbhakusumānāṃ ca ūrṇākārpāsayos tathā prokṣaṇāt kathitā śuddhir ity āha bhagavān yamaḥ  Hbhv manuḥ  adbhis tu prokṣaṇaṃ śaucaṃ bahūnāṃ dhānyavāsasām prakṣālanena tv alpānām adbhiḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate  Hbhv cailavatcarmaṇāṃ śuddhir vaidalānāṃ tathāeva ca śākamūlaphalānāṃ ca dhānyavatśuddhir iṣyate  Hbhv prokṣaṇāt tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca palālaṃ caiva śudhyati mārjanaupāñjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛtmayam  Hbhv kiṃ ca manu yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktād gandho lepaś ca tatkṛtaḥ tāvan mṛdvāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu  Hbhv bṛhaspatiḥvastravaidalacarmādeḥ śuddhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ smṛtam atiduṣṭasya tanmātraṃ tyajec chittvā tu śuddhaye  Hbhv viṣṇuḥmṛtparṇatṛṇakāṣṭhānāṃ śvāsthicāṇḍālavāyasaiḥ sparśane vihitaṃ śaucaṃ somasūryāṃśumārutaiḥ  Hbhv baudhāyanaḥāsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ nāvaḥ panthās tṛṇāni ca mārutārkeṇa śudhyanti pakveṣṭaracitāni ca  Hbhv atha dhānyādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥtatra baudhāyanaḥvrīhayaḥ prokṣaṇād adbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca tanmātrasyāpahārād vā nistuṣīkaraṇena ca  Hbhv śaṅkhaḥśrapaṇaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya ca bhāṇḍāni plāvayed adbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca  Hbhv brāhmedravadravyāṇi bhūrīṇi pariplāvyāni cāmbhasā  Hbhv śasyāni vrīhayaś caiva śākamūlaphalāni ca tyaktvā tu dūṣitaṃ bhāgaṃ plāvyāny atha jalena tu  Hbhv bṛhaspatiḥtāpanaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya ca tanmātram uddhṛtaṃ śudhyet kaṭhinaṃ tu payodadhi  Hbhv avilīnaṃ tathā sarpir vilīnaṃ śrapaṇena tu ādhāradoṣe tu nayet pātrāt pātrāntaraṃ dravam  Hbhv ghṛtaṃ ca pāyasaṃ kṣīraṃ tathaikṣavaraso guḍaḥ śūdrabhāṇḍasthitaṃ takraṃ tathā madhu na duṣyati  Hbhv kiṃ ca manuḥ ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭo dravyahastaḥ kathaṃ cana anidhāyaiva tad dravyam ācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt  Hbhv itianyepi śuddhividhayo dravyāṇāṃ smṛtiśāstrataḥ apekṣyā vaiṣṇavair jñeyās tattadvistāraṇair alam  Hbhv atha pūjārthatulasīpuṣpādyāharaṇampraṇamyātha mahāviṣṇuṃ prārthyānujñāṃ tu vaiṣṇavaḥ samāharet śrītulasīṃ puṣpādi ca yathoditam  Hbhv yac ca hārītavacanamsnānaṃ kṛtvā tu ye kecit puṣpaṃ gṛhṇanti vai dvijāḥ devatās tan na gṛhṇanti bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat  Hbhv ititac ca madhyāhnasnānaviṣayamyata uktaṃ pādme  vaiśākhamāhātmyeasnātvā tulasīṃ chittvā devārthaṃ pitṛkarmaṇi tat sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ yāti pañcagavyena śudhyati  Hbhv atha gṛhasnānavidhiḥsvagṛhe vācaran snānaṃ prakṣālyāṅghrī karau tathā ācamyāyamya ca prāṇān kṛtanyāso hariṃ smaret  Hbhv tato gaṅādikaṃ smṛtvā tulasīmiśritair jalaiḥ pūrṇe pātre samastāni tīrthāny āvāhayet kṛtī  Hbhv āvāhanamantraś cāyamgaṅge ca yamune caiva godāvari sarasvati narmade sindhu kāveri jalesmin sannidhiṃ kuru  Hbhv iti athavā jāhnavīm eva sarvatīrthamayīṃ budhaḥ āvāhayed dvādaśabhir nāmabhir jalabhājane  Hbhv dvādaśanāmāninalinī nandinī sītā mālinī ca mahāpagā viṣṇupādārghyasambhūtā gaṅgā tripathagāminī bhāgīrathī bhogavatī jāhnavī tridaśeśvarī  Hbhv padmapurāṇe  ca vaiśākhamāhātmyenandinīty eva te nāma vedeṣu nalinīti ca dakṣā pṛthvī ca vihagā viśvagāthā śivapriyā  Hbhv vidyādharī mahādevī tathā lokaprasādinī kṣemaṃkarī jāhnavī ca śāntā śāntipradāyinī  Hbhv athācamya guruṃ smṛtānujñāṃ prārthya ca pūrvavat kṛṣṇapādābjato gaṅgāṃ patantīṃ mūrdhni cintayet  Hbhv tathā coktaṃ śrīnāradapañcarātresvasthitaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ mantramūrtiṃ prabhuṃ smaret anantādityasaṅkāśaṃ vāsudevaṃ caturbhujam  Hbhv śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ pītāmbarāvṛtam śyāmalaṃ śāntavadanaṃ prasannaṃ varadekṣaṇam  Hbhv divyacandanaliptāṅgaṃ cārahāsamukhāmbujam anekaratnasaṃchannajvalanmakarakuṇḍalam  Hbhv vanamālāparivṛtaṃ nāradādibhir arcitam keyūravalayopetaṃ suvarṇamukuṭojjvalam sarvāṅgasundaraṃ devaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Hbhv tatpādapaṅkajād dhārāṃ nipatantīṃ svamūrdhani cintayed brahmarandhreṇa praviśantīṃ svakāṃ tanum tayā saṃkṣālayet sarvam antardehagataṃ malam  Hbhv tatkṣaṇād virajā mantrī jāyate sphaṭikopamaḥ idaṃ snānāntaraṃ māntrāt sahasram adhikaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv itisakṛn nārāyaṇety ādi vacanaṃ tatra kīrtayet snānakāle tu tannāma saṃsmarec ca mahāprabhum  Hbhv tathā ca kūrmapurāṇeāpo nārāyaṇodbhūtās tā evāsyāyanaṃ yathaḥ tasmān nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānakāle smared budhaḥ  Hbhv itisnāyād uṣṇodakenāpi śakto py āmalakais tathā tilais tailaiś ca saṃvarjya pratiṣiddhadināni tu  Hbhv athoṣṇodakasnānamṣaṭtriṃśanmateāpaḥ svabhāvato medhyā viśeṣād agniyogataḥ tena santaḥ praśaṃsanti snānam uṣṇena vāriṇā  Hbhv yamaś caāpaḥ svayaṃ sadā pūtā vahnitaptā viśeṣataḥ tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu uṣṇāmbhaḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv yac coktaṃ śaṅkhenasnātasya vahnitaptena tathaivātapavāriṇā śarīraśuddhir vijñeyā na tu snānaphalaṃ bhavet  Hbhv ititat tu kāmyanaimittikaviṣayam ata evoktaṃ gargeṇakuryān naimittikaṃ snānaṃ śītādbhiḥ kāmyam eva ca nityaṃ yādṛcchikaṃ caiva yathāruci samācaret  Hbhv atha tatra niṣiddhadinānitatra yamaḥputrajanmani saṅkrāntau grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ aspṛśyasparśane caiva na snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā  Hbhv vṛddhamanuḥpaurṇamāsyāṃ tathā darśe yaḥ snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā sa gohatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prāpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv athāmalakasnānamtatra mārkaṇḍeyaḥtuṣyaty āmalakair viṣṇur ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ śrīkāmaḥ sarvadā snānaṃ kurvītāmalakair naraḥ  Hbhv saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ nīlīvastraṃ na dhārayet na cāpy āmalakaṃ snāyān na kuryāt kalahaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv bhṛguḥamāṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ saptamīṃ ca navamīṃ ca trayodaśīm saṅkrāntau ravivāre ca snānamālakais tyajet  Hbhv yājñavalkyaḥdhātrīphalair amāvasyāsaptamīnavamīṣu ca yaḥ snāyāt tasya hīyante tejaś cāyurdhanaṃ sutāḥ  Hbhv atha tilasnānamtatra bṛhaspatiḥsarvakālaṃ tilaiḥ snānaṃ punar vyāso bravīn muniḥ  Hbhv ṣaṭtriṃśanmatetathā saptamyamāvasyāsaṅkrāntigrahaṇeṣu ca dhanaputrakalatrārthī tilaspṛṣṭaṃ na saṃspṛśet  Hbhv atha tailasnānamtatraivaṣaṣṭhyāṃ tailam anāyuṣyaṃ caturthīṣv api ca parvasu  Hbhv yogīyājñavalkyaḥdaśamyāṃ tailam apṛṣṭvā yaḥ snāyād avicakṣaṇaḥ catvāri tasya naśyanti āyuḥ prajñā yaśodhanam  Hbhv mohāt pratipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ kuhūṃ riktātithiṃ tathā tailenābhyañjayed yas tu caturbhiḥ parihīyate  Hbhv pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ saptamyāṃ ravisaṅkrame dvādaśyāṃ saptamīṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ tailasparśaṃ vivarjayet  Hbhv anyac casaptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ navamyāṃ pratipady api aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃm amāvasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv kiṃ casnāne vā yadi vāsnāne pakkatailaṃ na duṣyati  Hbhv kiṃ ca atrismṛtautailābhyukto ghṛtābhyakto viṇmūtre kurute dvijaḥ ahorātroṣito bhūtvā pañcagavyena śudhyati  Hbhv athāṅgam alam uttārya snātvā vidhivad ācaret nāsālagnena culukodakenaivāghamarṣaṇam  Hbhv tato gurvādipādodaiḥ prāgvat kṛtvābhiṣecanam kāryo bhiṣekaḥ śaṅkhena tulasīmiśritair jalaiḥ  Hbhv atha tulasījalābhiṣekamāhatmyamgāruḍemārjayaty abhiṣeke tu tulasyā vaiṣṇavo naraḥ sarvatīrthamayaṃ dehaṃ tatkṣaṇāt dvija jāyate  Hbhv tulasīdalajasnāne ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ mucyate sarvapāpebhyo yadyapi brahmahā bhavet  Hbhv tanmūlamṛttikābhyaṅgaṃ kṛtvā snāti dine dine daśāśvamedhāvabhṛtaṃ labhate snānajaṃ phalam  Hbhv tulasīdalasaṃmiśraṃ toyaṃ gaṅgāsamaṃ viduḥ yo vahec chirasā nityaṃ dhṛtā bhavati jāhnavī  Hbhv pādodakaṃ tāmrapātre kṛtvā satulasīdalam śaṅkhaṃ kṛtvābhiṣiñceta mūlenaiva svamūrdhani  Hbhv tanmāhātmye coktaṃ pādme kārttikamāhātmyedvārakācakrasaṃyuktaśālagrāmaśilājalam śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu nikṣiptaṃ snānārthaṃ tāmrabhājane tulasīdalasaṃyuktaṃ brahmahatyāvināśanam  Hbhv itisnānaśāṭītareṇaiva vāsasāmbhāṃsi gātrataḥ saṃmārjya vāsasī dadhyāt paridhānottarīyake  Hbhv atha vastradhāraṇavidhiḥtatrātriḥadhautaṃ kārudhautaṃ vā paredyudhautam eva vā kāṣāyaṃ malinaṃ vastraṃ kaupīnaṃ ca parityajet  Hbhv na cārdram eva vasanaṃ paridadhyāt kadācana  Hbhv nagno malinavastraḥ syāt nagnaś cārdhapaṭas tathā nagno dviguṇavastraḥ syān nagno raktapaṭas tathā  Hbhv nagnaś ca syūtavastraḥ syān nagnaḥ snigdhapaṭas tathā dvikaccho nuttarīyaś ca nagnaś cāvastra eva ca  Hbhv śrautaṃ smārtaṃ tathā karma na nagnaś cintayed api mohāt kurvann adho gacchet tad bhaved āsuraṃ smṛtam  Hbhv japahomopavāseṣu dhautavastradharo bhavet alaṅkṛtaḥ śucir maunī śrāddhādau ca jitendriyaḥ  Hbhv gobhilaḥekavastro na bhuñjīta na kuryād devanārcanam  Hbhv trailokyasammohanapañcarātreśuklavāso bhaven nityaṃ raktaṃ caiva vivarjayet  Hbhv aṅgirāḥśaucaṃ sahasraromāṇāṃ vāyvagnyarkenduraśmibhiḥ retaḥspṛṣṭaṃ śavaspṛṣṭam āvikaṃ naiva duṣyati  Hbhv anyatra cachinnaṃ vā sandhitaṃ dagdhm āvikaṃ na praduṣyati āvikena tu vastreṇa mānavaḥ śrāddham ācaret gayāśrāddhasamaṃ proktaṃ pitṛbhyo dattam akṣayam  Hbhv na kuryāt sandhitaṃ vastraṃ devakarmaṇi bhūmipa na dagdhaṃ na ca vai chinnaṃ pārakyaṃ na tu dhārayet  Hbhv kākaviṣṭhāsamaṃ hy uktam avidhautaṃ ca yad bhavet rajakād āhṛtaṃ yac ca na tad vastraṃ bhavec chuci  Hbhv kīṭaspṛṣṭaṃ tu yad vastraṃ purīṣaṃ yena kāritam mūtraṃ vā maithunaṃ vāpi tad vastraṃ parivarjayet  Hbhv āvikaṃ tu sadā vastraṃ pavitraṃ rājasattama pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ kriyāyāṃ ca praśasyate  Hbhv dhautādhautaṃ tathā dagdhaṃ sandhitaṃ rajakāhṛtam śukramūtraraktaliptaṃ tathāpi paramaṃ śuci  Hbhv agnir āvikavastraṃ ca brahmaṇāś ca tathā kuśāḥ caturṇāṃ na kṛto doṣo brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā  Hbhv kiṃ cānyatradhārayed vāsasī śuddhe paridhānottarīyake acchinnasudaśe śukle ācāmet pīṭhasaṃsthitaḥ  Hbhv atha pīṭhambahvṛcapariśiṣṭeyatīnām āsanaṃ śuklaṃ kūrmākāraṃ tu kārayet anyeṣāṃ tu catuṣpādaṃ caturasraṃ tu kārayet  Hbhv gośakṛnmayaṃ bhinnaṃ tathā palāśapaippalam lohabaddhaṃ sadaivārkaṃ varjayed āsanaṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv athāsanavidhiḥtatraivadānam ācamanaṃ homaṃ bhojanaṃ devatārcanam prauḍhapādo na kurvīta svādhyāyaṃ caiva tarpaṇam  Hbhv āsanārūḍhapādas tu jānunor vātha jaṅghayoḥ kṛtāvaskthiko yas tu prauḍhapādaḥ sa ucyate  Hbhv ititato bhūmigatāṅghriḥ san niviśyācamya darbhabhṛt ūrdhvapuṇḍrādikaṃ kuryāt śrīgopīcandanādinā  Hbhv tatrādāv anulepena bhagavaccaraṇābjayoḥ nirmālyena prasādena sarvāṇy aṅgāni mārjayet  Hbhv tad uktaṃ brāhme śrībhagavatāśālagrāmaśilālagnaṃ candanaṃ dhārayet sadā sarvāṅgeṣu mahāśuddhisiddhaye kamalāsana  Hbhv ititato dvādaśabhiḥ kuryān nāmabhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ dvādaśāṅgeṣu vidhivad ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṇi vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv atha dvādaśatilakavidhiḥpadmapurāṇe uttarakhaṇḍe lalāṭe keśavaṃ dhyāyen nārāyaṇam athodare vakṣaḥsthale mādhavaṃ tu govindaṃ kaṇṭhakūpake  Hbhv viṣṇuṃ ca dakṣiṇe kukṣau bāhau ca madhusūdanam trivikramaṃ kandhare tu vāmanaṃ vāmapārśvake  Hbhv śrīdharaṃ vāmabāhau tu hṛṣīkeśaṃ tu kandhare pṛṣṭhe tu padmanābhaṃ ca kaṭyāṃ dāmodaraṃ nyaset  Hbhv tatprakṣālanatoyaṃ tu vāsudeveti mūrdhani  Hbhv kiṃ ca ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ lalāṭe tu sarveṣāṃ prathamaṃ smṛtam lalāṭādikrameṇaiva dhāraṇaṃ tu vidhīyate  Hbhv itievaṃ nyāsaṃ samācarya sampradāyānusārataḥ nyaset kirīṭamantraṃ ca mūrdhni sarvārthasiddhaye  Hbhv atha kirīṭamantraḥoṃ śrīkirīṭakeyūrahāramakarakuṇḍalacakraśaṅkhagadāpadmahastapītāmbaradharaśrīvatsāṅkitavakṣaḥsthala śrībhūmisahitasvātmajyotir dīptikarāya sahasrādityatejasenamo namaḥ  Hbhv itiathordhvapuṇḍranityatāpādme śrībhagavaduktaumatpriyārthaṃ śubhārthaṃ vā rakṣārthe caturānana matpūjāhomakāle ca sāyaṃ prātaḥ samāhitaḥ madbhakto dhārayen nityam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ bhayāpaham  Hbhv tatraiva śrīnāradoktauyajño dānaṃ tapo homaḥ svādhyāyaḥ pitṛtarpaṇam vyarthaṃ bhavati tat sarvam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam  Hbhv tatraivottarakhaṇḍeūrdhvapuṇḍrair vihīnas tu kiṃcit karma karoti yaḥ iṣṭāpūrtādikaṃ sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv ūrdhvapuṇḍrair vihīnas tu sandhyākarmādikaṃ caret tat sarvaṃ rākṣasaṃ nityaṃ narakaṃ cādhigacchati  Hbhv anyac caūrdhvapuṇḍre tripuṇḍraṃ yaḥ kurute narādhamaḥ bhaṅktvā viṣṇugṛhaṃ puṇḍraṃ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv ata eva pādme śrīnāradoktauyac charīraṃ manuṣyāṇām ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam draṣṭavyaṃ naiva tat tāvat śmaśānasadṛśaṃ bhavet  Hbhv padmapurāṇeūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ mṛdā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate sa cāṇḍālo pi śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv skāndetiryakpuṇḍraṃ na kurvīta samprāpte maraṇepi ca naivānyan nāma ca brūyāt pumān nārārāyaṇād ṛte  Hbhv dhārayed viṣṇunirmālyaṃ dhūpaśeṣaṃ vilepanam vaiṣṇavaṃ kārayet puṇḍraṃ gopīcandanasambhavam  Hbhv tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅgeyasyordhvapuṇḍraṃ dṛśyeta lalāṭe no narasya hi taddarśanaṃ na kartavyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūryaṃ nirīkṣayet  Hbhv anyatrāpivaiṣṇavānāṃ brāhmaṇānām ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vidhīyate anyeṣāṃ tu tripuṇḍraṃ syād iti brahmavido viduḥ  Hbhv tripuṇḍraṃ yasya viprasya ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ na dṛśyate taṃ spṛṣṭvāpy athavā dṛṣṭvā sacelaṃ snānam ācaret  Hbhv ūrdhvapuṇḍre na kurvīta vaiṣṇavānāṃ tripuṇḍrakam kṛtatripuṇḍramartyasya kriyā na prītaye hareḥ  Hbhv ataevottarakhaṇḍeaśvatthapatrasaṅkāśo veṇupatrākṛtis tathā padmakuṭmalasaṅkāśo mohanaṃ tritayaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv athordhvapuṇḍramāhātmyamskānde kārttikaprasaṅgeūrdhvapuṇḍro mṛdā śubhro lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate caṇḍālo pi viśuddhātmā yāti braham sanātanam  Hbhv ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitā lakṣmīr ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitaṃ yaśaḥ ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitā muktir ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthito hariḥ  Hbhv padmapurāṇeūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ mudā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate sa cāṇḍālo pi śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv tatraivottarakhaṇḍe śivomāsaṃvāde  ūrdhvapuṇḍrasya madhye tu viśāle sumanohare lakṣmyā sārdhaṃ samāsīno devadevo janārdanaḥ  Hbhv tasmād yasya śarīre tu ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ dhṛto bhavet tasya dehaṃ bhagavato vimalaṃ mandiraṃ śubham  Hbhv ūrdhvapuṇḍradharo vipraḥ sarvalokeṣu pūjitaḥ vimānavaram āruhya yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  Hbhv ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate namaskṛtvāthavā bhaktyā sarvadānaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaṃ vipraṃ yaḥ śrāddhe bhojayiṣyati ākalpakoṭipitaras tasya tṛptā na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv ūrdhvapuṇḍradharo yas tu kuryāc chrāddhaṃ śubhānane kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi gayāśrāddhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv yajñadānatapaścaryājapahomādikaṃ ca yat ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaḥ kuryāt tasya puṇyam anantakam  Hbhv śrībrahmāṇḍapurāṇeaśucir vāpya nācāro manasā pāpam ācaran śucir eva bhaven nityam ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṅkito naraḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrībhagavadvacanamūrdhvapūṇḍradharo martyo mriyate yatra kutracit śvapāko pi vimānastho mama loke mahīyate  Hbhv ūrdhvapūṇḍradharo martyo gṛhe yasyānnam aśnute tadā viṃśatkulaṃ tasya narakād uddharāmy ahaṃ  Hbhv athohvapūṇḍrairmāṇavidhiḥśrībrahmāṇḍapurāṇevīkṣyādarśe jale vāpi yo vidadhyāt prayatnataḥ ūrdhvapūṇḍraṃ mahābhāga sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv daśāṅgulapramāṇaṃ tu uttamottamam ucyate navāṅgulaṃ madhyamaṃ syād aṣṭāṅgulam ataḥ param  Hbhv etair aṅgulibhedais tu kārayen na nakhaiḥ spṛśet  Hbhv padmapurāṇe uttarakhaṇḍe tatraiva   ekāntino mahābhāgāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ sāntarālaṃ prakurvīran puṇḍraṃ haripadākṛtim  Hbhv śyāmaṃ śāntikaraṃ proktaṃ raktaṃ vaśyakaraṃ tathā śrīkaraṃ pītam ity āhuḥ śvetaṃ mokṣakaraṃ śubham  Hbhv vartulaṃ tiryag achidraṃ hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ tataṃ tanum vakraṃ virūpaṃ baddhāgraṃ chinnamūlaṃ padacyutam  Hbhv aśubhaṃ rūkṣam āsaktaṃ tathā nāṅgulikalpitam vigandham avasahyaṃ ca puṇḍram āhur anarthakam  Hbhv ārabhya nāsikāmūlaṃ lalāṭāntaṃ likhen mṛdā nāsikāyās trayo bhāgā nāsāmūlaṃ pracakṣyate  Hbhv samārabhya bhruvor madhyam antarālaṃ prakalpayet  Hbhv tatraiva  nirantarālaṃ yaḥ kuryād ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ dvijādhamaḥ sa hi tatra sthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ śriyaṃ caiva vyapohati  Hbhv acchidram ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ tu ye kurvanti dvijādhamāḥ teṣāṃ lalāṭe satataṃ śunaḥ pādo na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv tasmāc chidrānvitaṃ puṇḍraṃ daṇḍākāraṃ suśobhanam viprāṇāṃ satataṃ kāryaṃ strīṇāṃ ca śubhadarśane  Hbhv harimandiralakṣaṇamnāsādikeśaprayantam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ suśobhanam madhye chidrasamāyuktaṃ tad vidyād harimandiram  Hbhv vāmapārśve sthito brahmā dakṣiṇe ca sadāśivaḥ madhye viṣṇuṃ vijānīyāt tasmān madhyaṃ na lepayet  Hbhv vāyupurāṇe sevāparādheadhṛtvā cordhvapuṇḍraṃ ca hareḥ pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ tiryakpuṇḍradharo yas tu yajed devaṃ janārdanam  Hbhv accidreṇordhvapuṇḍreṇa bhasmanā tiryagaṅginā adhṛtvā śaṅkhacakre ca cety ādinā doṣa uktaḥ  Hbhv śrutiś ca yajurvedasya hiraṇyakeśauryaśakhāyāmhareḥ padākrāntim ātmani dhārayati yaḥ sa parasya priyo bhavati sa puṇyavān madhye chidram ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃyo dhārayati sa muktibhāg bhavati  Hbhv ititilakaracanāṅguliniyamaḥsmṛtiḥanāmikā kāmadoktā madhyam āyuskarī bhavet aṅguṣṭhaḥ puṣṭidaḥ proktas tarjanī mokṣadāyinī  Hbhv athordhvapuṇḍramṛttikāḥpadmapurāṇe  tatraivaparvatāgre nadītīre bilvamūle jalāśaye sindhutīre ca valmīke harikṣetre viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv viṣṇoḥ snānodakaṃ yatra pravāhayati nityaśaḥ puṇḍrāṇāṃ dhāraṇārthāya gṛhṇīyāt tatra mṛttikām  Hbhv śrīraṅge veṅkaṭādrau ca śrīkūrme dvārake śubhe prayāge nārasiṃhādrau vārāhe tulasīvane  Hbhv gṛhītvā mṛttikāṃ bhaktyā viṣṇupādajalaiḥ saha dhṛtvā puṇḍrāṇi cāṅgeṣu viṣṇusāyujyam āpnuyāt  Hbhv tatraivayat tu divyaṃ harikṣetre tasyaiva mṛdam āharet  Hbhv uktaṃ ca pādme śrīnāradenabrahmaghno vātha goghno vā haitukaḥ sarvapāpakṛt gopīcandanasamparkāt pūto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  Hbhv gopīcandanakhaṇḍaṃ tu yo dadātii hi vaiṣṇave kulam ekottaraṃ tena sambhavet tāritaṃ śatam  Hbhv skandapurāṇeśaṅkhacakrāṅkitatanuḥ śirasā mañjarīdharaḥ gopīcandanaliptāṅgo dṛṣṭaś cet tad aghaṃ kṛtaḥ  Hbhv gopīmṛttulasī śaṅkhaḥ śālagrāmaḥ sacakrakaḥ gṛhepi yasya pañcaite tasya pāpabhayaṃ kutaḥ  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīyamenaśrīkhaṇḍe kva sa āmodaḥ svarovarṇaḥ kva tādṛśaḥ tat pāvitryaṃ kva vai tīrthe śrīgopīcandane yathā  Hbhv atha gopīcandanordhvapuṇḍramāhātmyamuktaṃ ca garuḍapurāṇe nāradenayo mṛttikāṃ dvāravatīsamudbhavāṃkare samādāya lalāṭapaṭṭake karoti nityaṃ tv atha cordhvapuṇḍraṃkriyāphalaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ sadā bhavet  Hbhv kriyāvihīnaṃ yadi mantrahīnaṃśraddhāvihīnaṃ yadi kālavarjitam kṛtvā lalāṭe yadi gopīcandanaṃprāpnoti tat karmaphalaṃ sadā kṣayam  Hbhv gopīcandanasambhavaṃ suruciraṃ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dvijonityaṃ dhārayate yadi dvijapate rātrau divā sarvadā yat puṇyaṃ kurujāṅgale ravigrahe mādhyāṃ prayāge tathātat prāpnoti khagendra viṣṇusadane santiṣṭhate devavat  Hbhv yasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati gopīcandanaṃbhaktyā lalāṭe manujo bibharti tasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati sarvadā hariḥśraddhānvitaḥ kaṃsahā vihaṅgama  Hbhv yo dhārayet kṛṣṇapurīsamudbhavāṃsadā pavitrāṃ kalikilbiṣāpahām nityaṃ lalāṭe harimantrasaṃyutāṃyamaṃ na paśyed yadi pāpasaṃvṛtaḥ  Hbhv yasyāntakāle khaga gopīcandanaṃbāhvor lalāṭE hṛdi mastake ca prayāti lokaṃ kamalālayaṃ prabhorgobālaghātī yadi brahmahā bhavet  Hbhv grahā na pīḍanti na rakṣasāṃ gaṇāḥyakṣāḥ piśācoragabhūtadānavāḥ lalāṭapaṭṭe khaga gopīcandanaṃsantiṣṭhate yasya hareḥ prasādataḥ  Hbhv padmapurāṇe śrīgotamenaambarīṣa mahāghasya kṣayārthe kuru vīkṣaṇam lalāṭe yaiḥ kṛtaṃ nityaṃ gopīcandanapuṇḍrakam  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīyamenadūtāḥ śṛṇuta yadbhālaṃ gopīcandanalāñchitam jvaladindhanavat so pi tyājyo dūre prayatnataḥ  Hbhv itiatha tasyopari śrīmattulasīmūlamṛtsnayā tatraiva vaiṣṇavaiḥ kāryam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ manoharam  Hbhv atha śrītulasīmūlamṛttikāpuṇḍramāhātmyamtanmṛdaṃ gṛhya yaiḥ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dhāritaṃ naraiḥ pramāṇakaṃ kṛtaṃ tais tu mokṣāya gamanaṃ prati  Hbhv tatraiva ca kārttikamāhātmye brahmanāradasaṃvādetulasīmṛttikāpuṇḍraṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate dehaṃ na spṛśati pāpaṃ kriyamāṇas tu nārada  Hbhv garuḍapurāṇetulasīmṛttikāpuṇḍraṃ yaḥ karoti dine dine tasyāvalokanāt pāpaṃ yāti varṣakṛtaṃ nṛṇām  Hbhv ititasyopariṣṭhād bhagavannirmālyam anulepanam tathaiva dhāryam evaṃ hi trividhaṃ tilakaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv tato nārāyaṇīṃ mudrāṃ dhārayet prītaye hareḥ matsyakūrmādicihnāni cakrādīny āyudhāni ca  Hbhv atha mudrādhāraṇanityatāsmṛtauaṅkitaḥ śaṅkhacakrābhyām ubhayor bāhumūlayoḥ samarcayed dhariṃ nityaṃ nānyathā pūjanaṃ bhavet  Hbhv ādityapurāṇeśaṅkhacakrordhvapuṇḍrādirahitaṃ brāhmaṇādhamam gardabhaṃ tu samāropya rājā rāṣṭrāt pravāsayet  Hbhv gāruḍe śrībhagavaduktausarvakarmādhikāraś ca śucīnām eva coditaḥ śucitvaṃ ca vijānīyān madīyāyudhadhāraṇāt  Hbhv pādme cottarakhaṇḍeśaṅkhacakrādibhiś cihnair vipraḥ priyatamair hareḥ rahitaḥ sarvadharmebhyaḥ pracyuto narakaṃ vrajet  Hbhv śrutau ca yajuḥkaṭhaśākhāyāmdhṛtordhvapuṇḍraḥ kutacakradhārīviṣṇuṃ paraṃ dhyāyati yo mahātmā svareṇa mantreṇa sadā hṛdi sthitaṃparātparaṃ yan mahato mahāntam  Hbhv atharvaṇi caebhir vayam urukramasya cihnairaṅkitā loke subhagā bhavema tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃye gacchanti lāṅchitāḥ  Hbhv  ity ādi ataeva brahmapurāṇekṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sammānaṃ na karoti yaḥ dvādaśābdārjitaṃ puṇyaṃ cāphalayopagacchati  Hbhv atha mudrādhāraṇamāhātmyamskānde śrīsanatkumāramārkaṇḍeyasaṃvādeyo viṣṇubhakto viprendra śaṅkhacakrādicihnitaḥ sa yāti viṣṇulokaṃ vai dāhapralayavarjitam  Hbhv tatra vāntyatra canārāyaṇāyudhair nityaṃ cihnitaṃ yasya vigraham pāpakoṭiyuktasya tasya kiṃ kurute yamaḥ  Hbhv śaṅkhoddhāre tu yat proktaṃ vasatāṃ varṣakoṭibhiḥ tat phalaṃ likhite śaṅkhe pratyahaṃ dakṣiṇe bhuje  Hbhv yat phalaṃ puṣkare nityaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣadarśane śaṅkhopari kṛte padme tat phalaṃ samavāpnuyāt  Hbhv vāme bhuje gadā yasya likhitā dṛśyate kalau gadādharo gayāpuṇyaṃ pratyahaṃ tasya yacchati  Hbhv yac cānandapure proktaṃ cakrasvāmīsamīpataḥ gadādhollikhite cakre tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇadarśane  Hbhv śrībhagavaduktauyaḥ punaḥ kalikāle tu matpurīsambhavāṃ mṛdam matsyakūrmādikāṃ cihnaṃ gṛhītvā kurute naraḥ  Hbhv dehe tasya praviṣṭo haṃ jānantu tridaśottamāḥ tasya me nāntaraṃ kiṃcit kartavyaṃ śreya icchatā  Hbhv mamāvatāracihnāni dṛśyante yasya vigrahe martyair martyo na vijñeyaḥ sa nūnaṃ māmakī tanūḥ  Hbhv pāpaṃ sukṛtarūpaṃ tu jāyate tasya dehinaḥ mamāyudhāni tasyāṅge likhitāni kalau yuge  Hbhv ubhābhyām api cihnābhyāṃ yo ṅkito matsyamudrayā kūrmayāpi svakaṃ tejo nikṣiptaṃ tasya vigrahe  Hbhv śaṅkhaṃ ca padmaṃ ca gadāṃ rathāṅgaṃmatsyaṃ ca kūrmaṃ racitaṃ svadehe karoti nityaṃ sukṛtasya vṛddhiṃpāpakṣayaṃ janmaśatārjitasya  Hbhv tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvādekṛṣṇaśastrāṅkakavacaṃ durbhedyaṃ devadānavaiḥ adṛśyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ śatrūṇāṃ rakṣasām api  Hbhv lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī durgā sāvitrī harivallabhā nityaṃ tasya vased dehe yasya śaṅkhāṅkitā tanuḥ  Hbhv gaṅgā gayā kurukṣetraṃ prayāgaṃ puṣkarādi ca nityaṃ tasya sadā tiṣṭhed yasya padāṅkitaṃ vapuḥ  Hbhv yasya kaumodakīcihnaṃ bhuje vāme kalipriya pratyahaṃ tatra draṣṭavyo gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgamaḥ  Hbhv savye kare gadādhastad rathāṅgaṃ tiṣṭhate yadi kṛṣṇena sahitaṃ tatra trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  Hbhv trayo gnayas trayo devā viṣṇos trīṇi padāni ca nivasanti sadā yasya yasya dehe sudarśanam  Hbhv kiṃ cakṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitā mudrā yasya nārāyaṇī kare ūrdhvalokādhikārī ca sa jñeyas tridaśāṃ patiḥ  Hbhv kṛṣṇamudrāprayuktas tu daivaṃ pitryaṃ karoti yaḥ nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ pratyahaṃ cākṣayaṃ bhavet  Hbhv pīḍayanti na tatraiva grahā ṛkṣāṇi rāśayaḥ aṣṭākṣarāṅkitā mudrā yasya dhātumayī kare  Hbhv vārāhe śrīsanatkumāroktaukṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dehaṃ gopīcandanamṛtsnayā prayāgādiṣu tīrtheṣu sa gatvā kiṃ kariṣyati  Hbhv yadā yasya prapaśyeta dehaṃ śaṅkhādicihnitam tadā tasya jagatsvāmī tuṣṭo harati pātakam  Hbhv bhavate yasya dehe tu ahorātraṃ dine dine śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaṃ likhitaṃ so cyutaḥ svayam  Hbhv nārāyaṇāyudhair yuktaṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ kalau yuge kurute puṇyakarmāṇi merutulyāni tāni vai  Hbhv śaṅkhādināṅkito bhaktyā śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kurute dvija vidhihīnaṃ tu sampūrṇaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu gayāsamam  Hbhv yathāgnir dahate prabalam uttare dvandvaśastv evam abhyarcya dehalyāṃ vāstupuruṣam  Hbhv sanātanaḥ evaṃ sāmānyena sarveṣām eva pūjāvidhir likhitaḥ idānīṃ yathāsthānaṃ yathākramam iti yal likhitaṃtad eva vivicya likhatidvārāgra iti dvārābhyām tatrāpy ādau dvārasyāgre yat bhūrūpaṃ pīṭhaṃtatra samastaparivārānvitān śrīkṛṣṇapārṣadān yajet pūjayet anantaraṃ tasya dvārasyāgre garuḍaṃ yadyapi dvāraśriyo rcanaṃ prabalārcanānantaram eva kramadīpikāyām uktamtathāpi iṣṭveti kṭvāpratyayena caṇḍādipūjātaḥ pūrvakāla eveti bodhitam tathaivaa sadācārāt kiṃ ca dvandva ity agre likhanātcaṇḍapracaṇḍābhyāṃ namaḥ ity evaṃ yugmatvena prayogo jñeyaḥ  HbhvC dvārāntaḥpārśvayor gaṅgāṃ yamunāṃ ca tato rcayet tatpārśvayoḥ śaṅkhanidhiṃ tathā padmanidhiṃ yajet  Hbhv sanātanaḥ dvārasyāntaḥ abhyantare tatpārśvadvaye tayor gaṅgāyamunayoḥ pārśvadvaye  HbhvC gaṇeśaṃ mandirasyāgnikoṇe durgāṃ ca nairṛte vāṇīṃ vāyavya aiśāne kṣetrapālaṃ tathārcayet  Hbhv sanātanaḥ āgneye koṇe gaṇeśam arcayet tathā coktaṃ kramadīpikāyām parivārārāḥ kṛtāḥ sarve punaḥ śrīviṣṇupārṣadāḥ dvārāgrābalipīṭhercyāḥ pakṣīndraś ca tadagrataḥ caṇḍapracaṇḍau prāg dhātṛvidhātārau ca dakṣiṇe jayaḥ savijayaḥ paścād balaḥ prabala uttare ūrdhve dvāraśriyaṃ ceṣṭvā dvāry etān yugmaśo rcayet pūjyo vāstupumāṃs tatra tatra dvāḥpīthamadhyataḥ dvārāntaḥpārśvayor arcyā gaṅgā ca yamunā nadī koṇeṣu vighnaṃ durgāṃ ca vāṇīṃ kṣetre samarcayet  iti dvāḥśākhām āśrayan vāmāṃ saṅkocyāṅgāni dehalīm aspṛṣṭvā praviśed veśma nyasyan prāg dakṣiṇaṃ padam  Hbhv sanātanaḥ vāmāṃ svavāmabhāgavartinīṃ dvāraśākhāṃ āśrayan īṣat spṛṣad nijāṅgāni saṃkocya dehalīm aspṛṣṭvā na laṅghayitvety arthaḥ dakṣiṇaṃ padaṃ prāk ādau nyasyan dakṣiṇapādanyāsakrameṇety arthaḥ veśma śrībhagavanmandiraṃ harer gehaṃ pravekṣyann iti pūrvalikhanāt praviśet tanmadhyaṃ śanaiḥ pūjako gacchet  HbhvC tathā ca sāradātilakekiṃcit spṛśan vāmaśākhāṃ dehalīṃ laṅghayan guruḥ aṅgaṃ saṅkocayann antaḥ praviśed dakṣiṇāṅghriṇā  Hbhv sanātanaḥ gurur iti dīkṣāvidhānoktaḥ  HbhvC atha gṛhapraveśamāhātmyamtanmāhātmyaṃ ca haribhaktisudhodayepraviśann ālayaṃ viṣṇor arcanārthaṃ subhaktimān na bhūyaḥ praviśan mātuḥ kukṣikārāgṛhaṃ sudhīḥ  Hbhv atha gṛhāntaḥpūjānairṛte vāstupuruṣaṃ brahmāṇam api pūjayet āsanastho yajet tāṃs tān anyatra bhagavadgṛhāt  Hbhv tatpūjāmantraś coktaḥpraṇavādicaturthyantaṃ devanāma namo ntakam pūjāmantram idaṃ proktaṃ sarvatrārcanakarmaṇi  Hbhv  iti atha kṛṣṇāgratas tiṣṭhan kṛtvā digbandhanaṃ kṣipet puṣpākṣatān samastāsu dikṣu tatroktamantrataḥ  Hbhv atha pūjārthāsanamtataś cāsanamantreṇābhimantryābhyarcya cāsanam tasminn upaviśet padmāsanena svastikena vā  Hbhv tatra kṛṣṇārcakaḥ prāyo divase prāṅmukho bhavet udaṅmukho rajanyāṃ tu sthiramūrtiś ca sammukhaḥ  Hbhv tatra ca ekādaśaskandhe BhP āsīnaḥ prāg udagvārcet sthirāyāntv atha sammukhaḥ  Hbhv athāsanamantraḥāsanamantrasya merupṛṣṭha ṛṣiḥ sutalaṃ chandaḥ kūrmo devatā āsanābhimantreṇa viniyogaḥ  Hbhv pṛthvi tvayā dhṛtā lokā devi tvaṃ viṣṇunā dhṛtā tvaṃ ca dhāraya māṃ nityaṃ pavitraṃ kuru cāsanam  Hbhv athāsanavidhiḥnāradapañcarātrevaṃśāśmadārudharaṇītṛṇapallavanirmitam varjayed āsanaṃ vidvān dāridryavyādhiduḥkhadam kṛṣṇājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā nānyad āsanam iṣyate  Hbhv anyatra cakṛṣṇājinaṃ vyāghracarma kauṣeyaṃ vetranirmitam vastrājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā kalpayed āsanaṃ mṛdu  Hbhv atha viśeṣata āsanadoṣavidhiḥnāradapañcarātrevaṃśād āhur daridratvaṃ pāṣāṇe vyādhisambhavam dharaṇyāṃ duḥkhasambhūtiṃ daurbhāgyaṃ dāravāsane  Hbhv tṛṇāsane yaśohāniṃ pallave cittavibhramam darbhāsane vyādhināśaṃ kambalaṃ duḥkhamocanam  Hbhv kiṃ ca śrībhagavadgītāsu ṅītā śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ nātyucchritaṃ nātinīcaṃ cailājinakuśottaram  Hbhv  iti yathokatam upaviśyātha sampradāyānusārataḥ śaṅkhādipūjāsambhārān nyaset tattatpadeṣu tān  Hbhv atha pātrāsādanamsvasya vāmāgrataḥ śaṅkhaṃ sādhāraṃ sthāpayed budhaḥ tatraivārdhyādipātrāṇi nyasyec ca dvāri bhāgaśaḥ  Hbhv tulasīgandhapuṣpādibhājanāni ca dakṣiṇe vāme ca sthāpayet pārśve kalasaṃ pūrṇam ambhasā  Hbhv dakṣiṇe ghṛtadīpaṃ ca tailadīpaṃ ca vāmataḥ sambhārānaparān nyaset svadṛṣṭiviṣaye pade karaprakṣālanārthaṃ ca pātram ekaṃ svapṛṣṭhataḥ  Hbhv atha pātrāṇi tanmāhātmyaṃ cadevīpurāṇenānāvicitrarūpāṇi puṇḍarīkākṛtīni ca śaṅkhanīlotpalābhāni pātrāṇi parikalpayet  Hbhv ratnādiracitāny eva kāñcīmūlayutāni ca yathāśobhaṃ yathālābhaṃ tathā pātrāṇi kārayet  Hbhv kiṃ cahaṃsapātreṇa sarvāṇi cepsitāni labhen mune arghyaṃ dattvā tathā raupyeṇāyurājyaṃ śubhaṃ bhavet tāmrapātreṇa saubhāgyaṃ dharmaṃ mṛṇmayasambhavam  Hbhv vārāhesauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ kāṃsyaṃ yena dīyate bhājanam tān sarvān samparityajya tāmraṃ tu mama rocate  Hbhv pavitrāṇāṃ pavitraṃ yo maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam viśuddhānāṃ śuciṃ caiva tāmraṃ saṃsāramokṣaṇam  Hbhv dīkṣitānāṃ viśuddhānāṃ mama karmaparāyaṇaḥ sadā tāmreṇa kartavyam evaṃ bhūmi mama priyam  Hbhv  iti kecic ca tāmrapātreṣu gavyāder yogadoṣataḥ tāmrātiriktam icchanti madhuparkasya bhājanam  Hbhv tathaiva śaṅkham evārdhyapātram icchanti kecana śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu pānīyaṃ sapuṣpaṃ salilākṣatam arghyaṃ dadāti devasyety evaṃ skāndebhidhānataḥ  Hbhv atha maṅgalaghaṭasthāpanammaṅgalārthaṃ ca kalasaṃ sajalaṃ karakānvitam phalādisahitaṃ divyaṃ nyased bhagavato grataḥ  Hbhv tathā ca skāndekumbhaṃ sakarakaṃ divyaṃ phalakarpūrasaṃyutam nyased arcanakāle tu kṛṣṇasyātīva vallabham  Hbhv  iti kiṃ casanīraṃ ca sakarpūraṃ kumbhaṃ kṛṣṇāya yo nyaset kalpaṃ tasya na pāpekṣāṃ kurvanti prapitāmahāḥ  Hbhv athārghyādipātrāṇiprakṣiped arghyapātre tu gandhapuṣpākṣatān yavān kuśāgratiladūrvāś ca siddhārthān api sādhakaḥ kecic cātra jalādīni dravyāṇy aṣṭau vadanti hi  Hbhv yata uktaṃ bhaviṣyeāpaḥ kṣīraṃ kuśāgrāṇi dadhyakṣatatilas tathā yavāḥ siddhārthakāś caivam arghyo ṣṭāṅgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv pādyapātre ca kamalaṃ dūrvā śyāmākam eva ca nikṣiped viṣṇupatrīṃ cety evaṃ dravyacatuṣṭayam  Hbhv tathaivācamanīyārthaṃ pātre dravyatrayaṃ budhaḥ jātīphalaṃ lavaṅgaṃ ca kakkolam api nikṣipet  Hbhv madhuparkīyapātre ca gavyaṃ dadhi payo ghṛtam madhukhaṇḍam apīty evaṃ nikṣiped dravyapañcakam  Hbhv kecit trīṇy eva pātresmin dravyāṇīcchanti sādhavaḥ  Hbhv yata uktaṃ śrīviṣṇudharmeghṛtaṃ dadhi tathā kṣaudraṃ madhuparko vidhīyate  Hbhv ādivārāhe cadadhisarpir madhusamaṃ pātre auḍumbare mama madhunas tu alābhe tu guḍena saha miśrayet  Hbhv ghṛtasyālābhe suśroṇi lājaiś ca saha miśrayet tathā dadhno py alābhe tu kṣīreṇa saha miśrayet  Hbhv teṣām abhāve puṣpādi tattadbhāvanayā kṣipet nāradas tv āha vimalenodakenaiva pūryate  Hbhv mūlena pātreṇaikena maṣṭakṛtvo bhimantrayet kuryāc ca teṣāṃ pātrāṇāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ cakramudrayā  Hbhv pūjām ārabhamāṇo hi yathoktāsanam āsthitaḥ paṭhen maṅgalaśāntiṃ tāṃ yārcane sammatā satām  Hbhv atha maṅgalaśāntiḥoṃ bhadraṃ karṇebhiḥ śṛṇuyāma devābhadraṃ paśyemākṣabhir yajatrā sthirair aṅgais tuṣṭuvāṃsas tanubhirvyaśema devahitaṃ yad āyuḥ  Hbhv svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ svasti naḥ pūṣā viśvadevāḥ svasti nas tārkṣo riṣṭanemiḥ svasti no bṛhaspatir dadhātu  Hbhv  iti paṭhan oṃ śāntiḥ śrīkṛṣṇapādapadmārādhaneṣu śāntir bhavatu  iti atha vighnanivāraṇamapasarpantu te bhūtā ye bhūtā bhuvi saṃsthitāḥ ye bhūtā vighnakartāras te naśyantu śivājñayā  Hbhv ity udīryāstramantreṇa vāmapādasya pārṣṇinā ghātais tribhir budho vighnān bhaumān sarvān nivārayet  Hbhv āntarīkṣāṃś ca tenaivordhvordhvatālatrayeṇa hi nirasyotsārayed divyān māntriko divyadṛṣṭitaḥ  Hbhv śrīgurvādinatiḥtataḥ kṛtāñjalir vāme śrīguruṃ paramaṃ gurum parameṣṭhiguruṃ ceti named guruparamparām  Hbhv gaṇeśaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge durgām agretha pṛṣṭhataḥ kṣetrapālaṃ named bhaktyā madhye cātmeṣṭadaivatam  Hbhv tataś cāstreṇa saṃśodhya karau kurvīta tena hi tālatrayaṃ diśāṃ bandham agniprākāram eva ca  Hbhv atha bhūtaśuddhiḥśarīrākārabhūtānāṃ bhūtānāṃ yad viśodhanam avyayabrahmasamparkād bhūtaśuddhir iyaṃ matā  Hbhv bhūtaśuddhiṃ vinā kartur japahomādikāḥ kriyāḥ bhavanti niṣphalāḥ sarvā yathāvidhy apy aniṣṭhitāḥ  Hbhv tatprakāraś cakarakacchapikāṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ buddhyā hṛdabjataḥ śiraḥsahasrapatrābje paramātmani yojayet pṛthivyādīni tattvāni tasmin līnāni bhāvayet  Hbhv vāmahastaṃ tathottānam adho dakṣiṇabandhitam karakacchapikā mudrā bhūtaśuddhau prakīrtitā  Hbhv dehaṃ saṃśoṣya dagdhvedam āplāvyāmṛtavarṣataḥ utpādya draḍhayitvāsupratiṣṭhāṃ vidhinācaret  Hbhv ātmānam evaṃ saṃśodhya nītvā kṛṣṇārcanārhatām vātsalyād dhṛdgataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ yaṣṭuṃ hṛt punar ānayet  Hbhv tathā ca trailokyasaṃmohanatantrenābhisthavāyunā dehaṃ sapāpaṃ śodhayed budhaḥ vahninā hṛdayasthena dahet tac ca kalevaram  Hbhv sahasrāre mahāpadme lalāṭasthe sthitaṃ vidhum sampūrṇamaṇḍalaṃ śuddhaṃ cintayed amṛtātmakam  Hbhv tasmād galitadhārābhiḥ plāvayed bhasmasād budhaḥ ābhir varṇamayībhiś ca pañcabhūtātmakaṃ vapuḥ pūrvavad bhāvayed devīm  Hbhv  ity ādi kiṃ cāgretatas tasmāt samākṛṣya praṇavena tu mantravit tat tejo hṛdaye nyasya cintayed viṣṇum avyayam  Hbhv kiṃ vā cintanamātreṇa bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāya tām prāṇāyāmāṃś tataḥ kuryāt sampradāyānusarataḥ  Hbhv atha prāṇāyāmaḥrecaḥ ṣoḍaśamātrābhiḥ pūro dvātriṃśatā bhavet catuḥṣaṣṭhyā bhavet kumbha evaṃ syāt prāṇasaṃyamaḥ  Hbhv virecya pavanaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃkocya gudamaṇḍalam pūrayitvā vidhānena svaśaktyā kumbhake sthitaḥ  Hbhv tatra praṇavam abhyasyan bījaṃ vā mantram ūrdhvagam ṛṣyādismaraṇaṃ kṛtvā kuryād dhyānam atandritaḥ  Hbhv tad dhyānaṃ coktamviṣṇuṃ bhāsvatkirīṭāṅgadavalayakalākalpahārodarāṅghriśroṇībhūṣaṃ savakṣomaṇimakaramahākuṇḍalāmṛṣṭagaṇḍam hastodyacchaṅkhacakrāmbujagadam amalaṃ pītakauśeyavāsaṃvidyotadbhāsam udyaddinakarasadṛśaṃ padmasaṃsthaṃ namāmi  Hbhv kvacic carudras tu recake brahmā pūrake dhyeyadevatā śrīviṣṇuḥ kumbhake jñeyo dhyānasthānaṃ guror mukhāt  Hbhv tathā hinābhisthāne pūrakeṇa cintayet kamalāsanam brahmāṇaṃ raktagaurāṅgaṃ caturvaktraṃ pitāmaham  Hbhv nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ hṛdi madhye pratiṣṭhitam caturbhujaṃ mahātmānaṃ kumbhakena tu cintayet  Hbhv recekanaiśvaraṃ dhyānaṃ lalāṭe sarvapāpaham śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśaṃ kuryād vai nirmalaṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv  iti ekāntibhiś ca bhagavān sarvadevamayaḥ prabhuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ priyajanopetaś cintanīyo hi sarvataḥ  Hbhv atha prāṇāyāmamāhātmyampādme  devahūtivikuṇḍalasaṃvādeyamalokaṃ na paśyanti prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇāḥ api duṣkṛtakarmāṇas tair eva hatakilbiṣāḥ  Hbhv divase divase vaiśya prāṇāyāmās tu ṣoḍaśa api brahmahaṇaṃ sākṣāt punanty aharahaḥ kṛtāḥ  Hbhv tapāṃsi yāni tapyante vratāni niyamāś ca ye gosahasrapradānaṃ ca prāṇāyāmas tu tatsamaḥ  Hbhv ambubinduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māse māse naraḥ pibet saṃvatsaraśataṃ sāgraṃ prāṇāyāmas tu tatsamaḥ  Hbhv pātakaṃ tu mahad yac ca tathā kṣudropapātakam prāṇāyāmaiḥ kṣaṇāt sarvaṃ bhasmasāt kurute naraḥ  Hbhv  iti nyāsān vinā japaṃ prāhur āsuraṃ viphalaṃ budhāḥ ato yathāsampradāyaṃ nyāsān kuryād yathāvidhi  Hbhv tatrādau mātṛkānyāsaḥṛṣicchandodevatādi smṛtvādau mātṛkāmanoḥ śirovaktrahṛdādau ca nyasya taddhyānam ācaret  Hbhv tac coktampañcāśallipibhir vibhaktamukhadoḥpanmadhyavakṣaḥsthalīṃbhāvanmaulinibaddhacandraśakalām āpīnatuṅgastanīm mudrām akṣaguṇaṃ sudhāḍhyakalasaṃ vidyāṃ ca hastāmbujairbibhrāṇāṃ viśadaprabhāṃ trinayanāṃ vāgdevatām āśraye  Hbhv akārādīn kṣakārāntān varṇānādau tu kevalān lalāṭādiṣu cāṅgeṣu nyased vidvān yathākramam  Hbhv tac ca vivicyoktamlalāṭamukhabimbākṣiśrutighrāṇeṣu gaṇḍayoḥ oṣṭhadantottamāṅgāsye doḥpatsandhyagrakeṣu ca  Hbhv pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhato nābhau jaṭhare hṛdayeṃsake kakudyase ca hṛtpūrvaṃ pāṇipādayuge tataḥ jaṭharānanayor nyasen mātṛkārṇān yathākramam  Hbhv  iti sānusvārān visargāḍhyān sānusvāravisargakān nyased bhūyo pi tān vidvān evaṃ vāracatuṣṭayam  Hbhv atha mātṛkānyāsaḥkaṇṭhahṛnnābhiguhyeṣu pāyubhrūmahdyayos tathā sthite ṣoḍaśapatrābje krameṇa dvādaśacchade  Hbhv daśapatre ca ṣaṭpatre catuṣpatre dvipatrake nyased ekaikapatrānte sabindvekaikam akṣaram  Hbhv atha keśavādinyāsaḥsmṛtvā ṛṣyādikāṃ varṇān mūrtibhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ kīrtyādibhiḥ śaktibhiś ca nyaset tān pūrvavat kramāt  Hbhv nyasec caturthīn atyantā mūrtīḥ śaktīś ca yādibhiḥ saptadhātūn prāṇajīvau krodham apy ātmanentakān  Hbhv tatra dhyānamudyatpradyotanaśataruciṃ taptahemāvadānaṃpārśvadvandve jaladhisutayā viśvadhātryā ca juṣṭam nānāratnollasitavividhākalpam āpītavastraṃviṣṇuṃ vande darakamalakaumodakīcakrapāṇim  Hbhv atha śrīmūrtayaḥprathamaṃ keśavo nārāyaṇaḥ paścāc ca mādhavaḥ govindaś ca tathā viṣṇur madhusūdana eva ca  Hbhv trivikramo vāmano tha śrīdharaś ca tataḥ param ṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhas tato dāmodaras tathā  Hbhv vāsudevaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ pradyumno thāniruddhakaḥ cakrī gadī tathā śārṅgī khaḍgī śaṅkhī halī tathā  Hbhv muṣalī ca tathā śūlī pāśī caivāṅkuśī tathā mukundo nandajaś caiva tathā nandī naras tathā  Hbhv narakajid dhariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ satyaḥ sātvata eva ca tataḥ śauris tathā śūras tataḥ paścāj janārdanaḥ  Hbhv bhūdharo viśvamūrtiś ca vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ balo balānujo bālo vṛṣaghno vṛṣa eva ca  Hbhv haṃso varāho vimalo nṛsiṃhaś ceti mūrtayaḥ  Hbhv atha śaktayaḥkīrtiḥ kāntis tuṣṭipuṣṭī dhṛtiḥ śāntiḥ kriyā dayā medhā harṣā tathā śraddhā lajjā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī  Hbhv prītī ratir jayā durgā prabhā satyā ca caṇḍikā vāṇī vilāsinī caiva vijayā virajā tathā  Hbhv viśvā ca vinadā caiva sunandā ca smṛtis tathā ṛddhiḥ samṛddhiḥ śuddhiś ca buddhir mūrtir natiḥ kṣamā  Hbhv ramomā kledinī klinnā vasudā vasudhā parā parāyaṇā ca sūkṣmā ca sandhyā prajñā prabhā niśā  Hbhv amoghā vidyutety ekapañcāśat śaktayo matāḥ dadāty ayaṃ keśavādinyāso trākhilasampadam  Hbhv amutrācyutasārūpyaṃ nayati nyāsamātrataḥ  Hbhv tad uktaṃdhyātvaivaṃ paramapumāṃsam akṣarair yovinyased dinam anu keśavādiyuktaiḥ medhāyuḥsmṛtidhṛtikīrtikāntilakṣmīsaubhāgyaiś ciram upabṛṃhito bhavet saḥ  Hbhv anyatra cakeśavādir ayaṃ nyāso nyāsamātreṇa dehinaḥ acyutatvaṃ dadāty eva satyaṃ satyaṃna saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv  iti yaś ca kuryād imaṃ nyāsaṃ lakṣmībījapuraḥsaram bhaktiṃ muktiṃ ca bhuktiṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca labhatecirāt  Hbhv tathā coktamamum eva ramāpuraḥsaraṃprabhajed yo manujo vidhiṃ budhaḥ samupetya ramāṃ prathīyasīṃpunar ante haritāṃ vrajaty asau  Hbhv atha tattvanyāsaḥmakārādikakārāntavarṇair yuktaṃ sabindukaiḥ namaḥ parāyeti pūrvam ātmane nama ity anu  Hbhv nāma jīvāditattvānāṃ nyaset tattatpade kramāt nyāsenānena loko hi bhavet pūjādhikāravān  Hbhv tatrādau sakale nyasej jīvaprāṇau kalevare hṛdaye maty ahaṅkāramanāṃsīti trayaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv śabdaṃ sparśaṃ tato rūpaṃ rasaṃ gandhaṃ ca mastake mukhe hṛdi ca guhye ca pādayoś ca yathākramam  Hbhv śrotraṃ tvacaṃ dṛśaṃ jihvāṃ ghrāṇaṃ svasvapade tataḥ vākpāṇipāyūpasthāni svasvapade tathā  Hbhv ākāśavāyutejāṃsi jalaṃ pṛthvīṃ ca mūrdhani vadane hṛdaye liṅge pādayoś ca yathākramam  Hbhv hṛdi hṛtpuṇḍarīkaṃ ca dviṣaṭdvyaṣṭadaśādikam kalāvyāpteti pūrvaṃ ca sūryacandrāgnimaṇḍalam varṇaiḥ saha sarephaiś ca kramān nyaset sabindukaiḥ  Hbhv vāsudevaṃ ṣakāreṇa parameṣṭhiyutaṃ ca ke yakāreṇa mukhe saṅkarṣaṇaṃ nyaset pumanvitam  Hbhv hṛdi nyasel lakāreṇa pradyumnaṃ viśvasaṃyutam aniruddhaṃ nivṛttyāḍhyaṃ vakāreṇa ca guhyake nārāyaṇaṃ ca sarvāḍhyaṃ lakāreṇaiva pādayoḥ  Hbhv nṛsiṃhaṃ kopasaṃyuktaṃ tadbījenākhilātmani tattvanyāso yam acirāt kṛṣṇasānnidhyakārakaḥ  Hbhv tathā coktamatattvavyāptyarūpasya tatprāpter hetunā punaḥ tattvanyāsam iti prāhur nyāsatattvavido budhāḥ  Hbhv yaḥ kuryāt tattvavinyāsaṃ sa pūto bhavati dhruvam tadātmanānupraviśya bhagavān iha tiṣṭhati yataḥ sa eva tattvāni sarvaṃ tasmin pratiṣṭhitam  Hbhv atha punaḥ prāṇāyāṃaviśeṣaḥprāṇāyāmāṃs tataḥ kuryān mūlamantraṃ japan kramāt vārau dvau caturaḥ ṣaṭ ca recapūrakakumbhakaḥ  Hbhv athavā recakādīṃs tān kuryād vārāṃs tu ṣoḍaśa dvātriṃśac ca catuḥṣaṣṭhiṃ kāmabījaṃ japan kramāt  Hbhv tathā ca kramadīpikāyām recayen mārutaṃ dakṣayā dakṣiṇaḥpūrayed vāmayā madhyanāḍyā punaḥ dhārayed īritaṃ recakāditrayaṃ syātkalādantavidyākhyamātrācyukam  Hbhv sanātanaḥ tad eva kramadīpikoktyā saṃvādayan tatraiva kiṃcid viśeṣaṃ ca darśayatirecayed iti dakṣayā dakṣiṇanāḍyādakṣiṇaḥ vidvān janaḥ madhyanāḍyā suṣumṇayā dhārayet evaṃ recakapūrakakumbhakākhyaṃ trayaṃ syāt recakādiṣu triṣu krameṇāvadhikālam āhakalāḥ ṣoḍaśa dantā dvātriṃśat vidyāś catuḥṣaṣṭhis tattatsaṅkhyakamātrātmakam ity arthaḥ mātrā cavāmāṅguṣṭhena vāmakaniṣṭhādyaṅgulīnāṃ pratyekaṃ parvatrayasamparkakālaḥ vāmahastena vāmajānumaṇḍalasya prādakṣiṇyena sparśakālo vā tatrāpy aṅguliniyamo py uktaḥkaniṣṭhānāmikāṅguṣṭhair yan nāsāpuṭadhāraṇam prāṇāyāmaḥ sa vijñeyas tarjanīmadhyame vinā  iti tatra teṣu prāṇāyāmeṣu purvaṃ recakādiṣu saṅkhyoktā atra ca prāṇāyāmeṣv iti bhedaḥ  HbhvC tatra kālaḥ saṅkhyādikaṃ catatraiva purato japasya parato pivihitam atha tattrayaṃ budhaiḥ ṣoḍaśa ya iha samācared dineśaḥparipūyate sa khalu māsato ṃ haṃsaḥ  Hbhv sanātanaḥ japasya purata ādau parataḥ ante ca iti prāṇāyāmeṣu kālaḥ tat trayaṃ prāṇāyāmatrayam iti saṅkhyā yo jano dinaśaḥ pratyahaṃ ṣoḍaśaprāṇāyāmān ācaretsa māsataḥ māsenaikena aṃhasaḥ pāpāt paripūyate śuddho bhavatīti sāmānyataḥ phalam paraṃ ca sarvaṃ purvaṃ likhitam eva  HbhvC atha pīṭhanyāsaḥtato nijatanūm eva pūjāpīṭhaṃ prakalpayet pīṭhasyādhāraśaktyādīn nyaset svāṅgeṣu tāravat  Hbhv ādhāraśaktiṃ prakṛtiṃ kūrmānantau ca tatra tu pṛthivīṃ kṣīrasindhuṃ ca śvetadvīpaṃ ca bhāsvaram  Hbhv śrīratnamaṇḍapaṃ caiva kalpavṛkṣaṃ tathā hṛdi nyaset pradakṣiṇatvena dharmajñāne tato ṃsayoḥ  Hbhv ūrvor vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ tathaivādharmam ānane trikejñānam avairāgyam anaiśvaryaṃ ca pārśvayoḥ  Hbhv hṛdabjenantapadmaṃ ca sūryenduśikhinān tathā maṇḍalāni kramād varṇaiḥ praṇavāṃśaiḥ sabindukaiḥ  Hbhv sattva rajas tamaś cātmāntarātmānau ca tatra hi paramātmānam apy ātmādyādyavarṇaiḥ sabindukaiḥ  Hbhv jñānātmānaṃ ca bhuvaneśvarībījena saṃyutam tasyāṣṭadikṣu madhyepi navaśaktīś ca dikkramāt  Hbhv tāś coktāḥvimalotkarṣiṇī jñānā kriyā yogeti śaktayaḥ prahvī satyā tatheśānānugrahā navam smṛtā  Hbhv  iti nyaset tadupariṣṭhāc ca pīṭhamantraṃ yathoditam ṛṣyādikaṃ smared asyāṣṭādaśārṇamanos tataḥ  Hbhv jñeyāś caikāntibhiḥ kṣīrasamudrādicatuṣṭayam kramāc chrīmathurāvṛndāvanaṃ tatkuñjanīpakāḥ  Hbhv tato pīṭhanyāsaḥtathā ca brahmasaṃhitāyām ādipuruṣarahasyastotre sa yatra kṣīrābdhiḥ sravati surabhībhyaś ca sumahānnimeṣārdhākhyo vā vrajati na hi yatrāpi samayaḥ bhaje śvetadvīpaṃ tam aham iha golokam iti yaṃvidantas te santaḥ kṣitiviralacārāḥ katipaye  Hbhv kramadīpikāyāṃ evaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvānvitaś ca bhūtātmā ṅentāḥ savāsudevāḥ sarvātmayutaṃ ca saṃyogaṃ  Hbhv yogāvadhaś ca padmaṃ pīṭhāt ṅeyuto natiś cānte pīṭhamahāmanur vyaktaḥ paryāpto yaṃ saparyāsu  Hbhv sanātanaḥ tāraḥ praṇavaḥ tato hṛdayaṃ nama iti padam tataś ca bhagavān iti viṣṇur iti ca sarvānvitaḥ sarvaśabdayukto bhūtātmā sarvabhūtātmeti ete trayaḥ savāsudevā vāsudevasahitāḥ pratyekaṃ ṅentāś caturthyantāḥ tataś ca sarvātmanā yutaṃ saṃyogaṃ sarvātmasaṃyogam iti napuṃsakatvam ārṣam tataś ca yogasyāvadhau ante padmaṃ yogapadmam iti tadante ṅeyuktaś caturthyantaḥ pīṭhātmā tadante ca natiḥ namaḥśabdaḥ evaṃ oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarvabhūtātmane vāsudevāya sarvātmasaṃyogayogapadmapīṭhātmane nama iti siddham tathā ca śāradātilakenamo bhagavate brūyād viṣṇave ca padaṃ vadet sarvabhūtātmane vāsudevāyeti vadet tataḥ sarvātmasaṃyogapadād yogapadmapadaṃ punaḥ pīṭhātmane hṛdanto yaṃ mantras tārādir īritaḥ  iti sanatkumārakalpe caoṃ namaḥ padam ābhāṣya tathā bhagavatepadam vāsudevāya ity uktvā sarvātmeti padaṃ tathā saṃyogayogety uktvā ca tathā pīṭhātmane padam vahnipatnīsamāyuktaḥ pīṭhamantra itīritaḥ  iti  atha ṛṣyādismaraṇamoṃ aṣṭādaśākṣaramantrasya śrīnārada ṛṣir gāyatrīcchandaḥsakalalokamaṅgalo nandatanayo devatāhrīṃ bījaṃsvāhā śaktiḥkṛṣṇaḥ prakṛtirdurgādhiṣṭhātrī devatāabhimatārthe viniyogaḥ  Hbhv tathā ca saṃmohanatantre śivomāsaṃvādeṛṣir nārada ity ukto gāyatrīcchanda ucyate gopaveśadharaḥ kṛṣṇo devatā parikīrtitaḥ  Hbhv bījaṃ manmathasaṃjñaṃ tu priyā śaktir havir bhujaḥ tvam eva parameśāni asyādhiṣṭhātṛdevatā caturvargaphalāvāptyai viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv athāṅganyāsaḥcatuś caturbhir varṇaiś ca catvāry aṅgāni kalpayet dvābhyām astrākhyam aṅgaṃ ca tasyety aṅgāni pañca vai  Hbhv nyasyec ca vyāpakatvena tāny aṅgāni karadvaye tāny aṅgulīṣu pañcātha kecid varṇān svarān api  Hbhv te coktāḥdrāvaṇakṣobhaṇākarṣavaśīkṛtsrāvaṇās tathā śoṣaṇo mohanaḥ sandīpanas tāpanamādanau  Hbhv  iti kiṃ canamo ntaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāṅgaiḥ śiraḥ svāhānvitaṃ śikhām vaṣaḍyutaṃ ca kavacaṃ huṃyugastraṃ ca phaḍyutam  Hbhv nyasyanti punar aṅguṣṭhau tarjanyau madhyame tathā anāmike kaniṣṭhe ca kramād aṅgaiś ca pañcabhiḥ  Hbhv punaś ca hṛdayādīni tathāṅguṣṭhādikāni ca nyasyanti yugapat sarvāṇy aṅgais taiḥ pañcabhiḥ kramāt  Hbhv nyasyanti ca ṣaḍaṅgāni hṛdayādīni tanmanoḥ hṛdayādiṣu caiteṣāṃ pañcaikaṃ dikṣu ca kramāt  Hbhv ṣaḍaṅgāni coktāni sammohanatantre sanatkumārakalpevarrṇenaikena hṛdayaṃ tirbhir eva śiro matam caturbhiś ca śikhā proktā tathaiva kavacaṃ matam netraṃ tathā caturvarṇair astraṃ dvābhyāṃ tathā matam  Hbhv  iti tataś cāpādam ākeśān nyased dorbhyām imaṃ manum vārāṃs trīn vyāpakatvena nyasec ca praṇavaṃ sakṛt  Hbhv athākṣaranyāsaḥtato ṣṭādaśavarṇāṃś ca mantrasyāsya yathākramam dante lalāṭe bhrūmadhye karṇayor netrayor dvayoḥ  Hbhv nāsayor vadane kaṇṭhe hṛdi nābhau kaṭidvaye guhye jānudvaye caikaṃ nyased ekaṃ ca pādayoḥ  Hbhv santo nyasyanti tārādinamo nantāṃs tān sabindukān śrīśaktikāmabījaiś ca sṛṣṭyādikramato pare  Hbhv atha padanyāsaḥtāraṃ śirasi vinyasya pañca mantrapadāni ca nyasen netradvaye vaktre hṛdguhyāṅghriṣu ca kramāt  Hbhv dehe ca vyāpakatvena nyaset tāny akhile punaḥ kecit tāni namo ntāni nyasyanty ādyākṣaraiḥ saha  Hbhv svāhāntāni tathā trīṇi saṃmiśrāṇy uttarottaraiḥ guhyād galān mastakāc ca vyāpayya caraṇāvadhi  Hbhv nyāso tra jñānaniṣṭhānāṃ guhyādiviṣayas tu yaḥ svasvavarṇatanoḥ kāryas tattadvarṇeṣu vaiṣṇavaiḥ  Hbhv atha ṛṣyādinyāsaḥṛṣyādīn saptabhāgāṃś ca nyased asya manoḥ kramāt mūrdhāsyahṛtsu kucayoḥ punar hṛdi punar hṛdi  Hbhv atha mudrāpañcakamveṇvākhyāṃ vanamālākhyāṃ mudrāṃ sandarśayet tataḥ śrīvatsākhyāṃ kaustubhākhyāṃ blivākhyāṃ ca manoramām  Hbhv itthaṃ naystaśarīraḥ san kṛtvā digbandhanaṃ punaḥ karakacchapikāṃ kṛtvā dhāyec chrīnandanandanam  Hbhv atha śrīnandandanabhagavaddhyānavidhiḥKramadīpikā atha prakaṭasaurabhodgalitamādhvikotphullasatprasūnanavapallavaprakaranamraśākhair drumaiḥ praphullanavamañjarīlalitavallarīveṣṭitaiḥsmarec chiśiritaṃ śivaṃ sitamatis tu vṛndāvanam  Hbhv athānantaraṃ sitamatiḥ śuddhamanāḥ san vṛndāvanaṃ cintayet kīdṛśaṃ  drumaiḥ śiśiritaṃ śītalīkṛtam kīdṛśaiḥ  prakaṭam udbhaṭaṃ saurabhaṃ yasya tac ca tad udgalitamādhvīkaṃ ca pracyutamadhu utphullaṃ ca vikasitaṃ sac ca uttamaṃ yat prasūnaṃ puṣpaṃ navapallavaṃ ca tayoḥ prakaraḥ samūhaḥ tena namrāḥ śākhā yeṣāṃ taiḥ mādhviketihrasvatvaṃ mahākavinibaddhatvāt soḍhavyam prakaṭasaurabhākulitamattabhṛṅgollasad iti pāṭhas tu sugama eva punaḥ kīdṛśaiḥ praphullābhir navamañjarībhir lalitā manoharā yā vallaryaḥ agraśākhā latā vātabhir veṣṭitaiḥ śivaṃ maṅgalarūpaṃnirbādhatvāt paramakalyāṇakaratvāc ca  HbhvC vikāsisumanorasāsvādanamañjulaiḥ sañcaracchilīmukhamukhodgatair mukharitāntaraṃ jhaṅkṛtaiḥ kapotaśukaśārikāparabhṛtādibhiḥ patribhirvirāṇitam itas tato bhujagaśatrunṛtyākulam  Hbhv kalindaduhituś calallaharivipruṣāṃ vāhibhirvinidrasarasīruhodararajaścayoddhūsaraiḥ pradīpitamanobhavavrajavilāsinīvāsasāṃvilolanavihāribhiḥ satatasevitaṃ mārutaiḥ  Hbhv pravālanavapallavaṃ marakatacchadaṃ vajramauktikaprakarakorakaṃ kamalarāganānāphalam sthaviṣṭham akhilartubhiḥ satatasevitaṃ kāmadaṃtadantar api kalpakāṅghripam udañcitaṃ cintayet  Hbhv suhemaśikharāvaler uditabhānuvad bhāsvaramadho sya kanakasthalīm amṛtaśīkarāsāriṇaḥ pradīptamaṇikuṭṭimāṃ kusumareṇupuñjojjvalāṃsmaret punar atandrito vigataṣaṭtaraṅgāṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv tadratnakuṭṭimaniviṣṭamahiṣṭhayogapīṭheṣṭapatram araṇaṃ kamalaṃ vicintya udyadvirocanasarocir amuṣya madhyesañcintayet ssukhaniviṣṭam atho mukundam  Hbhv sūtrāmaratnadalitāñjanameghapuñjapratyagranīlajalajanmasamānabhāsam uccalacillimālam  Hbhv āpūrṇaśāradagatāṅkaśaśāṅkabimbakāntānanaṃ kamalapatraviśālanetram ratnasphuranmakarakuṇḍalaraśmidīptagaṇḍasthalīmukuram unnatacārunāsam  Hbhv sindūrasundaratarādharam cārūrujānumanuvṛttamanojñajaṅghaṃkāntonnataprapadaninditakūrmakāntim māṇikyadarāṇalasannakharājirājadratnāṅgulicchadanasundarapādapadmam  Hbhv āsyāravindaparipūritaveṇurandhralolatkarāṅgulisamīritadivyarāgaiḥ śaśvadddravīkṛtavikṛṣṭasamastajantusantānasantatim anantasukhāmburāśim  Hbhv gobhir mukhāmbujavilīnavilocanābhirūdhobharaskhalitamantharamandagābhiḥ dantāgradaṣṭapariśiṣṭatṛṇāṅkurābhirālambvāladhilatābhivītam  Hbhv pratyagraśṛṅgamṛdumastakasamprahārasaṃrambhavalganavilolakhurāgrapātaiḥ āmedurair bahulasāsnagalair udagrapucchaiś ca vatsataravatsatarīnikāyaiḥ  Hbhv hambāravakṣubhitadigvalayair mahadbhirapy mandroccatārapaṭagānaparair viloladorvallarīlalitalāsyavidhānadakṣaiḥ  Hbhv jaṅghāntapīvarakaṭīrataṭīnibaddhavyālolakiṅkiṇighaṭāraṭitair aṭadbhiḥ mugdhais Hbhv tadatimadhuracāruveṇuvādyāmṛtarasapallavitāṅgajāṅghripāṇām mukulavisararamyarūḍharomodgamasamalaṅkṛtagānavallarīṇām  Hbhv tadatiruciramandahāsacandrātapaparijṛmbhitarāgavārirāśeḥ taralatarataraṅgabhaṅgavipruṭprakarasamaśramabindusantatānām  Hbhv tadatilalitamandacillicāpacyutaniśitekṣaṇamārabāṇavṛṣṭyā dalitasakalamarmavihvalāṅgapravisṛtaduḥsahavepathuvyathānām  Hbhv padmaṃ vāmano vahate sadā padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ śrīdharo vahate bhujaiḥ  Hbhv cakraṃ padmaṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ narasiṃho bibharti yaḥ padmaṃ sudarśanaṃ śaṅkhaṃ gadāṃ dhatte janārdanaḥ  Hbhv aniruddhaś cakragadāśaṅkhapadmalasadbhujaḥ hṛṣīkeśo gadāṃ cakraṃ padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca dhārayet  Hbhv padmanābho vahet śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ tathā padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ dhatte dāmodaraḥ sadā  Hbhv śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ sarojaṃ ca gadāṃ vahati yo hariḥ śaṅkhaṃ kaumodakīṃ padmaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇur bibharti yaḥ  Hbhv etāś ca mūrtayo jñeyā dakṣiṇādhaḥkarakramāt  Hbhv matsyapurāṇe caetaduddeśataḥ proktaṃ pratimālakṣaṇaṃ tathā vistareṇa na śaknoti bṛhaspatir api dvijāḥ  Hbhv  iti sevāniṣṭhā hareḥ śrīmadvaiṣṇavāḥ pāñcarātrikāḥ prākaṭyād akhilāṅgānāṃ śrīmūrtiṃ bahu manyate  Hbhv sevyā nijanijair eva mantraiḥ svasveṣṭamūrtayaḥ śālagrāmātmake rūpe niyamo naiva vidyate  Hbhv dvibhujā jaladaśyāmā tribhaṅgī madhurākṛtiḥ sevyā dhyānānurūpaiś ca mūrtiḥ kṛṣṇasya daivataiḥ  Hbhv anyāś ca vividhā śrīmadavatārādimūrtayaḥ prādurbhāvavidhāv agre lekhyās tattadviśeṣataḥ  Hbhv nityakarmaprasaṅgetra mūrtijanmapratiṣṭhayoḥ vidhir na likhituṃ yogyaḥ sa tu lekhiṣyategrataḥ  Hbhv atha śālagrāmaśilāḥgautamīyatantregaṇḍakyāś caiva deśe ca śālagrāmasthalaṃ mahat pāṣāṇaṃ tadbhavaṃ yat tat śālagrāmam iti smṛtam  Hbhv skandapurāṇesnigdhā kṛṣṇā pāṇḍarā vā pītā nīlā tathaiva ca vakrā rukṣā ca raktā ca mahāsthūlā tv alāñchitā  Hbhv kapilā dardurā bhagnā bahucakraikacakrikā bṛhanmukhī bṛhaccakrā lagnacakrāthavā punaḥ baddhacakrāthavā kācid bhagnacakrā tv adhomukhī  Hbhv atha tāsāṃ varṇādibhedena guṇadoṣautatraivasnigdhā siddhikarī mantre kṛṣṇā kīrtiṃ dadāti ca pāṇḍarā pāpadahanī pītā putraphalapradā  Hbhv nīlā sandiśate lakṣmīṃ raktā rogapradāyikā rakṣā codvegadā nityaṃ vakrā dāridryadāyikā  Hbhv sthūlā nihati caivāyur niṣphalā tu alāñchitā kapilā karburā bhagnā bahucakraikacakrikā  Hbhv bṛhanmukhī bṛhaccakrā lagnacakrāthavā punaḥ  Hbhv baddhacakrāthavā yā syād bhagnacakrā tv adhomukhī pūjayed yaḥ pramādena duḥkham eva labheta saḥ  Hbhv agnipurāṇe catathā vyālamukhī bhagnā viṣayā baddhacakrikā vikārāvartanābhiś ca nārasiṃhī tathaiva ca  Hbhv kapilā vibhramāvartā rekhāvartā ca yā śilā duḥkhadā sā tu vijñeyā sukhadā na kadācana  Hbhv snigdhā śyāmā tathā muktāmāyā vā samacakrikā ghoṇimūrtir anantākhyā gambhīrā sampuṭā tathā  Hbhv sūkṣmamūrtir amūrtiś ca sammukhā siddhidāyikā dhātrīphalapramāṇā yā kareṇobhayasampuṭā pūjanīyā prayatnena śilā caitādṛśī śubhā  Hbhv iṣṭā tu yasya yā mūrtiḥ sa tāṃ yatnena pūjayet pūjite phalam āpnoti ihaloke paratra ca  Hbhv doṣāś caite sakāmārcanaviṣayāḥyata uktaṃ śrībhagavatā brāhmekhaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ bhagnaṃ pārśvabhinnaṃ vibheditam śālagrāmasamudbhūtaṃ śailaṃ doṣāvahaṃ na hi  Hbhv śrīrudreṇa ca skāndekhaṇḍitaṃ truṭitaṃ bhagnaṃ śālagrāme na doṣabhāk iṣṭā tu yasya yā mūrtiḥ sa tāṃ yatnena pūjayet  Hbhv tathācakraṃ vā kevalaṃ tatra padmena saha saṃyutam kevalā vanamālā vā harir lakṣmyā saha sthitaḥ  Hbhv mukhyāḥ snighdādayas tatrāmukhyā raktādayo matāḥ mukhyābhāve tv amukhyā hi pūjyā ity ucyate paraiḥ  Hbhv atha tāsām eva lakṣaṇaviśeṣeṇa saṃjñaviśeṣaḥbrāhme śrībhagavadbrahmasaṃvādenivasāmi sadā brahman śālāgrāmākhyaveśmani tatraiva rathacakrāṅkabhedanāmāni me śṛṇu  Hbhv dvāradeśe same cakre dṛśyate nāntarīyake vāsudevaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ śuklābhaś cātiśobhanaḥ  Hbhv dve cakre ekalagne tu pūrvabhāgas tu puṣkalaḥ saṅkarṣaṇākhyo vijñeyo raktābhiś cātiśobhanaḥ  Hbhv pradyumnaḥ sūkṣmacakras tu pītadīptis tathaiva ca śuṣiraṃ chidrabahulaṃ dīrghākāraṃ tu tad bhavet  Hbhv aniruddhas tu nīlābho vartulaś cātiśobhanaḥ rekhātrayaṃ tu tad dvāri pṛṣṭhaṃ padmena lāñchitam  Hbhv saubhāgyaṃ keśavo dadyāt catuṣkoṇo bhavet tu yaḥ śyāmaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ vidyān nābhicakraṃ tathonnatam  Hbhv dīrgharekhāsamopetaṃ dakṣiṇe śuṣiraṃ pṛthu ūrdhvaṃ mukhaṃ vijānīyāt dvāre ca harirūpiṇam  Hbhv kāmadaṃ mokṣadaṃ caiva arthadaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ parameṣṭhī lohitabhaḥ padmacakrasamanvitaḥ  Hbhv bilvākṛtis tathā pṛṣṭhe śuṣiraṃ cātipuṣkalam kṛṣṇavarṇas tathā viṣṇuḥ sthūle cakre suśobhanaḥ bramacaryeṇa pūjyo sāv anyathā vighnado bhavet  Hbhv kvacic cakapilo narasiṃho tha pṛthucakre ca śobhane brahmacaryādhikārī syān nānyathā pūjanaṃ bhavet  Hbhv narasiṃhas tribinduḥ syāt kapilaḥ pañcabindukaḥ brahmacaryeṇa pūjyaḥ syād anyathā sarvavighnadaḥ  Hbhv sthūlaṃ cakradvayaṃ madhye guḍalākṣāsavarṇakam dvāropari tathā rekhā padmākārā suśobhanā  Hbhv sphuṭitaṃ viṣamaṃ cakraṃ nārasiṃhaṃ tu kāpilam sampūjya muktim āpnoti saṃgrāme vijayī bhavet  Hbhv pādme kārttikamāhātmye cayasya dīrghaṃ mukhaṃ pūrvakathitair lakṣaṇair yutam rekhāś ca keśarākārā nārasiṃho mato hi saḥ  Hbhv brāhme PadmaP vārāhaṃ śaktiliṅge ca cakre ca viṣame smṛte indranīlanibhaṃ sthūlaṃ trirekhālāñchitaṃ śubham  Hbhv pādme ca tatraivavarāhākṛtir ābhugnaś cakrarekhāsv alaṅkṛtaḥ vārāha iti sa prokto bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ  Hbhv brāhma evadīrghā kāñcanavarṇā yā bindutrayavibhūṣitā matsyākhyā sā śilā jñeyā bhuktimuktiphalapradā  Hbhv kvacic camatsyarūpaṃ tu deveśaṃ dīrghākāraṃ tu yad bhavet bindutrayam āyuktaṃ kāsyavarṇaṃ viśobhanam  Hbhv brāhma PadmaP  evakūrmas tathonnataḥ pṛṣṭhe vartulāvartapūritaḥ haritaṃ varṇam ādhatte kaustubhena ca cihnitaḥ  Hbhv pādme ca tatraivakūrmākārā ca cakrāṅkā śilā kūrmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv brāhma PadmaP  evahayagrīvo ṅkuśākāro rekhā cakraśamīpagāḥ bahucakrasamāyuktaṃ pṛṣṭhe nīradanīlakam  Hbhv kvacic cahayagrīvāṅkuśākāre rekhāḥ pañca bhavanti hi bahubindusamākīrṇe dṛśyante nīlarūpakāḥ  Hbhv pādme ca tatraivahāyagrīvā yathā lambā rekhāṅkā yā śilā bhavet tathāsau syād dhayagrīvaḥ pūjito jñānado bhavet  Hbhv kiṃ caaśvākṛti mukhaṃ yasya sākṣamālaṃ śiras tathā padmākṛtir bhaved vāpi hayaśīrṣas tv asau mataḥ  Hbhv brāhme PadmaP  evavaikuṇṭham maṇivarṇābhaṃ cakram ekaṃ tathā dhvajam dvāropari tathā rekhā padmākārā suśobhanā  Hbhv śrīdharas tu tathā devaś cihnito vanamālayā kadambakusumākāro rekhāpañcakabhūṣitaḥ  Hbhv vartulaś cātihrasvaś ca vāmanaḥ parikīrtitaḥ atasīkusumaprakhyo bindunā pariśobhitaḥ  Hbhv anyatra cavāmanākhyo bhaved devo hrasvo yaḥ syān mahādyutiḥ ūrdhvacakras tv adhaś cakraḥ so bhīṣṭārthaprado rcitaḥ  Hbhv brāhme PadmaP  evasudarśanas tathā devaḥ śyāmavarṇo mahādyutiḥ vāmapārśve gadācakre rekhe caiva tu dakṣiṇe  Hbhv pādme kārttikamāhātmyecakrākāreṇa paṅktiḥ sā yatra rekhāmayī bhavet sa sudarśana ity evaṃ khyātaḥ pūjāphalapradaḥ  Hbhv brāhme PadmaP dāmodaras tathā sthūlo madhye cakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam dūrvābhaṃ dvārasaṅkīrṇaṃ pītā rekhā tathaiva ca  Hbhv pādme ca tatraivauparyadhaś ca cakre dve nātidīrghaṃ mukhe bilam cakre ca rekhā lambaikā sa ca dāmodaraḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv anyatra casthūlo dāmodaro jñeyaḥ sūkṣmarandhro bhavet tu yaḥ cakre ca madhyadeśasthe pūjitaḥ sukhadaḥ sadā  Hbhv nānāvarṇo hy anantākhyo nāgabhogena cihnitaḥ anantaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ sarvapūjāphalapradaḥ  Hbhv pādme ca tatraivaanantacakro bahubhiś cihnair apy upalakṣitaḥ anantaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ sarvapūjāphalapradaḥ  Hbhv PadmaP dṛśyate śikhare liṅgaṃ śālagrāmasamudbhavam yasya yogeśvaro nāma brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati  Hbhv āraktaḥ padmanābhākhyaṃ paṅkajacchatrasaṃyutam tulasyā pūjayen nityaṃ daridras tv īśvaro bhavet  Hbhv candrākṛtiṃ hiraṇyākhyaṃ raśmijālaṃ vinirdiśet suvarṇarekhābahulaṃ sphaṭikadyutiśobhitam  Hbhv kiṃ caardhacandrākṛtir devo hṛṣīkeśa udāhṛtaḥ tam arcya labhate svargaṃ viṣayāṃś ca samīhitām  Hbhv vāmapārśve same cakre kṛṣṇavarṇaḥ sa bindukaḥ lakṣmīnṛsiṃho vikhyāto bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ  Hbhv trivikramas tathā devaḥ śyāmavarṇo mahādyutiḥ vāmapārśve tathā cakre rekhā caiva tu dakṣiṇe  Hbhv pradakṣiṇāvartakṛtavanamālāvibhūṣitā yā śilā kṛṣṇasaṃjñā sā dhanadhānyasukhapradā  Hbhv gautamīyebahubhir janmabhiḥ puṇyair yadi kṛṣṇaśilāṃ labhet goṣpadena tu cihnena janus tena samāpyate  Hbhv catasro yatra dṛśyante rekhāḥ pārśvasamīpagāḥ dve cakre madhyadeśe tu sā śilā tu caturmukhā  Hbhv kiṃ ca pādme tatraivavajrakīṭodbhavā rekhāḥ paṅktībhūtāś ca yatra vai śālagrāmaśilā yā sā viṣṇupañjarasaṃjñitā  Hbhv nāgavat kuṇḍalībhūtarekhāpaṅktiḥ sa śeṣakaḥ padmākāre ca paṅktī dve madhye lambā ca rekhikā garuḍaḥ sa tu vijñeyaś catuś cakro janārdanaḥ  Hbhv catuś cakraḥ sūkṣmadvāro vanamālāṅkitodaraḥ lakṣmīnārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ  Hbhv etal lakṣaṇayuktās tu śālagrāmaśilāḥ śubhāḥ yāś ca tāsv api sūkṣmāḥ syus tāḥ praśastakarāḥ smṛtāḥ  Hbhv tathā ca śrībhagavadbrahmasaṃvāde tatraivayathā yathā śilā sūkṣmā mahat puṇyaṃ tathā tathā tasmāt tāṃ pūjayen nityaṃ dharmakāmārthasiddhaye  Hbhv tatrāpy āmalakītulyā sūkṣmā cātīva yā bhavet tasyām eva sadā brahman śriyā saha vasāmy aham  Hbhv atha śrīśālagrāmaśilāmāhātmyamśālagrāmaśilāsparśāt koṭijanmāghanāśanam kiṃ punar yajanaṃ tatra harisānnidhyakārakam  Hbhv pādme māghamāhātmye tatraivayaḥ pūjayed dhariṃ cakre śālagrāmaśilodbhave rājasūyasahasreṇa teneṣṭaṃ prativāsaram  Hbhv yad āmananti vedāntā brahma nirguṇam acyutam tatprasādo bhaven nṛṇāṃ śālagrāmaśilārcanāt  Hbhv mahākāṣṭhasthito vahnir mathyamānaḥ prakāśate yathā tathā harir vyāpī śālagrāme prakāśate  Hbhv api pāpasamācārāḥ karmaṇy anadhikāriṇaḥ śālagrāmārcakā vaiśya naiva yānti yamālayam  Hbhv na tathā ramate lakṣmyāṃ na tathā nijamandire śālagrāmśilācakre yathā sa ramate sadā  Hbhv agnihotraṃ hutaṃ tena dattā pṛthvī sasāgarā yenārcito hariś cakre śālagrāmaśilodbhave  Hbhv kāmaiḥ krodhaiḥ pralobhaiś ca vyāpto yo tra narādhamaḥ so pi yāti harer lokaṃ śālagrāmaśilārcanāt  Hbhv yaḥ pūjayati govindaṃ śālagrāme sadā naraḥ āhūtasamplavaṃ yāvat na sa pracyavate divaḥ  Hbhv vinā tīrthair vinā dānair vinā yajñair vinā matim muktiṃ yāti naro vaiśya śālagrāmaśilārcanāt  Hbhv narakaṃ garbhavāsaṃ ca tiryaktvaṃ kṛmiyonitām na yāti vaiśya pāpo pi śālagrāmecyutārcakaḥ  Hbhv dīkṣāvidhānamantrajñaś cakre yo balim āharet sa yāti vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma satyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam  Hbhv naivedyair vividhaiḥ puṣpair dhūpair dīpair vilepanaiḥ gītavāditrastotrādyaiḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv kurute mānavo yas tu kalau bhaktiparāyaṇaḥ kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi ramate sannidhau hareḥ  Hbhv liṅgais tu koṭibhir dṛṣṭair yat phalaṃ pūjitais tu taiḥ śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu ekenāpīha tat phalam  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilārūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ tatra devāsurā yakṣā bhuvanāni caturdaśa  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ pitaras tasya tiṣṭhanti tṛptāḥ kalpaśataṃ divi  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilā yatra tattīrthaṃ yojanatrayam yatra dānaṃ japo homaḥ sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  Hbhv śālagrāmasamīpe tu krośamātraṃ samantataḥ kīkaṭo pi mṛto yāti vaikuṇṭhabhavanaṃ nara  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilācakraṃ yo dadyād dānam uttamam bhūcakraṃ tena dattaṃ syāt saśailavanakānanam  Hbhv skānde kārttikamāhātmye padma  śrīśivaskandasaṃvādeśālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu trailokyaṃ sacarācaram mayā saha mahāsena līnaṃ tiṣṭhati sarvadā  Hbhv dṛṣā praṇamitā yena snāpitā pūjitā tathā yajñakoṭisamaṃ puṇyaṃ gavāṃ koṭiphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv kāmāsakto pi yo nityaṃ bhaktibhāvavivarjitaḥ śālagrāmaśilāṃ vipra sampūjyaivācyuto bhavet  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilābimbaṃ hatyākoṭivināśanam smṛtaṃ saṅkīrtitaṃ dhyātaṃ pūjitaṃ ca namaskṛtam  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilāṃ dṛṣṭvā yānti pāpāny anekaśaḥ siṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā yathā yānti vane mṛgagaṇā bhayāt  Hbhv namaskaroti manujaḥ śālagrāmaśilārcane pāpāni vilayaṃ yānti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā  Hbhv kāmāsakto thavā kruddhaḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam bhaktyā vā yadi vābhaktyā kṛtvā muktim avāpnuyāt  Hbhv vaivasvataṃ bhayaṃ nāsti tathā maraṇajanmanoḥ yaḥ kathāṃ kurute viṣṇoḥ śālagrāmaśilāgrataḥ  Hbhv gītair vādyais tathā stotraiḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam kurute mānavo yas tu kalau bhaktiparāyaṇaḥ kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi ramate viṣṇusadmani  Hbhv śālagrāmanamaskārebhāvenāpi naraiḥ kṛte bhayaṃ naiva kariṣyanti madbhaktā ye narā bhuvi  Hbhv madbhaktibaladarpiṣṭhā matprabhuṃ na namanti ye vāsudevaṃ na te jñeyā madbhaktāḥ pāpino hi te  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu sadā putra vasāmy aham dattaṃ devena tuṣṭena svasthānaṃ mama bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv padmakoṭisahasrais tu pūjite mayi yat phalam tat phalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv pūjito haṃ na tair martyair namito haṃ na tair naraiḥ na kṛtaṃ martyaloke yaiḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilāgre tu yaḥ karoti mamārcanam tenārcito haṃ satataṃ yugānām ekaviṃśatim  Hbhv kim arcitair liṅgaśatair viṣṇubhaktivivarjitaiḥ śālagrāmaśilābimbaṃ nārcitaṃ yadi putraka  Hbhv anarhaṃ mama naivedyaṃ patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ jalam śālagrāmaśilālagnaṃ sarvaṃ yāti pavitratām  Hbhv yo hi māheśvaro bhūtvā vaiṣṇavaliṅgam uttamam dveṣṭi vai yāti narakaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa  Hbhv sakṛd apy arcite bimbe śālagrāmaśilodbhave muktiṃ prayānti manujā nūnaṃ sāṅkhyena varjitāḥ  Hbhv malliṅgaiḥ koṭibhir dṛṣṭair yat phalaṃ pūjitais tu taiḥ śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu ekenāpi hi tad bhavet  Hbhv tasmād bhaktyā ca madbhaktaiḥ prītyarthe mama putraka kartavyaṃ satataṃ bhaktyā śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilārūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ tatra devāsurā yakṣā bhuvanāni caturdaśa  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilāgre tu sakṛt piṇḍena tarpitāḥ vasanti pitaras tasya na saṅkhyā tatra vidyate  Hbhv pramāṇam asti sarvasya sukṛtasya hi putraka phalaṃ pramāṇahīnaṃ tu śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv yo dadāti śilāṃ viṣṇoḥ śālagrāmasamudbhavām viprāya viṣṇubhaktāya teneṣṭaṃ bahubhiḥ makhaiḥ  Hbhv atraprabhṛti ślokā ākare na dṛśyantemānuṣye durlabhā loke śālagrāmodbhavā śilā prāpyate na vinā puṇyaiḥ kalikāle viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv sa dhanyaḥ puruṣo loke saphalaṃ tasya jīvitam śālagrāmaśilā śuddhā gṛhe yasya ca pūjitā  Hbhv saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ śālagrāmaśilārcanam yaḥ kuryān mānavo bhaktyā puṣpe puṣpeśvamedhabhāk  Hbhv kāle vā yadi vākāle śālagrāmaśilārcanam bhaktyā vā yadi vābhaktyā yaḥ karoti sa puṇyabhāk  Hbhv dveṣeṇāpi ca lobhena dambhena kapaṭena vā śālagrāmodbhavaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpāt pramucyate  Hbhv aśucir vā durācāraḥ satyaśaucavivarjitaḥ śālagrāmaśilāṃ spṛṣṭvā sadya eva śucir bhavet  Hbhv tilaprasthaśataṃ bhaktyā yo dadāti dine dine tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ mūlaṃ toyaṃ dūrvākṣataṃ suta jāyate meruṇā tulyaṃ śālagrāmaśilārpitam  Hbhv vidhihīno pi yaḥ kuryāt kriyāmantravivarjitaḥ cakrapūjām avāpnoti samyak śāstroditaṃ phalam  Hbhv tatraiva cānyatraskandhe kṛtvā tu yo dhvānaṃ vahate śailanāyakam tenoḍhaṃ tu bhavet sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  Hbhv brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ yat kiñcit kurute naraḥ tat sarvaṃ nirdahaty āśu śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv na pūjanaṃ na mantrāś ca na japo na ca bhāvanā na stutir nopacāraś ca śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilā yatra tat tīrthaṃ yojanatrayam tatra dānaṃ ca homaś ca sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ pitaras tasya tiṣṭhanti tṛptāḥ kalpaśataṃ divi  Hbhv śālagrāmasamīpe tu krośamātraṃ samantataḥ kīkaṭo pi mṛto yāti vaikuṇṭhabhuvanaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv pādme caśālagrāmaśilācakraṃ yo dadyād dānam uttamam bhūcakraṃ tena dattaṃ syāt saśailavanakānanam  Hbhv garuḍapurāṇetiṣṭhanti nityaṃ pitaro manuṣyāstīrthāni gaṅgādikapuṣkarāṇi yajñāś ca medhā hy api puṇyaśailāścakrāṅkitā yasya vasanti gehe  Hbhv pādme kārttikamāhātmye śrīyamadhūmrakeśasaṃvādeśālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu yair naraiḥ pūjito hariḥ bṛhannāradīye  ca yajñadhvajopākhyānānteśālagrāmaśilārūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ na bādhantesurās tatra bhūtavetālakādayaḥ  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilā yatra tattīrthaṃ tat tapovanam yataḥ sannihitas tatra bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilās tāś ca yadi dvādaśa pūjitāḥ śataṃ vā pūjitaṃ bhaktyā tadā syād adhikaṃ phalam  Hbhv atha bāhulye tāsāṃ phalaviśeṣaḥpādme māghamāhātmye  devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvādeśilā dvādaśa bho vaiśya śālagrāmaśilodbhavāḥ vidhivat pūjitā yena tasya puṇyaṃ vadāmi te  Hbhv koṭidvādaśaliṅgais tu pūjitaiḥ svarṇapaṅkajaiḥ yat syād dvādaśakāleṣu dinenaikena tad bhavet  Hbhv yaḥ punaḥ pūjayed bhaktyā śālagrāmaśilāśatam uṣitvā sa harer loke cakravartīha jāyate  Hbhv skānde kārttikamāhātmye padma  śrīśivaskandasaṃvādedvādaśaiva śilā yo vai śālagrāmasamudbhavāḥ arcayed vaiṣṇavo nityaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ nibodha me  Hbhv koṭiliṅgasahasrais tu pūjitair jāhnavītaṭe kāśīvāse yugāny aṣṭau dinenaikena tad bhavet  Hbhv kiṃ punar bahunā yas tu pujayed vaiṣṇavo naraḥ na hi brahmādayo devāḥ saṃkhyāṃ kurvanti puṇyataḥ  Hbhv atha tatkrayavikrayaniṣedhaḥtatraiva padma śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ yo mūlyam udghātayen naraḥ vikretā cānumantā ca yaḥ parīkṣām udīrayet  Hbhv sarve te narakaṃ yānti yāvad āhūtasamplavam ataḥ saṃvarjayed vipra cakrasya krayavikrayam  Hbhv atha pratiṣṭhā niṣedhaḥtatraivaśālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu pratiṣṭhā naiva vidyate mahāpūjāṃ tu kṛtvādau pūjyo haṃ śucer apy aśucer api strīśūdrakarasaṃsparśo vajrād api suduḥsahaḥ  Hbhv praṇavoccāraṇārcaiva śālagrāmaśilārcanāt brāhmaṇīgamanāc caiva śūdraś caṇḍālatām iyāt  Hbhv sanātanaḥ tad eva  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye ca dvārakāgatānāṃ śrībrahmādīnām uktauetad vai cakratīrthaṃ tu yac chilā cakracihnitā muktidā pāpināṃ loke mlecchadeśepi pūjitā  Hbhv atha teṣv eva cakrabhedena vyaktaṃ dvividhaṃ tat prakīrtitam  Hbhv śilāmṛddārulohādyaiḥ kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ hareḥ śrautasmārtāgamaproktavidhinā sthāpanaṃ hi yat  Hbhv tat sthāpanaṃ iti proktaṃ svayaṃ vyaktaṃ hi me śṛṇu yasmin haribhaktisudhodayenaikaṃ svavaṃśaṃ tu naras tārayaty akhilaṃ jagat arcāyām īpsitaṃ nṝṇāṃ phalaṃ yāgādidurlabham pratimām āśrito bhīṣṭapradāṃ kalpalatāṃ yathā  Hbhv athaśrīmūrteḥ prasādanam ātmādiśuddhayaś caśrīmūrtiṃ kṣālanārhāṃ tu śastagandhajalādinā praksālayet tad anyāṃ tu mūlamantreṇa mārjayet  Hbhv śrīmūrtihṛdayaṃ spṛṣṭvā svamantraṃ cāṣṭadhā japet evaṃ prasādanaṃ mūrter ātmanas tatprasādanāt śuddhir ekā dvitīyā tu syād avyagratayāpi ca  Hbhv sthānaśuddhis tathā dravyaśuddhiś ca likhitā purā iti prakārabhedena bhavec chuddhicatuṣṭayam  Hbhv uktaṃ ca śrīnāradenapuṣpeṇāmbu gṛhītvā tu prokṣayete sarvasādhanam malasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryāt pātre devaṃ nidhāya ca  Hbhv anyenāpipuṣpākṣatādidravyānāṃ kuryān mantrādiśodhanam kṣālanenāmbulepāder mūrtiśuddiṃ samācaret avyagratvenātmaśuddhiṃ ksitiśuddhiṃ tataś caret  Hbhv  iti mantraśuddhiṃ parāṃ cittaśuddhiṃ cecchanti kecana evaṃ ṣaṭ śuddhayaḥ puṇyāḥ sampradāyānusārataḥ  Hbhv atha pīṭhapūjātāmrādipīṭhe śrīkhaṇḍādyālipteṣṭadalaṃ likhet sakarṇikaṃ trivṛttāḍhyaṃ padmaṃ ṣoḍaśakeśaram  Hbhv sadalāgraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ caturdvāravibhūṣitam pūjāyantraṃ samuddhṛtya pīṭhārcāṃ tatra sādhayet  Hbhv pīṭhe bhagavato vāme śrīgurūn gurupādukām nāradādīn pūrvasiddhān yajed anyāṃś ca vaiṣṇavān  Hbhv dakṣiṇe cārcayed durgāṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca sarasvatīm tatra prāglikhitanyāsasyānusāreṇa pūjayet  Hbhv madhye ādhāraśaktyādīn dharmādīṃś ca vidikṣv atha adharmādīṃś caturdikṣv anantādīn madhyataḥ punaḥ  Hbhv śaktīr navāṣṭapatreṣu karṇikāyāṃ ca pūjayet tathā tadupariṣṭhāc ca pīṭhamantraṃ yathoditam  Hbhv tatpīṭhe mūlamantreṇa śrīmūrtiṃ sthāpayed atha puṣpāñjaliṃ gṛhitveṣṭadevarūpaṃ vicintayet  Hbhv tataś ca mūlamantreṇa kṣiptvā puṣpāñjalitrayam nijeṣṭadevamūrteś ca param aikyaṃ vibhāvayet  Hbhv athāvāhanādīnitato devārcane prauḍhapādatāyā niṣedhanāt bhūmai nihitapādaḥ san kuryād āvāhanādikam  Hbhv yac cāvāhyam adhiṣṭhānaṃ tatrāvāhanam ācaret śālagrāmasthāpane ca nāvāhanavisarjane  Hbhv tathā coktamudvāsāvāhane na staḥ sthāvare vai yathā tathā śālagrāmārcane naiva hy āvāhanavisarjane  Hbhv śālagrāme tu bhagavān āvirbhūto yathā hariḥ na tathānyatra sūryādau vaikuṇṭhepi ca sarvagaḥ  Hbhv athāvāhanādividhiḥāvāhanādimudrāś ca saṃdarśyāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ tathā saṃsthāpanaṃ sannidhāpanaṃ sannirodhanam  Hbhv sakalīkaraṇaṃ cāvaguṇṭhanaṃ ca yathāvidhi amṛtīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt paramīkaraṇaṃ tathā  Hbhv tathāvāhanādyarthaḥāgameāvāhanaṃ cādareṇa sammukhīkaraṇaṃ prabhoḥ bhaktyā niveśanaṃ tasya saṃsthāpanamudrāhṛtam  Hbhv tavāsmīti tvadīyatvadarśanaṃ sannidhāpanam kriyāsamāptiparyantaṃ sthāpanaṃ sannirodhanam  Hbhv saklaīkaraṇaṃ coktaṃ tatsarvāṅgaprakāśanam ānandaghanatātyantaprakāśo hy avaguṭhanam  Hbhv amṛtīkaraṇaṃ sarvair evāṅgair avaruddhatā paramīkaraṇaṃ nāmābhīṣṭasampādanaṃ param  Hbhv athāvāhanamāhātmyamnārasiṃheāgaccha narasiṃheti āvāhyākṣatapuṣpakaiḥ etāvatāpi rājendra sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv  itinyased yathāsampradāyaṃ deveṅgādīni pūrvavat śaṅkhacakrādikāś cātha mudrā vidvān pradarśayet  Hbhv tathā ca tattvasāgareāvāhanādimudrāś ca darśayitvā tataḥ punaḥ aṅganyāsaṃ ca devasya kṛtvā mudrāḥ pradarśayet  Hbhv atha mudrāḥāgameāvāhanīṃ sthāpanīṃ ca tathānyāṃ sannidhāpanīm saṃnirodhakarīṃ cānyāṃ sakalīkaraṇīṃ parām  Hbhv tathāvaguṇṭhanīṃ paścād amṛtīkaraṇīṃ tathā paramīkaraṇaṃ cānyā prāg aṣṭau darśayed imāḥ  Hbhv śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaṃ muṣalaṃ śārṅgam eva ca khaḍgaṃ pāśāṅkuśī tadvad vainateyaṃ tathaiva ca  Hbhv śrīvatsakaustubhau veṇum abhītivaradau tathā vanamālāṃ tathā mantrī darśayet kṛṣṇapūjane  Hbhv mudrā cāpi prayoktavyā nityaabilvaphalākṛtiḥ ity etāś ca punaḥ saptadaśa mudrāḥ pradarśayet  Hbhv gandadigdhau karau kṛtvā mudrāḥ sarvatra yojayet yo nyathā kurute mūḍho na siddhaḥ phalabhāg bhavet  Hbhv atha mudrāmāhātmyamagastyasaṃhitāyāmetābhiḥ saptadaśabhir mudrābhis tu vicaksaṇaḥ yo vai mām arcayen nityaṃ mohayet sa sureśvaram drāpayed api viprendra tataḥ prārthitam āpnuyat  Hbhv kramadīpikāyāṃ  bilvamudrām adhikṛtya manovāṇīdehair yad iha ca purā vāpi vihitaṃtvamatyā matyā vā tad akhilam asau duṣkṛticayam imāṃ mudrāṃ jānan kṣapayati naras taṃ suragaṇānamanty asyādhīnā bhavati satataṃ sarvajanatā  Hbhv athāsanādyarpaṇamtato nikṣipya devasyopari puṣpāñjalitrayam dattvāsanārthaṃ puspaṃ ca svāgataṃ vidhinācaret  Hbhv āsanādyupacāreṣu mudrāḥ ṣoḍaśa darśayet prasiddhāḥ padmasvastyādyā vidvān ṣoḍaśasu kramāt  Hbhv śrīkṛṣṇāyārpayed arghyaṃ pādyam ācamanīyakam madhuparkaṃ punaś cācamanīyaṃ ca vidhir yathā  Hbhv tathā ca smṛtyarthasāre āvāhanāsanaṃ pādyam arghyam ācamanīyakam snānam ācamanaṃ vastrācamanaṃ copavītakam  Hbhv ācamanaṃ gandhapuṣpaṃ dhūpadīpaṃ prakalpayet naivedyaṃ punar ācāmaṃ natvā stutvā visarjayet  Hbhv anyatra ca ādau puṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā pādārcanam ataḥ param pādyam arghaṃ tv ācamanaṃ madhuparkaṃ yathoditam  Hbhv abhyaṅgodvartane kṛtvā mahāsnānaṃ samācaret abhiṣekāṅgavastraṃ ca dattvā nīrājayed dharim  Hbhv  itiśrīmūrtau tu śirasy arghyaṃ dadyāt pādyaṃ ca pādayoḥ mukhe cācamanīyaṃ trir madhuparkaṃ ca tatra hi  Hbhv sarveṣv apy upacāreṣu pādyādiṣu pṛthak pṛthak ādau puṣpāñjaliṃ kecid icchanti bhagavatparāḥ  Hbhv athāsanādyarpaṇamāhātmyamnarasiṃhapurāṇe Hbhv tatas tv arhaṇadānena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate tathaivācamaīyasya dātā brāhamaṇasattamāḥ  Hbhv tīrthatoyaṃ tathā dattvā devasyācamanaṃ punaḥ svargalokam avāpnoti sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ naras tv ācamanīyasya dātā bhavati nirmalaḥ  Hbhv madhuparkasya dānena paraṃ padam ihāśnute  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe  ca madhuparkavidhiṃ kṛtvā madhuparkaṃ prayacchati brahman sa yāti paramaṃ sthānam etan na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv atha snānamvijñāpya devaṃ snānārthaṃ pāduke purato rpayet mahāvidyādinā taṃ ca snānasthānaṃ tato nayet  Hbhv prāgvat tatrāsanaṃ pādyaṃ tatraivācamanīyakam nivedya darśayen mudrām amṛtīkaraṇīṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilārūpaṃ tato devaṃ niveśayet snānapātre nijābhīṣṭāṃ calāṃ śrīmūrtim eva vā  Hbhv atha snānapātramskandapurāṇe kṛtvā tāmramaye pātre yo rcayen madhusūdanam phalam āpnoti pūjāyāḥ pratyahaṃ śatvārṣikam  Hbhv yo rcayen mādhavaṃ bhaktyā aśvatthadalasaṃsthitam pratyahaṃ labhate puṇyaṃ padmayutasamudbhavam  Hbhv rambhādalopari hariṃ kṛtvā yo bhyarcayen naraḥ varṣāyutaṃ bhavet pītaḥ keśavaḥ priyayā saha  Hbhv ye paśyanti sakṛd bhaktyā padmapatropari sthitam bhaktyā padmālayākāntaṃ tair āptaṃ durlabhaphalam  Hbhv  ititataḥ śaṅkhenābhiṣekaṃ kuryād ghaṇṭādiniḥsvanaiḥ mūlenāṣṭākṣareṇāpi dhūpayann antarāntarā  Hbhv tatra tu prathamaṃ bhaktyā vidadhīta sugandhibhiḥ divyais tailādibhir dravyair abhyaṅgaṃ śrīhareḥ śanaiḥ  Hbhv athābhyaṅgadravyāṇi tanmāhātmyaṃ caskande puṣpatailena divyauṣadhiyutena hi  Hbhv abhyaṅgaṃ kurute viṣṇor madhye kṣiptvā tu kuṅkumam romāñcitatanur bhūtvā priyayā saha mādhavaḥ prītyā bibharti svotsaṅge manvantaraśataṃ hariḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare ca gandhatailāni divyāni sugandhīni śucīni ca keśavāya naro dattvā gandharvaiḥ saha modate  Hbhv atha pañcāmṛtasnapanamtataḥ śaṅkhabhṛtenaiva kṣīreṇa snāpayet kramāt dadhnā ghṛtena ghṛtābhyaṅgas tato bhavet palāni tasya deyāni śraddhayā pañcaviṃśatiḥ  Hbhv aṣṭottarapalaśataṃ deyaṃ ca sarvadā dve sahasre palānāṃ tu mahāsnāne ca saṅkhyayā  Hbhv dātavye yena sarvāsu dikṣu niryāti ity abhidhīyate  Hbhv  itikiṃ ca snānārthaṃ surabhīkṣīraṃ mahiṣyādyās tu kutsitāḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare ca śarīraduḥkhaśamanaṃ manoduḥkhavināśanam kṣīreṇa snapanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kṣīrābhodhipradaṃ tathā  Hbhv agnipurāṇe gavāṃ śatasya viprebhyaḥ samyagdattasya yat phalam ghṛtaprasthena tad viṣṇor labhet snānān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv indradyumnena samprāptā saptadvīpā vasundharā ghṛtodakena saṃyuktā pratimā snāpitā kila  Hbhv pratimāsaṃ sitāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtena jagatāṃ patim snāpayitvā samabhyarcya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv jñānato jñānato vāpi yat pāpaṃ kurute naraḥ tat kṣālayati sandhyāyāṃ ghṛtasnapanatoṣitaḥ  Hbhv yeṣu kṣīravahā nadyo pāyasakardamāḥ tān lokān puruṣā yānti kṣīrasnapanakā hareḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharme śrīpulastyaprahlādasaṃvāde ca dvādaśyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ ca gavyena havisā hareḥ snāpanaṃ daityaśārdūla mahāpātakanāśanam  Hbhv dadhyādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīrataḥ sambhavo yathā tathaivāśeṣakāmānāṃ kṣīrasnānaṃ tato hareḥ  Hbhv nārasiṃhe payasā yas tu deveśaṃ snāpayed garuḍadhvajam sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv snāpya dadhnā sakṛd viṣṇuṃ nirmalaṃ priyadarśanam viṣṇulokam avāpnoti sevyamānaḥ surottamaḥ  Hbhv duḥsvapnaśamanaṃ jñeyam amaṅgalyavināśanam māṅgalyavṛddhidaṃ dadhnā snapanaṃ narapuṅgava  Hbhv yaḥ karoti harer arcāṃ madhunā snāpitāṃ naraḥ agniloke sa moditvā punar viṣṇupure vaset  Hbhv madhunā snapanaṃ kṛtvā saubhāgyam adhigacchati lokamitrāṇy avāpnoti tathaivekṣurasena ca  Hbhv śrīdvārakāmāhātmye ca śrīmārkaṇḍeyendradyumnasaṃvāde kṣīrasnānaṃ prakurvanti ye narā viṣṇumūrdhani tenāśvamedhajaṃ puṇyaṃ bindunā bindunā smṛtam  Hbhv kṣīrād daśaguṇaṃ dadhnā ghṛtaṃ tasmād daśottaram ghṛtād daśaguṇaṃ kṣaudraṃ khaṇḍaṃ tasmād daśottaram  Hbhv puṣpodakaṃ ca gandhodaṃ vardhate ca daśottaram mantrodakaṃ ca darbhodaṃ tathaiva nṛpasattama  Hbhv drākṣārasaṃ cūtarasaṃ śatavājimakhaiḥ samam tathaiva tīrthanīraṃ ca phalaṃ yacchati bhūmipa  Hbhv snāpanaṃ kṛṣṇadevasya yaḥ karoti svaśaktitaḥ phalam āpnoti tat proktaṃ niṣkāmo muktim āpnuyāt  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottaretīrthodakāni puṇyāni svayam ānīya mānavaḥ tailasya snapanaṃ dattvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv atha snapane dhūpane dhūpanamāhātmyamskānde snānakāle tu kṛṣṇasya aguruṃ dahate tu bhavanti vaśagās tasya nāryaḥ sarvatra sarvadā  Hbhv puṣpadānāt tathā loke bhavatīha phalānvitaḥ dattvā mṛgamadasnānaṃ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv sarvauṣadhipradānena vājimedhaphalaṃ labhet dattvā
