navāni ca dattvā vāsāṃsi śubhrāṇi rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye canānādeśasamudbhūtaiḥ suvastraiś ca sukomalaiḥ dhūpayitvā subhaktyā ca pradhāpayati mādhavam manvantarāṇi vasate tantusaṃkhyaṃ harer gṛhe  Hbhv atha vastrārpaṇe niṣiddhamviṣṇudharmottarenīlīraktaṃ tathā jīrṇaṃ vastram anyadhṛtaṃ tathā devadevāya yo dadyāt sa tu pāpair hi yujyate  Hbhv atrāpavādaḥtatraivaāvike paṭṭavastre ca nīlīrāgo na duṣyati  Hbhv atha yajñopavītamvastrasyārpaṇamudrāṃ ca pradarśya paridhāpya tat upavītaṃ samārpyātha tanmudrāṃ ca pradarśayet  Hbhv athopavītārpaṇamāhātmyamtrivṛt śuklaṃ ca pītaṃ ca paṭṭasūtrādinirmitam yajñopavītaṃ govinde dattvā vedāntago bhavet  Hbhv nandipurāṇeyajñopavītadānena surebhyo brāhmaṇāya vā bhaved vidvāṃś caturvedī śuddhadhīr nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv atha pādyatilakācamanāniatha pādyaṃ nivedyādāv ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ manoharam nirmāya bhāle kṛṣṇasya dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv atha bhūṣaṇamtato devāya divyāni bhūṣaṇāni nivedya ca paridhāpya yathāyuktaṃ tanmudrāṃ ca pradarśayet  Hbhv atha bhūṣaṇārpaṇamāhātmyamskānde śivomāsaṃvādemaṇimauktikasaṃyuktaṃ dattvābharaṇam uttamam svaśaktyā bhūṣaṇaṃ dattvā agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv kiṃ caguñjāmātraṃ suvarṇasya yo dadyād viṣṇumūrdhani indrasya bhavane tiṣṭhed yāvad āhūtasamplavam  Hbhv tasmād ābharaṇaṃ devi dātavyaṃ viṣṇave sadā nārāyaṇo bhavet prīto bhaktyā paramayā mubhe  Hbhv nandipurāṇealaṅkāraṃ tu yo dadyād viprāyātha surāya vā sa gacched vāruṇaṃ lokaṃ nānābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ jātaḥ pṛthivyāṃ kāena bhaved dvīpapatir nṛpaḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarekarṇābharaṇadānena bhavec chrutidharo naraḥ aśvamedham avāpnoti saubhāgyaṃ cāpi vindati  Hbhv karṇapūrapradānena śrutiṃ sarvatra vindati  Hbhv mūrdhābharaṇadānena bhūr dhanyo bhūtale bhavet catuḥsamudravalayāṃ praśāsti ca vasundharām  Hbhv tatraiva tṛtīyakhaṇḍevibhūṣaṇapradānena mūrdhanyo bhūtale bhavet ramyāṇi ratnacitrāṇi saurvarṇāni dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv dattvābharaṇajātāni rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet pādāṅgulīyadānena guhyakādhipatir bhavet  Hbhv pādābharaṇadānena sthānaṃ sarvatra vindati  Hbhv śroṇīsūtrapradānena mahīṃ sāgaramekhalām praśāsti nihatāmitro nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv saubhāgyaṃ mahad āpnoti kiṅkiṇīṃ pradadad dhareḥ hastāṅgulīyadānena paraṃ saubhāgyam āpnuyāt  Hbhv tathaivāṅgadadānena rājā bhavati bhūtale keyūradānād bhavati śaturpakṣakṣayaṅkaraḥ  Hbhv graiveyakāṇi dattvā ca sarvaśāstrārthavid bhavet nāryaś ca vaśagās tasya bhavati dvijapuṅgavāḥ  Hbhv dattvā pratisarān mukhyān na bhūtair abhibhūyate  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraivakṛtrimaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ tathaivābharaṇaṃ divjāḥ pratirūpakṛtaṃ dattvā kṣipraṃ puṣṭyā prayujyate  Hbhv pādmeśaṅkhacakragadādīni pādādyavayaveṣu ca sauvarṇābharaṇaṃ kṛtvā viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv nārasiṃhesuvarṇābharaṇair divyair hārakeyūrakuṇḍalaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ kaṭakādyaiś ca yo viṣṇuṃ pūjayen naraḥ  Hbhv sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ indraloke vased dhīmān yāvad indraś caturdaśa  Hbhv garuḍapurāṇeyasyārcā tiṣṭhate viṣṇor hemabhūṣaṇabhūṣitā ratnair muktāviśeṣeṇa ahany ahani vāsava  Hbhv kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi tasya vai bhuvane hareḥ vāso bhavati devendra kathitaṃ brahmaṇā mama  Hbhv yaḥ paśyati naraḥ kṛṣṇaṃ hemabhūṣaṇabhūṣitam sakṛd bhaktyā kalau śakra punāty āsaptamaṃ kulam  Hbhv  itibahulaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ bhogāt paścād evānulepanam puṣpaṃ cecchanti santo nulepanārcānubhūṣaṇam  Hbhv samprārthyātha prabhuṃ prāgvat nivedya śucipāduke vādyagītātapatrānyaiḥ pūjāsthānaṃ punar nayet  Hbhv prāgvad dattvāsanādīni gandhaṃ tanmudrayārpayet śaṅkhe nidhāya tulasīdalenaivātha candanam  Hbhv atha gandhaḥāgamecandanāgurukarpūrapaṅkaṃ gandham ihocyate  Hbhv gāruḍekastūrikāyā dvau bhāgau catvāraś candanasya tu kuṅkumasya trayaś caikaḥ śaśinaḥ syāc catuḥsamam  Hbhv karpūraṃ candanaṃ darpaḥ kuṅkumaṃ ca catuḥsama sarvaṃ gandham iti proktaṃ samastasuravallabham  Hbhv vārāhekarpūraṃ kuṅkumaś caiva varaṃ tagaram eva ca rasyaṃ ca candanaṃ caiva aguruṃ guggulaṃ tathā etair vilepanaṃ dadyāt śubhaṃ cāru vicakṣaṇaḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarāgnipurāṇayoḥsugandhaiś ca murāmāṃsīkarpūrāgurucandanaiḥ tathānyaiś ca śubhair dravyair arcayej jagatīpatim  Hbhv vaśiṣṭhasaṃhitāyāmkarpūrāgurumiśreṇa candanenānulepayet mṛgadarpaṃ viśeṣeṇa abhīṣṭaṃ cakrapāṇinaḥ  Hbhv skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvādegandhebhyaś candanaṃ puṇyaṃ candanād agurur varaḥ kṛṣṇāgurus tataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kuṅkumaṃ tu tato dhikam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarena dātavyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha ato nyad anulepanam anulepanamukhyaṃ tu candanaṃ parikīrtitam  Hbhv nāradīyeyathā viṣṇoḥ sadābhīṣṭaṃ naivedyaṃ śālisambhavam śukenoktaṃ purāṇe ca tathā tulasicandanam  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ casaṃghṛṣya tulasīkāṣṭhaṃ yo dadyād rāmamūrdhani karpūrāgurukastūrīkuṅkumaṃ na ca tatsamam  Hbhv athānulepanamāhātmyamskānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde śaṅkhamāhātmyevilepayanti deveśaṃ śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu candanam paramātmā parāṃ prītiṃ karoti śatvārṣikīm  Hbhv gāruḍetulasīdalalagnena candanena janārdanam vilepayanti yo nityaṃ labhate vāñchitaṃ phalam  Hbhv nārasiṃhekuṅkumāguruśrīkhaṇḍakardamair acyutākṛtim vilipya bhaktyā rājendra kalpakoṭiṃ vased divi  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarāgnipurāṇayoḥcandanāgurukarpūrakuṅkumośīrapadmakaiḥ anulipto harir bhaktyā varān bhogān prayacchati  Hbhv kāleyakaṃ turuṣkaṃ ca raktacandanam uttamam  Hbhv nṛṇāṃ bhavanti dattāni puṇyāni puruṣottama  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarecandanenānulepyainaṃ candraloka avāpnuyāt śārīrair mānasair duḥkhais tathaiva ca vimucyate  Hbhv kuṅkumenānulepyainaṃ sūryaloke mahīyate saubhāgyam uttamaṃ loke tathā prāpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv karpūreṇānulpiyainaṃ vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnuyāt śārīrair mānasair duḥkhais tathaiva ca vimucyate  Hbhv dattvā mṛgamadaṃ mukhyaṃ yaśasā ca virājate dattvā jātaphalakṣodaṃ kriyāsāphalyam aśnute  Hbhv ramyeṇāgurusāreṇa anulipya janārdanam saubhāgyam atulaṃ loke balaṃ prāpnoti cottamam  Hbhv tathā bakulaniryāsair agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet bakulāgurumiśreṇa candanena sugandhinā samālipya jagannāthaṃ puṇḍarīkaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv ekīkṛtya tu sarvāṇi samālipya janārdanam aśvamedhasya mukhyasya phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam  Hbhv yo nulimpeta deveśaṃ kīrtitair anulepanaiḥ pārthivādyāni yāvanti paramāṇūni tatra vai  Hbhv tāvad abdāni lokeṣu kāmacārī bhavaty asau keśasaugandhyajananaṃ kṛtvā mṛgamadaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv sarvakāmasamṛddhasya yajñasya phalam aśnute  Hbhv yaḥ prayacchati gandhāni gandhayuktīkṛtāni ca gandharvatvaṃ dhruvaṃ tasya saubhāgyaṃ tathottamam  Hbhv atha śrītulasīkāṣṭhacandanamāhātmyamgāruḍe śrīnāradadhundhumāranṛpasaṃvādeyo dadāti harer nityaṃ tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam yugāni vasate svarge hy anantāni narottama  Hbhv mahāviṣṇau kalau bhaktyā dattvā tulasīcandanam yo rcayen mālatīpuṣpair na bhūyastanapo bhavet  Hbhv tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtaṃ candanam yacchato hareḥ nirdahet pātakaṃ sarvaṃ pūrvajanmaśataiḥ kṛtam  Hbhv sarveṣām api devānāṃ tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam pitṝṇāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa sadābhīṣṭaṃ harer yathā  Hbhv mṛtyukāle tu samprāpte tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam bhavate yasya dehe tu harir bhūtvā hariṃ vrajet  Hbhv tāvan malayajaṃ viṣṇor bhāti kṛṣṇāgurur nṛpa yāvan na dṛśyate puṇyaṃ tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam  Hbhv tāvat kastūrikāmodaḥ karpūrasya sugandhinā yāvan na dīyate viṣṇos tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam  Hbhv kalau yacchanti ye viṣṇau tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam dhundhumāra na vai martyāḥ punar āyānti te bhuvi  Hbhv yo hi bhāgavato bhūtvā kalau tulasīcandanam nārpayati sadā viṣṇor na sa bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv prahlādasaṃhitāyāṃna tena sadṛśo loke vaiṣṇavo vidyate bhuvi yaḥ prayacchati kṛṣṇāya tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam  Hbhv tulasīdārujātena candanena kalau naraḥ vilipya bhaktito viṣṇuṃ ramate sannidhau hareḥ  Hbhv tulasīkāṣṭhajātena candanena vilepanam yaḥ kuryād viṣṇutoṣāya kapilāgophalaṃ labhet  Hbhv tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtaṃ candanaṃ yas tu sevate mṛtyukāle viśeṣeṇa kṛtapāpo pi mucyate  Hbhv yo dadāti pitṝṇāṃ tu tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam teṣāṃ sa kurute tṛptiṃ śrāddhe vai śatavārṣikīm  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare catulasīcandanāktāṅgaḥ kurute kṛṣṇapūjanam pūjanena dinaikena labhate śatavārṣikīm  Hbhv vilepanārthaṃ kṛṣṇasya tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam mandire vasate yasya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv tilaprasthāṣṭakaṃ dattvā yat puṇyaṃ cottarāyaṇe tat tulyaṃ jāyate puṇyaṃ prasādāc cakrapāṇinaḥ  Hbhv  itideyaṃ malayajābhāve śītalatvāt kadambajam yathā kiñcit sugandhitvāc candanaṃ devadārujam  Hbhv gāruḍeharer malayajaṃ śreṣṭham abhāve devadārujam  Hbhv athānulepe niṣiddhāniviṣṇudharmottaredāridryaṃ padmakaṃ kuryād asvāsthyaṃ raktacandanam uśīraṃ cittavibhraṃśam anye kuryur upadravam  Hbhv  itipadmakādi na dātavyam aihikaṃ hīcchatā sukham mukhyālābhe tu tat sarvaṃ dātavyaṃ bhagavatparaiḥ  Hbhv tato bhagavataḥ kuryād anulepād anantaram vidvān vicitrair vyajanaiś cāmarair api vījanam  Hbhv vījanamāhātmyaṃ caviṣṇudharmottareanulipya jagannāthaṃ tālavṛntena vījayet vāyulokam avāpnoti puruṣas tena karmaṇā  Hbhv cāmarair vījayed yas tu devadevaṃ janārdanam tilaprasthapradānasya phalam āpnoty asaṃśayam  Hbhv vyajanenātha vastreṇa subhaktyā mātariśvana devadevasya rājendra kurute tāpavāraṇam  Hbhv tatkule yamaloke tu śamate nārako daraḥ vāyulokān mahīpāla na cyutir vidyate punaḥ  Hbhv calaccāmaravātena kṛṣṇaṃ santoṣayen naraḥ  Hbhv tasyottamāṅgaṃ deveśa stuvate svamukhena vai uṣṇakāle tv idaṃ jñeyaṃ yat santaḥ pauṣamāghayoḥ śītalatvān malayajam api naivārpayanti hi  Hbhv tathā coktamna śīte śītalaṃ deyam  Hbhv  itiiti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāsesnāpaniko nāma ṣaṣṭho vilāsaḥ   PratararcasamapanaVilasaaṣṭamavilāsaḥprātararcāsamāpanaḥśrīcaitanyaprabhuṃ vande yatpādāśrayavīryataḥ saṃgṛhṇāty ākaravrātād raṅko ratnāvalīmayam  Hbhv atha dhūpanaṃtataś ca dhūpam utsṛjya nīcais tanmudrayārpayet kṛṣṇaṃ saṅkīrtayan ghaṇṭam vāmahastena vādayan  Hbhv tathā ca bahvṛcapariśiṣṭe dhūpasya vijane caiva dhūpenāṅgavidhūpane nīrājaneṣu sarveṣu viṣṇor nāmāni kīrtayet  Hbhv jayaghoṣaṃ prakurvīta kāruṇyaṃ cābhikīrtayet tathā maṅgalaghoṣaṃ ca jagadbījasya ca stutim  Hbhv anyatra ca tataḥ samarpayed dhūpaṃ ghaṇṭavādyajayasvanaiḥ dhūpasthānaṃ samabhyarcya tarjanyā vāmayā hareḥ  Hbhv tatra mantraḥ vanaspatirasotpanno gandhāḍhyo gandha uttamaḥ aghreyaḥ sarvadevānāṃ dhūpo yaṃ pratigṛhyatam  Hbhv atha dhūpaḥvāmanapurāṇe ruhikākhyaṃ kaṇo dārusihlakaṃ cāguruḥ sitā śaṅkho jātiphalaṃ śrīśe dhūpāni syuḥ priyāṇi vai  Hbhv mūlāgamesaguggulvaguruśīrasitājyamadhucandanaiḥ sārāṅgāravinikṣiptaiḥ kalpayed dhūpam uttamam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare ca tathaiva śubhagandhā ye dhūpas te jagataḥ pateḥ vāsudevasya dharmajñair nivedya dānaveśvara  Hbhv atha dhūpeṣu niṣiddhaṃna dhūparthe jīvajatam  Hbhv tatraivāpavādaḥvinā mṛgamadaṃ dhūpe jīvajātaṃ vivarjayet  Hbhv kālikāpurāṇe na yakṣadhūpaṃ vitaren madhavaya kadacana  Hbhv agnipurāṇe na sallakijaṃ na tṛṇam na śalkarasasambhrtaṃ dhūpam pratyaṅganirmuktam dadyāt kṛṣṇāya buddhimān  Hbhv atha dhūpanamāhātmyamnārasiṃhe śrīmarkandeyasatanikasamvademahiṣākhyaṃ gugguluṃ ca ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram dhūpaṃ dadāti rajendra narasiṃhasya bhaktimān  Hbhv sa dhūpitaḥ sarvadikṣu sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ apsarogaṇayuktena vimānena virājatā vāyulokaṃ samāsādya viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv skānde ye kṛṣṇaguruṇā kṛṣṇaṃ dhūpayanti kalau narāḥ sakarpūreṇa rājendra kṛṣṇatulyā bhavanti te  Hbhv sājyena vai guggulunā sudhūpena janārdanam dhūpayitvā naro yāti padaṃ tasya sadāśivaṃ  Hbhv aguruṃ tu sakarpūradivyacandanasaurabham dattvā nityaṃ harer bhaktyā kulānāṃ tārayec chatam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottaratrtiyakhaṇḍe dhūpanam uttamaṃ tadvat sarvakamaphalapradam dhūpaṃ turuṣkakaṃ dattvā vahnistomaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv dattvā tu kṛtrimaṃ mukhyaṃ sarvakāmān avāpnuyāt gandhayuktakṛtaṃ dattvā yajñagosavaṃ āpnuyāt  Hbhv dattvā karpūraniryāsaṃ vājimedhaphalaṃ labhet vasante guggulaṃ dattvā vahnistomaṃ avāpnuyāt  Hbhv grīṣme candanasāreṇa rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet turuṣkasya pradānena pravṛṣy uttamatāṃ labhet  Hbhv karpūradānāc charadi rājasūyaṃ avāpnuyāt  Hbhv hemante mrgadarpeṇa vājimedhaphalaṃ labhet śiśire gurusarena sarvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv padam uttamaṃ āpnoti dhūpadaḥ puṣṭim aśnute dhūpalekha yathāivordhvam nityaṃ eva prasarpati tathāivordhvagato nityaṃ dhūpadānād bhaven naraḥ  Hbhv prahlādasaṃhitāyāṃ cayo dadāti harer dhūpam tulasīkāṣṭhavahninā śatakratusamaṃ puṇyaṃ go yutaṃ labhate phalaṃ  Hbhv iti dhūpayec ca tathā samyak śrīmadbhagavadālayaṃ dhūpaśeṣaṃ tato bhaktyā svayaṃ seveta vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv tathā ca brāhme ambarisaṃ prati gautamapraśne dhūpaśeṣaṃ tu kṛṣṇasya bhaktyā bhajasi bhūpate kṛtvā cārātrikaṃ viṣṇoḥ svamūrdhnā vandase nṛpa  Hbhv atha śrībhagavadalayadhūpanamāhātmyaṃkṛṣṇāgurusamutthena dhūpena śrīdharālayam dhūpayed vaiṣṇavo yas tu sa mukto narakārṇavat  Hbhv dhūpaśeṣasevanamāhātmyampādme śrīgautamāmbarīṣasaṃvāde tīrthakoṭiśatair dhauto yathā bhavati nirmalaḥ karoti nirmalaṃ dehaṃ dhūpaśeṣas tathā hareḥ  Hbhv na bhayaṃ vidyate tasya bhaumaṃ divyaṃ rāsātalam kṛṣṇadhūpāvaśeṣena yasyāṅgaṃ parivāsitam  Hbhv nāpado vipadas tasya bhavanti khalu dehinaḥ harer dattāvaśeṣena dhūpayed yas tanuṃ sadā  Hbhv nāsaukhyaṃ na bhayaṃ duḥkhaṃ nādhijaṃ naiva rogajam yaḥ sevayed dhūpaśeṣaṃ viṣṇor adbhutakarmaṇaḥ  Hbhv krūrasattvabhayaṃ naiva na ca caurabhayaṃ kvacit sevayitvā harer dhūpaṃ nirmālyaṃ padayor jalam  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodaye caāghrāṇaṃ yad dharer dattaṃ dhūpocchiṣṭasya sarvataḥ tadbhavavyāladaṣṭānāṃ bhavet karmaviṣāpahaṃ  Hbhv iti darśanād api dhūpasya dhūpadānādijaṃ phalam sarvaṃ anyepi vindanti tac cāgre vyatiṃ eṣyati  Hbhv atha dīpanaṃtathaiṭa dīpam utsṛjya prāgvad ghaṇṭaṃ ca vādayan padābjād adṛgabjāntaṃ mudrayoccaiḥ pradīpayet  Hbhv tatra mantraḥgautamīyesuprakāśo mahātejah sarvatas timirāpahaḥ sabāhyābhyantarajyotir dīpo yaṃ pratigṛhyatām  Hbhv atha dīpaḥdīpaṃ prajvalayet śaktau karpūrena ghṛtena vā gavyena tatrāsāmārthye tailenāpi sugandhinā  Hbhv tathā ca nāradīyakalpesaghṛtaṃ guggulaṃ dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ goghṛtadīpitam samastaparivārāya haraye śraddhayārpayet  Hbhv bhaviṣyottareghṛtena dīpo dātavyo rājan tailena vā punaḥ  Hbhv mahābhārate cahaviṣā prathamaḥ kalpo dvitīyaś cauṣadhorasaiḥ  Hbhv atha dīpe niṣiddhaṃbhaviṣyottarevasāmajjādibhir dīpo na tu deyaḥ kadācana  Hbhv mahābhāratevasāmajjāsthiniryāsair na kāryaḥ puṣṭiṃ icchata  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare tṛtīyakhaṇḍenīlaraktadaśaṃ dīpaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet  Hbhv kālikāpurāṇedīpavṛkṣaś ca kartavyas taijāsādyaiś ca bhairava vṛkṣeṣu dīpo dātavyo na tu bhūmau kadācana  Hbhv atha dīpamāhātmyaṃskānde brahmanāradasaṃvādeprajvālya devadevasya karpūrena ca dīpakam aśvamedhaṃ avāpnoti kulaṃ caiva samuddharet  Hbhv atraivānyatra cayo dadāti mahīpāla kṛṣṇasyāgre tu dīpakam pātakaṃ tu samutsṛjya jyotīrūpaṃ labhet phalam  Hbhv vārāhedīpaṃ dadāti yo devi madbhaktyā tu vyavasthitaḥ nātrāndhatvaṃ bhavet tasya saptajanmani sundari  Hbhv yas tu dadyāt pradīpaṃ me sarvataḥ sraddhayānvitaḥ svayamprabheṣu deśeṣu tasyotpattir vidhīyate  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodayedattaṃ svajyotiṣe jyotir yad vistārayati prabhām tadvad dharyati sajjyotir dātuḥ pāpatamo pahaṃ  Hbhv nārasiṃheghṛtena vātha tailena dīpaṃ prajvalayen naraḥ viṣṇave vidhivad bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv vihāya pāpaṃ sakalaṃ sahasrādityasaprabhaḥ jyotiṣmatā vimānena viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv prahlādasaṃhitāyāṃca tulasīpavakenaiva dīpaṃ yaḥ kurute hareḥ dīpalakṣasahasrāṇāṃ puṇyaṃ bhavati daityaja  Hbhv iti paścād dīpaṃ ca taṃ bhaktyā mūrdhnā vandeta vaiṣṇavaḥ dhūpasyevekṣaṇāt tasya labhantenyepi tat phalam  Hbhv kecic cānena dīpena śrīmūrter mūrdhni vaiṣṇavaḥ nīrājanaṃ ihecchanti mahānīrājane yathā  Hbhv tathā ca rāmārcanacandrikāyāṃ dhūpānantaraṃ dīpaprasaṅgeārātrikaṃ tu viṣamabahuvartisamanvitam abhyarcya rāmacandrāya vāmamadhyam athārpayet  Hbhv namo dīpeśvarāyeti dadyāt puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ avadhūpyābhyarcya vādyair mūrdhni nīrājayet prabhum  Hbhv iti ata eveṣyate tasya karābhyāṃ vandanaṃ ca taiḥ nāma cārātrikety ādi vartyo pi bahulāḥ samāḥ  Hbhv prasaṅgāl likhyatetraiva śrīmadbhagavadālaye dīpadānasya māhātmyaṃ kārttikīyaṃ ca tad vinā  Hbhv atha śrībhagavadālaye dīpapradānamāhātmyamviṣṇudharmottare prathamakāṇḍe ff mixed updīpadānāt paraṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati keśavāyatane kṛtvā dīpavṛkṣāmanoharam atīva bhrājate lakṣmyā divam āsādya sarvataḥ  Hbhv dīpamālāṃ prayacchanti ye narāḥ śārṅgiṇo gṛhe bhavanti te candrasamāḥ svargam āsādya mānavāḥ  Hbhv dīpāgāraṃ naraḥ kṛtvā kūtāgāranibhaṃ śubham keśavālayam āsādya loke bhāti sa śakravat  Hbhv yathojjvalo bhaved dīpaḥ sampradātāpi yādava tathā nityojjvalo loke nākapṛṣṭhe virājate  Hbhv sadīpe ca yathā dese cakṣūṃsi phalavanti ca tathā dīpasya dataro bhavanti saphalekṣanaḥ  Hbhv ekādaśyāṃ ca dvādaśyāṃ pratipakṣaṃ tu yo naraḥ dīpaṃ dadāti kṛṣṇāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyam manojñam atisundaram dīpamālākulaṃ divyaṃ vimānam adhirohati  Hbhv padmasutrodbhavaṃ vartti gandhatailena dīpakān virogaḥ subhagaś caiva dattvā bhavati mānavaḥ  Hbhv dīpadanaṃ mahāpuṇyam anyadeveṣv api dhruvam kiṃ punar vāsudevasyānantasya tu mahātmanaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva tṛtīyakhaṇḍedīpaṃ cakṣuḥpradaṃ dadyāt tathaivordhvagatipradam ūrdhvaṃ yathā dīpaśikhā dātā cordhvagatis tathā  Hbhv yāvad akṣinimeṣāṇi dīpo devālaye jvalet tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi nākapṛṣṭhe mahīyate  Hbhv brhannāradīye vitihotraṃ prati yajñadhvajasya pūrvajanmavṛttakathanepradīpaḥ sthāpitas tatra suratārthaṃ dvijottama tenāpi mama duṣkarma nihśeṣaṃ kṣayam agatam  Hbhv viṣṇudharme cavilīyate svahaste tu svatantre sati dīpakaḥ mahāphalo viṣṇugṛhe na datto narakāya saḥ  Hbhv nāradīye mohinīṃ prati śrīrukmāṅgadoktautiṣṭhantu bahuvittāni dānārthaṃ varavarṇini hṛdayāyāsakartṛṇi dīpadānād divaṃ vrajet  Hbhv tasyāpy abhāve subhage paradīpaprabodhanam kartavyaṃ bhaktibhāvena sarvadānādhikaś ca yat  Hbhv iti sada kalaviśeṣepi bhaktyā bhagavadālaye mahādīpapradānasya mahimāpy atra likhyāte  Hbhv atha mahādīpamāhātmyamviṣṇudharmottare prathamakhaṇḍemahāvarttiḥ sadā deyā bhūmipāla mahāphalā kṛṣṇapakṣe viśeṣeṇa tatrāpi sa viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv amāvasyā ca nirdiṣṭā dvādaśī ca mahāphalā aśvayujyām atītāyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣaś ca yo bhavet  Hbhv amāvasyā tadā puṇyā dvādaśī ca viśeṣataḥ devasya dakṣiṇe pārśve deyā tailatulā nṛpa  Hbhv palāṣṭakayutāṃ rājan vartti tatra ca dāpayet vāsasā tu samagreṇa sopavāso jitendriyaḥ  Hbhv mahāvarttidvayam idaṃ sakṛd dattvā mahāmate svarlokaṃ suciraṃ bhuktvā jāyate bhūtale yadā  Hbhv tadā bhavati lakṣmīvān jayadraviṇasamyutaḥ rāṣṭre ca jāyate svasmin deśe ca nagare tathā  Hbhv kule ca rājaśārdūla tatra syād dīpavatprabhaḥ pratyujjvalaś ca bhavati yuddheṣu kalaheṣu ca  Hbhv khyātiṃ yāti tathā loke sadguṇānāṃ ca sadguṇaiḥ ekam apy atha yo dadyād abhīṣṭatamayor dvayoḥ  Hbhv manuṣye sarvam āpnoti yad uktaṃ te mahānagha svarge tathātvam āpnoti bhogakāle tu yādava  Hbhv samānyasya tu dīpasya rājan dānaṃ mahāphalam kiṃ punar mahato dīpasyātreyatta na vidyate  Hbhv atha sonamalinadivastravarttya dīpadananisedhaḥśoṇaṃ vādarakaṃ vastraṃ jīrṇaṃ malinam eva ca upabhuktaṃ na vā dadyāt varttikārthaṃ kadācana  Hbhv iti svayam anyena vā dattaṃ dīpān na śrīharer haret nirvāpayen na hiṃsāc ca śubhaṃ icchan kadācana  Hbhv atha dīpanirvāpanādidoṣaḥviṣṇudharmottare prathamakhaṇḍedattvā dīpo na hartavyas tena karma vijānatā nirvāpanaṃ ca dīpasya hiṃsanaṃ ca vigarhitam  Hbhv yaḥ kuryād dhiṃsanaṃ tena karmaṇā puṣpitekṣaṇaḥ dīpahartā bhaved andhaḥ kaṇo nirvāṇakṛd bhavet  Hbhv viṣṇudharme ca nārakān prati śrīdharmarājoktauyuṣmābhir yauvanonmādam uditair avivekibhiḥ dyutodyotaya govindagehād dīpaḥ purā hṛtaḥ  Hbhv tenādya narake ghore kṣuttṛṣṇāparipīḍitāḥ bhavanti patitās tīvre śītavātavidāritāḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrīpulastyoktau catasmād āyātane viṣṇor dadyād dīpān dvijottama tāmś ca dattvā na hiṃseta na ca tailaviyojitān  Hbhv kurvīta dīpahantā ca mūko ndho jāyate mṛtaḥ andhe tamasi duṣpare narake pacyate kila  Hbhv bhūmau dīpadananisedhaḥkālikāpurāṇedīpavṛkṣaś ca kartavyas taijāsādyaiś ca bhairava vṛkṣeṣu dīpo dātavyo na tu bhūmau kadācana  Hbhv atha naivedyaṃdattvā puṣpāñjaliṃ pīṭhaṃ padyam ācamanaṃ tathā kṛtvā pātreṣu kṛṣṇāyārpayed bhojyaṃ yathāvidhi  Hbhv atha naivedyarpanavidhiḥastraṃ japtvāmbunā prokṣya naivedyaṃ cakramudrayā saṃrakṣya prokṣayed vāyubījajaptajalena ca  Hbhv tena saṃśoṣya taddoṣam agnibījaṃ ca dakṣiṇe dhyātvā karatalenyat tat pṛṣṭhe saṃyojya darśyate  Hbhv tadutthavahninā tasya śuṣkadoṣaṃ hṛdā dahet tataḥ karatale savyemṛtabījaṃ vicintayet  Hbhv tatpṛṣṭhe dakṣiṇaṃ panitalaṃ saṃyojya darśayet tadutthayā nivedyaṃ tat siced amṛtadhārayā  Hbhv jalena mūlajaptena prokṣya tac cāmṛtātmakam sarvaṃ vicintya saṃspṛśya mūlaṃ vārāṣṭakaṃ japet  Hbhv amṛtīkṛtya tad dhenumudrayā salilādibhiḥ tac ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca sampūjya gṛhitvā kusumāñjalim  Hbhv śrīkṛṣṇaṃ prārthya tadvaktrāt tejo dhyātvā vinirgatam saṃyojya ca nivedyaitat patraṃ vāmena saṃspṛśan  Hbhv dakṣeṇa pāṇinādāya gandhapuṣpānvitaṃ jalam svāhāntaṃ mūlam uccārya tajjalaṃ visṛjed bhuvi  Hbhv tat pāṇibhyāṃ samutthāya nivedyaṃ tulasīyutam patrāḍhyaṃ tasya mantreṇa bhaktyā bhāgavaterpayet  Hbhv nivedanamantraś cayaṃnivedayami bhavate jusanedaṃ havir hare  Hbhv iti amṛtopastaranam asi svāhety uccārayan hareḥ dattvātha vidhivad vārigaṇḍūṣaṃ vāmapāṇinā darśayed grāsamudrāṃ tu praphullotpalasannibham  Hbhv prāṇādimudrāhastena dakṣiṇena tu darśayet mantraiś caturthīsvāhāntais tārādyais tattadāhvayaiḥ  Hbhv tataḥ spṛśamś ca karayor aṅguṣṭhābhyām anāmike pradarśayen nivedyasya mudrāṃ tasya manuṃ japan  Hbhv mantraś cāyaṃ kramadīpikāyām  nandajo mbumanubinduyuṅ natiḥpārśvarāmarudavātmane ni ca ruddhaṅeyutanivedyam ātmabhūrmāsapārśvam anilas tathāmiyuk  Hbhv nivedyasya manutvena svābhīṣṭaṃ manum eva te ekāntino japantas tu grāsamudrāṃ vitanvate  Hbhv na ca dhyāyante te kṛṣṇavaktrāt tejovinirgamam mañjulavyavahāreṇa bhojayanti hariṃ mudā  Hbhv anyatra caśālībhaktaṃ subhaktaṃ śiśirakarasitaṃ pāyasaṃ pūpasūpamlehyaṃ peyaṃ sucūṣyaṃ sitam amṛtaphalaṃ ghārikādyaṃ sukhādyam ājyaṃ prājyaṃ samijyaṃ nayanarucikaraṃ vājikailamarīcasvādiyaḥ śākarājiparikaram amṛtāhārajoṣaṃ juṣasva  Hbhv kiṃ cagaruḍapurāṇenaivedyaṃ parayā bhaktyā ghaṇṭādyair jayanisvanaiḥ nīrājanaiś ca haraye dadyād dīpāsanaṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv atha naivedyapatrāṇiskānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvādenaivedyapātraṃ vakṣyāmi keśavasya mahātmanaḥ hairaṇyaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ kaṃsyaṃ mṛnmayam eva ca palāśaṃ padmapatraṃ ca pātraṃ viṣṇor atipriyam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottarepatrāṇāṃ tu pradānena narakaṃ ca na gacchati  Hbhv patraparimanaṃdevīpurāṇeṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaṃ pātram uttamaṃ parikīrtitam madhyamaṃ ca tribhāgonaṃ kanyasaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam vasvaṅgulavihīnaṃ tu na pātraṃ kārayet kvacit  Hbhv atha bhojyaniekādaśaskande guḍapāyasasarpīṃṣi saṣkulyāpūpamodakān saṃyāvadadhisūpāmś ca naivedyaṃ sati kalpayet  Hbhv kiṃ cayad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cātipriyam ātmanaḥ tat tan nivedayen mahyaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate  Hbhv aṣṭamaskānde naivedyaṃ cādhiguṇavad dadyāt puruṣatuṣṭidam  Hbhv baudhāyanasmṛtau canānāvidhānnapānaiś ca bhakṣanādyair manoharaiḥ naivedyaṃ kalpayed viṣṇos tadabhāve ca pāyasaṃkevalaṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ  Hbhv vāmanapurāṇehaviṣā saṃskṛtā ye ca yavagodhūmaśalayaḥ tilamudgādayo māṣā vrīhayaś ca priyā hareḥ  Hbhv gāruḍeannaṃ caturvidhaṃ puṇyam guṇāḍhyaṃ cāmṛtopamam niṣpaṇṇaṃ svagṛhe yad vā śraddhayā kalpayed dhareḥ  Hbhv bhaviṣyepuṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ tathā dīpaṃ naivedyaṃ sumanoharam khaṇḍalaḍḍukaśrīvestakāsārāśokavartikāḥ  Hbhv svastikollasikadugdhatilaveṣṭakilāṭikāḥ phalāni caiva pakvāni nāgaraṅgādikāni ca  Hbhv anyāni vidhinā dattvā bhakṣyāṇi vividhāni ca evam ādini dāpayed bhaktito nrpa  Hbhv vārāheyas tu bhāgavato devi annād yena tu prīṇayet prīṇitas tiṣṭhatesau vā bahujanmāni mādhavi  Hbhv sarvavrīhimayaṃ gṛhyam śubhaṃ sarvarasānvitam mantreṇa me pradīyeta na kiṃcid api saṃspṛśet  Hbhv iṅgudiphalabilvāni badarāmalakāni ca kharjurāmś cāsanāmś caiva mānavāmś ca parūṣakān  Hbhv śāloḍḍambarikāmś caiva tathā plakṣaphalāni ca paippalaṃ kaṇṭakīyaṃ ca tumburuṃ ca priyaṅgukam  Hbhv marīcaṃ śiṃśapākaṃ ca bhallātakaramardakam drākṣāṃ ca dāḍimaṃ caiva piṇḍakharjūram eva ca  Hbhv sauvīraṃ kelikaṃ caiva tathā śubhaphalāni ca piṇḍārakaphalaṃ caiva punnāgaphalam eva ca  Hbhv śamīṃ caiva kavīraṃ ca kharjūrakamahāphalam kumudasya phalaṃ caiva vaheḍakaphalaṃ tathā  Hbhv ajaṃ karkoṭakaṃ caiva tathā talaphalāni ca kadambaḥ kaumudaṃ caiva dvividhaṃ sthalakañjayoḥ  Hbhv piṇḍikaṇḍeti vikhyātaṃ vaṃśanīpaṃ tataḥ param madhukaṇḍeti vikhyātaṃ māhiṣaṃ kaṇḍam eva ca  Hbhv karamardakakandaṃ ca tathā nilotpalasya ca mṛṇālaṃ pauṣkaraṃ caiva śālūkasya phalaṃ tathā  Hbhv ete cānye ca bahavaḥ kāṇḍamūlaphalāni ca etāni copayojyāni ye mayā parikalpitāḥ  Hbhv mūlakasya tataḥ śākam ciñcaśākaṃ tathaiva ca śākaṃ caiva kalāyasya sarṣapasya tathaiva ca  Hbhv vaṃsakasya tu śākaṃ ca śākam eva kalambikam ārdrakasya ca śākaṃ vai pālaṅkaṃ śākam eva ca  Hbhv ambiloḍakaśākaṃ ca kāśaṃ kaumārakaṃ tathā śukamaṇḍalapatraṃ ca dvāv eva taruvānakau  Hbhv carasya caiva śākaṃ ca madhukoḍḍumbaraṃ tathā ete cānye ca bahavah śataśo tha sahasraśaḥ karmaṇyāś caiva sarve vai ye mayā parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv vrīhīṇāṃ ca pravakṣyāmi upayogāmś ca mādhavi ekacittaṃ samādhāya tat sarvaṃ śṛṇu sundari  Hbhv dharmādhārmikaraktaṃ ca sugandhaṃ raktaśālikam dīrghaśūkaṃ mahāśāliṃ varakuṅkumapatrakam  Hbhv grāmaśāliṃ samadrāśām saśrīśāṃ kuśaśālikām yavāś ca dvividhā jñeyāḥ karmaṇyā mama sundari  Hbhv karmaṇyāś caiva mudgāś ca tilāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kulatthakāḥ godhūmakaṃ mahāmudgamudgāṣṭakam avāṭajit  Hbhv karmaṇy etāni coktāni vyajanāni priyānvitān pratigṛhṇāmy ahaṃ hy etān sarvān bhāgavatān priyān  Hbhv kiṃ caye mayaivopayojyāni gavyaṃ dadhi payo ghṛtam  Hbhv skānde ca brahmanāradasaṃvādehaviḥ śalyodanaṃ divyam ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram naivedyaṃ devadevāya yāvakaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā  Hbhv naivedyānām abhāve tu phalāni vinivedayet phalānām apy abhāve tu tṛṇagulmauṣadhīr api  Hbhv auṣadhīnām alābhe tu toyaṃ ca vinivedayet tadalābhe tu sarvatra mānasaṃ pravaraṃ smṛtam  Hbhv skānde mahendraṃ prati śrīnāradavacanaṃyacchanti tulasīśākaṃ śrutaṃ ye mādhavāgrataḥ kalpāntaṃ viṣṇuloke tu vasanti pitṛbhiḥ saha  Hbhv atha naivedyaniṣiddhānihāritasmṛtaunābhakṣyaṃ naivedyārthe bhakṣyesv apy ajāmahiṣīkṣīraṃ pañcanakhā matsyāś ca  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmyenīlīkṣetraṃ vāpayanti mūlakaṃ bhakṣayanti ye naivāsti narakottārah kalpakoṭiśatair api  Hbhv vārāhemāhiṣaṃ cāvikaṃ cājam ayajñīyam udāhṛtam  Hbhv kiṃ camāhiṣaṃ varjayen mahyaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ yadi  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare tṛtīyakhaṇḍeabhakṣyaṃ capy ahṛdyaṃ ca naivedyaṃ na nivedayet keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca tathā cāvihitaṃ ca yat  Hbhv mūṣikālāṅgulopetam avadhūtam avakṣutam uḍḍumbaraṃ kapitthaṃ ca tathā dantaśaṭhaṃ ca yat evam ādīni devāya na deyāni kadācana  Hbhv athābhakṣyāṇikaurmevṛntākaṃ jālikāśākaṃ kusumbhāśmantakaṃ tathā palāṇḍuṃ laśunaṃ śuklam niryāsaṃ caiva varjayet  Hbhv gṛñjanaṃ kiṃśukaṃ caiva kukuṇḍaṃ ca tathaiva ca uḍumbaram alābuṃ ca jagdhvā patati vai dvijaḥ  Hbhv vaiṣṇavebhuñjītoddhṛtasārāṇi na kadācin nareśvara  Hbhv skāndena bhakṣayati vṛntākaṃ tasya dūrataro hariḥ  Hbhv kiṃ cānyatradorbhyāṃ pādbhyāṃ ca jānubhyām urasā śirasā dṛśā manasā vacasā ceti praṇāmo ṣṭāṅga īritaḥ  Hbhv  jānubhyām caiva bāhubhyāṃ śirasā vacasā dhiyā pañcāṅgakaḥ praṇāmaḥ syāt pūjāsu pravarāv imau  Hbhv  ata evoktaṃ yāmaleyatra madyaṃ tathā māṃsam tathā vṛntākamūlake nivedayen naiva tatra harer aikāntikī ratiḥ  Hbhv atha naivedyarpanamāhātmyaṃskāndenaivedyāni manojñāni kṛṣṇasyāgre nivedayet kalpāntaṃ tatpitṝṇaṃ tu tṛptir bhavati śāśvatī  Hbhv phalāni yacchate yo vai suhṛdyāni nareśvara kalpāntaṃ jāyate tasya saphalaṃ ca manorathaḥ  Hbhv nārasiṃhehaviḥ śālyodanaṃ diyyam ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram nivedya narasiṃhāya yāvakaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā  Hbhv samās taṇḍulaśaṅkhyāyā yāvatyas tāvatīr nṛpa viṣṇuloke mahābhogan bhuñjānas te savaiṣṇavāḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottareannadas tṛptim āpnoti svargalokaṃ ca gacchati dattvā ca saṃvibhāgāya tathaivānnam atandritaḥ trailokyatarpite puṇyaṃ tatkṣanāt samavāpnuyāt  Hbhv akṣayyam annapānaṃ ca pitṛbhyaś copatiṣṭhate odanaṃ vyajanopetam dattvā svargam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv paramānnaṃ tathā dattvā tṛptim āpnoti śaśvatim viṣṇulokam avāpnoti kulam uddharate tathā  Hbhv ghṛtaudanapradānena dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt dadhyodanapradānena śriyam āpnoty anuttamām  Hbhv kṣīrodanapradānena dīrghajīvitam āpnuyāt ikṣūṇāṃ ca pradānena paraṃ saubhāgyam aśnute  Hbhv ratnānāṃ caiva bhāgī syāt svargalokaṃ ca gacchati phāṇitasya pradānena agnyādhānaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv tathā guḍapradānena kāmitābhīṣṭam āpnuyāt  Hbhv nivedyekṣurasaṃ bhaktyā paraṃ saubhāgyam āpnuyāt sarvān kāmān avāpnoti kṣaudraṃ yaś ca prayacchati  Hbhv tad eva tuhitopetam rājasūyam avāpnuyāt vahniṣṭomam avāpnoti yavākasya nivedakaḥ atirātram avāpnoti tathā pūpanivedakaḥ  Hbhv vaidalānāṃ ca bhakṣyāṇāṃ dānāt kāmān avāpnuyāt dīrghajīvitam āpnoti ghṛtapūranivedakaḥ  Hbhv modakānāṃ pradānena kāmān āpnoty abhīpsitān  Hbhv nānāvidhānāṃ bhakṣyāṇāṃ dānāt svargam avāpnuyāt bhojanīyapradānena tṛptim āpnoty anuttamām  Hbhv tathā lehyapradānena saubhāgyam adhigacchati balavarṇam avāpnoti cūṣyāṇāṃ ca nivedane  Hbhv kulmāṣollāsikadātā vahnyādheyaṃ phalaṃ labhet tathā kṛṣāradānena vahniṣṭomam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv dhanānāṃ kṣaudrayuktānāṃ lājānāṃ ca nivedakaḥ mukhyaṃ caiva śaktūnāṃ vahniṣṭomam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv vānaprasthāśritaṃ puṇyam labhec chākanivedakaḥ dattvā haritakaṃ caiva tad eva phalam āpnuyāt  Hbhv dattvā śākāni ramyāṇi viśokas tv abhijāyate dattvā ca vyajanārthāya tathopakaraṇāni ca  Hbhv sukule labhate janma kandamūlanivedakaḥ nīlotpalavidarīṇāṃ taruṭasya tathā dvijaḥ  Hbhv kandadānād avāpnoti vānaprasthaphalaṃ śubham trapuṣer vārukaṃ dattvā puṇḍarīkaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv karkandhuvadare dattvā tathā pāraivataṃ kalam parūṣakaṃ tathābhraṃ ca panasaṃ nārikelakam  Hbhv bhavyaṃ mocaṃ tathā cocam kharjūram atha dāḍimam āmrātakasruvāmloṭaphalamānapriyālakam  Hbhv jambūbilvāmalaṃ caiva jātyaṃ vīṇātakaṃ tathā nāraṅgabījapūre ca bījaphalguphalany api  Hbhv evam ādīni divyani yaḥ phalāni prayacchati tathā kandāni mukhyāni devadevāya bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv kriyāsāphalyam āpnoti svargalokaṃ tathaiva ca prāpnoti phalam ārogyam mṛdvīkānāṃ nivedakaḥ  Hbhv rasān mukhyān avāpnoti saubhāgyam api cottamam āmrair abhyarcya deveśam aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv kiṃ camocakaṃ panasaṃ jambū tathānyat kumbhāliphalam prācīnāmalakaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ madhukoḍḍumbarasya ca yatnapakvam api grāhyaṃ kadalīphalam uttamam  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodaye cayat kiñcid alpaṃ naivedyam bhaktabhaktirasaplutam pratibhojayati śrīśas taddātṝn svasukhaṃ drutam iti  Hbhv tataḥ prāgvad vicitrāṇi panakāny uttamāni ca sugandhi śītalaṃ svacchaṃ jalam apy arpayet tataḥ  Hbhv atha panakānitanmāhātmyaṃ caviṣṇudharmottarepānakāni sugandhīni śītalāni viśeṣataḥ nivedya devadevāya vājimedham avāpnuyāt  Hbhv tvagelānāgakusumakarpūrasitasaṃyutaiḥ sitākṣaudraguḍopetair gandhavarṇaguṇānvitaiḥ  Hbhv bījapūrakanāraṅgasahakārasamanvitaiḥ rājasūyam avāpnoti panakair viniveditaiḥ  Hbhv nivedya nārikelāmbuvahniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet sarvakāmavahā nadyo nityaṃ yatra manoramāḥ tatra pānapradā yānti yatra rāmā guṇānvitāḥ  Hbhv iti itthaṃ samarpya naivedyam dattvā javanikaṃ tataḥ bahirbhūya yathāsakti japaṃ sandhyānam ācaret  Hbhv atha dhyānambrahmeśādyaiḥ parita ṛṣibhiḥ sūpaviṣṭaiḥ sametolakṣmyā śiñjadvalayakarayā sādaraṃ vījyamana marmakrīḍaprahasitamukho hāsayan paṅktibhoktṝnbhuṅkte pātre kanakaghaṭite ṣaḍrasaṃ śrīrameśaḥ  Hbhv iti ekantibhiś cātmakṛtaṃ savayasyasya gokule yaśodālālyamānasya dhyeyaṃ kṛṣṇasya bhojanam  Hbhv atha homaḥnityaṃ cāvaśyakaṃ homaṃ kuryāt śaktyanusārataḥ homāśaktau tu kurvīta japaṃ tasya caturguṇam  Hbhv kepy evaṃ manvatevaśyam nityahomaṃ sadācaret puraścaranahomasyāśaktau hi sa vidhir mataḥ  Hbhv pūrvaṃ dīkṣāvidhau homavidhiś ca likhitaḥ kiyān tadvistāraś ca vijñeyas tattacchāstrāt tadicchubhiḥ  Hbhv samāptiṃ bhojane dhyātvā dattvā gaṇḍūṣikaṃ jalam amṛtāpidhānam asi svāhety uccārayet sudhīḥ  Hbhv visṛjed devavaktre tat tejaḥ saṃhāramudrayā naikantī tejasaḥ kuryān niṣkrāntiṃ iva saṅkramam  Hbhv atha balidānamtato javanikā vidvān apasārya yathāvidhi viṣvaksenāya bhagavannaivedyāṃśaṃ nivedayet  Hbhv tathā ca pañcarātre śrīnāradavacanamviśvaksenāya dātavyaṃ naivedyaṃ tacchatāṃśakam pādodakaṃ prasādaṃ ca liṅge caṇḍeśvarāya ca  Hbhv tadvidhiḥmukhyād īsānataḥ pātrān naivedyāṃśaṃ samuddharet sarvadevasvarupāya parāya parameṣṭhine  Hbhv śrīkṛṣṇasevayuktāya viṣvaksenāya te namaḥ ity uktvā śrīharer vāme tīrthaklinnaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv sataṃsaṃ vā sahasrāṃśam anyathā niṣphalaṃ bhavet  Hbhv paścāc ca balir ity ādi ślokāv uccārya vaiṣṇavaḥ sarvebhyo vaiṣṇavebhyas tacchatāṃsaṃ vinivedayet  Hbhv tau ca ślokau balir vibhīṣaṇo bhīṣmaḥ kapilo nārado rjunaḥ prahlādaś cāmbarīṣaś ca vasur vāyusutaḥ sivaḥ  Hbhv viṣvaksenoddhavākrūraḥ sanakādyāḥ śukādayaḥ śrīkṛṣṇasya prasādo yaṃ sarve gṛhṇantu vaiṣṇavāḥ  Hbhv idaṃ yadyapi yujyeta darpaṇārpaṇataḥ param tathāpi bhaktavātsalyāt kṛṣṇasyātrāpi sambhavet  Hbhv atha balidanamāhātmyaṃnārasiṃhetatas tadannaśeṣeṇa pārṣadebhyaḥ samantataḥ puṣpākṣatair vimiśreṇa baliṃ yas tu prayacchati  Hbhv balinā vaiṣṇavenātha tṛptaḥ santo divaukasaḥ śāntiṃ tasya prayacchanti śriyam ārogyam eva ca  Hbhv atha jalagandusadyarpanaṃupalipya tato bhūmiṃ punar gāṇḍūṣikaṃ jalam dadyāt trir agre kṛṣṇasya tato smai dantasodhanam  Hbhv punar ācamanaṃ dattvā śrīpāṇyoḥ śrīmukhasya ca mārjanāyāṃśukaṃ dattvā sarvāṇy aṅgāni mārjayet  Hbhv paridhāpy apare vastre punar dattvāsanāntaram padyam ācamanīyaṃ ca pūrvavat punar arpayet  Hbhv candanāgurucūrṇādi pradadyāt karamārjanam karpūradyāsyavāsaṃ ca tāmbūlaṃ tulasīm api  Hbhv atha mukhavasadimāhātmyaṃviṣṇudharmottare trtīyakhaṇḍepūgajātiphalaṃ dattvā jātipatraṃ tathaiva ca lavaṅgaphalakakkolamelakataphalaṃ tathā  Hbhv tāmbūlīnāṃ kiśalayaṃ svargalokam avāpnuyāt saubhāgyam atulaṃ loke tathā rūpam anuttamam  Hbhv skāndetāmbūlaṃ ca sakarpūram sapūgaṃ naranāyaka kṛṣṇāya yacchati prītyā tasya tuṣṭo hariḥ sadā  Hbhv atha punar gandharpanaṃdivyaṃ gandhaṃ punar dattvā yatheṣṭam anulepanaiḥ divyair vicitraiḥ śrīkṛṣṇam bhakticchedena lepayet  Hbhv ramyāṇi cordhvapuṇḍrāṇi sadvarṇena yathāspadam sugandhinānulepena kṛṣṇasya racayettarām  Hbhv tathā cāgame dhyānaprasaṅgelalāṭe hṛdaye kukṣau kaṇṭhe bahvoś ca pārśvayoḥ virājatordhvapuṇḍreṇa sauvarṇena vibhūṣitam  Hbhv iti divyāni kañcukoṣṇīṣakāñcyādīni parāṇy api vastrāṇi suvicitrāṇi śrīkṛṣṇaṃ paridhāpayet  Hbhv tato divyakirīṭādibhūṣaṇani yathāruci vicitradivyamālyāni paridhāpya vibhūṣayet  Hbhv atha mahārajopacararpanaṃtataś ca cāmaracchatrapādukādīn parān api mahārājopacārāmś ca dattvādarśaṃ pradarśayet  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottareyathādeśaṃ yathākalaṃ rājaliṅgaṃ surālaye dattvā bhavati rājaiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv tatra cāmaramāhātmyaṃtathā cāmaradānena śrīmān bhavati bhūtale mucyate ca tathā pāpaiḥ svargalokaṃ ca gacchati  Hbhv chatrasya māhātmyaṃtatraivachatraṃ bahuśalākaṃ ca jhallarīvastrasaṃyutam divyavastraiś ca saṃyuktaṃ hemadaṇḍasamanvitam  Hbhv yaḥ prayacchati kṛṣṇasya chatralakṣayutair vṛtaḥ prārthyate so maraiḥ sarvaiḥ krīḍate pitṛbhiḥ saha  Hbhv tatraiva vānyatrarājā bhavati lokesmin chatraṃ dattvā dvijottamaḥ nāpnoti ripujaṃ duḥkhaṃ saṅgrāme ripujid bhayet  Hbhv upānatsampradānena vimānam adhirohati yatheṣṭaṃ tena lokeṣu vicaraty amaraprabhaḥ  Hbhv dhvajasya māhātmyaṃtatraivalokeṣu dhvajabhūtaḥ syād dattvā viṣṇor varaṃ dhvajam śakralokam avāpnoti bahūn abdagaṇān naraḥ  Hbhv kiṃ cayuktaṃ pītapatākābhir nivedya garuḍadhvajam keśavāya dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sarvaloke mahīyate iti  Hbhv yatprasāde dhvajāropamāhātmyaṃ likhitaṃ purā tad atrāpy akhilaṃ jñeyaṃ tatrātratyaṃ idaṃ tathā  Hbhv kiṃ ca bhaviṣyeviṣṇor dhvaje tu sauvarṇam daṇḍaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ patākā cāpi pītā syād garuḍasya samīpagā  Hbhv vyajanasya māhātmyaṃviṣṇudharmottaretalavrṇtapradānena nirvṛtiṃ prāpnuyāt param  Hbhv vitanasya māhātmyaṃtatraivavitānakapradānena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate paraṃ nirvṛtim āpnoti yatra tatrābhijāyate  Hbhv khadgadīnāṃ māhātmyaṃdattvā nistriṃśakān mukhyān śatrubhir nābhibhūyate dattvā tadbandhanaṃ mukhyam agnyādheyaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv kiṃ capatadgrahaṃ tathā dattvā śubhadas tv abhijāyate pādapīṭhapradānena sthānaṃ sarvatra vindati  Hbhv darpaṇasya pradānena rūpavān darpavān bhavet mārjayitvā tathā taṃ ca śubhagas tv abhijāyate  Hbhv yat kiñcid devadevāya dadyād bhaktisamanvitaḥ tad evākṣayam āpnoti svargalokaṃ sa gacchati  Hbhv kiṃ ca vāmanapurāṇe śrībaliṃ prati śrīprahlādoktauśraddadhānair bhaktiparair yāny uddiśya janārdanam balidānāni dīyante akṣayāni vidur budhaḥ  Hbhv atrāpi kecid icchanti dattvā puṣpāñjalitrayam pūrvokta daśa śaṅkhādyā mudrāḥ sandarśayet  Hbhv iti atha gītavadyanṛtyanitato vicitrair lalitaiḥ kāritair vā svayaṃ kṛtaiḥ gītair vādyaiś ca nṛtyaiś ca śrīkṛṣṇaṃ paritoṣayet  Hbhv atha tatra niṣiddhaṃnṛtyādi kurvato bhaktān nopaviṣṭo valokayet na ca tiryag vrajet tatra taiḥ sahāntarayan prabhum  Hbhv tathā coktaṃnṛtyantaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ harsād āsīno yas tu paśyati khañjo bhavati rājendra so yaṃ janmani janmani  Hbhv kiṃ canṛtyatāṃ gāyatāṃ madhye bhaktānāṃ keśavasya ca tān ṛte yas tiro yāti tiryagyoniṃ sa gacchati  Hbhv atha gītadimāhātmyamadau samanyataḥnārasiṃhegītavādyādikaṃ nāṭyam śaṅkhaturyādinisvanam yaḥ kārayati viṣṇos tu sandhyāyāṃ mandire naraḥ sarvakāle viśeṣeṇa kāmagaḥ kāmarūpavān  Hbhv susaṅgītavidagdhaiś ca sevyamāno psarogaṇaiḥ mahārheṇa vimānena vicitreṇa virājatā svargāt svargam anuprāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv skānde viṣṇunāradasaṃvādegītaṃ vādyaṃ ca nṛtyaṃ ca nāṭyaṃ viṣṇukathāṃ mune yaḥ karoti sa puṇyātmā trailokyopari saṃsthitaḥ  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye śrīyamabhagīrathasaṃvādedevatāyatane yas tu bhaktiyuktaḥ pranṛtyati gītāni gāyaty athavā tatphalaṃ śṛṇu bhūpate  Hbhv gandharvarājatāṃ gaṇair nṛtyād rudragaṇeśatām prāpnoty aṣṭakulair yuktas tataḥ syān mokṣabhāṅ naraḥ  Hbhv laiṅge śrīmārkaṇḍeyāmbarīṣasaṃvādeviṣṇukṣetre tu yo vidvān kārayed bhaktisaṃyutaḥ gananṛtyādikaṃ caiva viṣṇvākhyaṃ ca kathāṃ tathā  Hbhv jātiṃ smṛtiṃ ca medhāṃ ca tathaiva paramāṃ sthitim prāpnoti viṣṇusālokyaṃ satyam etan nārādhipa  Hbhv anyatra ca śrībhagavaduktauvisṛjya lajjāṃ yo dhīte gāyate nṛtyatepi ca kulakoṭisamāyukto labhate māmakaṃ padam  Hbhv ata evoktaṃbhārate nṛtyagīte tu kuryāt svābhāvikepi vā svābhāvikena bhagavān prīṇātīty āha śaunakaḥ  Hbhv ata eva nāradīyeviṣṇor gītaṃ ca nṛtyaṃ ca naṭānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ brahman brāhmaṇajātīnāṃ kartavyaṃ nityakarmavat  Hbhv kintu smṛtaugītanṛtyāni kurvīta devadvijādituṣṭaye na jīvanāya yuñjīta vipro pāpabhiyā kvacit  Hbhv evaṃ kṛṣṇaprīṇanatvād gītāder nityatā parā saṃsiddhair aviśeṣena jñeyā sā harivasare  Hbhv tathā coktaṃkeśavāgre nṛtyagītaṃ na karoti harer dine vahninā kiṃ na dagdho sau gataḥ kiṃ na rasātalaṃ  Hbhv atha viśeṣato gītasya māhātmyaṃdvārakāmāhātmye śrīmarkandeyendradyumnasaṃvādekṛṣṇaṃ santoṣayed yas tu sugītair madhurasvanaiḥ sarvavedaphalaṃ tasya jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv skānde śrīmahādevoktauśrutikoṭisamaṃ japyaṃ japakoṭisamaṃ haviḥ havihkoṭisamaṃ geyaṃ geyaṃ geyasamaṃ viduḥ  Hbhv kasikhaṇḍe viṣṇudūtaśivaśarmasaṃvādeyadi gītaṃ kvacid gītaṃ śrīmaddhariharāṅkitam mokṣaṃ tu tat phalaṃ prāhuh sānnidhyam athavā tayoḥ  Hbhv viṣṇuśarme śrībhagavaduktaurāgeṇākṛṣyate ceto gāndharvābhimukhaṃ yadi mayi buddhiṃ samāsthāya gāyetha mama satkathāḥ  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodayeyo gāyati sam aniśaṃ bhuvi bhaktā uccaiḥsa drāṇ samastajanapāpabhidelam ekaḥ dīpesv asatsv api nanu pratigeham antardhvāntaṃ kim atra vilasaty amale dyunāthe  Hbhv yad ānandakalaṃ gāyan bhaktaḥ puṇyāśru varṣati tat sarvatīrthasalilasnānaṃ svamalaśodhanaṃ  Hbhv vārāhe brāhmaṇo vāsudevārthaṃ gāyamano niśaṃ param samyak tālaprayogeṇa sannipātena vā punaḥ  Hbhv nava varṣasahasrāṇi nava varṣaśatāni ca kuverabhavanaṃ gatvā modate vai yadṛcchayā  Hbhv kuverabhavanād bhraṣṭaḥ svacchandagamanālayaḥ phalam āpnoti suśroṇi mama karmaparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv nārāyaṇānāṃ vidhinā gānaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam gānenārādhito viṣṇuh svakīrtijanavarcasā dadāti tuṣṭaḥ sthānaṃ svaṃ yathāsmai kauśikayā vai  Hbhv kiṃ caeṣa vo muniśārdūlaḥ prokto gītakramo muneḥ brāhmaṇo vāsudevākhyaṃ gāyamāno niśaṃ param  Hbhv hareḥ sālokyam āpnoti rudragānādhiko bhavet karmaṇā manasā vācā vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ gāyan nṛtyaṃs tam āpnoti tasmād geyaṃ paraṃ viduḥ  Hbhv prathamaskandhe śrīnāradoktau pragāyataḥ svavīryāṇi tīrthapadaḥ priyaśravaḥ ahuta iva me sighram darśanaṃ yāti cetasi  Hbhv dvādaśaskandhe śrīsūtoktaumṛṣā giras tā hy asatīr asatkathāna kathyate yad bhagavān adhokṣajaḥ tad eva satyaṃ tad uhaiva maṅgalaṃtad eva puṇyaṃ bhagavadgunodayam  Hbhv tad eva ramyaṃ ruciraṃ navaṃ navaṃtad eva śaśvan manaso mahotsavam tad eva śokārṇavaśoṣaṇaṃ nṝṇāṃyad uttamaślokayaśo nugīyate  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottaredattvā ca gītaṃ dharmajñā gandharvaiḥ saha modate svayaṃ gītena sampūjya tasyaivānucaro bhavet  Hbhv pādme śrīkṛṣṇasatyabhāmāsaṃvādīyakārttikamāhātmye śrīpṛthunāradasaṃvāde śrībhagavaduktaunāhaṃ vasāmi vaikuṇṭhe na yogihṛdayeṣu vā madbhaktā yatra gāyanti tatra tiṣṭhāmi nārada  Hbhv teṣāṃ pūjādikaṃ gandhapadyādyaiḥ kriyate naraiḥ tena prītiṃ parāṃ yāmi na tathā matpūjanāt  Hbhv ata evoktaṃkarmāṇy aupāyikatvena brāhmaṇo nya iti smṛtaḥ kārikāyām ataḥ proktaṃ haribhaktisudhodayabahudhotsāryate harṣād viṣṇubhaktasya nṛtyataḥ padbhyāṃ bhūmer diśo kṣibhyāṃ dorbhyāṃ vāmaṅgalaṃ divaḥ  Hbhv vārāheyaś ca nṛtyati suśroṇi purāṇoktaṃ samāsataḥ triṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi pradakṣiṇācatuṣṭayam tepi yanti paraṃ sthānam sarvalokottamottamam  Hbhv iti tat khyātaṃ yat sudharmasya pūrvasmin gṛdhrajanmani kṛṣṇapradakṣiṇābhyāsān mahāsiddhir abhūd iti  Hbhv atha pradakṣiṇāyaṃ niṣiddhaṃviṣṇusmṛtauekahastapraṇāmaś ca ekā caiva pradakṣiṇā akāle darśanaṃ viṣṇor hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv kiṃ cakṛṣṇasya purato naiva sūryasyaiva pradakṣiṇām kuryād bhramarikārūpāṃ vaimukhyapadanīṃ prabhoḥ  Hbhv tathā coktaṃpradakṣiṇāṃ na kartavyaṃ vimukhatvāc ca kāraṇāt  Hbhv atha karmādyarpaṇamtataḥ śrīkṛṣṇapādābje dāsyenaiva samarpayet tribhir mantraiḥ svakarmāṇi sarvāṇy ātmānam apy atha  Hbhv mantraś caitaḥ pūrvaṃ prāṇabuddhidharmādhikārato jāgratsvapnasuṣuptyavasthāsu manasā vācākarmaṇā hastābhyāṃ padbhyām udareṇa śiśnā yat smṛtaṃ yad uktaṃ yat kṛtaṃ tat sarvaṃśrīkṛṣṇārpaṇaṃ bhavatu svāhā māṃ madīyaṃ ca sakalaṃ haraye samarpayāmīti oṃ tat sat  Hbhv iti atha tatra karmarpanaṃbṛhannāradīyevirāgī cet karmaphale na kiñcid api kārayet arpayet svakṛtaṃ karma prīyatām iti me hariḥ  Hbhv ata eva kūrmapurāṇeprīṇātu bhagavān īśaḥ karmaṇānena śāśvataḥ karoti satataṃ buddhyā brahmārpaṇam idaṃ param  Hbhv yad vā phalānāṃ sannyāsaṃ prakuryāt parameśvare karmaṇām etad apy āhur brahmārpaṇam anuttamam  Hbhv atha karmārpaṇavidhiḥdakṣeṇa pāṇinārghyasthaṃ gṛhītvā culukodakam nidhāya kṛṣṇapādābjasamīpe prārthayed idam  Hbhv pādatrayakramākrānta trailokeśvara keśava tvatprasādād idaṃ toyaṃ pādyaṃ testu janārdana  Hbhv atha karmarpanamāhātmyaṃbṛhannāradīyeparalokaphalaprepsuḥ kuryāt karmāṇy atandritaḥ harer nivedayet tāni tat sarvaṃ tv akṣayaṃ bhavet  Hbhv ata eva nārāyaṇavyūhastavekṛṣṇārpitaphalāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ svadharmeṇa yajanti ye viṣṇubhaktyarthino dhanyās tebhyo pīha namo namaḥ  Hbhv atha svārpaṇavidhiḥahaṃ bhagavato ṃśo smi sadā dāso smi sarvathā tatkṛpāpekṣako nityam i ty ātmānaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv tathā coktaṃ śrīśaṅkarācāryapādaiḥ saty api bhedāpagame nātha tavāhaṃ na māmakīnas tvam sāmudro hi taraṅgaḥ kvacana samudro na tāraṅgaḥ  Hbhv athātmārpaṇamāhātmyamsaptamaskandhe śrīprahlādoktau BhP  dharmārthakāma iti yo bhihitas trivargaīkṣā trayī nayadamau vividhā ca vārtā manye tad etad akhilaṃ nigamasya satyaṃsvātmārpaṇaṃ svasuhṛdaḥ paramasya puṃsaḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  martyo yadā tyaktasamastakarmāniveditātmā vicikīrṣito me tadāmṛtatvaṃ pratipadyamānomayātmabhūyāya ca kalpate vai  Hbhv atha japaḥjapasya purataḥ kṛtvā prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ budhaḥ mantrārthasmṛtipūrvaṃ ca japed aṣṭottaraṃ śatam mūlaṃ lekhyena vidhinā sadaiva japamālayā  Hbhv śaktauṣṭādhikasāhasram japet taṃ cārpayan japam prāṇāyāmāṃś ca kṛtvā trīn dadyāt kṛṣṇakare jalam  Hbhv tatra cāyaṃ mantraḥguhyātiguhyagoptā tvaṃ gṛhāṇāsmatkṛtaṃ japam siddhir bhavatu me deva tvatprasādāt tvayi sthite  Hbhv iti japaprakāro yo pekṣyo mālādiniyamātmakaḥ puraścaryāprasaṅge tu sa vilikhyategrataḥ  Hbhv arpitaṃ taṃ ca sañcintya svīkṛtaṃ prabhuṇākhilam punaḥ stutvā yathāśakti praṇamya prārthayed idam  Hbhv  āgamemantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ bhaktihīnaṃ janārdana yat pūjitaṃ mayā deva paripūrṇaṃ tad astu me  Hbhv kiṃ cayad dattaṃ bhaktimātreṇa patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ jalam āveditaṃ nivedyaṃ tu tad gṛhāṇānukampayā  Hbhv vidhihīnaṃ mantrahīnaṃ yat kiñcid upapāditam kriyāmantravihīnaṃ vā tat sarvaṃ kṣantum arhasi  Hbhv kiṃ caajñānād athavā jñānād aśubhaṃ yan mayā kṛtam kṣantum arhasi tat sarvaṃ dāsyenaiva gṛhāṇa mām  Hbhv sthitiḥ sevā gatir yātrā smṛtiś cintā stutir vacaḥ bhūyāt sarvātmanā viṣṇo madīyaṃ tvayi ceṣṭitam  Hbhv api cakṛṣṇa rāma mukunda vāmana vāsudeva jagadguro matsya kacchapa nārasiṃha varāha rāghava pāhi mām  Hbhv devadānavanāradādivandya dayānidhe devakīsuta dehi me tava pādabhaktim acalām  Hbhv śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  nātha yonisahasreṣu yeṣu yeṣu vrajāmy aham teṣu teṣv acyutā bhaktir acyutestu sadā tvayi  Hbhv yā prītir avivekānāṃ viṣayeṣv anapāyinī tvām anusmarataḥ sā me hṛdayān nāpasarpatu  Hbhv pāṇḍavagītāyāṃ kīṭeṣu pakṣiṣu mṛgeṣu sarīsṛpeṣurakṣaḥpiśācamanujeṣv api yatra tatra jātasya me bhavatu keśava te prasādāttvayy eva bhaktir atulāvyabhicāriṇī ca  Hbhv pādme yuvatīnāṃ yathā yūni yūnāṃ ca yuvatau yathā mano bhiramate tadvan mano bhiramatāṃ tvayi  Hbhv athāparādhakṣamāpaṇamtato parādhān śrīkṛṣṇaṃ kṣamāśīlaṃ kṣamāpayet sakāku kīrtayan ślokān uttamān sāmpradāyikān  Hbhv tathā hiaparādhasahasrāṇi kriyanteharniśaṃ mayā dāso ham iti māṃ matvā kṣamasva madhusūdana  Hbhv kiṃ capratijñā tava govinda na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati iti saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya prāṇān saṃdhārayāmy aham  Hbhv athāparādhāḥāgame yānair vā pādukair vāpi gamanaṃ bhagavadgṛhe devotsavādyasevā ca apraṇāmas tadagrataḥ  Hbhv ucchiṣṭe vāpy aśauce vā bhagavadvandanādikam ekahastapraṇāmaś ca tatpurastāt pradakṣiṇam  Hbhv pādaprasāraṇaṃ cāgre tathā paryaṅkabandhanam śayanaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ cāpi mithyābhāṣaṇam eva ca  Hbhv uccair bhāṣā mitho jalpo rodanāni ca vigrahaḥ nigrahānugrahau caiva nṛṣu ca krūrabhāṣaṇam  Hbhv kambalāvaraṇaṃ caiva paranindā parastutiḥ aślīlabhāṣaṇaṃ caiva adhovāyuvimokṣaṇam  Hbhv śaktau gauṇopacāraś ca aniveditabhakṣaṇam tattatkālodbhavānāṃ ca phalādīnām anarpaṇam  Hbhv viniyuktāvaiśiṣṭhasya pradānaṃ vyañjanādike pṛṣṭhīkṛtyāsanaṃ caiva pareṣām abhivādanam  Hbhv gurau maunaṃ nijastotraṃ devatānindanaṃ tathā aparādhās tathā viṣṇor dvātriṃśat parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv vārāhedvātriṃśadaparādhā ye kīrtyante vasudhe mayā vaiṣṇavena sadā te tu varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ  Hbhv ye vai na varjayanty etān aparādhān mayoditān sarvadharmaparibhraṣṭāḥ pacyante narake ciram  Hbhv rājānnabhakṣaṇaṃ caivam āpady api bhayāvaham dhvāntāgāre hareḥ sparśaḥ paraṃ sukṛtanāśanaḥ  Hbhv tathaiva vidhim ullaṅghya sahasā sparśanaṃ hareḥ dvārodghāṭo vinā vādyaṃ kroḍamāṃsanivedanam  Hbhv pādukābhyāṃ tathā viṣṇor mandirāyopasarpaṇam kukkurocchiṣṭakalanaṃ maunabhaṅgo cyutārcane  Hbhv tathā pūjanakāle viḍutsargāya sarpaṇam śrāddhādikam akṛtvā ca navānnasya ca bhakṣaṇam  Hbhv adattvā gandhamālyādi dhūpanaṃ madhughātinaḥ akarmaṇy aprasūnena pūjanaṃ ca hares tathā  Hbhv  akṛtvā dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca kṛtvā nidhūvanaṃ tathā spṛṣṭvā rajasvalāṃ dīpaṃ tathā mṛtakam eva ca  Hbhv raktaṃ nīlam adhautaṃ ca pārakyaṃ malinaṃ paṭam paridhāya mṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā vimucyāpānamārutam  Hbhv krodhaṃ kṛtvā śmaśānaṃ ca gatvā bhuktāpy ajīrṇayuk bhakṣayitvā kroḍamāṃsaṃ pinyākaṃ jālapādakam  Hbhv tathā kusumbhaśākaṃ ca tailābhyaṅgaṃ vidhāya ca hareḥ sparśo hareḥ karmakaraṇaṃ pātakāvaham  Hbhv kiṃ tatraivamama śāstraṃ bahiṣkṛtya asmākaṃ yaḥ prapadyate muktvā ca mama śāstrāṇi śāstram anyat prabhāṣase  Hbhv madyapas tu samāsādya praviśed bhavanaṃ mama  Hbhv yo me kusumbhaśākena prāpaṇaṃ kurute naraḥ  Hbhv api camama dṛṣṭer abhimukhaṃ tāmbūlaṃ carvayet tu yaḥ kurūvakaḥ palāśasthaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kuryān mamārcanam  Hbhv mamārcām āsure kāle yaḥ karoti vimūḍhadhīḥ pīṭhāsanopaviṣṭo yaḥ pūjayed vā nirāsanaḥ  Hbhv vāmahastena māṃ dhṛtvā snāpayed vā vimūḍhadhīḥ pūjā paryuṣitaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ṣṭhīvanaṃ garvakalpanam  Hbhv tiryakpuṇḍradharo bhūtvā yaḥ karoti mamārcanam yācitaiḥ patrapuṣpādyair yaḥ karoti mamārcanam  Hbhv aprakṣālitapādo yaḥ praviśen mama mandiram avaiṣṇavasya pakvānnaṃ yo mahyaṃ vinivedayet  Hbhv avaiṣṇaveṣu paśyatsu mama pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ apūjayitvā vighneśaṃ sambhāṣya ca kapālinam  Hbhv naraḥ pūjāṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt snapanaṃ ca nakhāmbhasā amaunī dharmaliptāṅgo mama pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ  Hbhv jñeyāḥ parepi bahavo parādhāḥ sadasammataiḥ ācāraiḥ śāstravihitaniṣiddhātikramādibhiḥ tatrāpi sarvathā kṛṣṇanirmālyaṃ tu na laṅghayet  Hbhv tathā ca nārasiṃhe śantanuṃ prati nāradavākyam ataḥ paraṃ tu nirmālyaṃ na laṅghaya mahīpate narasiṃhasya devasya tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām  Hbhv kṛṣṇasya paritoṣepsur na tacchapatham ācaret nānādevasya nirmālyam upayuñjīta na kvacit  Hbhv tathā viṣṇudharmottareāpādy api ca kaṣṭāyāṃ deveśaśapathaṃ naraḥ na karoti hi yo brahmaṃs tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv na dhārayati nirmālyam anyadevadhṛtaṃ tu yaḥ bhuṅkte na cānyanaivedyaṃ tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv iti athāparādhaśamanamsaṃvatsarasya madhye tu tīrthe śaukarake mama kṛtopavāsaḥ snānena gaṅgāyāṃ śuddhim āpnuyāt  Hbhv  mathurāyāṃ tathāpy evaṃ sāparādhaḥ śuci bhavet  Hbhv  anayos tīrthayor ekaṃ yaḥ seveta sukṛtī naraḥ sahasrajanmajanitān aparādhān jahāti saḥ  Hbhv  skānde ahany ahani yo martyo gītādhyāyaṃ paṭhet tu vai dvātriṃśadaparādhāṃs tu kṣamate tasya keśavaḥ  Hbhv  tatra kārttikamāhātmye tulasyā ropaṇaṃ kāryaṃ śrāvaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ aparādhasahasrāṇi kṣamate puruṣottamaḥ  Hbhv  tatraivānyatra dvādaśyāṃ jāgare viṣṇor yaḥ paṭhet tulasīstavam dvātriṃśadaparādhāni kṣamate tasya keśavaḥ  Hbhv  yaḥ karoti hareḥ pūjāṃ kṛṣṇaśatrāṅkito naraḥ aparādhasahasrāṇi nityaṃ harati keśavaḥ  Hbhv atha śeṣagrahaṇamtato bhagavatā dattaṃ manyamāno dayālunā mahāprasāda ity uktvā śeṣaṃ śirasi dhārayet  Hbhv atha nirmālyadhāraṇanityatāpādme śrīgautamāmbarīṣasaṃvādeambarīṣa harer lagnaṃ nīraṃ puṣpaṃ vilepanam bhaktyā na dhatte śirasā śvapacād adhiko hi saḥ  Hbhv atha śrībhagavannirmālyamāhātmyaṃskānde brahmanāradasaṃvādekṛṣṇottīrṇaṃ tu nirmālyaṃ yasyāṅgaṃ spṛśate mune sarvarogair tathā pāpair mukto bhavati nārada  Hbhv viṣṇor nirmālyaśeṣeṇa yo gātraṃ parimārjayet duritāni vinaśyanti vyādhayo yānti khaṇḍaśaḥ  Hbhv mukhe śirasi dehe tu viṣṇūttirnaṃ tu yo vahet tulasīṃ muniśārdūla na tasya spṛśate kaliḥ  Hbhv kiṃ caviṣṇumūrtisthitaṃ puṣpaṃ śirasā yo vahen naraḥ aparyūṣitapāpas tu yāvad yugacatuṣṭayam  Hbhv kiṃ kariṣyati susnāto gaṅgāyāṃ bhūsurottama yo vahet śirasā nityaṃ tulasīṃ viṣṇusevitāṃ  Hbhv viṣṇupādābjasaṃlagnām ahorātroṣitāṃ śubhām tulasīṃ dhārayed yo vai tasya puṇyam anantakam  Hbhv ahoratraṃ śire yasya tulasī viṣṇusevitā na sa lipyati pāpena padmapatram ivāmbhasā  Hbhv kiṃ caviṣṇoḥ śiraḥparibhraṣṭam bhaktyā yas tulasīṃ vahet sidhyānti sarvakāryāṇi manasā cintitāni ca  Hbhv api capramārjayati yo deham tulasyā vaiṣṇavo naraḥ sarvatīrthamayaṃ dehaṃ tatkṣanāt dvija jāyate  Hbhv gāruḍeharer mūrtyavaśeṣaṃ tu tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam nirmālyaṃ tu vahed yas tu koṭitīrthaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv nāradapañcarātrebhojananāntaraṃ viṣṇor arpitaṃ tulasīdalam tatkṣanāt pāpanirmoktas cāndrāyaṇaśatādhikaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ cānyatrakautukaṃ śṛṇu me devi viṣṇor nirmālyavahninā tāpitaṃ nāśam āyāti brahmahatyādipātakam  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe śrībhagavantaṃ praty uddhavoktautvayopayuktasraggandhavāso laṅkāracarcitaḥ ucchistabhojino dāsās tava māyāṃ jayema hi  Hbhv ata eva skānde śrīyamasya dūtānuśāsanepādodakaratā ye ca harer nirmālyadhārakāḥ viṣṇubhaktiratā ye vai te tu tyājyaḥ sudurataḥ  Hbhv iti visarjanaṃ tu cet kāryaṃ visṛjyavaraṇāni tat deve tanmudrayā prārthya devaṃ hṛdi visarjayet  Hbhv tathā coktaṃpūjito si mayā bhaktyā bhagavan kamalapate sa lakṣmīko mama svāntaṃ viśa viśrāntihetave  Hbhv prārthyaivaṃ pāduke dattvā saṅgam udvāsayed dharim prāṇāyāmaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ca kṛtvā mudrāṃ visarjanīm  Hbhv atha pūjavidhivivekaḥayaṃ pūjavidhir mantrasiddhyarthasya japasya hi aṅgaṃ bhaktes tu tanniṣṭhair nyāsādīn antareṣyate  Hbhv tatra devalaye pūja nityatvena mahāprabhoḥ kāmyatvenāpi gehe tu prāyo nityatayā matā  Hbhv sevādiniyamo devālaye devasya ceṣyate prāyaḥ svagehe svacchandasevā svavratarakṣayā  Hbhv kiṃ ca viṣṇudharmottareghṛtena snapitaṃ devaṃ candanenānulepayet sitajātyāś ca kusumaih pūjayet tadanantaram  Hbhv śvetena vastrayugmena tathā muktāphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ mukhyakarpūradhūpena payasā pāyasena ca  Hbhv padmasūtrasya varttyā ca ghṛtadhūpena cāpy atha pūjayet sarvathā yatnāt sarvakāmapradārcanam  Hbhv kṛtvemaṃ mucyate rogī rogāt śīghram asaṃśayam duḥkhārto mucyate duḥkhād baddho mucyeta bandhanāt  Hbhv rājagrastaś ca mucyeta tathā rājabhayān naraḥ kṣemeṇa gacched adhvānam sarvānarthavivarjitaḥ  Hbhv iti iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāseprātararcāsamāpano nāmāṣṭamo vilāsaḥ   MahaprasadaVilasanavamavilāsaḥmahāprasādaḥsa prasdatu caitanyadevo yasya prasādataḥ mahāprasādajātārhaḥ sadyaḥ syād adhamo py aham  Hbhv atha śakhodakaṃ tac ca kṛṣñadṛṣṭisudhokṣitam vaiṣñavebhyaḥ pradāyābhivandya mūrdhani dhārayet  Hbhv śakhodakamāhātmyaṃskānde brahmanāradasaṃvādeśakhodakaṃ harer bhaktir nirmālyaṃ pādayor jalaṃ candanaṃ dhūpaśeṣaṃ tu brahmahatyāpahārakam  Hbhv tatraiva śakhamāhātmyeśakhasthitaṃ tu yat toyaṃ bhrāmitaṃ keśavopari vandate śirasā nityaṃ gagāsnānena tasya kim  Hbhv na dāho na klamo nārtir narakāgnibhayaṃ na hi yasya śakhodakaṃ mūrdhni kṛṣñadṛṣṭyavalokitam  Hbhv na grahā na ca kuṣmāñḍāḥ piśācoragarakṣasāḥ dṛṣṭvā śakhodakaṃ mūrdhni vidravanti diśo daśa  Hbhv kṛṣñamūrdhni bhrāmitaṃ tu jalaṃ tacchakhasaṃsthitam kṛtvā mūrdhany avāpnoti muktiṃ viṣñoḥ prasādataḥ  Hbhv bhrāmayitvā harer mūrdhni mandiraṃ śakhavāriñā prokṣayed vaiṣñavo yas tu nāśubhaṃ tadgṛhe bhavet  Hbhv nrājanajalaṃ yatra yatra pādodakaṃ hareḥ tiṣṭhate muniśārdūla vardhante tatra sampadaḥ  Hbhv tatraivāgrenrājanajalaṃ viṣñor yasya gātrāñi saṃspṛśet yajñāvabhṛtalakṣañaṃ snānajaṃ labhate phalam  Hbhv tatraiva śrśivoktaupādodakena devasya hatyāyutasamanvitaḥ śudhyate nātra sandehas tathā śakhodakena hi  Hbhv bṛhadviṣñupurāñe catrthādhikaṃ yajñaśatāc ca pāvanaṃjalaṃ sadā keśavadṛṣṭisaṃsthitam chinatti pāpaṃ tulasvimiśritaṃviśeṣataś cakraśilāvinirmitam  Hbhv atha trthadhārānaṃkṛṣñapadabjatrthaṃ ca vaiṣñavebhyaḥ pradāya hi svayaṃ bhaktyabhivandyādau ptvā śirasi dhārayet  Hbhv tasya mantravidhiś ca prāk prātaḥsnānaprasagataḥ likhito hy adhunā pāne viśeṣo likhyate kiyān  Hbhv sa coktaḥoṃ carañaṃ pavitraṃ vitataṃ purāñaṃyena pūtas tarati duṣkṛtāni tena pavitreña śuddhena pūtāapi pāpmānam arātiṃ tarema  Hbhv  lokasya dvāram ārcayat pavitraṃ jyotiṣmat vibhrājamānaṃ mahas tad amṛtasya dhārā bahudhā dohamānaṃ carañaṃ loke sudhitaṃ dadhatu  Hbhv   iti  imaṃ mantraṃ samuccārya sarvaduṣṭagrahāpaham prāśnyāt prokṣayed dehaṃ putramitraparigraham  Hbhv kiṃ caviṣñoḥ pādodakaṃ ptaṃ koṭihatyāghanāśanam tad evaṣṭagunaṃ pāpaṃ bhumau bindunipatanat  Hbhv atha śrcaranodakapanamāhātmyaṃpādme gautamāmbarṣasaṃvādehareḥ snānāvaśeṣas tu jalaṃ yasyodare sthitam ambarṣa prañamyoccaiḥ pādapāṃśuḥ pragṛhyatām  Hbhv tatraiva devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvādeye pibanti narā nityaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam pañcagavyasahasrais tu sevitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  Hbhv koṭitrthasahasrais tu sevitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam nityaṃ yadi pibet puñyaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam  Hbhv śālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ yaḥ pibed bindunā samam mātuḥ stanyaṃ punar naiva na pibed bhaktibhā naraḥ  Hbhv kiṃ cadahanti narakān sarvān garbhavāsaṃ ca dāruñam ptaṃ yais tu sadā nityaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam  Hbhv tatraiva śryamadhumraketusaṃvādeśālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ bindumātraṃ tu yaḥ pibet sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyeta bhaktimārge kṛtodyamaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva pulastyabhagrathasaṃvādepādodakasya māhātmyaṃ bhagratha vadāmi te pāvanaṃ sarvatrthebhyo hatyākoṭivināśakam  Hbhv dhṛte śirasi pte ca sarvās tusyanti devatāḥ prāyaścittaṃ tu pāpānāṃ kalau pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv kiṃ catribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ saptāhena tu nārmadam sadyaḥ punāti gāgeyaṃ darśanād eva yāmunam  Hbhv punanty etāni toyāni snānadarśanakrtanaiḥ punāti smarañād eva kalau pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv kiṃ caarcitaiḥ koṭibhir ligair nityaṃ yat kriyate phalam tat phalaṃ śatasahasraṃ pite pādodake hareḥ  Hbhv aśucir vā durācāro mahāpātakasaṃyutaḥ spṛṣṭvā pādodakaṃ viṣñoḥ sadā śudhyati mānavaḥ  Hbhv pāpakoṭiyuto yas tu mṛtyukāle śiromukhe dehe pādodakaṃ tasya na prayāti yamālayam  Hbhv na dānaṃ na havir yeṣāṃ svādhyāyo na surārcanam te pi pādodakaṃ ptvā prayanti paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv kārttike kārttikyoge kiṃ kariṣyati puṣkare nityaṃ ca puṣkaraṃ tasya yasya pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv viśākhāṛkṣasaṃyukta vaiśākh hi kariṣyati piñḍārake mahātrthe ujjāyinyāṃ bhagratha  Hbhv māghamāse prayāge tu snānaṃ kiṃ kariṣyati prayāgaṃ satataṃ tasya yasya pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv prabodhavāsare prāpte mathurāyāṃ ca tasya kim nityaṃ ca yāmunaṃ snānaṃ yasya pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv kasyām uttaravāhinyāṃ gagāyāṃ tu mṛtasya kim yasya pādodakaṃ viṣñor mukhe caivāvatiṣṭhate  Hbhv kiṃ cahitvā pādodakaṃ viṣñor yo nyatrthāni gacchati anarghaṃ ratnam utsṛjya loṣṭraṃ vāñchati durmatiḥ  Hbhv kurukṣetrasamo deśo binduḥ pādodakaṃ mataḥ  Hbhv pated yatrākṣayaṃ puñyaṃ nityaṃ bhavati tadgṛhe gayāpiñḍasamaṃ puñyaṃ putrāñām api jāyate  Hbhv pādodakena devasya ye kuryuḥ pitṛtarpañam nāsurāñāṃ bhayaṃ tasya pretajanyaṃ ca rākṣasam  Hbhv na rogasya bhayaṃ caiva nāsti vighnakṛtaṃ bhayam na duṣṭā naiva ghorākṣāḥ svāpadotthabhayaṃ na hi  Hbhv grahāḥ pdāṃ na kurvanti caurā naśyanti dāruñāḥ kiṃ tasya trthagamane devarṣñāṃ ca darśane  Hbhv yasya pādodakaṃ mūrdhni śālagrāmaśilodbhavam prto bhavati mārtañḍaḥ prto bhavati keśavaḥ brahmā bhavati suprtaḥ prto bhavati sakaraḥ  Hbhv pādodakasya māhātmyaṃ yaḥ paṭhet keśavagrataḥ sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra devo janardanaḥ  Hbhv brahmāñḍapurāñe śrbrahmanāradasaṃvādeprāyaścittaṃ yadi prāptaṃ kṛcchraṃ vā tv aghamarṣañam so pi pādodakaṃ ptvā śuddhiṃ prāpnoti tatkṣañāt  Hbhv aśaucaṃ naiva vidyeta sūtake mṛtake pi ca yeṣāṃ pādodakaṃ mūrdhni prāśanaṃ ye ca kurvate  Hbhv antakāle pi yasyeha dyate pādayor jalam so pi sadgatim āpnoti sadācārair bahiṣkṛtaḥ  Hbhv apeyaṃ pibate yas tu bhukte yaś cāpy abhojanam agamyāgamanā ye vai pāpācārāś ca ye narāḥ te pi pūjyā bhavanty āśu sadyaḥ pādāmbusevanāt  Hbhv kiṃ caapavitraṃ yadannaṃ syāt pānyaṃ cāpi pāpinām bhuktvā ptvā viśuddhaḥ syāt ptvā pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv taptakṛcchrāt pañcagavyān mahākṛcchrād viśiṣyate cāndrāyañāt pārakṛcchrāt parākād api suvrata kāyaśuddhir bhavaty āśu ptvā pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv aguruṃ kukumaṃ cāpi karpūraṃ cānulepanam viṣñupādāmbusaṃlagnaṃ tad vai pāvanapāvanam  Hbhv dṛṣṭipūtaṃ tu yat toyaṃ viṣñunā prabhaviṣñunā tad vai pāpaharaṃ putra kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam  Hbhv etadartham ahaṃ putra śirasā viṣñutatparaḥ dhārāyāmi pibāmy adya māhātmyaṃ viditaṃ mama  Hbhv priyas tvam agrajaḥ putras tadarthaṃ gaditaṃ mayā rahasyaṃ me tv anarhasya na vaktavyaṃ kadācana  Hbhv dhārayasva sadā mūrdhni prāśanaṃ kuru nityaśaḥ janmamṛtyujarāduḥkhair mokṣaṃ yāsyasi putraka  Hbhv viṣñudharmottaresadyaḥ phalapradaṃ puñyaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam sarvamagalamagalyaṃ sarvaduḥkhavināśanam  Hbhv duḥsvapnanāśanaṃ puñyaṃ viṣñupādodakaṃ śubham sarvopadravahantāraṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam  Hbhv sarvotpātapraśamanaṃ sarvapāpanivārañam sarvakalyāñasukhadaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam  Hbhv sarvasiddhipradaṃ dhanyaṃ sarvadharmavivardhanam sarvaśatrupraśamanaṃ sarvabhogapradāyakam  Hbhv sarvatrthasya phaladam mūrdhni pādāmbudhārañam prayāgasya prabhāsasya puṣkarasya ca sevane pṛthūdakasya trthasya ācānto labhate phalam  Hbhv cakratrthaṃ phalaṃ yādṛk tādṛñ pādāmbudhārañāt sarasvatyāṃ gayāyāṃ ca gatvā yat prāpnuyāt phalam tat phalaṃ labhate śreṣṭhaṃ mūrdhni pādāmbudhārañāt  Hbhv skāndepādodakasya māhātmyaṃ devo jānāti śakaraḥ viṣñupādacyutā gagā śirasā yena dhāritā sthānaṃ naivāsti pāpasya dehināṃ dehamadhyataḥ  Hbhv sabāhyābhyantaraṃ yasya vyāptaṃ pādodakena vai pādodaṃ viṣñunaivedyam udare yasya tiṣṭhati  Hbhv nāśrayaṃ labhate pāpaṃ svayam eva vinaśyati mahāpāpagrahagrasto vyāpto rogaśatair yadi  Hbhv hareḥ pādodakaṃ ptvā mucyate nātra saṃsayaḥ śirasā tiṣṭhate yeṣāṃ nityaṃ pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv kiṃ kariṣyati te loke trthakoṭimanorathaiḥ ayam eva paro dharma idam eva paraṃ tapaḥ idam eva paraṃ trthaṃ viṣñupādāmbu yat pibet  Hbhv tatraiva śrśivomāsaṃvādevilayaṃ yānti pāpāni pte pādodake hareḥ kiṃ punar viṣñupādodaṃ śālagrāmaśilācyutam  Hbhv viśeṣena haret pāpaṃ brahmahatyādikaṃ priye pte pādodake viṣñor yadi prāñair vimucyate hatvā yamabhaṭān sarvān vaiṣñavaṃ lokam āpnuyāt  Hbhv tatraiva śrśivakārttikeyasaṃvāde śrśālagrāmaśilāmāhātmyechinnas tena mahāsena garbhāvāsaḥ sudāruñaḥ ptaṃ yena sadā viṣñoḥ śālagrāmaśilājalam  Hbhv ye pibanti narā nityaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam pañcagavyasahasrais tu prāśitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  Hbhv prāyaścitte samutpanne kiṃ dānaiḥ kim upoṣañaiḥ cāndrāyañaiś ca trthaiś ca ptvā pādodakaṃ śuci  Hbhv bṛhannāradiye lubdhakopākhyānārambheharipādodakaṃ yas tu kṣañamātraṃ ca dhārayet sa snātaḥ sarvatrthesu viṣñoḥ priyataras tathā  Hbhv akālamṛtyuśamanaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam sarvaduḥkhopaśamanaṃ haripādodakaṃ śubham  Hbhv tatraiva tadupākhyānānteharipādodakasparśāl lubdhako vtakalmaṣaḥ divyaṃ vimānam āruhya munim enam athābravt  Hbhv haripādodakaṃ yasmān mayi tvaṃ kṣiptavān mune prāpito smi tvayā tasmāt tad viṣñoḥ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodayepādaṃ pūrvaṃ kila spṛṣṭvā gagābhūt smartṛmokṣadā viṣñoḥ sadyas tu satsagi pādāmbu katham ḍyate  Hbhv tāpatrayānalo yo sau na śāmyet sakalābdhibhiḥ drutaṃ śāmyati so lpena śrmadviṣñupadāmbunā  Hbhv yuddhāstrābhedyakavacaṃ bhavāgnistambhanauṣadham sarvāgaiḥ sarvathā dhāryaṃ pādyaṃ śucipadaḥ sadā  Hbhv amṛtatvāvahaṃ nityaṃ viṣñupādāmbu yaḥ pibet sa pibaty amṛtaṃ nityaṃ māse māse tu devatāḥ  Hbhv māhātmyam iyad ity asya vaktā yo pi sa nirbhayaḥ nanv anarghamañer mūlyaṃ kalpayann agham aśnute  Hbhv anyatrapisa brahmacār sa vrat āśram ca sadāśuciḥ viṣñupādodakaṃ yasya mukhe śirasi vigrahe  Hbhv janmaprabhṛtipāpānāṃ prāyaścittaṃ yadcchati śālagrāmaśilāvari pāpahāri niṣevyatām  Hbhv ata eva tejodravinapañcaratre śrbrahmañoktampṭhaprañālād udakaṃ pṛthag ādāya putraka siñcayen mūrdhni bhaktānāṃ sarvatrthamayaṃ hi tat  Hbhv  iti pādodakasya māhātmyaṃ vikhyātaṃ sarvaśāstrataḥ likhituṃ śaknuyat ko hi sindhūrmn gañayann api  Hbhv viśeṣataś ca pādodaṃ tulasdalasaṃyutam śakhe kṛtvā vaiṣñavebhyo dattvā prāgvat pibet svayam  Hbhv atha śakhakṛtapādodakamāhātmyaṃskānde śrbrahmanāradasaṃvādekṛtvā pādodakaṃ śakhe vaiṣñavānāṃ mahātmanām yo dadyāt tulasmiśraṃ cāndrāyañaśataṃ labhet  Hbhv gṛhtvā kṛṣñapādāmbu śakhe kṛtvā tu vaiṣñavaḥ yo vahet śirasā nityaṃ sa munis tapasottamaḥ  Hbhv pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvādeśālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ yadi śakhabhṛtaṃ pibet hatyākoṭivināśaṃ ca kurute nātra saṃsayaḥ  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāmśālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ tulasdalavāsitam ye pibanti punas teṣāṃ stanyapānaṃ na vidyate  Hbhv  iti śrviṣñor vaiṣñavānāṃ ca pāvanaṃ carañodakam sarvatrthamayaṃ ptvā kuryād ācamanaṃ na hi  Hbhv tad uktaṃ skānde śivenaviṣñoḥ pādodakaṃ ptvā paścād aśuciśakayā ācamati ca yo mohād brahmahā sa nigadyate  Hbhv srutiś cabhagavān pavitraṃ bhagavatpādau pavitraṃbhagavatpādodakaṃ pavitraṃna tatpāna ācamanyam yathā hi soma iti  Hbhv sauparñe caviṣñupādodakaṃ ptvā bhaktapādodakaṃ tathā ya ācamati saṃmohād brahmahā sa nigadyate  Hbhv  iti tataḥ śuddhaṃ payaḥpūrñaṃ gandhapuṣpākṣatānvitam adharopari sannyasec chakhaṃ bhagavadagrataḥ  Hbhv atha śrbhagavadagrataḥ śakhasthapanamahatamyaṃskānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde śakhamāhātmyepurato vāsudevasya sapuṣpaṃ sajalākṣatam śakham abhyarcitaṃ paśyet tasya lakṣmr na durlabhā  Hbhv sapuṣpaṃ vārijaṃ yasya durvākṣatasamanvitam purato vāsudevasya tasya śrḥ sarvatomukh  Hbhv  iti bhūtvātha bhaktimān śrmattulasyā kānane prabhum sampūjyābhyarcayet taṃ ca śrkṛṣñacarañapriyam  Hbhv atha śrtulasvanapūjāprāg dattvārghyaṃ tato vyarcya gandhapuṣpākṣatādinā stutvā bhagavatṃ tāṃ ca prañamet prārhtya dañḍavat  Hbhv athārghyamantraḥśriyaḥ śriye śriyāvāse nityaṃ śrdhārāsatkṛte bhaktyā dattaṃ mayā devi arghyaṃ gṛhña namo stu te  Hbhv pūjā mantraḥnirmitā tvaṃ purā devair arcitā tvaṃ surāsuraiḥ tulas hara me pāpaṃ pūjāṃ gṛhña namo stu te  Hbhv stutiś camahāprasādajanan sarvasaubhāgyavardhin ādhivyādhiharo nityaṃ tulas tvaṃ namo stu te  Hbhv prārthanāśryaṃ dehi yaśo dehi krtim āyus tathā sukham balaṃ puṣṭiṃ tathā dharmaṃ tulas tvaṃ prasda me  Hbhv prañāmavākyamavantkhañḍeyā dṛṣṭā nikhilāghasaghaśaman spṛṣṭā vapuḥpāvanrogāñām abhivanditā nirasin siktāntakatrāsin pratyāsattividhāyin bhagavataḥ kṛṣñasya saṃropitānyastā taccarañe vimuktiphaladā tasyai tulasyai namaḥ  Hbhv bhagavatyās tulasyās tu māhātmyāmṛtasāgare lobhāt kūrditum icchāmi kṣudras tat kṣamyatāṃ tvayā  Hbhv atha tulasivanapujamahatmyamskāndeśrāvañadvādaśyoge śālagrāmaśilārcane yat phalaṃ sagame proktaṃ tulaspūjanena tat  Hbhv gāruḍedhātrphalena yat puñyaṃ jayantyāṃ samupoṣañe khagendra bhavate nṛñāṃ tulaspūjanena tat  Hbhv prayāgasnānaniratau kasyāṃ prāñavimokṣañe yat phalaṃ vihitaṃ devais tulaspūjanena tat  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāmcaturñām api varñānām āśramāñām viśeṣataḥ strñāṃ ca puruṣāñāṃ ca pūjiteṣṭaṃ dadāti hi  Hbhv tulas ropitā siktā dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā ca pāvayet ārādhitā prayatnena sarvakāmaphalapradā  Hbhv atha tulasvanapūjamāhātmyaṃpradakṣiñaṃ bhramitvā ye namaskurvanti nityaśaḥ na teṣāṃ duritaṃ kiñcid akṣñam avaśiṣyate  Hbhv bṛhannāradiye yajñadhvajopākhyānāntepūjyamānā ca tulas yasya veśmani tiṣṭhati tasya sarvāñi śreyāṃsi vardhante harahar dvijāḥ  Hbhv ata eva pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvādepakṣe pakṣe tu samprāpte dvādaśyāṃ vaiśyasattama brahmādayo pi kurvanti tulasvanapūjanam  Hbhv ata eva śrtulasstutimahimāananyamanasā nityaṃ tulasṃ stauti yo naraḥ pitṛdevamanuṣyāñāṃ priyo bhavati sarvadā  Hbhv atha tulasvanamāhātmyaṃskānderatiṃ badhnāti nānyatra tulaskānanam vinā devadevo jagatsvām kalikāle viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv hitvā trthasahasrāñi sarvān api śiloccayan tulaskānane nityaṃ kalau tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ  Hbhv nirkṣitā narair yais tu tulasvanavāṭikā ropitā yaiś ca vidhinā samprāptaṃ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv na dhātr saphalā yatra na viṣñus tulasvanam tat śmaśānasamaṃ sthānaṃ santi yatra na vaiṣñavāḥ  Hbhv keśavārthe kalau ye tu ropayantha bhūtale kiṃ kariṣyaty asantuṣṭo yamo pi saha kikaraiḥ  Hbhv tulasyā ropañaṃ kāryaṃ śravañena viśeṣataḥ aparādhasahasrāñi kṣamate puruṣottamaḥ  Hbhv devālayeṣu sarveṣu puñyakṣetreṣu yo naraḥ vāpayet tulasṃ puñyāṃ tat trthaṃ cakrapāñinaḥ  Hbhv ghaṭair yantraghaṭbhiś ca siñcitaṃ tulasvanam jaladhārābhir viprendra prñitaṃ bhuvanatrayam  Hbhv tatraiva śrbrahmanāradasaṃvādetulasgandham ādāya yatra gacchati mārutaḥ diśo daśa ca pūtāḥ syur bhūtagrāmāś caturvidhāḥ  Hbhv tulaskānanodbhūtā chāyā yatra bhaved dvija tatra śrāddhaṃ pradātavyam pitñāṃ tṛptihetave  Hbhv tulasbjanikarāḥ patate yatra nārada piñḍadānaṃ kṛtaṃ tatra pitñāṃ dattam akṣayam  Hbhv tatraivāgredṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā tathā dhyātā krtitā namitā śrutā ropitā sevitā nityaṃ pūjitā tulas śubhā  Hbhv navadhā tulasṃ nityaṃ ye bhajanti dine dine yugakoṭisahasrāñi te vasanti harer gṛhe  Hbhv ropitā tulas yāvat kurute mūlavistaraṃ tāvat koṭisahasraṃ tu tanoti sukṛtaṃ kalau  Hbhv yāvac chākhāpraśākhābhir bjapuṣpaiḥ phalair mune ropitā tulas pumbhir vardhate vasudhātale  Hbhv kule teṣāṃ tu ye jātā ye bhaviṣyanti ye mṛtaḥ ākalpaṃ yugasāhasraṃ teṣāṃ vāso harer gṛhe  Hbhv tatraiva cāvantkhañḍetulasṃ ye vicinvanti dhanyās tatkarapallavāḥ keśavārthe kalau ye ca ropayantha bhūtale  Hbhv snāne dāne tathā dhyāne prāśane keśavārcane tulas dahate pāpaṃ ropañe krtane kalau  Hbhv kāśkhañḍe svadūtān prati śryamānuśāsanetulasyalakṛtā ye ye tulasnāmajāpakāḥ tulasvanapālā ye te tyājyā dūrato bhaṭāḥ  Hbhv tatraiva dhruvacaritetulas yasya bhavane pratyahaṃ paripūjyate tadgṛhe nopasarpanti kadācid yamakikarāḥ  Hbhv pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvādena paśyanti yamaṃ vaiśya tulasvanaropañāt sarvapāpaharaṃ sarvakāmadaṃ tulasvanam  Hbhv tulaskānanaṃ vaiśya gṛhe yasmiṃs tu tiṣṭhate tadgṛhaṃ trthbhūtaṃ hi no yānti yamakikarāḥ  Hbhv tāvad varṣasahasrāñi yāvad bjadalāni ca vasanti devaloke tu tulasṃ ropayanti ye  Hbhv tulasgandham āghrāya pitaras tuṣṭamānasāḥ prayānti garuḍārūḍhās tat padaṃ cakrapāñinaḥ  Hbhv darśanaṃ narmadāyās tu gagāsnānaṃ viśāṃ vara tulasdalasaṃsparsaḥ samam etat trayaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv ropañāt pālanāt sekād darśanāt sparśanān nṛñām tulas dahate pāpaṃ vāmanaḥkāyasañcitam  Hbhv āmravṛkṣasahasreña pippalānāṃ śatena ca yat phalaṃ hi tad ekena tulasvitapena tu  Hbhv viṣñupūjanasaṃyuktas tulasṃ yas tu ropayet yugāyutadaśaikaṃ sa ropako ramate divi  Hbhv tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmyepuṣkarādni trthāni gagādyāḥ saritas tathā vāsudevādayo devā vasanti tulasdale  Hbhv dāridryaduḥkharogārtipāpāni subahūny api tulas harati kṣipraṃ rogān iva hartak  Hbhv tatraiva kārttikamāhātmyeyadgṛhe tulas bhāti rakṣābhir jalasecanaiḥ tadgṛhe yamadūtāś ca dūrato varjayanti hi  Hbhv tulasyās tarpañaṃ ye ca pitn uddiśya mānavāḥ kurvanti teṣāṃ pitaras tṛptā varṣayutaṃ jalaiḥ  Hbhv paricaryāṃ ca ye tasya rakṣayābālabandhanaiḥ śuśrūṣito haris tais tu nātra kāryā vicārañā  Hbhv nāvajñā jātu kāryāsyā vṛkṣabhāvān manṣibhiḥ yathā hi vāsudevasya  Hbhv tulas vāpitā yena puñyārāme vane gṛhe pakṣndra tena satyoktaṃ lokāḥ sapta pratiṣṭhitāḥ  Hbhv tulaskānane yas tu muhūrtam api viśramet janmakoṭikṛtāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv pradakṣiñāṃ yaḥ kurute paṭhan nāmasahasrakam tulaskānane nityaṃ yajñāyutaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodayenityaṃ sannihito viṣñuḥ saspṛhas tulasvane api mekṣatapatraikaṃ kaścid dhanyo rpayed iti  Hbhv bṛhannāradye gagāprasagesaṃsārapāpavicchedi gagānāma prakrtitam tathā tulasyā bhaktiś ca harikrtipravaktari  Hbhv tulaskānanaṃ yatra yatra padmavanāni ca purāñapaṭhanaṃ yatra tatra sannihito dhātrphaladalānvitaḥ  Hbhv dhātrphalāni yo nityaṃ vahate karasampuṭe tasya nārāyaño devo varam ekaṃ prayacchati  Hbhv dhatrphalaṃ ca bhoktavyaṃ kadācit karasampuṭāt yaśaḥ śriyam avāpnoti prasādāc cakrapāñinaḥ  Hbhv dhātrphalaṃ ca tulas mṛttikā dvārakodbhavā saphalaṃ jvitaṃ tasya tritayaṃ yasya veśmani  Hbhv dhātrphalais tu saṃmiśraṃ tulasdalavāsitam pibate vahate yas tu trthakoṭiphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv yasmin gṛhe bhavet toyaṃ tulasdalavāsitam dhātrphalaiś ca viprendra gāgeyaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  Hbhv tulasdalanaivedyaṃ dhātryā yasya phalaṃ gṛhe kavacaṃ vaiṣñavaṃ tasya sarvapāpavināśanam  Hbhv brahmapurāñe cadhātrphalāni tulas hy antakāle bhaved yadi mukhe caiva śirasy age pātakaṃ nāsti tasya vai  Hbhv kṛtvā tu bhagavatpūjāṃ na trthaṃ snānam ācaret na ca devālayopetāspṛśyasaṃsparśanādinā  Hbhv atha snānaviśeṣakalaḥsmṛtyarthasārena snāyād utsave trthe māgalyaṃ vinivartya ca anuvrajya suhṛdbandhūn arcayitveṣṭadevatām  Hbhv viṣñusmṛtau caviṣñvālayasampasthān viṣñusevārtham āgatān cāñḍālān śaktyā kuryād vipro viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv yad uktamśrutismṛt ubhe netre viprāñaṃ parikrtite ekena vikalaḥ kāño dvābhyām andhaḥ prakrtitaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca kaurme vyasagtāyāmyo nyatra kurute yatnaṃ anādhtya syāt pramṛtaṃ karṣañaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv satyānṛtaṃ tu vāñijyaṃ śvavṛttir ncasevanam  Hbhv ātmano ncalokānāṃ sevanaṃ vṛttisiddhaye nitarāṃ nindyate sadbhir vaiṣñavasya viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv tad uktaṃsevā śvavṛttir yair uktā na samyak tair udāhṛtam svacchandacaritaḥ kva śvā vikrtāsuḥ kva sevakaḥ  Hbhv pañkṛtyātmanaḥ prāñān ye vartante dvijādhamāḥ teṣāṃ durātmanām annaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyañaṃ caret  Hbhv gunānvitebhyo viprasya śuklaṃ tat trividhaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv yuddhopakārāl labdhaṃ ca dañḍāc ca vyavahārataḥ kṣatriyasya dhanaṃ śuklaṃ trividhaṃ parikrtitam  Hbhv kṛṣivāñijyagorakṣaḥ kṛtvā śuklaṃ tathā viśaḥ dvijaśuśrūṣayā labdhaṃ śuklaṃ śūdrasya krtitam  Hbhv kramāgataṃ prtidānaṃ prāptaṃ ca saha bhāryayā aviśeṣena sarveṣāṃ dhanaṃ śuklaṃ prakrtitam  Hbhv atha grāhyāgrāhyāñikaurme tatraivanādyāc chūdrasya vipro nnaṃ mohād vā yadi kāmataḥ na śūdrayoniṃ vrajati yas tu bhukte hy anāpadi  Hbhv duṣkṛtaṃ hi manuṣyasya sarvam anne pratiṣṭhitam yo yasyānnaṃ samaśnāti sa tasyāśnāti kilbiṣam  Hbhv ārdhikaḥ kulamitraś ca svagopālaś ca nāpitaḥ ete śūdreṣu bhojyānnā dattvā svalpapañaṃ budhaiḥ  Hbhv pāyasaṃ snehapakvaṃ yad gorasaṃ caiva śaktavaḥ piñyākaṃ caiva tailaṃ ca śūdrād grāhyaṃ tathaiva ca  Hbhv agirāḥgorasaṃ caiva śaktūṃś ca tailapiñyākam eva ca apūpān bhakṣayec chūdrāt yat kiñcit payasā kṛtam  Hbhv atrismṛtausvasutāyāś ca yo bhukte sa bhukte pṛthivmalam narendrabhavane bhuktvā viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ  Hbhv dāsanāpitagopāla kulamitrārdhasriñaḥ bhojyānnāḥ śūdravarge m tathātmavinivedakaḥ  Hbhv madhūdakaṃ phalaṃ mūlam edhāṃsyabhayadakṣiñā abhyudyatāni tv etāni grāhyāñy api nikṛṣṭataḥ  Hbhv khalakṣetragataṃ dhanyaṃ kūpavāpisu yaj jalam agrāhyād api tadgrāhyaṃ yac ca goṣṭhagataṃ payaḥ  Hbhv pānyaṃ pāyasaṃ bhakṣyaṃ ghṛtaṃ lavañam eva ca hastadattaṃ na gṛhñyāt tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣañaiḥ  Hbhv manusmṛtausamudraṃ saindhavaṃ caiva lavañe paramādbhute pratyakṣe api tu grāhye niṣedhas tv anyagocaraḥ  Hbhv āyasenaiva pātreña yad annam upanyate bhoktā tad viṭsamaṃ bhukte dātā ca narakaṃ vrajet  Hbhv gorakṣakān vāñijakān tathā kārukaślinaḥ proṣyān vārdhūṣikāṃś caiva viprān śūdravad ācaret  Hbhv kaurme ca tatraivatṛñaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ prakāśaṃ vai harer budhaḥ dharmārthaṃ kevalaṃ vipra hy anyathā patito bhavet  Hbhv tilamudgayavādnāṃ muṣṭir grāhyā pathi sthitaiḥ kṣudhārthair nānyathā vipra dharmavidbhir iti sthitiḥ  Hbhv vaiṣñavānāṃ hi bhoktavyaṃ prārthyānnaṃ vaiṣñavaiḥ sadā avaiṣñavānām annaṃ tu parivarjyam amedhyavat  Hbhv tathā ca pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvādeprārthayed vaiṣñavād annaṃ prayatnena vicakṣañaḥ sarvapāpaviśudhyarthaṃ tadabhāve jalaṃ pibet  Hbhv nāradiyemahāpātakasaṃyukto vrajed vaiṣñavamandiram yācayed annam amṛtaṃ tadabhāve jalaṃ pibet  Hbhv viṣñusmṛtauśrotriyānnaṃ vaiṣñavānnaṃ hutaśeṣaṃ ca yaddhaviḥ ānakhāt śodhayet pāpaṃ tuṣāgniḥ kanakaṃ yathā  Hbhv skānde mārkañḍeyabhagrathasaṃvādeśuddhaṃ bhāgavatasyānnaṃ śuddhaṃ bhagrathijalam śuddhaṃ viṣñuparaṃ cittaṃ śuddham ekādaśvratam  Hbhv avaiṣñavagṛhe bhuktvā ptvā vā jānato pi vā śuddhiś cāndrāyañe prokta iṣṭāpūrtaṃ vṛthā sadā  Hbhv śrprahlādavākye cakeśavārcā gṛhe yasya na tiṣṭhati mahpate tasyānnaṃ naiva bhoktavyam abhakṣyeña samaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv kecid vṛttyanapekṣasya japaśraddhāvataḥ prabho viśvastasyādiśanty asmin kāle pi kṛtino japam  Hbhv atha madhyāhnikakṛtyānimadhyāhne snānataḥ pūrvaṃ puṣpādy āhṛtya vā svayam bhṛtyādinā vā sampādya kuryān madhyāhnikḥ kriyāḥ  Hbhv snānāśaktau ca madhyāhne snānam ācārya māntrikam yathoktaṃ bhagavatpūjāṃ śaktaś cet prāgvad ācaret  Hbhv atha vaiṣñavavaisvadevadividhiḥtataḥ kṛṣñārpitenaiva śuddhenānena vaiṣñavaḥ vaiśvadevādikaṃ daivaṃ karma paitraṃ ca sādhayet  Hbhv tad uktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe dinavibhāge tu kuryāt pañca mahāmakhān daivo homena yajñaḥ syāt bhautas tu balidānatah  Hbhv paitro viprānnadānena paitreña balināthavā kiñcid annapradānād vā tarpañād vā caturvidhaḥ  Hbhv nṛyajño tithisatkārāt hantakāreña cāmbunā brahmayajño vedajapāt purāñapaṭhanena vā  Hbhv tannityatākaurmeakṛtvā tu dvijaḥ pañca mahāyajñān dvijottamaḥ bhuñjta cet sumūḍhātmā tiryagyoniṃ sa gacchati  Hbhv atha vaiṣñavaśrāddhavidhiḥprāpte śrāddhadine pi prāg annaṃ bhagavate rpayet taccheṣeñaiva kurvta śrāddhaṃ bhāgavato narah  Hbhv yac ca smṛtaugṛhāgniśiṣudevānāṃ yatnāṃ brahmācāriñām pitṛpāko na dātavyo yāvat piñḍān na nirvapet  Hbhv  iti dṛñ sāmānyavacanam viśeṣavacanavrajaih śrutismṛtipurāñādi varttibhir bādhyate dhruvam  Hbhv tathā ca pādmeviṣñor niveditānnena yaṣṭavyaṃ devatāntaram pitṛbhyaś cāpi tad deyam tad ānantyāya kalpate  Hbhv mokṣadharme nāradoktausātvataṃ vidhim āsthāya prāñ sūryamukhanisṛtam pūjāyām āsa deveśaṃ taccheṣeña pitāmahān  Hbhv brahmāñḍapurāñeyaḥ śrāddhakāle haribhuktaśeṣamdadāti bhaktyā pitṛdevatānām tenaiva piñḍāṃs tulasvimiśrānākalpakoṭiṃ pitaraḥ sutṛptāḥ  Hbhv skāndedevān pitn samuddiśya yad viṣñor viniveditam tān uddiśya tathā kuryāt pradānaṃ tasya caiva hi  Hbhv prayānti tṛptim atulāṃ sodakena tu tena vai mukundagātralagnena brāhmañānāṃ vilepanam  Hbhv candanena tu piñḍanam kartavyaṃ pitṛtṛptaye devānāṃ ca pitñāṃ ca jāyate tṛptirakṣayā  Hbhv evaṃ kṛte mahpala mā bhavet saṃśayaḥ kvacit  Hbhv tatraiva śrpurusottamakhañḍeannādyaṃ śrāddhakāle tu patitādyair nirkṣitam tulasdalamiśreña salilenābhiṣiñcayet  Hbhv tadannaṃ śuddhatām eti viṣñor naivedyamiśritam viṣñor naivedyaśeṣaṃ tu tasmād deyaṃ dvijātmanām piñḍe caiva viśeṣena pitñāṃ tṛptim icchatā  Hbhv tatraiva śrbrahmanāradasaṃvādepitn uddiśya yaiḥ pūjā keśavasya kṛtā naraih tyaktvā te nārakṃ pḍāṃ muktiṃ yānti mahāmune  Hbhv dhanyās te mānavā loke kalikāle viśeṣatah ye kurvanti harer nityaṃ pitrarthaṃ pūjanaṃ mune  Hbhv kiṃ dattair bahubhir piñḍair gayāśrāddhādibhir mune yair arcito harir bhaktyā pitrarthaṃ ca dine dine  Hbhv yam uddiśya hareḥ pūjā kriyate munipugava uddhṛtya narakāvāsāt taṃ nayet paramaṃ padam  Hbhv yo dadāti hareḥ sthānaṃ pitn uddiśya nārada kartavyaṃ hi pitñāṃ yat tat kṛtaṃ tena bho dvija  Hbhv śrutau caeka eva nārāyaña āstna brahmāneme dyāvāpṛthivyausarve devāḥsarve pitaraḥsarve manusyāḥ viṣñunā aśitam aśnanti viṣñunāghrātaṃ jighrantiviṣñunā ptaṃ pibantitasmād vidhvaṃso viṣñūpāhṛtaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ  Hbhv  iti ata evoktaṃ śrbhagavatā viṣñudharmeprāñebhyo juhuyād annaṃ manniveditam uttamam tṛpyanti sarvadā prāñā manniveditabhakṣañāt  Hbhv tasmāt sarvaprayatnena pradeyaṃ manniveditam mamāpi hṛdayasthasya pitñāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraivānyatrabhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca yat kiñcid anivedyāgrabhoktari na deyaṃ pitṛdevebhyaḥ prāyaścitt yato bhavet  Hbhv svargādau kathito devair agrabhug bhagavān hariḥ yajñabhāgabhujo devās tatas tena prakalpitāḥ  Hbhv skānde śrmārkañḍeyabhagrathasaṃvādeyas tu vidyāvinirmuktaṃ mūrkhaṃ matvā tu vaiṣñavam vedavidbhyo vadād vipraḥ śrāddhaṃ tad rākṣasaṃ bhavet  Hbhv sikthamātraṃ tu yad bhukte jalaṃ gañḍūṣamātrakam tadannaṃ meruñā tulyaṃ taj jalaṃ sāgaropamam  Hbhv brahmapurāñe śrbrahmavacanamśakhākitatanur vipro bhukte yasya ca veśmani tadannaṃ svayam aśnāti pitṛbhiḥ saha keśavaḥ  Hbhv smṛtiś casurābhāñḍasthapyūṣaṃ yathā naśyati tatkṣañāt cakrākarahitaṃ śrāddhaṃ tathā śātātapo bravt  Hbhv kiṃ ca śrviṣñurahasyeniveśayen naro mohād anyapaktau hareḥ priyam sa paten niraye ghore paktibhed narādhamaḥ  Hbhv atha śrbhagavadarpañe niṣiddhamniveditaṃ yad anyasmai tad ucchiṣṭaṃ hi kathyate ataḥ kathañcid api tan na śrbhagavaterpayet  Hbhv tathā caikādaśaskandhe śrbhagavaduktau BhP api dpāvalokaṃ me nopayuñjyān niveditam  Hbhv nāradyepitṛśeṣaṃ tu you dadyād dharaye paramātmane retodāḥ pitaras tasya bhavanti kleśabhāginaḥ  Hbhv śr viṣñudharmehariśeṣaṃ havir dadyāt pitñām akṣayaṃ bhavet na punaḥ pitṛśeṣaṃ tu harer brahmādisadguroḥ  Hbhv anyatra cadakṣādayaś ca pitaro bhṛtyā indrādayaḥ surāḥ atas tadbhaktaśeṣaṃ tu viṣñor naiva nivedayet  Hbhv  iti evam āvaśyakaṃ kṛtvā vaiṣñavebhyo vibhajya ca śrmanmahāprasādānnaṃ bhuñjta saha bandhubhiḥ  Hbhv tathā ca prahlādapañcarātresvabhāvasthaiḥ karmajaḍān vañcayan draviñādibhiḥ harer naivedyasambhārān vaiṣñavebhyaḥ samarpayet  Hbhv ataiva vaiṣñavatantreharer niveditaṃ kiñccin na dadyāt karhicid budhaḥ abhaktebhyaḥ saśalyebhyo yad davan niraye vrajet  Hbhv viṣñudharmottareavaiṣñave devadhṛtaṃ nirmālyaṃ na prayacchati naivedyaṃ vā mahābhāga tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv  iti kathañcid api nāśnyād akṛtvā kṛṣñapūjanam na cāsamarpya govinde kiñcid bhuñjta vaiṣñavaḥ  Hbhv atha pūjāvyatiriktabhojanadoṣāḥśrkūrmapurāñeanarcayitvā govindaṃ yair bhuktaṃ dharmavarjitaiḥ śvānaviṣṭhāsamaṃ cānnaṃ nraṃ ca surayā samam  Hbhv kiṃ cayo mohād athavālasyād akṛtvā devatārcanam bhukte sa yāti narakaṃ śūkareṣv iha jāyate  Hbhv viṣñudharmottareekakālaṃ dvikālaṃ vā trikālaṃ pūjayed dharim apūjya bhojanaṃ kurvan narakāñi vrajen naraḥ  Hbhv nāradye caprātar madhyandinaṃ sāyaṃ viṣñupūjā smṛtā budhaiḥ aśakto vistareñaiva prātaḥ sampūjya keśavam  Hbhv madhyāhne caiva sāyaṃ ca puṣpāñjalim api kṣipet madhyāhne vā vistareña saṃkṣepeñāthavā harim  Hbhv sambhojya bhojanaṃ kuryād anyathā narakaṃ vrajet  Hbhv athānarpitabhoganiṣedhaḥhāyaśrṣapañcarātrena tv evāpūjya bhuñjta bhagavantaṃ janārdanam na tat svayaṃ samaśnyāt yad viṣñau na nivedayet  Hbhv brahmāñḍapurāñe patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyam annapānādyam auṣadham anivedya ca bhuñjta yad āhārāya kalpitam  Hbhv anivedyaṃ tu bhuñjānaḥ prāyaścitt bhaven naraḥ tasmāt sarvaṃ nivedyaiva viṣñor bhuñjta sarvadā  Hbhv pādme gautamāmbarṣasaṃvādeambarṣa gṛhe pakvaṃ yad abhṣṭaṃ sadātmanaḥ anivedya harer bhuñjan saptakalpāni nārak  Hbhv tatraivottarakāñḍe śivomāsaṃvāde avaiṣñavānāṃ yac cānnaṃ patitānāṃ tathaiva ca anarpitaṃ tathā viṣñau śvamāṃsasadṛśaṃ bhavet  Hbhv viṣñusmṛtauanivedya tu yo bhukte haraye paramātmane majjanti pitaras tasya narake śāśvatḥ samāḥ  Hbhv ataiva gautmāmbarṣasaṃvādeambarṣa navaṃ vastraṃ phalam annaṃ rasādikam kṛtvā viṣñūpabhuktaṃ tu sadā sevyaṃ hi vaiṣñavaiḥ  Hbhv viṣñudharmāgnipurāñayoḥgandhānnavarabhakṣyāṃś ca srajo vāsāṃsi bhūṣañam dattvā tu devadevāya taccheṣāñy upabhuñjate  Hbhv gāruḍepādodakaṃ piben nityaṃ naivedyaṃ bhakṣayed dhareḥ śeṣāś ca mastake dhāryā iti vedānuśāsanam  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhaskandhe puṃsavanavrataprasage BhP udvāsya devaṃ sve dhāmni tan niveditam agrataḥ adyād ātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ sarvakāmārthasiddhaye  Hbhv aṣṭamaskandhe ca payovrataprasage BhP niveditaṃ tadbhaktāya dadyād bhuñjta vā svayam  Hbhv gautamyatantreśuklopacārasambhārair nityaśo harim arcayet nivedya kṛṣñāya vidhivad annaṃ bhuñjta tat svayam athavā sātvate dadyād yadi labhyate bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv śaratpradpe cabhaktakṣañakṣaño devaḥ smṛtiḥ sevā svaveśmani svabhojyasyārpañaṃ dānaṃ phalam indrādidurlabham  Hbhv atha naivedyabhakṣañavidhiḥdṛṣṭvā mahāprasādānnaṃ tat prā natvābhimantrayet sveṣṭanāmnā tato mūlamanunā vārasaptakam  Hbhv dharmarājādibhāgaṃ cāpāsya śrcarañāmṛtam tulasṃ cātra
