nikṣipya ślokān sakrtayed imān  Hbhv yasyocchiṣṭaṃ hi vāñchanti brahmādyā ṛṣayo malāḥ siddhādyāś ca hares tasya vayam ucchiṣṭabhojinaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ cayasya nāmnā vinaśyanti mahāpātakarāśayaḥ tasya śrkṛṣñadevasya vayam ucchiṣṭabhojinaḥ  Hbhv ucchiṣṭabhojinas tasya vayam adbhutakarmañaḥ yo bālyallayā tāṃs tān pūtanādn apātayat  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe BhP tvayopabhuktasraggandhavāso lakāracarcitāḥ ucchiṣṭabhojino dāsās tava māyāṃ jayemahi  Hbhv yato mṛtopastarañam asty uktvā yathāvidhi pañca prāñāhutḥ kṛtvā bhuñjta purataḥ prabhoḥ  Hbhv śrviṣñupurāñe ViP      aurvasagarasaṃvādepraśastaratnapāñis tu bhuñjta prayato gṛh  Hbhv puñyagandhau śastamālyadhār caiva nareśvara naikavastradharo thārdrapāñipādo mahpate  Hbhv viśuddhavadanaḥ prto bhuñjta na vidimukhaḥ prāmukhodamukho vāpi na caivānyamanā naraḥ  Hbhv dattvā tu bhaktaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ kṣudhitebhyas tathā gṛh praśastaśuddhapātre tu bhuñjtākupito dvijaḥ  Hbhv nāsandisaṃsthite pātre nādeśe ca nareśvara nākāle nātisakrñe dattvāgraṃ ca naro gnaye nāśeṣaṃ puruṣo śnyād anyatra jagatpate  Hbhv madhvambhudadhisarpibhyaḥ saktubhyaś ca vivekavān aśnyāt tanmayo bhūtvā pūrvaṃ tu madhuraṃ rasam  Hbhv lavañāmle tathā madhye kaṭutiktādikāṃs tataḥ prāg dravaṃ puruṣo śnyān madhye kaṭhināśanam  Hbhv ante punar dravāś tu balārogye na muñcati pañcagrāsaṃ mahāmaunaṃ prāñādyāpyāyanāya tat  Hbhv bhuktvā samyag athācamya prāmukhodamukho pi vā yathāvat punar ācāmet pāñ prakṣālya mūlataḥ  Hbhv svasthaḥ praśāntacittas tu kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ abhṣṭadevatānāṃ tu kurvta smarañaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv agastir agnir baḍavānalaś cabhuktaṃ mayānnaṃ jarayatv aśeṣam sukhaṃ ca me tatpariñāmasambhavaṃyacchantv arogo mama cāstu dehe  Hbhv viṣñuḥ samastendriyadehadehpradhānabhūto bhagavān yathaikaḥ satyena tenāttam aśeṣam annamārogyadaṃ me pariñāmam etu  Hbhv ity uccārya svahastena parimṛjya tathodaram anāyāsapradāyni kuryāt karmāñy atandritaḥ  Hbhv kaurme vyāsagtāyāmprāmukho nnāni bhuñjta sūryābhimukham eva vā āsnaḥ svāsane siddhe bhūmyāṃ pādau nidhāya ca  Hbhv āyuṣyaṃ prāmukho bhukte yaśasyaṃ dakṣiñāmukhaḥ śriyaṃ pratyamukho bhukte ṛtaṃ bhukte udamukhaḥ  Hbhv pañcārdro bhojanaṃ kuryād bhūmau pātraṃ nidhāya ca upavāsena tat tulyaṃ manur āha prajāpatiḥ  Hbhv upalipte śucau deśe pādau prakṣālya vai karau ācamyārdrānano krodhaḥ pañcārdro bhojanaṃ caret  Hbhv mahāvyāhṛtibhis tv annaṃ parivāryodakena tu amṛtopastarañam astyapośānakriyāṃ caret  Hbhv svāhāprañavasaṃyuktāṃ prāñāyety āhutiṃ tataḥ apānāya tato hutvā vyānāya tadanantaram  Hbhv udānāya tataḥ kuryāt samānāyeti pañcamm vijñāya tattvam eteṣāṃ juhuyād ātmani dvijāḥ  Hbhv śeṣam annaṃ yathākāmaṃ bhuñjta vyañjanair yutam dhyātvā tanmanasā devam ātmānaṃ vai prajāpatim  Hbhv amṛtāpidhānam asty upariṣṭād apaḥ pibet  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraivayad bhukte veṣṭitaśirā yac ca bhukte vidimukhaḥ sopānatkaś ca yad bhukte sarvaṃ vidyāt tad āsuram  Hbhv nārdharātre na madhyāhne nājrñaṃ nārdravastradhṛk na ca bhinnāsanagato na yāne saṃsthito pi vā  Hbhv na bhinnabhājane caiva na bhūmyāṃ na ca pāñiṣu anārogyam anāyuṣyam asvargyaṃ cātibhojanam apuñyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet  Hbhv kiṃ cana vāmahastenoddhṛtya pibed vaktreña vā jalam  Hbhv viṣñusmṛtaupibataḥ patate toyaṃ bhājane mukhanirgayam abhojyaṃ tad bhaved annaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyañaṃ caret  Hbhv mārkañḍeyebhuñjtānnaṃ ca taccitto hy antarjāsu sadā naraḥ upaghātād ṛte doṣānnānnasyodrayed budhaḥ  Hbhv anyatra cahastādṛtembunānyenān aśnan pātrād ṛte pibet dakṣiñaṃ tu parityajya vāme nraṃ nighāpayet abhojyaṃ tad bhaved annaṃ pānyaṃ ca surāsamam  Hbhv tṛpto dadyād dhi tadannaṃ śeṣaṃ durgatatṛptaye  Hbhv samyag ācamya dakṣāghrer aguṣṭhe vāri nikṣipet  Hbhv tataḥ saṃsmṛtya santuṣṭaḥ puṣṭidām iṣṭadevatām sannikṛṣṭair vṛtaḥ śiṣṭair japed annapater manūn annapatennasya no dehi  Hbhv  ity ādi bhakṣayed atha tāmbūlaṃ prasādaṃ vallavprabhoḥ śiṣṭair iṣṭair japed divyaṃ bhagavan nāmamagalam  Hbhv atha naivedyamāhātmyamvārāheyo mamaivārcanaṃ kṛtvā tatra prāpañam uttamam śeṣam annaṃ śam aśnāti tataḥ saukhyataraṃ nu kim  Hbhv skāndetavopahāraṃ bhuktvā yaḥ sevate yajñapūruṣam sevitaṃ tena niyataṃ puroḍāśo mahādhiyā  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraivaśakhodakaṃ trthavarād variṣṭhaṃpādodakaṃ trthagañād gariṣṭham naivedyaśeṣaṃ kratukoṭipuñyaṃnirmālyaśeṣaṃ vratadānatulyam  Hbhv naivedyaśeṣaṃ tulasvimiśraṃviśeṣataḥ pādajalena siktam yo śnāti nityaṃ purato murāreḥprāpnoti yajñāyutakoṭipuñyam  Hbhv ṣaḍbhir māsopavāsais tu yat phalaṃ parikrtitam viṣñor naivedyaśeṣe yat phalaṃ tad bhuñjatāṃ kalau  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatra śrśālagrāmaśilāmāhātmyebhaktyā bhunakti naivedyaṃ śālagrāmaśilārpitam koṭiṃ makhasya labhate phalaṃ śatasahasraśaḥ  Hbhv brahmavārigṛhasthaiś ca vānaprasthaiś ca bhikṣubhiḥ bhoktavyaṃ viṣñunaivedyaṃ nātra kāryā vicārañā  Hbhv bhuktvānyadevanaivedyaṃ dvijaś cāndrāyañaṃ caret bhuktvā keśavanaivedyaṃ yajñakoṭiphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv tatraiva śrbrahmanāradasaṃvādeagniṣṭomasahasrais tu vājapeyaśatair api tat phalaṃ prāpyate nūnaṃ viṣñor naivedyabhakṣañāt  Hbhv hṛdi rūpaṃ mukhe nāma naivedyam udare hareḥ pādodakaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ mastake yasya so cyutaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ capāvanaṃ viṣñunaivedyaṃ surasiddharṣibhiḥ smṛtam anyadevasya naivedyaṃ bhuvattvācāndrāyañaṃ caret  Hbhv koṭiyajñais tu yat puñyaṃ māsopoṣañakoṭibhiḥ tat phalaṃ prāpyate pumbhir viṣñor naivedyabhakṣañāt  Hbhv tulasyāś ca rajojuṣṭaṃ naivedyasya ca bhakṣañam nirmālyaṃ ca dhṛtaṃ yena mahāpātakanāśanam  Hbhv bṛhadviṣñupurāñe naivedyaṃ jagadśasya annapānādikaṃ ca yat brahmavan nirvikāraṃ hi yathā viṣñus tathaiva tat  Hbhv vikāraṃ ye prakurvanti bhakṣañe tad dvijātayaḥ  Hbhv kuṣṭhavyādhisamāyuktāḥ putradāravivarjitāḥ nirayaṃ yānti te viprā yasmān nāvartate punaḥ  Hbhv viṣñudharmottarenavam annaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ nivedya madhusūdane paścād bhukte svayaṃ yaś ca tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv brahmāñḍapurāñemukundāśanaśeṣaṃ tu yo hi bhukte dine dine sikthe sikthe bhavet puñyaṃ cāndrāyañaśatādhikam  Hbhv anyatrāpiekādaśsahasrais tu māsopoṣañakoṭibhiḥ tat phalaṃ prāpyate pumbhir viṣñor naivedyabhakṣañāt  Hbhv  iti tato yathoktam ācamya tāmbūlādi vibhajya ca mahāprasādaṃ dāsyena gṛhñyāt prayataḥ svayam  Hbhv tathā ca navamaskandhe śrmadambarṣacarite BhP kāmaṃ ca dāsye na tu kāmakāmyayāyathottamaślokajanāśrayā ratiḥ  Hbhv naivedyabhakṣañe yac ca nirmālyagrahañe ca yat māhātmyam ādau likhitaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvam ihāpi tat  Hbhv iti śrgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrbhagavadbhaktivilāsemahāprasādo nāma navamo vilāsaḥ   SatsamgamaVilasadaśamavilāsaḥśrīkṛṣṇacaraṇāmbhojamadhupebhyo namo namaḥ kathañcid āśrayād yeṣāṃ śvāpi tadgandhabhāg bhavet  Hbhv atha śrīkṛṣṇabhaktānāṃ sabhāṃ savinayaṃ śubhām gacched vaiṣṇavacihnāḍhyaḥ pātuṃ kṛṣṇakathāsudhām  Hbhv tathā ca smṛtiḥ itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhasaptamakau nayet  Hbhv atha śrībhagavadbhaktānāṃ lakṣaṇāni sāmānyataḥ laiṅge viṣṇur eva hi yasyaiṣa devatā vaiṣṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv atra viśeṣaḥ vratakarmaguṇajñānabhogajanmādimatsv api śaiveṣv api ca kṛṣṇasya bhaktāḥ santi tathā tathā  Hbhv atra vratiṣu madhye bhagavadbhaktihetuvrataparatā bhagavadbhaktalakṣaṇamtathā skānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktaṃ dinaṃ vaiṣṇavavallabham nopāsate mahīpāla te vai bhāgavatā narāḥ  Hbhv prāṇātyaye na cāśnanti dinaṃ prāpya harer narāḥ kurvanti jāgaraṃ rātrau sadā bhāgavatā hi te  Hbhv upoṣya dvādaśīṃ śuddhāṃ rātrau jāgaraṇānvitām alpāṃ tu sādhayed yas tu sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv bhaktir na vicyutā yeṣāṃ na cyutāni vratāni ca supriyaḥ śrīpatir yeṣāṃ te syur bhāgavatā narāḥ  Hbhv karmiṣu bhagavadarpaṇādinā tadājñābuddhyā vā bhaktihetuḥ sadācāraparatā dharmārthaṃ jīvitaṃ yeṣāṃ santānārthaṃ ca maithunam pacanaṃ vipramukhyārthaṃ jñeyās te vaiṣṇavā narāḥ  Hbhv adhvagaṃ tu pathi śrāntaṃ kāletra gṛham āgatam yo tithiṃ pūjayed bhaktyā vaiṣṇavaḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv sadācāraratāḥ śiṣṭāḥ sarvabhūtānukampakāḥ śucayas tyaktarāgā ye sadā bhāgavatā hi te  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde  jīvitaṃ yasya dharmārthaṃ dharmo haryartham eva ca ahorātrāṇi puṇyārthaṃ taṃ manye vaiṣṇavaṃ bhuvi  Hbhv laiṅge ca viṣṇubhaktisamāyuktān śrautasmārtapravartakān prīto bhavati yo dṛṣṭvā vaiṣṇavo sau prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv guṇavatsu bhaktihetuḥ kṛpālutvādisadguṇaśīlatā skānde tatraiva paraduḥkhenātmaduḥkhaṃ manyante ye nṛpottama bhagavaddharmaniratās te narā vaiṣṇavā nṛpa  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde  titikṣavaḥ kāruṇikāḥ suhṛdaḥ sarvadehinām ajātaśatravaḥ śāntāḥ sādhavaḥ sādhubhūṣaṇāḥ  Hbhv pañcamaskandhe ṛṣabhadevasya putrānuśāsane y mahatsevāṃ dvāram āhur vimuktestamodvāraṃ yoṣitāṃ saṅgisaṅgam mahāntas te samacittāḥ praśāntāvimanyavaḥ suhṛdaḥ sādhavo ye  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe bhagavatpradattoddhavapraśnottare  kṛpālur akṛtadrohas titikṣuḥ sarvadehinām satyasāro navadyātmā samaḥ sarvopakārakaḥ  Hbhv kāmair ahatadhīr dānto mṛduḥ śucir akiñcanaḥ anīho mitabhuk śāntaḥ sthiro maccharaṇo muniḥ  Hbhv apramatto gabhīrātmā dhṛtimāñ jitaṣaḍguṇaḥ amānī mānadaḥ kalyo maitraḥ kāruṇikaḥ kaviḥ  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe yamatadbhaṭasaṃvāde ViP  na calati nijavarṇadharmato yaḥsamamatir ātmasuhṛdvipakṣapakṣe na harati na hanti kiñcid uccaiḥsthitamanasaṃ tam avehi viṣṇubhaktam  Hbhv jñāniṣu bhaktihetur jñānavattā ekādaśe haviyogeśvarottare BhP  sarvabhūteṣu yaḥ paśyed bhagavadbhāvam ātmanaḥ bhūtāni bhagavaty ātmany eṣa bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv na yasya svaḥ para iti vitteṣv ātmani vā bhidā sarvabhūtasamaḥ śāntaḥ sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe śrībhagavaduktau BhP  jñātvājñātvātha ye vai māṃ yāvān yaś cāsmi yādṛśaḥ bhajanty ananyabhāvena te me bhaktatamā matāḥ  Hbhv tatraiva haviyogeśvarottare BhP īśvare tadadhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca premamaitrīkṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ  Hbhv arcāyām eva haraye pūjāṃ yaḥ śraddhayehate na tadbhakteṣu cānyeṣu sa bhaktaḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv bhogavatsu bhaktihetur bhogānāsaktatā haviyogeśvarottare BhP gṛhītvāpīndriyair arthān yo na dveṣṭi na hṛṣyati viṣṇor māyām idaṃ paśyan sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv sajjanmavidyādimatsu bhaktihetur nirabhimānitā  tatraiva BhP  na yasya janmakarmabhyāṃ na varṇāśramajātibhiḥ sajjate sminn ahambhāvo dehe vai sa hareḥ priyaḥ  Hbhv bhāvāḥ kathañcid bhaktaiva jñānānāsaktyamānitā bhaktiniṣṭhāpakā jātās tato hy uttamatoditā  Hbhv śaiveṣu śrīśivakṛṣṇabhedakāḥ bṛhannāradīye NārP  śive ca parameśāne viṣṇau ca paramātmani samabuddhyā pravarttante te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv anyac ca teṣāṃ bhagavacchāstrārthaparatādikam sākṣādbhaktyātmakaṃ mukhyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ likhyatedhunā  Hbhv skānde yeṣāṃ bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ sadā tiṣṭhati sannidhau pūjayanti ca ye nityaṃ te syur bhāgavatā narāḥ  Hbhv yeṣāṃ bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ jīvitād adhikaṃ bhavet mahābhāgavatāḥ śreṣṭhā viṣṇunā kathitā narāḥ  Hbhv vaiṣṇavasammānaniṣṭhā  laiṅge viṣṇubhaktam athāyātaṃ yo dṛṣṭvā sumukhaḥ priyaḥ praṇāmādi karoty eva vāsudeve yathā tathā sa vai bhakta iti jñeyaḥ sa punāti jagat trayam  Hbhv rukṣākṣarā giraḥ śṛṇvan tathā bhāgavateritāḥ praṇāmapūrvakaṃ kṣāntvā yo vaded vaiṣṇavo hi saḥ  Hbhv bhojanācchādanaṃ sarvaṃ yathāśaktyā karoti yaḥ viṣṇubhaktasya satataṃ sa vai bhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv gāruḍe yena sarvātmanā viṣṇubhaktyā bhāvo niveśitaḥ vaiṣṇaveṣu kṛtātmatvān mahābhāgavato hi saḥ  Hbhv śrītulasīsevāniṣṭhā NārP  tulasīkānanaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye namaskurvate narāḥ tatkāṣṭhāṅkitakarṇā ye te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv tulasīgandham āghrāya santoṣaṃ kurvate tu ye tanmūlam ṛddhūtā yaiś ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv śrībhagavataḥ kathāparatābṛhannāradīye  śrībhagavanmārkaṇḍeyasaṃvāde matkathāśravaṇe yeṣāṃ vartate sāttvikī matiḥ tadbhaktaviṣṇubhaktāś ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv skānde śrībhagavadarjunasaṃvāde matkathāṃ kurute yas tu matkathāṃ ca śṛṇoti yaḥ hṛṣyate matkathāyāṃ ca sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  tatraiva madāśrayāḥ kathā mṛṣṭāḥ śṛṇvanti kathayanti ca tapanti vividhās tāpā naitān madgatacetasaḥ  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye  tatraiva manmānasāś ca madbhaktā madbhaktajanalolupāḥ mannāmaśravaṇāsaktās te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv yebhinandanti nāmāni hareḥ śrutvātiharṣitāḥ romāñcitaśarīrāśca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv tatraivānyatra  anyeṣām udayaṃ dṛṣṭvā yebhinandanti mānavāḥ harināmaparā ye ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv smaraṇaparatā tatra svadharmaniṣṭhayā rāgadveṣanivṛttyā smaraṇamśrīviṣṇupurāṇe yamatadbhaṭasaṃvāde ViP  na calati ya uccaiḥ śrībhagavatpadāravinde sitamanās tam avehi viṣṇubhaktam  Hbhv kalikaluṣamalena yasya nātmāvimalamater malinīkṛtas tam enam manasi kṛtajanārdanaṃ manuṣyaṃsatatam avehi harer atīvabhaktam  Hbhv kanakam api rahasy avekṣya buddhyātṛṇam iva yaḥ samavaiti parasvam bhavati ca bhagavaty ananyacetāḥpuruṣavaraṃ tam avehi viṣṇubhaktam  Hbhv sphaṭikagiriśilāmalaḥ kva viṣṇurmanasi nṝṇāṃ kva ca matsarādidoṣaḥ na hi tuhinamayūkharaśmipuñjebhavati hutāśanadīptijaḥ pratāpaḥ  Hbhv vimalamatir amatsaraḥ praśāntaḥśucicarito khilasattvamitrabhūtaḥ priyahitavacano stumānamāyovasati sadā hṛdi tasya vāsudevaḥ  Hbhv vasati hṛdi sanātane ca tasminbhavati pumān jagato sya saukhyarūpaḥ kṣitirasam atiramyam ātmano ntaḥkathayati cārutayaiva śālapotaḥ  Hbhv anyavijaye vairāgyādinā ca smaraṇamekādaśaskandhe haviyogeśvarottare BhP  dehendriyaprāṇamanodhiyāṃ yojanmāpyayakṣudbhayatarṣakṛcchraiḥ saṃsāradharmair avimuhyamānaḥsmṛtyā harer bhāgavatapradhānaḥ  Hbhv tribhuvanavibhavahetave py akuṇṭhasmṛtir ajitātmasurādibhir vimṛgyāt na calati bhagavatpadāravindāllavanimiṣārdham api yaḥ sa vaiṣṇavāgryaḥ  Hbhv bhagavata uruvikramāṅghriśākhānakhamaṇicandrikayā nirastatāpe hṛdi katham upasīdatāṃ punaḥ saprabhavati candra ivodite rkatāpaḥ  Hbhv skānde tatraiva yercayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ yajñeśaṃ varadaṃ harim dehinaḥ puṇyakarmāṇaḥ sadā bhāgavatā hi te  Hbhv laiṅge viṣṇukṣetre śubhāny eva karoti snehasaṃyutaḥ pratimāṃ ca harer nityaṃ pūjayet pratayāmavān  Hbhv viṣṇubhaktaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ karmaṇā manasā girā nārāyaṇaparo nityaṃ bhūpa bhāgavato hi saḥ  Hbhv atha vaiṣṇavadharmaniṣṭhādipādmottarakhaṇḍe tāpādipañcasaṃskārī navejyākarmakārakaḥ arthapañcakavid vipro mahābhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv ekāntikatāgāruḍe ekāntena sadā viṣṇau yasmād deve parāyaṇāḥ tasmād ekāntinaḥ proktās tadbhāgavatacetasaḥ  Hbhv tadvijñānenānanyaparatāekādaśe BhP  uddhavapraśnottare jñātvājñātvātha ye vai mām yāvān yaś cāsmi yādṛśaḥ bhajanty ananyabhāvena te vai bhāgavatā matāḥ  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe BhP  na kāmakarmabījānāṃ yasya cetasi sambhavaḥ vāsudevaikanilayaḥ sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv sā ca ekāntitā caturdhātatra dharmānādareṇa śrīmaduddhavapraśnottara eva BhP  ājñāyaivaṃ guṇān doṣān mayādiṣṭān api svakān dharmān santyajya yaḥ sarvān māṃ bhajeta sa tu sattamaḥ  Hbhv śrībhagavadgītāyām Gītā  sarvadharmān parityajya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ  Hbhv caturthaskandhe BhP  yadā yasyānugṛhṇāti bhagavān atmabhāvitaḥ na jahāti matiṃ loke vede ca pariniṣṭhitām  Hbhv anyasarvanirapekṣatāśrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  ailopākhyāne santo napekṣā maccittāḥ praśāntāḥ samadarśinaḥ nirmamā nirahaṅkārā nirdvandvā niṣparigrahāḥ  Hbhv ataeva śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde  ta ete sādhavaḥ sādhvi sarvasaṅgavivarjitāḥ saṅgas teṣv atha te prārthyaḥ saṅgadoṣaharā hi te  Hbhv vighnākulatvepi manoratiparatā skānde tatraiva yasya kṛcchragatasyāpi keśave ramate manaḥ na vicyutā ca bhaktir vai sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv āpadgatasya yasyeha bhakir avyabhicāriṇī nānyatra ramate cittaṃ sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv premaikarasatā śrīṛṣabhadevasya putrānuśāsane BhP  ye vā mayīśe kṛtasauhṛdārthājaneṣu dehambharavārtikeṣu gṛheṣu jāyātmajarātimatsuna prītiyuktā yāvadarthāś ca loke  Hbhv tridhā premaikaparatā premṇaḥ syāt tāratamyataḥ uttamā madhyamā cāsau kaniṣṭhā ceti bhedataḥ  Hbhv tatrottamā yathā ekādaśe haviyogeśvarottare BhP  sarvabhūteṣu yaḥ paśyed bhagavadbhāvam ātmanaḥ bhūtāni bhagavaty ātmany eṣa bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv sveṣṭadevasya bhāvaṃ yaḥ sarvabhūteṣu paśyati bhāvayanti ca tāny asminn ity arthaḥ sammataḥ satām  Hbhv śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde  mayy ananyena bhāvena bhaktiṃ kurvanti ye dṛḍhām matkṛte tyaktakarmāṇas tyaktasvajanabāndhavāḥ  Hbhv śrīhaviyogeśvarottare BhP  visṛjati hṛdayaṃ na yasya sākṣāddharir avaśābhihito py aghaughanāśaḥ praṇayarasanayā dhṛtāṅghripadmaḥsa bhavati bhāgavatapradhāna uktaḥ  Hbhv tatra madhyamā śrīhaviyogeśvarottare BhP  īśvare tadadhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca premamaitrīkṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ  Hbhv tatra kaniṣṭhā tatraiva BhP  arcāyām eva haraye pūjāṃ yaḥ śraddhayehate na tadbhakteṣu cānyeṣu sa bhaktaḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv śraddhayā pūjanaṃ premabodhakaṃ bhakta ity api lakṣaṇāni ca yāny agre bhakter lekhyāni tāny api  Hbhv vandanādīni vidyante yeṣu bhāgavatā hi te etāni lakṣaṇānītthaṃ gauṇamukhyādibhedataḥ  Hbhv ūhyāni lakṣaṇāny evaṃ vivecyāni parāṇy api  Hbhv īdṛglakṣaṇavantaḥ syur durlabhā bahavo janāḥ divyā hi maṇayo vyaktaṃ na varterann itas tataḥ  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ mokṣadharme nārāyaṇīye Mbh  jāyamānaṃ hi puruṣaṃ yaṃ paśyen madhusūdanaḥ sāttvikas tu sa vijñeyo bhaven mokṣe ca niścitaḥ  Hbhv evaṃ saṅkṣipya likhitād vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu lakṣaṇāt māhātmyam api vijñeyaṃ likhyatenyac ca tat kiyat  Hbhv atha bhagavadbhaktānāṃ māhātmyam sauparṇe śrīśakroktau kalau bhāgavataṃ nāma yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate jananī putriṇī tena pitṝṇāṃ tu dhurandharaḥ  Hbhv kalau bhāgavataṃ nāma durlabhaṃ naiva labhyate brahmarudrapadotkṛṣṭaṃ guruṇā kathitaṃ mama  Hbhv yasya bhāgavataṃ cihnaṃ dṛśyate tu harir mune gīyate ca kalau devā jñeyās te nāsti saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv śrīmārkaṇḍeyoktau samīpe tiṣṭhate yasya ha antakālepi vaiṣṇavaḥ gacchate paramaṃ sthānaṃ yadyapi brahmahā bhavet  Hbhv nāradīye śrīvāmadevarukmāṅgadasaṃvāde NārP  śvapaco pi mahīpāla viṣṇubhakto dvijādhikaḥ viṣṇubhaktivihīnas tu dvijo pi śvapacādhikaḥ  Hbhv skānde revākhaṇḍe śrībrahmoktau indro maheśvaro brahmā paraṃ brahma tadaiva hi śvapaco pi bhavaty eva yadā tuṣṭāsi keśava  Hbhv śvapacād api kaṣṭatvaṃ brahmeśānādayaḥ surāḥ tadaivācyuta yānty ete yadaiva tvaṃ parāṅmukhaḥ  Hbhv sa kartā sarvadharmāṇāṃ bhakto yas tava keśava sa kartā sarvapāpānāṃ yo na bhaktas tavācyuta  Hbhv dharmo bhavaty adharmo pi kṛto bhaktais tavācyuta pāpaṃ bhavati dharmo pi tavābhaktaiḥ kṛto hareḥ  Hbhv niḥśeṣadharmakartā vāpy abhakto narake hare sadā tiṣṭhati bhaktas te brahmahāpi viśudhyati  Hbhv niścalā tvayi bhaktir yā saiva muktir janārdana muktā eva hi bhaktās te tava viṣṇo yato hare  Hbhv tatraiva durvāsonāradasaṃvāde nūnaṃ bhāgavatā loke lokarakṣāviśāradāḥ vrajanti viṣṇunādiṣṭā hṛdisthena mahāmune  Hbhv bhagavān eva sarvatra bhūtānāṃ kṛpayā hariḥ rakṣaṇāya caran lokān bhaktarūpeṇa nārada  Hbhv tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde yas tu viṣṇuparo nityaṃ dṛḍhabhaktir jitendriyaḥ svagṛhepi vasan yāti tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv aśvamedhasahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ yaḥ karoti vai nāsau tatphalam āpnoti tadbhaktair yad avāpyate  Hbhv tatraivāmṛtasāroddhāre śrīyamatadbhaṭasaṃvāde sarvatra vaiṣṇavāḥ pūjyāḥ svarge martye rasātale devatānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tathaivoragarakṣasām  Hbhv yeṣāṃ smaraṇamātreṇa pāpalakṣaśatāni ca dahyante nātra sandeho vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv yeṣāṃ pādarajenaiva prāpyate jāhnavījalam nārmadaṃ yāmunaṃ caiva kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam  Hbhv yeṣāṃ vākyajalaughena vinā gaṅgājalair api vinā tīrthasahasreṇa snāto bhavati mānavaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva cāturmāsyamāhātmye tāvad bhramanti saṃsāre pitaraḥ piṇḍatatparaḥ yāvat kule bhaktiyuktaḥ suto naiva prajāyate  Hbhv sa eva jñānavān loke yogināṃ prathamo hi saḥ mahākratūnām āhartā haribhaktiyuto hi yaḥ  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍe dhruvacarite na cyavante hi yadbhaktyā mahatyāṃ pralayāpadi ato cyuto khile loke sa ekaḥ sarvago vyayaḥ  Hbhv na tasmād bhagavadbhaktād bhetavyaṃ kenacit kvacit niyataṃ viṣṇubhaktā yena te syuḥ paratāpinaḥ  Hbhv tatraivāgre brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā yadi vetaraḥ viṣṇubhaktisamāyukto jñeyaḥ sarvottamottamaḥ  Hbhv śaṅkhacakrāṅkitatanuḥ śirasā mañjarīdharaḥ gopīcandanaliptāṅgo dṛṣṭaś ced tadaghaṃ kutaḥ  Hbhv mahābhārate rājadharmeīśvaraṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam bhaktā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ durgāṇy atitaranti te  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottareśayanād utthito yas tu kīrtayen madhusūdanam kīrtanāt tasya pāpāni nāśam āyānty aśeṣataḥ  Hbhv tatraivayasyāpy anante jagatām adhīśebhaktiḥ parā yādavadevadeve tasmāt paraṃ nāparam asti kiñcitpātraṃ triloke puruṣapravīra  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye śrīprahlādabalisaṃvādenityaṃ ye prātar utthāya vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu kīrtanam kurvanti te bhāgavatāḥ kṛṣṇatulyāḥ kalau bale  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodayesvadarśanasparśanapūjanaiḥ kṛtītamāṃsi viṣṇupratimeva vaiṣṇavaḥ dhunvan vasaty atra janasya yan na tatsvārthaṃ paraṃ lokahitāya dīpavat  Hbhv itihāsasamuccaye śrīlomaśavākyeye bhajanti jagadyoniṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam na tebhyo vidyate tīrtham adhikaṃ rājasattama  Hbhv yatra bhāgavatāḥ snānaṃ kurvanti vimalāśrayāḥ tattīrtham adhikaṃ viddhi sarvapāpaviśodhanam  Hbhv yatra rāgādirahitā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ tatra sannihito viṣṇur nṛpate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv na gandhair na tathā toyair na puṣpaiś ca manoharaiḥ sānnidhyaṃ kurute devo yatra santi na vaiṣṇavāḥ  Hbhv balibhiś copavāsaiś ca nṛtyagītādibhis tathā nityam ārādhyamāno pi tatra viṣṇur na tṛpyati  Hbhv tasmād ete mahābhāgā vaiṣṇavā vītakalmaṣāḥ punanti sakalān lokāṃs tat tīrtham adhikaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv śūdraṃ vā bhagavadbhaktaṃ niṣādaṃ śvapacaṃ tathā vīkṣataṃ jātisāmānyāt sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv tasmād viṣṇuprasādāya vaiṣṇavān paritoṣayet prasādasumukho viṣṇus tenaiva syān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrīnāradapuṇḍarīkasaṃvāde ye nṛśaṃsā durātmānaḥ pāpācāraratāḥ sadā tepi yānti paraṃ dhāma nārāyaṇaparāśrayāḥ  Hbhv lipyante na ca pāpena vaiṣṇavā viṣṇutatparāḥ punanti sakalān lokān sahasrāṃśur ivoditaḥ  Hbhv janmāntarasahasreṣu yasya syād buddhir īdṛśī dāso haṃ vāsudevasya sarvān lokān samuddharet  Hbhv sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ punas tadgataprāṇāḥ puruṣāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ  Hbhv smṛtaḥ sambhāṣito vāpi pūjito vā dvijottamāḥ punāti bhagavadbhaktaś cāṇḍālo pi yadṛcchayā  Hbhv śrīvyāsavākye janmāntarasahasreṣu viṣṇubhakto na lipyate yasya sandarśanād eva bhasmībhavati pātakam  Hbhv itihāsasamuccaye śrībhagavadvākye na me priyaś caturvedī madbhaktaḥ śvapacaḥ priyaḥ tasmai deyaṃ tato grāhyaṃ sa ca pūjyo yathā hy aham  Hbhv tatraiva brahmavākye sabhartṛkā vā vidhavā viṣṇubhaktiṃ karoti yā samuddharati cātmānaṃ kulam ekottaraṃ śatam  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye prahlādabalisaṃvāde saṅkīrṇayonayaḥ pūtā ye bhaktā madhusūdane mlecchatulyāḥ kulīnās te ye na bhaktā janārdane  Hbhv ādipurāṇe śrīkṛṣṇārjunasaṃvāde vaiṣṇavān bhaja kaunteya mā bhajasvānyadevatāḥ punanti vaiṣṇavāḥ sarve sarvadevam idaṃ jagat madbhakto durlabho yasya sa eva mama durlabhaḥ  Hbhv tatparo durlabho nāsti satyaṃ satyaṃ dhanañjaya jagatāṃ guravo bhaktā bhaktānāṃ guravo vayam sarvatra guravo bhaktā vayaṃ ca guravo yathā asmākaṃ bāndhavā bhaktā bhaktānāṃ bāndhavā vayam  Hbhv asmākaṃ guravo bhaktā bhaktānāṃ guravo vayam madbhaktā yatra gacchanti tatra gacchāmi pārthiva bhaktānām anugacchanti muktayaḥ śrutibhiḥ saha  Hbhv ye me bhaktajanāḥ pārtha na me bhaktāś ca te janāḥ madbhaktānāṃ ca ye bhaktās te me bhaktatamā matāḥ  Hbhv ye kecit prāṇino bhaktā madarthe tyaktabāndhavāḥ teṣām ahaṃ parikrīto nānyakrīto dhanañjaya  Hbhv eṣāṃ bhakṣyaṃ sunirṇītaṃ śrūyatāṃ niścitaṃ mama ucchiṣṭam avaśiṣṭaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhojanadvayam  Hbhv nāmayuktajanāḥ kecij jātyantarasamanvitāḥ kurvanti me yathā prītiṃ na tathā vedapāragāḥ  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye mārkaṇḍeyaṃ prati śrībhagavaduktau  viṣṇur bhaktakuṭumbīti vadanti vibudhāḥ sadā tad eva pālayiṣyāmi majjano nānṛtaṃ vadet  Hbhv mama janma kule yasya tat kulaṃ mokṣagāmi vai mayi tuṣṭe muniśreṣṭha kim asādhyaṃ jagattraye  Hbhv mayi bhaktiparo yas tu madyājī matkathāparaḥ maddhyānī svakulaṃ sarvaṃ nayaty acyutarūpatām  Hbhv madarthaṃ karma kurvāṇo matpraṇāmaparo naraḥ manmanāḥ svakulaṃ sarvaṃ nayaty acyutarūpatām  Hbhv aham eva dvijaśreṣṭha nityaṃ pracchannavigrahaḥ bhagavadbhaktarūpeṇa lokān rakṣāmi sarvadā  Hbhv tatraivāditimāhātmye śrīsūtoktau viprāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ māhātmyaṃ haribhaktiratātmanām haridhyānaparāṇāṃ tu kaḥ samarthaḥ prabādhitum  Hbhv haribhaktiparo yatra tatra brahmā hariḥ śivaḥ tatra devāś ca siddhādyā nityaṃ tiṣṭhanti sattamāḥ  Hbhv nimiṣaṃ nimṣārdhaṃ vā yatra tiṣṭhanti sattamāḥ tatraiva sarvaśreyāṃsi tat tīrthaṃ tat tapovanam  Hbhv tatraivāditiṃ prati śrībhagavaduttare NārP rāgadveṣavihīnā ye madbhaktā matparāyaṇāḥ vadanti satataṃ te māṃ gatāsūyā adāmbhikāḥ  Hbhv paropatāpavimukhāḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ matkathāśravaṇāsaktā vahanti satataṃ hi mām  Hbhv tatraiva dhvajāropaṇamāhātmye śrīviṣṇudūtoktau NārP  yatīnāṃ viṣṇubhaktānāṃ paricaryāparāyaṇāḥ īkṣitā api gacchanti pāpino pi parāṃ gatim  Hbhv tatraiva śrībhagavattoṣaprakārapraśnottare NārP  ripavas taṃ na hiṃsanti na bādhante grahāś ca tam rākṣasāś ca na cekṣante naraṃ viṣṇuparāyaṇam  Hbhv bhaktir dṛḍhā bhaved yasya devadeve janārdane śreyāṃsi tasya sidhyanti bhaktimanto dhikās tataḥ  Hbhv tatraivāgre NārP  adyāpi ca muniśreṣṭha brahmādyā api devatāḥ prabhāvaṃ na vijānanti viṣṇubhaktiratātmanām  Hbhv kiṃ ca NārP  dharmārthakāmamokṣākhyāḥ puruṣārthā dvijottamāḥ haribhaktiparāṇāṃ vai sampadyante na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva lubdhakopākhyānasyādau NārP  ye viṣṇuniratāḥ śāntā lokānugrahatatparāḥ sarvabhūtadayāyuktā viṣṇurūpāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv viṣṇubhaktivihīnā ye caṇḍālāḥ parikīrtitāḥ caṇḍālā api vai śreṣṭhā haribhaktiparāyaṇāḥ  Hbhv tatraiva yajñadhvajopākhyānasyādau śrīsūtavākyam NārP  haribhaktirasāsvādamuditā ye narottamāḥ namaskaromy ahaṃ tebhyo yatsaṅgān muktibhāg naraḥ  Hbhv haribhaktiparā ye tu harināmaparāyaṇāḥ durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā tebhyo nityaṃ namo namaḥ  Hbhv aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ viṣṇubhaktiratātmanām yasmān muktiḥ karasthaiva yoginām api durlabhā  Hbhv tatraiva kaliprasaṅge NārP ghore kaliyuge prāpte sarvadharmavivarjite vāsudevaparā martyāḥ kṛtārthā nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv asty antar durlabhā proktā haribhaktiḥ kalau yuge haribhaktiratānāṃ vai pāpabandho na jāyate  Hbhv vedavādaratāḥ sarve tathā tīrthaniṣeviṇaḥ haribhaktirataiḥ sārdhaṃ kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ devais tatraiva bhāratavarṣaprasaṅge NārP  harikīrtanaśīlo vā tadbhaktānāṃ priyo pi vā śuśrūṣur vāpi mahatāṃ sa vandyo smābhir uttamaḥ  Hbhv pādme śrībhagavadbrahmasaṃvāde darśanadhyānasaṃsparśair martyakūrmavihaṅgamāḥ puṣṇanti svāny apatyāni tathāham api padmaja  Hbhv muhūrtenāpi saṃhartuṃ śaktau yadyapi dānavāt madbhaktānāṃ vinodārthaṃ karomi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ  Hbhv tatraiva māghamāhātmye devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde na vayaṃ yamaṃ yamalokaṃ na na dūtān ghoradarśanāt paśyanti vaiṣṇavā nūnaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam  Hbhv śvapākam iva nekṣeta loke vipram avaiṣṇavam vaiṣṇavo varṇabāhyo pi punāti bhuvanatrayam  Hbhv na śūdrā bhagavadbhaktās te tu bhāvanā matāḥ sarvavarṇeṣu te śūdrā ye na bhaktā janārdana  Hbhv viṣṇubhaktasya ye dāsā vaiṣṇavānnabhujaś ca ye tepi kratubhujāṃ gvaiśya gatiṃ yānti nirākulāḥ  Hbhv tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye pañcapuruṣāṇām uktau bhavyāni bhūtāni janārdanasyaparopakārāya caranti viśvam  Hbhv tathā santaḥ pratiṣṭhā dīnānāṃ daivād udbhūtapāpmanām ārtānām ārtihantāro darśanād eva sādhavaḥ  Hbhv tatraivottarakhaṇḍe śivapārvatīsaṃvāde PadmaP na karmabandhanaṃ janma vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vidyate viṣṇor anucaratvaṃ hi mokṣayāhur manīṣiṇaḥ  Hbhv na dāsyam amareśasya bandhanaṃ parikīrtitam sarvabandhananirmuktā haridāsā nirāmayāḥ  Hbhv brahmāṇḍapurāṇe janmāṣṭamīvratamāhātmye śrīcitraguptoktau darśanasparśanālāpasahavāsādibhiḥ kṣaṇāt bhaktāḥ punanti kṛṣṇasya sākṣād api ca pukkaśam  Hbhv tyaktasarvakulācāro mahāpātakavān api viṣṇor bhaktaṃ samāśritya naro nārhati yātanām  Hbhv vāśiṣṭhe yasmin deśe marau tajjño nāsti sajjanapādapaḥ saphalaḥ śītalacchāyo na tatra divasaṃ vaset  Hbhv sadā santo bhigantavyā yadyapy upadiśanti na yā hi svairakathās teṣām upadeśā bhavanti te  Hbhv gāruḍe satrayājisahasrebhyaḥ sarvavedāntapāragaḥ sarvavedāntavitkoṭyā viṣṇubhakto viśiṣyate  Hbhv vaiṣṇavānāṃ sahasrebhya ekānty eko viśiṣyate ekāntinas tu puruṣā gacchanti paramaṃ padam  Hbhv śrībhagavadgītāsu Gītā  api cet sudurācāro bhajate mām ananyabhāk sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥ  Hbhv kṣipraṃ bhavati dharmātmā śaśvacchāntiṃ nigacchati kaunteya pratijānīhi na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati  Hbhv māṃ hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye pi syuḥ pāpayonayaḥ striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te pi yānti parāṃ gatim kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayas tathā  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraiva Gītā  yoginām api sarveṣāṃ madgatenāntarātmanā śraddhāvān bhajate yo māṃ sa me yuktatamo mataḥ  Hbhv śrībhāgavatasya prathamaskandhe śrīparīkṣitoktau BhP  yeṣāṃ saṃsmaraṇāt puṃsāṃ sadyaḥ śuddhyanti vai gṛhāḥ kiṃ punar darśanasparśa pādaśaucāsanādibhiḥ  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe śrīvidurasya BhP  śrutasya puṃsāṃ suciraśramasyananv añjasā sūribhir īḍito rthaḥ tattadguṇānuśravaṇaṃ mukundapādāravindaṃ hṛdayeṣu yeṣām  Hbhv devahūtiṃ prati kapiladevasya BhP  na karhicin matparāḥ śāntarūpenaṅkṣyanti no me nimiṣo leḍhi hetiḥ yeṣām ahaṃ priya ātmā sutaś casakhā guruḥ suhṛdo daivam iṣṭam  Hbhv caturthe śrīdhruvasya BhP  yā nirvṛtis tanubhṛtāṃ tava pādapadmadhyānād bhavajjanakathāśravaṇena vā syāt sā brahmaṇi svamahimany api nātha mā bhūtkiṃ tv antakāsilulitāt patatāṃ vimānāt  Hbhv śrīrudrasya BhP svadharmaniṣṭhaḥ śatajanmabhiḥ pumānviriñcatām eti tataḥ paraṃ hi mām avyākṛtaṃ bhāgavato tha vaiṣṇavaṃpadaṃ yathāhaṃ vibudhāḥ kalātyaye  Hbhv pañcame śrījaḍabharatasya BhP  rahūgaṇaitat tapasā na yātina cejyayā nirvapaṇād gṛhād vā na cchandasā naiva jalāgnisūryairvinā mahatpādarajobhiṣekam  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhe śrīparīkṣitaḥ BhP  rajobhiḥ samasaṅkhyātāḥ pārthivair iha jantavaḥ teṣāṃ ye kecanehante śreyo vai manujādayaḥ  Hbhv prāyo mumukṣavas teṣāṃ kecanaiva dvijottama mumukṣūṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaścin mucyeta sidhyati  Hbhv muktānām api siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣv api mahāmune  Hbhv śrīśivasya BhP  nārāyaṇaparāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati svargāpavarganarakeṣv api tulyārthadarśinaḥ  Hbhv saptame śrīprahlādasya BhP  naiṣāṃ matis tāvad urukramāṅghriṃspṛśaty anarthāpagamo yadarthaḥ mahīyasāṃ pādarajobhiṣekaṃniṣkiñcanānāṃ na vṛṇīta yāvat  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  viprād dviṣaḍguṇayutād aravindanābhapādāravindavimukhāt śvapacaṃ variṣṭham manye tadarpitamanovacanehitārthaprāṇaṃ punāti sa kulaṃ na tu bhūrimānaḥ  Hbhv aṣṭame śrīgajendrasya BhP  ekāntino yasya na kañcanārthaṃvāñchanti ye vai bhagavatprapannāḥ atyadbhutaṃ taccaritaṃ sumaṅgalaṃgāyanta ānandasamudramagnāḥ  Hbhv navame śrībhagavataḥ BhP   ahaṃ bhaktaparādhīno hy asvatantra iva dvija sādhubhir grastahṛdayo bhaktair bhaktajanapriyaḥ  Hbhv nāham ātmānam āśāse madbhaktaiḥ sādhubhir vinā śriyaṃ cātyantikīṃ brahman yeṣāṃ gatir ahaṃ parā  Hbhv ye dārāgāraputrāpta prāṇān vittam imaṃ param hitvā māṃ śaraṇaṃ yātāḥ kathaṃ tāṃs tyaktum utsahe  Hbhv mayi nirbaddhahṛdayāḥ sādhavaḥ samadarśanāḥ vaśe kurvanti māṃ bhaktyā satstriyaḥ satpatiṃ yathā  Hbhv sādhavo hṛdayaṃ mahyaṃ sādhūnāṃ hṛdayaṃ tv aham madanyat te na jānanti nāhaṃ tebhyo manāg api  Hbhv tatraiva śrīdurvāsasaḥ BhP  duṣkaraḥ ko nu sādhūnāṃ dustyajo vā mahātmanām yaiḥ saṅgṛhīto bhagavān sātvatām ṛṣabho hariḥ  Hbhv yannāmaśrutimātreṇa pumān bhavati nirmalaḥ tasya tīrthapadaḥ kiṃ vā dāsānām avaśiṣyate  Hbhv daśame devastutau BhP  tathā na te mādhava tāvakāḥ kvacidbhraśyanti mārgāt tvayi baddhasauhṛdāḥ tvayābhiguptā vicaranti nirbhayāvināyakānīkapamūrdhasu prabho  Hbhv śrībādarāyaṇeḥ BhP  nāyaṃ sukhāpo bhagavān dehināṃ gopikāsutaḥ jñānināṃ cātmabhūtānāṃ yathā bhaktimatām iha  Hbhv tatraiva śrībhagavataḥ BhP  sādhūnāṃ samacittānāṃ mukundacaraṇaiṣiṇām upekṣyaiḥ kiṃ dhanastambhair asadbhir asadāśrayaiḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  na hy ammayāni tīrthāni na devā mṛcchilāmayāḥ te punanty urukālena darśanād eva sādhavaḥ  Hbhv api ca BhP  nāgnir na sūryo na ca candratārakāna bhūr jalaṃ khaṃ śvasano tha vāṅ manaḥ upāsitā bhedakṛto haranty aghaṃvipaścito ghnanti muhūrtasevayā  Hbhv yasyātmabuddhiḥ kuṇape tridhātukesvadhīḥ kalatrādiṣu bhauma ijyadhīḥ yattīrthabuddhiḥ salile na karhicijjaneṣv abhijñeṣu sa eva gokharaḥ  Hbhv śrutistutau BhP  tava pari ye caranty akhilasattvaniketatayāta uta padākramanty avigaṇayya śiro nirṛteḥ parivayase paśūn iva girā vibudhān api tāṃstvayi kṛtasauhṛdāḥ khalu punanti na ye vimukhāḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe śrīvasudevasya BhP  bhūtānāṃ devacaritaṃ duḥkhāya ca sukhāya ca sukhāyaiva hi sādhūnāṃ tvādṛśām acyutātmanām  Hbhv bhajanti ye yathā devān devā api tathaiva tān chāyeva karmasacivāḥ sādhavo dīnavatsalāḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrībhagavataḥ BhP  na mayy ekāntabhaktānāṃ guṇadoṣodbhavā guṇāḥ sādhūnāṃ samacittānāṃ buddheḥ param upeyuṣām  Hbhv evam etān mayā diṣṭān anutiṣṭhanti me pathaḥ kṣemaṃ vindanti matsthānaṃ yad brahma paramaṃ viduḥ  Hbhv nimajjyonmajjatāṃ ghore bhavābdhau paramāyaṇam santo brahmavidaḥ śāntā nor dṛḍhevāpsu majjatām  Hbhv annaṃ hi prāṇināṃ prāṇā ārtānāṃ śaraṇaṃ tv aham dharmā vittaṃ nṝṇāṃ pretya santo rvāgbibhyato raṇam  Hbhv santo diśanti cakṣūṃṣi bahir arkaḥ samutthitaḥ devatā bāndhavāḥ santaḥ santa ātmāham eva ca  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  na kiñcit sādhavo dhīrā bhaktā hy ekāntino mama vāñchanty api mayā dattaṃ kaivalyam apunarbhavam  Hbhv dvādaśe ca śrīparīkṣitaḥ BhP  nātyadbhutam ahaṃ manye mahatām acyutātmanām ajñeṣu tāpatapteṣu bhūteṣu yad anugrahaḥ  Hbhv śrīrudrasya ca mārkaṇḍeyam adhikṛtya BhP  śravaṇād darśanād vāpi mahāpātakino pi vaḥ śudhyerann antyajāś cāpi kim u sambhāṣaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv ataeva śrīdharmarājasya svadūtānuśāsane ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  te devasiddhaparigītapavitragāthāye sādhavaḥ samadṛśo bhagavatprapannāḥ tān nopasīdata harer gadayābhiguptānnaiṣāṃ vayaṃ na ca vayaḥ prabhavāma daṇḍe  Hbhv tathā śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  yamaniyamavidhūtakalmaṣāṇāmanudinam acyutasaktamānasānām apagatam adamānamatsarāṇāṃvraja bhaṭa dūratareṇa mānavānām  Hbhv sakalam idam ahaṃ ca vāsudevaḥparamapumān parameśvaraḥ sa ekaḥ iti matir acalā bhavaty anantehṛdayagate vraja tān vihāya dūrāt  Hbhv kamalanayana vāsudeva viṣṇodharaṇidharācyuta śaṅkhacakrapāṇe bhava śaraṇam itīrayanti ye vaityaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa tān apāpān  Hbhv vasati manasi yasya so vyayātmā puruṣavarasya na tasya dṛṣṭipāte tava gatir atha vā mamāsti cakrapratihatavīryabalasya so nyalokyaḥ  Hbhv nārasiṃhe viṣṇupurāṇe ca ViP aham amarārcitena dhātrāyama iti lokahitāhite niyuktaḥ hariguruvaśago smi na svatantraḥprabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi viṣṇuḥ  Hbhv sugatim abhilaṣāmi vāsudevāvaham api bhāgavatasthitāntarātmā madhuvara vaśago smi na svatantraḥprabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi kṛṣṇaḥ  Hbhv na hi śaśakaluṣacchaviḥ kadācittimiraparābhavatām upaiti candraḥ bhagavati ca harāv ananyacetābhṛśamalino pi virājate manuṣyaḥ  Hbhv pādme devadyūtivikuṇḍalasaṃvāde PadmaP  prāhāsmān yamunā bhrātā sadaiva hi punaḥ punaḥ bhavadbhir vaiṣṇavās tyājyā na te syur mama gocarāḥ  Hbhv durācāro duṣkṛto pi sadācārarato pi yaḥ bhavadbhiḥ sa sadā tyājyo viṣṇuṃ ca bhajate naraḥ  Hbhv vaiṣṇavo yadgṛhe bhuṅkte yeṣāṃ vaiṣṇavasaṅgatiḥ tepi vaḥ parivāryāḥ syus tatsaṅgahatakilbiṣāḥ  Hbhv skānde amṛtasāroddhāre ekādaśyām abhuñjānā yuktāḥ pāpaśatair api bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyā hitā me yadi sarvadā  Hbhv ye smaranti jagannāthaṃ mṛtyukāle janārdanam pāpakoṭiśatair yuktā na te grāhyā mamājñayā  Hbhv na brahmā na śivāgnīndrā nāhaṃ nānye divaukasaḥ śaktā na nigrahaṃ kartuṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv ato haṃ sarvakālaṃ ca vaiṣṇavānāṃ bibhemi vai bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyā vaiṣṇavā ye sadaiva hi  Hbhv vaiṣṇavā viṣṇuvat pūjyā mama mānyā viśeṣataḥ teṣāṃ kṛtepamānepi vināśo jāyate dhruvam  Hbhv kiṃ ca yeṣāṃ smaraṇamātreṇa pāpalakṣaśatāni ca dahyante nātra sandeho vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv yeṣāṃ pādarajenaiva prāpyate jāhnavījalam nārmadaṃ yāmunaṃ caiva kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam  Hbhv yeṣāṃ vākyajalaughena vinā gaṅgājalair api vinā tīrthasahasreṇa snāto bhavati mānavaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca brahmaloke na me vāso na me vāso harālaye nālaye lokapālānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ parābhave  Hbhv na devā na ca gandharvā na yakṣoragarākṣasāḥ trātuṃ samarthā ṛṣayo vaiṣṇavānāṃ parābhave  Hbhv karomi karmaṇā vācā manasāpi na vipriyam vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahābhāgāḥ sudarśanabhayād api  Hbhv ekato dhāvate cakram ekato harivāhanam ekato viṣṇudūtāś ca vaiṣṇave cārdite mayā  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye caikādaśīmāhātmye NārP   ye viṣṇupūjanaratāḥ prayatāḥ kṛtajñāścaikādaśīvrataparā vijitendriyāś ca nārāyaṇācyuta hare śaraṇaṃ bhavetiśāntā vadanti satataṃ tarasā tyajadhvam  Hbhv nārāyaṇārpitadhiyo haribhaktabhaktānsvācāramārganiratān gurusevakāṃś ca satpātradānaniratān harikīrtibhaktāndūtās tyajadhvam aniśaṃ harināmasaktān  Hbhv pāṣaṇḍasaṅgarahitān haribhaktituṣṭānsatsaṅgalolupatarāṃś ca tathātipuṇyān śambhor hareś ca samabuddhimatas tathaivadūtās tyajadhvam upakāraparāñ narāṇām  Hbhv ye vīkṣitā harikathāmṛtasevakaiś canārāyaṇasmṛtiparāyaṇamānasaiś ca viprendrapādajalasevanasamprahṛṣṭaistān pāpino pi ca bhaṭā satataṃ tyajadhvam  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ śrīnāradena caturthaskandhaśeṣe BhP śriyam anucaratīṃ tadarthinaś cadvipadapatīn vibudhāṃś ca yat svapūrṇaḥ na bhajati nijabhṛtyavargatantraḥkatham amum udvisṛjet pumān kṛtajñaḥ  Hbhv ataeva prārthanam nārāyaṇavyūhastave nāhaṃ brahmāpi bhuyāsaṃ tvadbhaktirahito hare tvayi bhaktas tu kīṭo pi bhūyāsaṃ janmajanmasu  Hbhv śrībrahmastutau ca daśamaskandhe BhP  tad astu me nātha sa bhūribhāgobhavetra vānyatra tu vā tiraścām yenāham eko pi bhavajjanānāṃbhūtvā niṣeve tava pādapallavam  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ śrīnārāyaṇavyūhastave ye tyaktalokadharmārthā viṣṇubhaktivaśaṃ gatāḥ bhajanti paramātmānaṃ tebhyo nityaṃ namo namaḥ  Hbhv evaṃ śrībhagavadbhaktamāhātmyāmṛtavāridheḥ vicitrabhaṅgalekhārho lobhalolaṃ vināsti kaḥ  Hbhv ataḥ śrībhagavadbhaktajanānāṃ saṅgatiḥ sadā kāryā sarvaprayatnena dvau lokau vijigīṣubhiḥ  Hbhv atha śrībhagavadbhaktasaṅgamāhātmyambhagavadbhaktapādābjapādukābhyo namo stu me yatsaṅgamaḥ sādhanaṃ ca sādhyaṃ cākhilam uttamam  Hbhv tatra sarvapātakamocakatābṛhannāradīye NārP  yajñamālyupākhyānānte haribhaktiparāṇāṃ tu saṅgināṃ saṅgamātrataḥ mucyate sarvapāpebhyo mahāpātakavān api  Hbhv sāmānyato narthanivartakatāarthaprāpakatā ca pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye PadmaP  śrīmuniśarmāṇaṃ prati pretānām uktau vināśayaty apayaśo buddhiṃ viśadayaty api pratiṣṭhāpayati prāyo nṛṇāṃ vaiṣṇavadarśanam  Hbhv tatra  śrīyamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde mahārathanṛpoktau yathā prapadyamānasya bhagavantaṃ vibhāvasum śītaṃ bhayaṃ tamo py eti sādhūn saṃsevataḥ sadā  Hbhv tatraiva pretopākhyāne pretoktau PadmaP  apākaroti duritaṃ śreyaḥ saṃyojayaty api yaśo vistārayaty āśu nṝṇāṃ vaiṣṇavasaṅgamaḥ  Hbhv atha sarvatīrthādhikatātatraiva PadmaP  gaṅgādipuṇyatīrtheṣu yo naraḥ snātum icchati yaḥ karoti satāṃ saṅgāṃ tayoḥ satsaṅgamo varaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva bhagīrathanṛpoktau PadmaP  yaḥ snātaḥ śāntisitayā sādhusaṅgatigaṅgayā kiṃ tasya dānaiḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ  Hbhv atha sarveṣṭasādhakatāyāni yāni durāpāṇi vāñchitāni mahītale prāpyante tāni tāny eva sādhūnām eva saṅgamāt  Hbhv atha anarthasyāpy arthatvāpādakatāvāśiṣṭhe śūnyam āpūrṇatām eti mṛtir apy amṛtāyate āpat sampad iva bhāti vidvajjanasamāgame  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  saṅgo yaḥ saṃsṛter hetur asatsu vihito dhiyā sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto niḥsaṅgatvāya kalpate  Hbhv śrīkapiladevoktau BhP  prasaṅgam ajaraṃ pāśam ātmanaḥ kavayo viduḥ sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto mokṣadvāram apāvṛtam  Hbhv yataḥ arir mitraṃ viṣaṃ pathyam adharmo dharmatāṃ vrajet prasanne puṇḍarīkākṣe viparīte viparyayaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca śrībhagavadvākyaṃ BhaktiS  attributed to PadmaP mannimittaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpam api dharmāya kalpate mām anādṛtya dharmo pi pāpaṃ syān matprabhāvataḥ  Hbhv caturthaskandhe śrīdhruvoktau BhP  te na smaranty atitarāṃ priyam īśa martyaṃye cānv adaḥ sutasuhṛdgṛhavittadārāḥ ye tv abjanābha bhavadīyapadāravindasaugandhyalubdhahṛdayeṣu kṛtaprasaṅgāḥ  Hbhv pādme tatraiva pretoktau PadmaP  rasāyanamayī śītā paramānandadāyinī nānandayati kaṃ nāma vaiṣṇavāśrayacandrikā  Hbhv atha mokṣadatvam daśamaskandhe śrīmucukundastutau BhP  bhavāpavargo bhramato yadā bhavejjanasya tarhy acuta satsamāgamaḥ satsaṅgamo yarhi tadaiva sadgatauparāvareśe tvayi jāyate matiḥ  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ śrīpracetobhiś caturthaskandhe BhP yatreḍyante kathā mṛṣṭās tṛṣṇāyāḥ praśamo yataḥ nirvairaṃ yatra bhūteṣu nodvego yatra kaścana  Hbhv yatra nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣād bhagavān nyāsināṃ gatiḥ saṃstūyate satkathāsu muktasaṅgaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ  Hbhv teṣāṃ vicaratāṃ padbhyāṃ tīrthānāṃ pāvanecchayā bhītasya kiṃ na roceta tāvakānāṃ samāgamaḥ  Hbhv atha sarvasāratā bṛhannāradīye śrīnāradasanatkumārasaṃvāde NārP  asārabhūte saṃsāre sāram etad ajātmaja bhagavadbhaktasaṅgaś ca haribhaktis titikṣutā  Hbhv pādme tatraiva mahārathanṛpoktau asāgarotthaṃ pīyūṣam adravyaṃ vyasanauṣadham harṣaś cālokaparyantaḥ satāṃ kila samāgamaḥ  Hbhv atha bhagavatkathāmṛtapānaikahetutā pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye śrīnāradoktau PadmaP prasaṅgena satām ātmamanaḥ śrutirasāyanāḥ bhavanti kīrtanīyasya kathāḥ kṛṣṇasya nirmalāḥ  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  śrīkapiladevoktau satāṃ prasaṅgān mama vīryasaṃvidobhavanti hṛtkarṇarasāyanāḥ kathāḥ tajjoṣaṇād āśv apavargavartmaniśraddhā ratir bhaktir anukramiṣyati  Hbhv caturthe śrīnāradoktau BhP  yatra bhāgavatā rājan sādhavo viśadāśayāḥ bhagavadguṇānukathana śravaṇavyagracetasaḥ  Hbhv tasmin mahanmukharitā madhubhiccaritrapīyūṣaśeṣasaritaḥ paritaḥ sravanti tā ye pibanty avitṛṣo nṛpa gāḍhakarṇaistān na spṛśanty aśanatṛḍbhayaśokamohāḥ  Hbhv pañcame BhP  śrībrāhmaṇarahūgaṇasaṃvāde yatrottamaślokaguṇānuvādaḥprastūyate grāmyakathāvighātaḥ niṣevyamāṇo nudinaṃ mumukṣormatiṃ satīṃ yacchati vāsudeve  Hbhv ekādaśe śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde śrīailopākhyānānte BhP  teṣu nityaṃ mahābhāga mahābhāgeṣu matkathāḥ sambhavanti hi tā nṇāṃ juṣatāṃ prapunanty agham  Hbhv tā ye śṛṇvanti gāyanti hy anumodanti cādṛtāḥ matparāḥ śraddadhānāś ca bhaktiṃ vindanti te mayi  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye tatraiva  bhaktis tu bhagavadbhaktasaṅgena parijāyate satsaṅgaḥ prāpyate pumbhiḥ sukṛtaiḥ pūrvasañcitaiḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  athaitat paramaṃ guhyaṃ śṛṇvato yadunandanasugopyam api vakṣyāmi tvaṃ me bhṛtyaḥ suhṛt sakhā  Hbhv no rodhayati māṃ yogo na sāṅkhyaṃ dharma eva ca na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo neṣṭāpūrtaṃ na dakṣiṇā  Hbhv vratāni yajñaś chandāṃsi tīrthāni niyamā yamāḥ yathāvarundhe satsaṅgaḥ sarvasaṅgāpaho hi mām  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ vidureṇa tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  yatsevayā bhagavataḥ kūṭasthasya madhudviṣaḥ ratirāso bhavet tīvraḥ pādayor vyasanārdanaḥ  Hbhv prathamaskandhe śrīśaunakādīnāṃ BhP caturthe ca śrīpracetasām uktau BhP  tulayāma lavenāpi na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ  Hbhv caturthe ca śrīpracetasaḥ prati śrīśivopadeśaḥ BhP  kṣaṇārdhenāpi tulaye na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ  Hbhv dvādaśe śrīmārkaṇḍeyopākhyāne śrīśivasya BhP  athāpi saṃvadiṣyāmo bhavāny etena sādhunā ayaṃ hi paramo lābho nṛṇāṃ sādhusamāgamaḥ  Hbhv ataeva śrīprahlādaṃ prati śrīdharaṇyoktaṃ haribhaktisudhodaye akṣṇoḥ phalaṃ tvādṛśadarśanaṃ hitanvāḥ phalaṃ tvādṛśagātrasaṅgaḥ jihvāphalaṃ tvādṛśakīrtanaṃ hisudurlabhā bhāgavatā hi loke  Hbhv ataeva vidureṇa tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  durāpā hy alpatapasaḥ sevā vaikuṇṭhavartmasu yatropagīyate nityaṃ devadevo janārdanaḥ  Hbhv śrīvidehenāpy ekādaśaskandhe BhP  durlabho mānuṣo deho dehināṃ kṣaṇabhaṅguraḥ tatrāpi durlabhaṃ manye vaikuṇṭhapriyadarśanam  Hbhv ataeva hi prārthitaṃ śrīdhruveṇa caturthaskandhe BhP  bhaktiṃ muhuḥ pravahatāṃ tvayi me prasaṅgobhūyād ananta mahatām amalāśayānām yenāñjasolbaṇam uruvyasanaṃ bhavābdhiṃneṣye bhavadguṇakathāmṛtapānamattaḥ  Hbhv pracetasaḥ pratyupadeśe śrīśivena ca BhP  athānaghāṅghres tava kīrtitīrthayorantarbahiḥsnānavidhūtapāpmanām bhūteṣv anukrośasusattvaśīlināṃsyāt saṅgamo nugraha eṣa nas tava  Hbhv śrīpracetobhiś ca BhP  yāvat te māyayā spṛṣṭā bhramāma iha karmabhiḥ tāvad bhavatprasaṅgānāṃ saṅgaḥ syān no bhave bhave  Hbhv śrīprahlādenāpi saptamaskandhe BhP  tasmād amūs tanubhṛtām aham āśiṣo jñaāyuḥ śriyaṃ vibhavam aindriyam āviriñcyāt necchāmi te vilulitān uruvikrameṇakālātmanopanaya māṃ nijabhṛtyapārśvam  Hbhv  iti athāsatsaṅgadoṣāḥ śrīkātyāyanavākye varaṃ hutavahajvālāpañjarāntarvyavasthitiḥ na śauricintāvimukhajanasaṃvāsavaiśasam  Hbhv pādme uttarakhaṇḍe śrīumāmaheśvarasaṃvāde avaiṣṇavās tu ye viprāś cāṇḍālād adhamāḥ smṛtāḥ teṣāṃ sambhāṣaṇaṃ sparśaṃ somapānādi varjayet  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde BhP satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā maunaṃ buddhiḥ śrīr hrīr yaśaḥ kṣamā śamo damo bhagaś ceti yatsaṅgād yāti saṅkṣayam  Hbhv teṣv aśānteṣu mūḍheṣu khaṇḍitātmasv asādhuṣu saṅgaṃ na kuryāc chocyeṣu yoṣitkrīḍāmṛgeṣu ca  Hbhv na tathāsya bhaven moho bandhaś cānyaprasaṅgataḥ yoṣitsaṅgād yathā puṃso yathā tatsaṅgisaṅgataḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  saṅgaṃ na kuryād asatāṃ śiśnodaratṛpāṃ kvacit tasyānugas tamasy andhe pataty andhānugāndhavat  Hbhv bhagavadbhaktihīnā ye mukhyāsantas ta eva hi teṣāṃ niṣṭhā śubhā kvāpi na syāt saccaritair api  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye prāyaścittaprakaraṇānte kiṃ vedaiḥ kim u vā śāstraiḥ kim u tīrthaniṣevaṇaiḥ viṣṇubhaktivihīnānāṃ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ  Hbhv śrīgāruḍe antaṃ gato pi vedānāṃ sarvaśāstrārthavedy api yo na sarveśvare bhaktas taṃ vidyāt puruṣādhamam  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  ahny āpṛtārtakaraṇā niśi niḥśayānānānāmanorathadhiyā kṣaṇabhagnanidrāḥ daivāhatārtharacanā ṛṣayo pi devayuṣmatprasaṅgavimukhā iha saṃsaranti  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe BhP  prāyaścittāni cīrṇāni nārāyaṇaparāṅmukham na niṣpunanti rājendra surākumbham ivāpagāḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare kutaḥ pāpakṣayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ ca maṅgalam yeṣāṃ naiva hṛdistho yaṃ maṅgalāyatano hariḥ  Hbhv ataeva bṛhannāradīye lubdhakopākhyānārambhe haripūjāvihīnāś ca vedavidveṣiṇas tathā dvijagodveṣiṇaś cāpi rākṣasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv ataeva nijadūtān prati dharmarājasyānuśāsanaṃ ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  tān ānayadhvam asato vimukhān mukundapādāravindamakarandarasād ajasram niṣkiñcanaiḥ paramahaṃsakulair asaṅgairjuṣṭād gṛhe nirayavartmani baddhatṛṣṇān  Hbhv jihvā na vakti bhagavadguṇanāmadheyaṃcetaś ca na smarati taccaraṇāravindam kṛṣṇāya no namati yacchira ekadāpitān ānayadhvam asato kṛtaviṣṇukṛtyān  Hbhv skānde mārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde yo hi bhāgavataṃ lokam upahāsaṃ nṛpottama karoti tasya naśyanti arthadharmayaśaḥsutā  Hbhv nindāṃ kurvanti ye mūḍhā vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām patanti pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ mahārauravasaṃjñite  Hbhv hanti nindati vai dveṣṭi vaiṣṇavān nābhinandati krudhyate yāti no harṣaṃ darśane patanāni ṣaṭ  Hbhv tatraivāmṛtasāroddhāre śrīyamoktau janmaprabhṛti yat kiñcit sukṛtaṃ samupārjitam nāśam āyāti tat sarvaṃ pīḍayed yadi vaiṣṇavān  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye prahlādabalisaṃvāde karapatraiś ca phālyante sutīvrair yamaśāsanaiḥ nindāṃ kurvanti ye pāpā vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv pūjito bhagavān viṣṇur janmāntaraśatair api prasīdati na viśvātmā vaiṣṇave cāpamānite  Hbhv daśamaskandhe ca BhP  nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śṛṇvaṃs tatparasya janasya vā tato nāpaiti yaḥ so pi yāty adhaḥ sukṛtāc cyutaḥ  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ viṣṇudharmottare jīvitaṃ viṣṇubhaktasya varaṃ pañcadināni ca na tu kalpasahasrāṇi bhaktihīnasya keśave  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ śrībhāgavate ailopākhyānānte BhP  tato duḥsaṅgam utsṛjya satsu sajjeta buddhimān santa evāsya chindanti manovyāsaṅgam uktibhiḥ  Hbhv atha śrīvaiṣṇavasamāgamavidhiḥatha śrībhagavadbhaktān sallakṣaṇavibhūṣitān gatvā tān dūrato dṛṣṭvā daṇḍavat praṇamen mudā  Hbhv tejodraviṇapañcarātre vaiṣṇavo vaiṣṇavaṃ dṛṣṭvā daṇḍavat praṇamed bhuvi ubhayor antarā viṣṇuḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ  Hbhv tatra ca viśeṣo bṛhannāradīye  sabhāyāṃ yajñaśālāyāṃ devatāyataneṣv api pratyekaṃ tu namaskāro hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv puṇyakṣetre puṇyatīrthe svādhyāyasamaye tathā pratyekaṃ tu namaskāro hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv vaiṣṇavaṃ cāgataṃ vīkṣyābhigamyāliṅga vaiṣṇavam vaideśikaṃ prīṇayeyur darśayantaḥ svavaiṣṇavān  Hbhv tathā coktaṃ śrībrahmaṇā tejodraviṇapañcarātre nārāyaṇāśrayaṃ bhaktaṃ deśāntarasamāgatam prīṇayed darśayaṃs tasya bhaktyā nārāyaṇāśrayān  Hbhv  ititataś ca vaiṣṇavaḥ prāptaḥ santarpya vacanāmṛtaiḥ sadbandhur iva sammānyo nyathā doṣo mahān smṛtaḥ  Hbhv atha vaiṣṇavasammānananityatāskānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde dṛṣṭvā bhāgavataṃ daivāt sammukhe yo na yāti hi na gṛhṇāti haris tasya pūjāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm  Hbhv yo na gṛhṇāti bhūpāla vaiṣṇavaṃ gṛham āgatam tadgṛhaṃ pitṛbhis tyaktaṃ śmaśānam iva bhīṣaṇam  Hbhv athavābhyagataṃ dūrād yo nārcayanti vaiṣṇavam svaśaktyā nṛpaśārdūla nānyaḥ pāparatas tataḥ  Hbhv śrāntaṃ bhāgavataṃ dṛṣṭvā kaṭhinaṃ yasya mānasam prasīdati na duṣṭātmā śvapacād adhiko hi saḥ  Hbhv vipraṃ bhāgavataṃ dṛṣṭvā dīnam āturamānasam na karoti paritrāṇaṃ keśavo na prasīdati  Hbhv dṛṣṭvā bhāgavataṃ vipraṃ namaskāreṇa nārcayet dehinas tasya pāpasya na ca vai kṣamate hariḥ  Hbhv apūjito yadā gacchad vaiṣṇavo gṛhamedhinaḥ śatajanmārjitaṃ bhūpa puṇyam ādāya gacchati  Hbhv anabhyarcya pitṝn devān bhuñjate harivāsare tat pāpaṃ jāyate bhūpa vaiṣṇavānām atikrame  Hbhv pūrvaṃ kṛtvā tu sammānam avajñāṃ kurute tu yaḥ vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahīpāla sānvayo yāti saṅkṣayam  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde PadmaP vaiṣṇavaṃ janam ālokya nābhyutthānaṃ karoti yaḥ praṇayādarato vipra sa naro narakātithiḥ  Hbhv caturthaskandhe BhP  ca vyālālayadrumā vai teṣv ariktākhilasampadaḥ yadgṛhās tīrthapādīya pādatīrthavivarjitāḥ  Hbhv atha vaiṣṇavastutiḥskānde dahnyo haṃ kṛtakṛtyo haṃ yad yūyaṃ gṛham āgatāḥ durlabhaṃ darśanaṃ nūnaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ yathā hareḥ  Hbhv merumandaratulyā vai puṇyapuñjā mayā kṛtāḥ samprāptaṃ darśanaṃ yad vai vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv daśamaskandhe śrīgargācāryaṃ prati śrīnandasya vākyam BhP  mahadvicalanaṃ nṝṇāṃ gṛhiṇāṃ dīnacetasām niḥśreyasāya bhagavan kalpate nānyathā kvacit  Hbhv caturthaskandhe BhP   aho ācaritaṃ kiṃ me maṅgalaṃ maṅgalāyanāḥ yasya vo darśanaṃ hy āsīd durdarśānāṃ ca yogibhiḥ  Hbhv adhanā api te dhanyāḥ sādhavo gṛhamedhinaḥ yadgṛhā hy arhavaryāmbu tṛṇabhūmīśvarāvarāḥ  Hbhv kaccin naḥ kuśalaṃ nāthā indriyārthārthavedinām vyasanāvāpa etasmin patitānāṃ svakarmabhiḥ  Hbhv bhavatsu kuśalapraśna ātmārāmeṣu neṣyate kuśalākuśalā yatra na santi mativṛttayaḥ  Hbhv atha vaiṣṇavābhigamanamāhātmyamskānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvādesammukhaṃ vrajamānasya vaiṣṇavānāṃ narādhipa pade pade yajñaphalaṃ prāhuḥ paurāṇikā dvijāḥ  Hbhv atha vaiṣṇavastutimāhātmyam  tatraivapratyakṣaṃ vā parokṣaṃ vā yaḥ praśaṃsati vaiṣṇavam brahmahā madyapaḥ steyī gurugāmī sadā nṝṇām mucyate pātakāt sadyo viṣṇur āha nṛpottama  Hbhv kiṃ capratyakṣaṃ vā parokṣaṃ vā ye praśaṃsanti vaiṣṇavam prasādād vāsudevasya te taranti bhavārṇavam  Hbhv atha vaiṣṇavasammānamāhātmyam tatraivāmṛtasāroddhāreśraddhayā dattam annaṃ ca vaiṣṇavāgniṣu jīryati tadannaṃ meruṇā tulyaṃ bhavate ca dine dine  Hbhv daive paitre ca yo dadyād vārimātraṃ tu vaiṣṇave saptodadhisamaṃ bhūtvā pitṝṇām upatiṣṭhati  Hbhv viṣṇudharmekiṃ dānaiḥ kiṃ tapobhir vā yajñaiś ca vividhaiḥ kṛtaiḥ sarvaṃ sampadyate puṃsāṃ viṣṇubhaktābhipūjanāt  Hbhv pūjayed vaiṣṇavān etān prayatnena vicakṣaṇaḥ svaśaktyā vaiṣṇavebhyo yad dattaṃ syād akṣayaṃ bhavet  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye yajñamālyupākhyāne NārP haribhaktiratān yas tu haribuddhyā prapūjayet tasya tuṣyanti viprendra brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  Hbhv haripūjāparāṇāṃ ca harināmaratātmanām śuśrūṣāniratā yānti pāpino pi parāṃ gatim  Hbhv tatraiva yajñadhvajopākhyānasyārambhe NārP saṃsārasāgaraṃ tartuṃ ya icchen munipuṅgava sa bhajed dharibhaktānāṃ bhaktān vai pāpahāriṇaḥ  Hbhv tadante ca NārP  yo viṣṇubhaktān niṣkāmān bhojayet śraddhayānvitaḥ triḥsaptakulasaṃyuktās te yānti harimandiram  Hbhv viṣṇubhaktāya yo dadyān niṣkāmāya mahātmane pānīyaṃ vā phalaṃ vāpi sa eva bhagavatpriyaḥ  Hbhv viṣṇubhaktiparāṇāṃ tu śuśrūṣāṃ kurvate tu ye te yānti viṣṇubhavanaṃ yāvadābhūtasamplavam  Hbhv devapūjāparo yasya gṛhe vasati sarvadā tatraiva sarvadevāś ca tiṣṭhanti śrīharis tathā  Hbhv laiṅgenārāyaṇaparo vidvān yasyānnaṃ prītamānasaḥ aśnāti taddharer āsyaṃ gatam annaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv sarvārcanād api viśvātmā prīto bhavati mādhavaḥ dṛṣṭvā bhāgavatasyānnaṃ sa bhuṅkte bhaktavatsalaḥ  Hbhv brāhme śrībhagavadvākyamnaivedyaṃ purato nyastaṃ dṛṣṭvaiva svīkṛtaṃ mayā bhaktasya rasanāgreṇa rasam aśnāmi padmaja  Hbhv pādmottarakhaṇḍe śrīśivomāsaṃvāde ārādhanānāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ param tasmāt parataraṃ devi tadīyānāṃ samarcanam  Hbhv arcayitvāpi govindaṃ tadīyān nārcayet punaḥ na sa bhāgavato jñeyaḥ kevalaṃ dāmbhikaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv pumāṃs tasmāt prayatnena vaiṣṇavān pūjayet sadā sarvaṃ tarati duḥkhaughaṃ mahābhāgavatārcanāt  Hbhv ekādaśe śrībhagavadvākyam BhP   vaiṣṇave bandhusatkṛtyā  Hbhv madbhaktapūjābhyadhikā  Hbhv kiṃ ca skānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde karmaṇā manasā vācā yercayanti sadā harim teṣāṃ vākyaṃ naraiḥ kāryaṃ te hi viṣṇusamā narāḥ  Hbhv ity ādṛto nuśṛṇuyād bhaktiśāstrāṇi tatra ca śrībhāgavatam atrāpi kṛṣṇalīlākathāṃ muhuḥ  Hbhv atha vaiṣṇavaśāstramāhātmyam skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde vaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye śṛṇvanti paṭhanti ca dhanyās te mānavā loke tesāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati  Hbhv vaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye rcayanti gṛhe narāḥ sarvapāpavinirmuktā bhavanti suravanditāḥ  Hbhv sarvasvenāpi viprendra kartavyaḥ śāstrasaṅgrahaḥ vaiṣṇavais tu mahābhaktyā tuṣṭyarthaṃ cakrapāṇinaḥ  Hbhv tiṣṭhate vaiṣṇavaṃ śāstraṃ likhitaṃ yasya mandire tatra nārāyaṇo devaḥ svayaṃ vasati nārada  Hbhv paurāṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ślokaṃ ślokārdham athavāpi ca ślokapādaṃ paṭhed yas tu gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv devatānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca yoginām api durlabham viprendra vaiṣṇavaṃ śāstraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ ca kā kathā  Hbhv tatraiva śrīkṛṣṇārjunasaṃvāde mama śāstrāṇi ye nityaṃ pūjayanti paṭhanti ca te narāḥ kuruśārdūla mamātithyaṃ gatāḥ sadā  Hbhv mama śākhyapravaktāraṃ mama śāstrānucintakam cintayāmi na sandeho naraṃ taṃ cātmavat sadā  Hbhv atha śrīmadbhāgavatamāhātmyamtatraiva jīvitād adhikaṃ yeṣāṃ śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau na teṣāṃ bhavati kleśo yāmyaḥ kalpaśatair api  Hbhv dhārayanti gṛhe nityaṃ śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ hi ye āsphoṭayanti valganti teṣāṃ prītāḥ pitāmahāḥ  Hbhv yāvad dināni viprarṣe śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ gṛhe tāvat pibanti pitaraḥ kṣīraṃ sarpir madhūdakam  Hbhv yercayanti sadā gehe śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ narāḥ prīṇitās taiś ca vibudhā yāvad āhūtasamplavam  Hbhv yaccanti vaiṣṇave bhaktyā śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ hi ye kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke vasanti te  Hbhv ślokārdhaṃ ślokapādaṃ vā varaṃ bhāgavataṃ gṛhe śataśo tha sahasraiś ca kim anyaiḥ śāstrasaṅgrahaiḥ  Hbhv na yasya tiṣṭhate gehe śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau na tasya punar āvṛttir yāmyāt pāśāt kadācana  Hbhv kathaṃ sa vaiṣṇavo jñeyaḥ śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau gṛhe na tiṣṭhate yasya sa vipraḥ śvapacādhamaḥ  Hbhv yatra yatra bhaved vipra śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau tatra tatra harir yāti tridaśaiḥ saha nārada  Hbhv tatra sarvāṇi tīrthāni nadīnadasarāṃsi ca yatra bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ tiṣṭhate munisattama  Hbhv tatra sarvāṇi tīrthāni sarve yajñāḥ sudakṣiṇāḥ yatra bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ pūjitaṃ tiṣṭhate gṛhe  Hbhv kiṃ ca nityaṃ bhāgavataṃ yas tu purāṇaṃ paṭhate naraḥ pratyakṣaraṃ bhavet tasya kapilādānajaṃ phalam  Hbhv ślokārdhaṃ ślokapādaṃ vā nityaṃ bhāgavatodbhavam paṭhet śṛṇoti vā bhaktyā gosahasraṃ phalaṃ labhet  Hbhv yaḥ paṭhet prayato nityaṃ ślokaṃ bhāgavataṃ mune aṣṭādaśapurāṇānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva mārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde yo hi bhāgavate śāstre vighnam ācarate pumān nābhinandati duṣṭātmā kulānāṃ pātayec chatam  Hbhv pādme gautamāmbarīṣasaṃvāde ambarīṣa śukaproktaṃ nityaṃ bhāgavataṃ śṛṇu paṭhasva svamukhenāpi yadīcchasi bhavakṣayam  Hbhv ślokaṃ bhāgavataṃ vāpi ślokardhapādam eva vā likhitaṃ tiṣṭhate yasya gṛhe tasya sadā hariḥ vasate nātra sandeho devadevo janārdanaḥ  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye śrīmārkaṇḍeyendradyumnasaṃvāde śrīmadbhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ paṭhate kṛṣṇasannidhau kulakoṭiśatair yuktaḥ krīḍate yogibhiḥ saha  Hbhv gāruḍeartho yaṃ brahmasūtrāṇāṃ bhāratārthavinirṇayaḥ gāyatrībhāṣyarūpo sau vedārthaparibṛṃhitaḥ  Hbhv purāṇānāṃ sāmarūpaḥ sākṣādbhagavatoditaḥ dvādaśaskandhayukto yaṃ śatavicchedasaṃyutaḥ grantho ṣṭādaśasāhasraḥ śrīmadbhāgavatābhidhaḥ  Hbhv tasminn eva śrībhāgavate prathamaskandhe BhP  dharmaḥ projjhitakaitavo tra paramo nirmatsarāṇāṃ satāṃvedyaṃ vāstavam atra vastu śivadaṃ tāpatrayonmūlanam śrīmadbhāgavate mahāmunikṛte kiṃ vā parair īśvaraḥsadyo hṛdy avarudhyate tra kṛtibhiḥ śuśrūṣubhis tatkṣaṇāt  Hbhv idaṃ bhāgavataṃ nāma purāṇaṃ brahmasammitam uttamaślokacaritaṃ cakāra bhagavān ṛṣiḥ  Hbhv niḥśreyasāya lokasya dhanyaṃ svastyayanaṃ mahat tad idaṃ grāhayām āsasutam ātmavatāṃ varam sarvavedetihāsānāṃ sāraṃ sāraṃ samuddhṛtam  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  kṛṣṇe svadhāmopagate dharmajñānādibhiḥ saha kalau naṣṭadṛśām eṣa purāṇārko dhunoditaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP anarthopaśamaṃ sākṣād bhaktiyogam adhokṣaje lokasyājānato vidvāṃś cakre sātvatasaṃhitām  Hbhv yasyāṃ vai śrūyamāṇāyāṃ kṛṣṇe paramapūruṣe bhaktir utpadyate puṃsaḥ śokamohabhayāpahā  Hbhv dvitīye śrīśukoktau BhP  pariniṣṭhito pi nairguṇya uttamaślokalīlayā gṛhītacetā rājarṣe ākhyānaṃ yad adhītavān  Hbhv rājante tāvad anyāni purāṇāni satāṃ gaṇe yāvad bhāgavataṃ naiva śrūyate mṛtasāgaram  Hbhv dvādaśe ca BhP    rājante tāvad anyāni purāṇāni satāṃ gaṇe yāvad bhāgavataṃ naiva śrūyatemṛtasāgaraḥ  Hbhv sarvavedāntasāraṃ hi śrībhāgavatam iṣyate tadrasāmṛtatṛptasya nānyatra syād ratiḥ kvacit  Hbhv nimnagānāṃ yathā gaṅgā devānām acyuto yathā vaiṣṇavānāṃ yathā śambhuḥ purāṇānām idaṃ tathā  Hbhv śrīmadbhāgavataṃ purāṇam amalaṃ yad vaiṣṇavānāṃ priyaṃyasmin pāramahaṃsyam ekam amalaṃ jñānaṃ paraṃ gīyate tatra jñānavirāgabhaktisahitaṃ naiṣkarmyam āviṣkṛtaṃtac chṛṇvan supaṭhan vicāraṇaparo bhaktyā vimucyen naraḥ  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ BhP  nigamakalpataror galitaṃ phalaṃśukamukhād amṛtadravasaṃyutam pibata bhāgavataṃ rasam ālayaṃmuhur aho rasikā bhuvi bhāvukāḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  yaḥ svānubhāvam akhilaśrutisāram ekamadhyātmadīpam atititīrṣatāṃ tamo ndham saṃsāriṇāṃ karuṇayāha purāṇaguhyaṃtaṃ vyāsasūnum upayāmi guruṃ munīnām  Hbhv atha śrībhagavacchāstravaktṛmāhātmyambhagavaddharmavaktāraṃ bhagavacchāstravācakam vaiṣṇavaṃ guruvad bhaktyā pūjayej jñānadāyakam  Hbhv nāradapañcarātre ṛṣīn prati śrīśāṇḍilyoktau vaiṣṇavaṃ jñānavaktāraṃ yo vidyād viṣṇuvad gurum pūjayed vāṅmanaḥkāyaiḥ sa śāstrajñaḥ sa vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv ślokapādasya vaktāpi yaḥ pūjyaḥ sa sadaiva hi kiṃ punar bhagavadviṣṇoḥ svarūpaṃ vitanoti yaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ brahma tajjñānenātha gamyate jñānasya sādhanaṃ śāstraṃ śāstraṃ ca guruvaktṛgam  Hbhv brahma prāptir ato hetor gurvadhīnā sadaiva hi hetunānena vai viprā gurur gurutaraḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv yasmād devo jagannāthaḥ kṛtvā maryamayīṃ tanum magnān uddharate lokān kāruṇyāc chāstrapāṇinā  Hbhv tasmād bhaktir gurau kāryā saṃsārabhayabhīruṇā śāstrajñānena yo jñānaṃ timiraṃ vinipātayet  Hbhv śāstraṃ pāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitraṃ bhogamokṣadam śāntidaṃ ca mahārthaṃ ca vakti yaḥ sa jagadguruḥ  Hbhv atha śrīkṛṣṇalīlākathāśravaṇamāhātmyamtatra pāpādiśodhakatvamskānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde teṣāṃ kṣīṇaṃ mahat pāpaṃ varṣakoṭiśatodbhavam viprendra nāsti sandeho ye śṛṇvanti hareḥ kathām  Hbhv tatraivānyatra sarvāśramābhigamanaṃ sarvatīrthāvagāhanam na tathā pāraṇaṃ nṝṇāṃ nārāyaṇakathā yathā  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye  yajñadhvajopākhyānānte aho harikathā loke pāpaghnī puṇyadāyinī śṛṇvatāṃ vadatāṃ caiva tadbhaktānāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv prathamaskandhe BhP  śṛṇvatāṃ svakathāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanaḥ hṛdy antaḥstho hy abhadrāṇi vidhunoti suhṛtsatām  Hbhv ekādaśe ca devastutau BhP  śuddhir nṛṇāṃ na tu tatheḍya durāśayānāṃvidyāśrutādhyayanadānatapaḥkriyābhiḥ sattvātmanām ṛṣabha te yaśasi pravṛddhasacchraddhayā śravaṇasambhṛtayā yathā syāt  Hbhv daśame BhP  śrībādarāyaṇiṃ prati śrīparīkṣiduktau naiṣātiduḥsahā kṣun māṃ tyaktodam api bādhate pibantaṃ tvanmukhāmbhoja cyutaṃ harikathāmṛtam  Hbhv skānde ca tatraiva śrīpradaṃ viṣṇucaritaṃ sarvopadravanāśanam sarvaduḥkhopaśamanaṃ duṣṭagrahanivāraṇam  Hbhv atha prakarṣeṇa sarvamaṅgalakāritvamtatraiva śrotavyaṃ sādhucaritaṃ yaśodharmajayārthibhiḥ pāpakṣayārthaṃ devarṣe svargārthaṃ dharmabuddhibhiḥ  Hbhv āyuṣyāmārogyakaraṃ yaśasyaṃ puṇyavardhanam caritaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ nityaṃ śrotavyaṃ sādhubuddhinā  Hbhv kuṭumbavṛddhiṃ vijayaṃ śatrunāśaṃ balam karoti viṣṇucaritaṃ sarvakālaphalapradam  Hbhv prathamaskandhe BhP  dharmaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ puṃsāṃ viṣvaksenakathāsu yaḥ notpādayed yadi ratiṃ śrama eva hi kevalam  Hbhv tṛtīye śrīviduramaitreyasaṃvāde BhP  ekāntalābhaṃ vacaso nu puṃsāṃsuślokamauler guṇavādam āhuḥ śruteś ca vidvadbhir upākṛtāyāṃkathāsudhāyām upasamprayogam  Hbhv dvitīye śrīśaunakoktau BhP āyur harati vai puṃsām udyann astaṃ ca yann asau tasyarte yatkṣaṇo nīta uttamaślokavārtayā  Hbhv tṛtīye śrīviduroktau BhP sā śraddadhānasya vivardhamānāviraktim anyatra karoti puṃsaḥ hareḥ padānusmṛtinirvṛtasyasamastaduḥkhāpyayam āśu dhatte  Hbhv caturthe śrīpṛthucaritānte śrīmaitreyoktau BhP chinnānyadhīr adhigatātmagatir nirīhastat tatyaje ñcchinad idaṃ vayunena yena tāvan na yogagatibhir yatir apramattoyāvad gadāgrajakathāsu ratiṃ na kuryāt  Hbhv ekādaśe ca śrībhagavantaṃ praty uddhavavākye BhP  tava vikrīḍitaṃ kṛṣṇa nṛṇāṃ paramamaṅgalam karṇapīyūṣam āsādya tyajanty anyaspṛhāṃ janāḥ  Hbhv caturthe pracetasaḥ prati śrībhagavaduktau BhP  gṛheṣv āviśatāṃ cāpi puṃsāṃ kuśalakarmaṇām madvārtāyātayāmānāṃ na bandhāya gṛhā matāḥ  Hbhv skānde tatraiva dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ yad iṣṭaṃ ca nṝṇām iha tat sarvaṃ labhate vatsa kathāṃ śrutvā hareḥ sadā  Hbhv dvādaśe ca śrīśukoktau BhP saṃsārasindhum atidustaram uttitīrṣornānyaḥ plavo bhagavato puruṣottamasya līlākathārasaniṣevanam antareṇapuṃso bhaved vividhaduḥkhadavārditasya  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye nityaṃ kṛṣṇakathā yasya prāṇād api garīyasī na tasya durlabhaṃ kiñcid iha loke paratra ca  Hbhv dvitīyaskandhe BhP jñānaṃ yad āpratinivṛttaguṇormicakramātmaprasāda uta yatra guṇeṣv asaṅgaḥ kaivalyasammatapathas tv atha bhaktiyogaḥko nirvṛto harikathāsu ratiṃ na kuryāt  Hbhv daśamaskandhe śrutistutau BhP  duravagamātmatattvanigamāya tavāttatanoścaritamahāmṛtābdhiparivartapariśramaṇāḥ na parilaṣanti kecid apavargam apīśvara tecaraṇasarojahaṃsakulasaṅgavisṛṣṭagṛhāḥ  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde BhP  naikātmatāṃ me spṛhayanti kecinmatpādasevābhiratā madīhāḥ ye nyonyato bhāgavatāḥ prasajyasabhājayante mama pauruṣāṇi  Hbhv dvitīye śrīsūtoktau BhP pibanti ye bhagavata ātmanaḥ satāṃkathāmṛtaṃ śravaṇapuṭeṣu sambhṛtampunanti te viṣayavidūṣitāśayaṃvrajanti taccaraṇasaroruhāntikam  Hbhv tṛtīye kapiladevastutau BhP  pānena te deva kathāsudhāyāḥpravṛddhabhaktyā viśadāśayā ye vairāgyasāraṃ pratilabhya bodhaṃyathāñjasānvīyur akuṇṭhadhiṣṇyam  Hbhv skānde amṛtasāroddhāre śrīyamasya dūtānuśāsane ye śṛṇvanti kathāṃ viṣṇor ye paṭhanti hareḥ kathām kalāyutaṃ nāvalokyaṃ gatās te brahma śāśvatam  Hbhv yasya viṣṇukathālāpair nityaṃ pramuditaṃ manaḥ tasya na cyavate lakṣmīs tatpadaṃ ca kare sthitam  Hbhv dvādaśe BhP  yat tūttamaḥślokaguṇānuvādaḥsaṅgīyate bhīkṣṇam amaṅgalaghnaḥ tam eva nityaṃ śṛṇuyād abhīkṣṇaṃkṛṣṇe malāṃ bhaktim abhīpsamānaḥ  Hbhv skānde yatra yatra mahīpāla vaiṣṇavī vartate kathā tatra tatra harir yāti gaur yathā sutavatsalā  Hbhv śrīviṣṇudharme śrībhagavaduktauskānde ca śrībhagavadarjunasaṃvāde matkathāvācakaṃ nityaṃ matkathāśravaṇe ratam matkathāprītamanasaṃ nāham tyakṣyāmi taṃ naram  Hbhv daśamaskandhe brahmastutau BhP  jñāne prayāsam udapāsya namanta evajīvanti sanmukharitāṃ bhavadīyavārtām sthāne sthitāḥ śrutigatāṃ tanuvāṅmanobhirye prāyaśo ñjita jito py asi tais trilokyām  Hbhv tṛtīye śrīsanakādistutau BhP  nātyantikaṃ vigaṇayanty api te prasādaṃkiṃ vānyad arpitabhayaṃ bhruva unnayais te ye ṅga tvadaṅghriśaraṇā bhavataḥ kathāyāḥkīrtanyatīrthayaśasaḥ kuśalā rasajñāḥ  Hbhv caturthe śrībhagavantaṃ prati siddhānāṃ stutau BhP  ayaṃ tvatkathāmṛṣṭapīyūṣanadyāṃmanovāraṇaḥ kleśadāvāgnidagdhaḥ tṛṣārto vagāḍho na sasmāra dāvaṃna niṣkrāmati brahmasampannavan naḥ  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ prathamaskandhe śrīśaunakādibhiḥ BhP  vayaṃ tu na vitṛpyāma uttamaślokavikrame yacchṛṇvatāṃ rasajñānāṃ svādu svādu pade pade  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  ko nāma tṛpyed rasavit kathāyāṃmahattamaikāntaparāyaṇasya nāntaṃ guṇānām aguṇasya jagmuryogeśvarā ye bhavapādmamukhyāḥ  Hbhv tṛtīye śrīvidureṇa BhP  krīḍan vidhatte dvijagosurāṇāṃkṣemāya karmāṇy avatārabhedaiḥ mano na tṛpyaty api śṛṇvatāṃ naḥsuślokamauleś caritāmṛtāni  Hbhv daśamaskandhe ca śrīparīkṣitā BhP  brahman kṛṣṇakathāḥ puṇyā mādhvīr lokamalāpahāḥ ko nu tṛpyeta śṛṇvānaḥ śrutajño nityanūtanaḥ  Hbhv ato hi śrīpṛthurājena prārthitaṃ BhP  na kāmaye nātha tad apy ahaṃ kvacinna yatra yuṣmaccaraṇāmbujāsavaḥ mahattamāntarhṛdayān mukhacyutovidhatsva karṇāyutam eṣa me varaḥ  Hbhv ataeva niścayoktaṃ pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye PadmaP  ambarīṣaṃ prati śrīnāradena nātaḥ paraṃ paramatoṣaviśeṣapoṣaṃpaśyāmi puṇyam ucitaṃ ca paraspareṇa santaḥ prasahya yad anantaguṇān anantaśreyonidhīn adhikabhāvabhujo bhajanti  Hbhv prathamaskandhe śrīsūtena BhP  yā yāḥ kathā bhagavataḥ kathanīyorukarmaṇaḥ guṇakarmāśrayāḥ pumbhiḥ saṃsevyās tā bubhūṣubhiḥ  Hbhv daśamaskandhaśeṣe ca śrībādarāyaṇinā BhP  itthaṃ parasya nijavartmarirakṣayāttalīlātanos tadanurūpaviḍambanāni karmāṇi karmakaṣaṇāni yadūttamasyaśrūyād amuṣya padayor anuvṛttim icchan  Hbhv atha śrībhagavatkathātyāgādidoṣaḥataḥ kṛṣṇakathāyāṃ tu satyām anyakathāśrutim tad aśrutiṃ ca vaimukhyaṃ tasyāṃ tṛptim api tyajet  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe kapiladevahūtisaṃvāde BhP  nūnaṃ daivena vihatā ye cācyutakathāsudhām hitvā śṛṇvanty asadgāthāḥ purīṣam iva viḍbhujaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrīvaikuṇṭhavarṇane BhP  yan na vrajanty aghabhido racanānuvādācchṛṇvanti ye nyaviṣayāḥ kukathā matighnīḥ yās tu śrutā hatabhagair nṛbhir āttasārāstāṃs tān kṣipanty aśaraṇeṣu tamaḥsu hanta  Hbhv kiṃ ca skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde vācyamānaṃ tu ye śāstraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ puruṣādhamāḥ na śṛṇvanti muniśreṣṭha teṣāṃ svāmī sadā yamaḥ  Hbhv na śṛṇvanti na hṛṣyanti vaiṣṇavīṃ prāpya ye kathām dhama āyur yaśo dharmaḥ santānaś caiva naśyati  Hbhv na śṛṇoti harer yas tu kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśinīm acirād eva devarṣe samūlaṃ tu vinaśyati  Hbhv dvitīyaskandhe śrīśaunakoktau BhP  bile batorukramavikramān yena śṛṇvataḥ karṇapuṭe narasya jihvāsatī dārdurikeva sūtana copagāyaty urugāyagāthāḥ  Hbhv tṛtīye śrībrahmastutau BhP  daivena te hatadhiyo bhavataḥ prasaṅgātsarvāśubhopaśamanād vimukhendriyā ye kurvanti kāmasukhaleśalavāya dīnālobhābhibhūtamanaso kuśalāni śaśvat  Hbhv BhP  tāñ chocyaśocyān avido nuśocehareḥ kathāyāṃ vimukhān aghena kṣiṇoti devo nimiṣas tu yeṣāmāyur vṛthāvādagatismṛtīnām  Hbhv śrīmaitreyoktau ca BhP  ko nāma loke puruṣārthasāravitpurākathānāṃ bhagavatkathāsudhām āpīya karṇāñjalibhir bhavāpahāmaho virajyeta vinā naretaram  Hbhv caturthe śrīpṛthustutau BhP yaśaḥ śivaṃ suśrava āryasaṅgameyadṛcchayā copaśṛṇoti te sakṛt kathaṃ guṇajño viramed vinā paśuṃśrīr yat pravavre guṇasaṅgrahecchayā  Hbhv daśamārambhe śrīparīkṣitpraśne BhP  nivṛttatarṣair upagīyamānādbhavauṣadhāc chrotramanobhirāmāt ka uttamaślokaguṇānuvādātpumān virajyeta vinā paśughnāt  Hbhv ataevoktaṃ devaiḥ pañcamaskandhe BhP  na yatra vaikuṇṭhakathāsudhāpagāna sādhavo bhāgavatās tadāśrayāḥ na yatra yajñeśamakhā mahotsavāḥsureśaloko pi na vai sa sevyatām  Hbhv atha bhagavatkathāsaktiḥato niṣevyamāṇāṃ ca sarvathā bhagavatkathām muhus tadrasikān pṛcchen mitho modavivṛddhaye  Hbhv daśamaskandhe BhP  satām ayaṃ sārabhṛtāṃ nisargoyadarthavāṇīśruticetasām api pratikṣaṇaṃ navyavad acyutasya yatstriyā viṭānām iva sādhu vārtā  Hbhv ataeva tatraiva BhP tulyaśrutatapaḥśīlās tulyasvīyārimadhyamāḥ api cakruḥ pravacanam ekaṃ śuśrūṣavo pare  Hbhv  iti atha śrībhagavaddharmapratipādanamāhātmyamtathā vaiṣṇavadharmāṃś ca kriyamānām api svayam sampṛcchet tadvidaḥ sādhūn anyonyaprītivṛddhaye  Hbhv śraddhayā bhagavaddharmān vaiṣṇavāyānupṛcchate avaśyaṃ kathayed vidvān anyathā doṣabhāg bhavet  Hbhv tad uktamnākhyāti vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaṃ viṣṇubhaktasya pṛcchataḥ kalau bhāgavato bhūtvā puṇyaṃ yāti śatābdikam  Hbhv skānde brahmanāradasaṃvādevaiṣṇave vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaṃ yo dadāti dvijottamaḥ sasāgaramahīdāne yat phalaṃ labhatedhikam  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraiva ajñānāya ca yo jñānaṃ dadyād dharmopadeśanam kṛtsnāṃ vā pṛthivīṃ dadyāt tena tulyaṃ hi tat smṛtam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare  tat kathāṃ śrāvayed yas tu tadbhaktān mānavottamaḥ godānaphalam āpnoti sa naras tena karmaṇā  Hbhv pādme devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde PadmaP  jñānam ajñāya yo dadyād vedaśāstrasamudbhavam api devās tam arcanti bhavabandhavidārakam  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye NārP satsaṅgadevārcanasatkathāsuhitopadeśe nirato manuṣyaḥ prayāti viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ yaddehāvasānecyutatulyatejāḥ  Hbhv atha bhagavaddharmāḥte ca śrībhagavaddharmā bhagavadbhaktalakṣaṇaiḥ vyañjitāḥ katicin mukhyā likhyantetra parepi te  Hbhv te tu yadyapi vikhyātāḥ śrīmadbhāgavatādiṣu tathāpi yatnād ekatra saṅgṛhyante samādhanāḥ  Hbhv te coktāḥ kāśīkhaṇḍe dvārakāmāhātmye candraśarmaṇā adya prabhṛti kartavyaṃ yan mayā kṛṣṇa tac chṛṇu ekādaśyāṃ na bhoktavyaṃ kartavyo jāgaraḥ sadā  Hbhv mahotsavaḥ prakartavyaḥ pratyahapūjanaṃ tava palārdhenāpi biddhaṃ tu bhoktavyaṃ vāsarāntare  Hbhv tvatprītyāṣṭau mayā kāryā dvādaśyo vratasaṃyutā bhaktir bhāgavatī kāryā prāṇair api dhanair api  Hbhv nityaṃ nāmasahasraṃ tu paṭhanīyaṃ tava priyam pūjā tu tulasīpatrair mayā kāryā sadaiva hi  Hbhv tulasīkāṣṭhāsambhūtā mālā kāryā sadā mayā nṛtyagītaṃ prakartavyaṃ samprāpte jāgare tava  Hbhv tulasīkāṣṭhāsambhūtacandanena vilepanam kariṣyāmi tavāgre ca guṇānāṃ tava kīrtanam  Hbhv mathurāyāṃ prakartavyaṃ pratyabdaṃ gamanaṃ mayā tatkathāśravaṇaṃ kāryaṃ tathā pustakavācanam  Hbhv nityaṃ pādodakaṃ mūrdhnā mayā dhāryaṃ prayatnataḥ naivedyabhakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kariṣyāmi yatavrataḥ  Hbhv nirmālyaṃ śirasā dhāryaṃ tvadīyaṃ sādaraṃ mayā tava dattvā yad iṣṭaṃ tu bhakṣaṇīyaṃ mudā mayā  Hbhv tathā tathā prakartavyaṃ tava tuṣṭiḥ prajāyate satyam etan mayā kṛṣṇa tavāgre parikīrtanam  Hbhv saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādena BhP  guruśuśrūṣayā bhaktyā sarvalabdhārpaṇena ca śraddhayā tatkathāyāṃ ca kīrtanair guṇakarmaṇām tatpādāmburuhadhyānāt talliṅgekṣārhaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv hariḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu bhagavān āsta īśvaraḥ iti bhūtāni manasā kāmais taiḥ sādhu mānayet  Hbhv ekādaśe ca śrīkaviyogeśvareṇa BhP ye vai bhagavatā proktā upāyā hy ātmalabdhaye añjaḥ puṃsām aviduṣāṃ viddhi bhāgavatān hi tān  Hbhv tatraiva prabuddhayogeśvareṇa BhP  sarvato manaso saṅgam ādau saṅgaṃ ca sādhuṣu dayāṃ maitrīṃ praśrayaṃ ca bhūteṣv addhā yathocitam  Hbhv śaucaṃ tapas titikṣāṃ ca maunaṃ svādhyāyam ārjavam brahmacaryam ahiṃsāṃ ca samatvaṃ dvandvasaṃjñayoḥ  Hbhv sarvatrātmeśvarānvīkṣāṃ kaivalyam aniketatām viviktacīravasanaṃ santoṣaṃ yena kenacit  Hbhv śraddhāṃ bhāgavate śāstre nindām anyatra cāpi hi manovākkarmadaṇḍaṃ ca satyaṃ śamadamāv api  Hbhv śravaṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ dhyānaṃ harer adbhutakarmaṇaḥ janmakarmaguṇānāṃ ca tadarthe khilaceṣṭitam  Hbhv iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ tapo japtaṃ vṛttaṃ yac cātmanaḥ priyam dārān sutān gṛhān prāṇān yat parasmai nivedanam  Hbhv evaṃ kṛṣṇātmanātheṣu manuṣyeṣu ca sauhṛdam paricaryāṃ cobhayatra mahatsu nṛṣu sādhuṣu  Hbhv parasparānukathanaṃ pāvanaṃ bhagavadyaśaḥmitho ratir mithas tuṣṭir nivṛttir mitha ātmanaḥ  Hbhv śrībhagavatā ca BhP  malliṅgamadbhaktajana darśanasparśanārcanam paricaryā stutiḥ prahva guṇakarmānukīrtanam  Hbhv matkathāśravaṇe śraddhā madanudhyānam uddhava sarvalābhopaharaṇaṃ dāsyenātmanivedanam  Hbhv majjanmakarmakathanaṃ mama parvānumodanam gītatāṇḍavavāditra goṣṭhībhir madgṛhotsavaḥ  Hbhv yātrā balividhānaṃ ca sarvavārṣikaparvasu vaidikī tāntrikī dīkṣā madīyavratadhāraṇam  Hbhv mamārcāsthāpane śraddhā svataḥ saṃhatya codyamaḥ udyānopavanākrīḍa puramandirakarmaṇi  Hbhv sammārjanopalepābhyāṃ sekamaṇḍalavartanaiḥ gṛhaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ mahyaṃ dāsavad yad amāyayā  Hbhv amānitvam adambhitvaṃ kṛtasyāparikīrtanam api dīpāvalokaṃ me nopayuñjyān niveditam  Hbhv yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cātipriyam ātmanaḥ tat tan nivedayen mahyaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP śraddhāmṛtakathāyāṃ me śaśvan madanukīrtanam pariniṣṭhā ca pūjāyāṃ stutibhiḥ stavanaṃ mama  Hbhv ādaraḥ paricaryāyāṃ sarvāṅgair abhivandanam madbhaktapūjābhyadhikā sarvabhūteṣu manmatiḥ  Hbhv madartheṣv aṅgaceṣṭā ca vacasā madguṇeraṇam mayy arpaṇaṃ ca manasaḥ sarvakāmavivarjanam  Hbhv madarthe rthaparityāgo bhogasya ca sukhasya ca iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ madarthaṃ yad vrataṃ tapaḥ  Hbhv api cāgre BhP  kuryāt sarvāṇi karmāṇi madarthaṃ śanakaiḥ smaran mayy arpitamanaścitto maddharmātmamanoratiḥ  Hbhv deśān puṇyān āśrayeta madbhaktaiḥ sādhubhiḥ śritān devāsuramanuṣyeṣu madbhaktācaritāni ca  Hbhv pṛthak satreṇa vā mahyaṃ parvayātrāmahotsavān kārayed gītanṛtyādyair mahārājavibhūtibhiḥ  Hbhv mām eva sarvabhūteṣu bahir antar apāvṛtam īkṣetātmani cātmānaṃ yathā kham amalāśayaḥ  Hbhv atha śrībhagavaddharmamāhātmyamuktaṃ ca saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādena BhP  evaṃ nirjitaṣaḍvargaiḥ kriyate bhaktir īśvare vāsudeve bhagavati yayā saṃlabhyate ratiḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe śrīnāradena BhP  śruto nupaṭhito dhyāta ādṛto vānumoditaḥsadyaḥ punāti saddharmo devaviśvadruho pi hi  Hbhv tatraiva śrīkaviyogeśvareṇa BhP  yān āsthāya naro rājan na pramādyeta karhicit dhāvan nimīlya vā netre na skhalen na pated iha  Hbhv śrīprabuddhayogeśvareṇa BhP  iti bhāgavatān dharmān śikṣan bhaktyā tadutthayā nārāyaṇaparo māyām añjas tarati dustarām  Hbhv śrībhagavatā ca BhP  evaṃ dharmair manuṣyāṇām uddhavātmanivedinām mayi sañjāyate bhaktiḥ ko nyo rtho syāvaśiṣyate  Hbhv kiṃ cāgre BhP  na hy aṅgopakrame dhvaṃso maddharmasyoddhavāṇv apimayā vyavasitaḥ samyaṅ nirguṇatvād anāśiṣaḥ  Hbhv  itialābhe satsabhāyās tu śuśrūṣuṃ ca nijālaye devālaye vā śāstrajñaḥ kīrtayed bhagavatkathām  Hbhv atha śrībhagavallīlākathākīrtanamāhātmyam uktaṃ ca skānde śrībhagavatā arjunaṃ prati matkathā kurute yas tu vaiṣṇavānāṃ sadāgrataḥ iha bhogān avāpnoti tathā mokṣaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv prathamaskandhe BhP  śrīnāradenaidaṃ hi puṃsas tapasaḥ śrutasya vāsviṣṭasya sūktasya ca buddhidattayoḥ avicyuto rthaḥ kavibhir nirūpitoyaduttamaślokaguṇānuvarṇanam  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP  etad dhy āturacittānāṃ mātrāsparśecchayā muhuḥ bhavasindhuplavo dṛṣṭo haricaryānuvarṇanam  Hbhv ekādaśe śrīśukenāpi BhP  itthaṃ harer bhagavato rucirāvatāravīryāṇi bālacaritāni ca śantamāni anyatra ceha ca śrutāni gṛṇan manuṣyobhaktiṃ parāṃ paramahaṃsagatau labheta  Hbhv ataeva śrīprahlādena nṛsiṃhastutāv uktam BhP  so haṃ priyasya suhṛdaḥ paradevatāyālīlākathās tava nṛsiṃha viriñcagītāḥ añjas titarmy anugṛṇan guṇavipramuktodurgāṇi te padayugālayahaṃsasaṅgaḥ  Hbhv gopikābhir api gītam BhP  tava kathāmṛtaṃ taptajīvanaṃkavibhir īḍitaṃ kalmaṣāpaham śravaṇamaṅgalaṃ śrīmadātataṃbhuvi grṇanti te bhuridā janāḥ  Hbhv kirtanepy atra taj jñeyaṃ māhātmyaṃ śravaṇesya yat sidhyati śravaṇam nūnaṃ kīrtanāt svayam eva hi  Hbhv śāstrābhyāsasya cābhāve pūrveṣāṃ lokaviśrutām satām ādhunikānāṃ ca kathāṃ bandhuṣu kīrtayet  Hbhv iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāsesatsaṅgamo nāmadaśamo vilāsaḥ  NityakrtyasamapanaVilasaekādaśavilāsaḥnityakṛtyasamāpanaḥśrīcaitanyaṃ prapadye taṃ mahāścaryaprabhāvakam prasāde yasya duṣṭo pi bhagavadbhaktimān bhavet  Hbhv tato dināntyabhāgeṣu bāhyeṣu surasadmasu yātrāṃ kṛtvā dvijaḥ sandhyām upāsīta yathāvidhi  Hbhv śrīviṣṇupurāṇe aurvasagarasaṃvāde ViP   dināntasandhyāṃ sūryeṇa pūrvā mṛkṣair yutāṃ budhaḥ upatiṣṭhed yathānyāyaṃ samyag ācamya pārthiva  Hbhv sarvakālam upasthānaṃ sandhyāyāḥ pārthiveṣyate anyatra sūtikāśaucavibhramāturabhītitaḥ  Hbhv upatiṣṭhanti vai sandhyāṃ ye na pūrvāṃ na paścimām vrajanti te durātmānas tāmisraṃ narakaṃ nṛpa  Hbhv iti tato yathāśramācāraṃ karma sāyantanaṃ kṛtī nirvartya pūrvavat kuryād bhaktyā bhagavadarcanam  Hbhv śrīkṛṣṇabhaktyāsaktyā tu sandhyopāsyādikaṃ yadi patet karma na pātityadoṣaśaṅkā kathañcana  Hbhv atha śrībhagavadbhaktānāṃ karmapātityaparihāraḥpādme  śrībhagavaduktau matkarma kurvatāṃ puṃsāṃ kriyālopo bhaved yadi teṣāṃ karmāṇi kurvanti tisraḥ koṭyo maharṣayaḥ  Hbhv ādipurāṇe ca smaranti mama nāmāni ye tyaktvā karma cākhilam teṣāṃ karmāṇi kurvanti ṛṣayo bhagavatparāḥ  Hbhv iti mṛduśraddhasya bhaktasya prauḍhatām anupeyuṣaḥ kiṃcit karmādhikāritvāt karmāsyaitat prapañcitam  Hbhv prauḍhaśraddhasya bhaktasyakarmasv anadhikārataḥ pātityaṃ na bhavaty eva lekhanīyaṃ tadagrataḥ  Hbhv kiṃcid dhyānādibhedena trisandhyaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak proktaḥ pūjāvidhiḥ prājñais tattatkāmāśusiddhaye  Hbhv atha trikālārcanavidhiviśeṣataḥśrīgautamīyatantre ārādhanavidhiṃ vakṣye prātaḥkāle viśeṣataḥ varaṃ vṛndāvanaṃ dhyāyet puṇyavṛkṣādisevitam  Hbhv punnāgair nāgavṛkṣaiś ca panasaiś caiva kāñcanaiḥ bakulaiś caiva bilvaiś ca vanyaiḥ kurvakair api  Hbhv sarvartukusumopetaiḥ puṣpāvanataśākhibhiḥ tanmadhye pulinaṃ dhyāyed bahupuṣpakacampakam  Hbhv dhūpadipair vitānena puṣpamālāvibhūṣitam muktādāmapatākābhir vanyapuṣpair alaṅkṛtam  Hbhv tanmadhye kalpavṛkṣasya cchāyāyāṃ paṅkajāsane susthitaṃ veṇugītāḍhyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Hbhv vanamālāparivṛtaṃ gopikāśataveṣṭitam devāsuraiś ca siddhaiś ca gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ  Hbhv yakṣair vidyādharagaṇair vihagair bhuvi saṃsthitaiḥ brahmarṣibhiḥ stūyamānaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ caiva śucismitam  Hbhv nānāvidhaiś ca gopālair mṛgapakṣivibhūṣitam lelihyamānaṃ praṇayāt paśūnāṃ śatakoṭibhiḥ  Hbhv indīvaranibhaṃ divyaṃ sundaraṃ tv indirālayam sampūrṇacandravadanaṃ padmapatranibhekṣaṇam  Hbhv padmābhapāṇipādaṃ ca padmarāgavarārcitam śaraṇyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ gopīnāṃ prāṇavallabham  Hbhv evaṃ dhyātvārcayen nityaṃ ṣoḍaśenopacārataḥ dugdhaṃ ca dadhikhaṇḍena sahitaṃ saṃnivedayet  Hbhv sauvarṇapātre gopānāṃ grāsaṃ kāṃsye nivedayet evaṃ samarcayed bhaktyā japan mantraṃ samāhitaḥ  Hbhv madhyāhne sampravakṣyāmi pūjāṃ sarvārthasiddhidām sauvarṇaparvate mūle dhātubhiḥ samalaṅkṛte  Hbhv puṇyavṛkṣasamākīrṇe puṇyapakṣininādite padmotpalādisaṅkīrṇe vāpībhiḥ samalaṅkṛte  Hbhv tasmin satpuline ramye chāyāyāṃ paṅkajāsane sauvarṇamaṇḍape samyagvitānādivibhūṣite  Hbhv mālādiracite ramye maṇibhiḥ puṣpaśobhitaiḥ suvarṇaratnasandohair antarāntaraśobhite  Hbhv siṃhāsane samāsīnaṃ viśrāntaṃ kaṃsasūdanam muktāmayaiḥ surucirair hārair dāmavibhūṣitam  Hbhv dhyātvā samyag viśuddhātmā jātīpuṣpaiḥ samarcayet mahārajatapātre tu naivedyānnaṃ nivedayet  Hbhv dadyād grāsaṃ sakhīnāṃ ca gopīnāṃ vijitendriyaḥ devakīparamānandam evaṃ dhyāyet sukhāsanam  Hbhv rātripūjāvidhiṃ vakṣye rukmiṇīvallabhasya ca adhastāt kalpavṛkṣasya sarvapuṣpaphalasya ca  Hbhv ratnamaṇḍapamadhyasthaṃ divyapītāmbaraṃ harim divyacandanaliptāṅgaṃ divyābharaṇabhūṣitam  Hbhv anekadivyamālābhir maṇḍitaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam ratnamaṇḍapamadhyasthaṃ sundaraṃ sundarasmitam  Hbhv śobhayantaṃ svavapuṣā sarvalokān nijaśriyā gopījanānāṃ hṛdayavallabhaṃ proktavarcasam  Hbhv sugandhipuṣpair ārādhyaṃ śrīkṛṣṇaṃ sarvanāyakam rājate tu payaḥ śuddhaṃ pakvaṃ pātre nivedayet  Hbhv evam abhyarcya manasā japen mantraṃ samāhitaḥ kālatrayārcane caiva sahasraṃ sāṣṭakaṃ japet eṣa nityakramaḥ proktaḥ kṛṣṇamantrasya sūribhiḥ  Hbhv tatraivādau saṃkṣiptatrikālapūjoktyanantarammanasā vā samabhyarcya triṣu sandhyāsu saṃyamī pratyahaṃ tu japen mantram aṣṭottarasahasrakam asāmarthye japen mantraṃ nityam aṣṭaśataṃ tathā  Hbhv iti atha naktaṃ kṛtyānitato yathāsampradāyaṃ homaṃ niṣpādya vaiṣṇavaḥ gītanṛtyādikaṃ bhaktyā vidhāya prārthayet prabhum  Hbhv tathā coktambalīyasā padā svāmin padavīm avadhāraya āgaccha śayanasthānaṃ priyābhiḥ saha keśava  Hbhv iti evaṃ prārthya samarpyāsmai pāduke śayanālayam ānīya devaṃ tatratyān upacārān prakalpayet  Hbhv viśeṣato rpayet tatra ghanaṃ dugdhaṃ saśarkaram tāmbūlaṃ ca sakarpūraṃ divyamālyānulepanam  Hbhv itthaṃ bhaktyā samārādhyaṃ bhagavantaṃ svaśaktitaḥ tatprītyai sarvakarmāṇi tat phalaṃ vārpayet kṛtī  Hbhv athāhorātrākhilakarmārpaṇavidhiḥekādaśaskandhe BhP  kāyena vācā manasendriyair vābuddhyātmanā vānusṛtasvabhāvāt karoti yad yat sakalaṃ parasmainārāyaṇāyeti samarpayet tat  Hbhv kiṃ cātra sādhu vāsādhu vā karma yad yad ācaritaṃ mayā tat sarvaṃ bhagavan viṣṇo gṛhāṇārādhanaṃ param  Hbhv kiṃ caapāṃ samīpe śayanāsane gṛhedivā ca rātrau ca yathā ca gacchatā yad asti kiṃcit sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ mayājanārdanas tena kṛtena tuṣyatu  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ tṛtīyaskandhe brahmāṇaṃ prati śrībhagavatā BhP  pūrtena tapasā yajñair dānair yogasamādhinā rāddhaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ puṃsāṃ matprītis tattvavinmatam  Hbhv iti ittham ārādhayen nityaṃ bhagavantaṃ yathā vidhi nyāyārjitāptavittena samagraphalasiddhaye  Hbhv atha pūjāphalasamprāptyupāyaḥdaśamaskandhe BhP  ayaṃ svastyayanaḥ panthā dvijāter gṛhamedhinaḥ yac chraddhayāptavittena śuklenejyeta pūruṣaḥ  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ canyāyāj jitaiḥ sādhanaiś ca dānahomārcanādikam kuryān na ced adho yāti bhaktyā kurvann api dvija  Hbhv iti yatnāt siddhair nijaiḥ śuddhair dravyair dhanyo rcayet prabhum pūjādravyāṇy aśaktaś ced dahyād īkṣeta vārcanam  Hbhv athāśaktasya pūjāprāptyupāyaḥagastyasaṃhitāyāṃārādhanāsamarthyaś ced dadyād arcanasādhanam yo dātuṃ naiva śaknoti kuryād arcanadarśanam  Hbhv nistārāya tad evālaṃ bhavābdher munisattama naikaṃ ca yasya vidyeta so dho yāty eva nānyathā  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraivayas tu bhaktyā prayatnena svayaṃ sampādya cākhilam sādhanaṃ cārcayed vidvān samagraṃ labhate phalam  Hbhv yo rcayed vidhivad bhaktyā parānītaiś ca sādhanaiḥ pūjāphalārdham eva syān na samagraṃ phalaṃ labhet  Hbhv kiṃ ca pādme śrīkṛṣṇasatyabhāmāsaṃvādīyakārttikamāhātmye dharmoddeśena yo dravyam aparaṃ yācate naraḥ tatpuṇyakarmajaṃ tasya dhanadas tv āpnuyāt phalam  Hbhv atha darśanamāhātmyampādme śrīpulastyabhagīrathasaṃvādepūjitaṃ pūjyamānaṃ ca ye paśyanti janārdanam kapilāśatadānasya nityaṃ bhavati tat phalam  Hbhv āgneyepūjitaṃ pūjyamānaṃ vā yo paśyed bhaktito harim śraddhayā modayed yas tu so pi yāgaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv sampūjyamānaṃ vidhinā yaḥ paśyet śraddhayā harim so pi yāgaphalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ prāpnuyāt nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv dṛṣṭvā sampūjitaṃ devaṃ nṛtyamāno numodayet asaṃśayamatiḥ śuddhaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati  Hbhv atha śrībhagavanmūrtidarśananityatāviṣṇudharmottaretāvad bhramanti saṃsāre manuṣyā mandabuddhayaḥ yāvad rūpaṃ na paśyanti keśavasya mahātmanaḥ  Hbhv pādme ca
