tatraivapūjyamānaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ ye na paśyanti vaiṣṇavāḥ teṣāṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ daiteyāyopatiṣṭhati  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraiva nārāyaṇanāradasaṃvāde pūjāvidhikathaneyatra kutrāpi pratimāṃ vedadharmasamanvitām na paśyanti janā gatvā te daṇḍyā yamakiṅkaraiḥ  Hbhv atha bhagavadarthe dravyadānamāhātmyamskāndeviṣṇum uddiśya yat kiñcid viṣṇubhaktāya dīyate dānaṃ tad vimalaṃ proktaṃ kevalaṃ mokṣasādhanam  Hbhv kaurmeyat kiñcid deyam īśānam uddiśya brāhmaṇāya ca prabhave viṣṇave cātha tad anantaphalaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare not foundanugraheṇa mahatā pretasya patitasya ca nārāyaṇabaliḥ kāryas tenāsyānugraho bhavet  Hbhv anādinidhano devaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ akṣayaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣas tatra dattaṃ na naśyati  Hbhv yathā kathañcid yad dattaṃ devadeve janārdane avināśi tu tad viddhi pātram eko janārdanaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva tṛtīyakāṇḍe not foundsāmānyabhaktyā yad dattaṃ tad dhi padbhyāṃ pratīcchati ekāntabhāvopagamair mūrdhnā divjavarottamāḥ  Hbhv ananto bhagavān viṣṇus tasya kāmavivarjitaiḥ yad eva dīyate kiñcit tad evākṣayam ucyate  Hbhv padbhyāṃ pratīcchate devaḥ sakāmena niveditam mūrdhnā pratīcchate dattam akāmena dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv tathaivoktaṃ mokṣadharme śrīnāradena not foundbrahmā yad ṛṣayaś caiva svayaṃ paśupatiś ca yat anye ca vibudhaśreṣṭhā daityadānavarākṣasāḥ  Hbhv nāgāḥ suvarṇāḥ gandharvāḥ siddhā rājarṣayas tathā havyaṃ kravyaṃ ca satataṃ vidhiyuktaṃ prabhuñjate kṛtsnaṃ tu tasya devasya caraṇāv upatiṣṭhati  Hbhv yāḥ kriyāḥ saṃprayuktās tu ekāntagatabuddhibhiḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ śirasā devaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vai svayam  Hbhv brahmavaivarteekām api naro dhenuṃ savatsāṃ vidhipūrvakam dattvoddeśena kṛṣṇasya prāpnoty evābhivāñchitam  Hbhv nārasiṃheyo gāṃ payasvinīṃ viṣṇoḥ kṛṣṇavarṇāṃ prayacchati aśvamedhasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpya hariṃ vrajet  Hbhv sarvapāpair virahitaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ gavāṃ sahasradānasya prāpyaṃ divyaṃ vrajet  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare gavāṃ lokam avāpnoti dhenuṃ dattvā payasvinīm dadhikṣīraghṛtārthāya vāsudevasya cālaye dattvā gāṃ madhuparkāya mahat phalam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv jalāśayaṃ tathā kṛtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv sapuṣpaiḥ saphalair vṛkṣair yutaṃ kṛtvā jalāśayam udyānaiḥ padminīṣaṇḍair āśramaiś ca manoharaiḥ śvedadvīpam avāpnoti punar nāvartate tataḥ  Hbhv devāgre kārayed yas tu ramyām āpaṇavīthikām rājā bhavati lokeṣu vijitārir mahāśayāḥ  Hbhv nagaraṃ ca tathā kṛtvā sāmrājyam adhigacchati śivikāṃ ye prayacchanti te prayānty amarāvatīm  Hbhv aśvadāḥ svargalokasthā rājante divi sūryavat kavīndradānāc chakrasya cirāl lokācyuto naraḥ  Hbhv rājā bhavati dharmātmā pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ  Hbhv viṣṇor āyatane dattvā tatkathāpustakaṃ naraḥ brahmalokam avāpnoti bahukālasthiraṃ dvijāḥ  Hbhv pustakāṃś ca tathaivānyān yaḥ pradadyān naras tv iha sārasvatam avāpnoti lokaṃ kālaṃ tathā bahum  Hbhv svabhṛtaṃ vācakaṃ kṛtvā devāgāre naraḥ sadā vidyādānaphalaṃ prāpya brahmaloke mahīyate  Hbhv viṣṇoḥ śaṅkhapradānena vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute mānuṣyam āsādya tathā khyātaśabdaś ca jāyate  Hbhv ghaṇṭāpradānena tathā mahadyaśa upāśnute kūṭāgāraṃ tathā dattvā nagarādhipatir bhavet  Hbhv dattvā tu devakarmārthaṃ navāṃ vedīṃ dṛḍhāṃ śubhām pārthivatvam avāpnoti vedī hi pṛthivī yataḥ  Hbhv toraṇaṃ kārayed yas tu devadevālaye naraḥ lokeṣu tasya dvārāṇi bhavanti vivṛtāni vai  Hbhv devaveśmopayogyāni śilpabhāṇḍāni yo naraḥ dadyād vā vādyabhāṇḍāni gaṇeśatvam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv yaḥ kumbhaṃ devakarmārthaṃ naro dadyān navaṃ śubham vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnoti sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv caturaḥ kalasān dadyād yas tu devagṛhe naraḥ catuḥsamudravalayāṃ sa hi bhuṅkte vasundharām  Hbhv dattvaikam api viprendrāḥ kalasaṃ susamāhitaḥ rājā bhavati dharmātmā bhūtale nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv vāridhānīṃ tathā dattvā vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute kamaṇḍalupradānena yajñasya phalam āpnuyāt  Hbhv mātrāṃ tu paricaryārthaṃ nivedya haraye tathā sarvakāmasamṛddhasya yajñasya phalam aśnute  Hbhv tālavṛntapradānena nirvṛtiṃ prāpnuyāt parām mālyādhāraṃ tathā dattvā dhūpādhāraṃ tathaiva ca gandhādhāraṃ tathā pātraṃ kāmānāṃ pātratāṃ vrajet  Hbhv saumdrajāni pātrāṇi dattvā vai taijasāni vā pātraṃ bhavati kāmānāṃ vidyānāṃ ca dhanasya ca  Hbhv śayanāsanadānena sthitiṃ vindati śāśvatīm uttaracchadadānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv naraḥ suvarṇadānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt rūpyado rūpam āpnoti viśeṣād bhuvi durlabham  Hbhv ratnadānena lokeṣu prāmāṇyam upagacchati anaḍvāhapradānena daśadhenuphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv ājñāvimahiṣoṣṭrāṇāṃ dānam aśvatarasya ca sahasraguṇitaṃ dānāt pūrvaproktāt prakīrtitam  Hbhv vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnoti dattvā vastuṃ dvijottamāḥ avipradānāc ca tathā tam enaṃ lokam aśnute  Hbhv uṣṭraṃ vā gardabhaṃ vāpi kharaṃ vā yaḥ prayacchati alakāṃ sa samāsādya yakṣendraiḥ saha modate  Hbhv āraṇyamṛgajātīnāṃ tathā dānāc ca pakṣiṇām agniṣṭomam avāpnoti subhagaś ca tathā bhavet  Hbhv dāsaṃ dattvā sukhe loke neṣṭabhraṣṭo vijāyate dāsīṃ dattvā tathā viprā nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv gaṇikāṃ ye prayacchanti nṛtyagītaviśāradām sarvaduḥkhavinirmuktās te prayānty amarāvatīm  Hbhv nṛtyaṃ dattvā tathāpnoti rudralokam asaṃśayam  Hbhv prekṣaṇīyapradānena śakraloke mahīyate gītaṃ dattvā tathāpnoti brahmalokam asaṃśayam  Hbhv dundubhiṃ ye prayacchanti kīrtimanto bhavanti te  Hbhv dattvā dhānyāni bījāni śasyāni vividhāni ca rūpakāni ca tāny eva prāpnuyāt surapūjyatām  Hbhv dattvā śākāni ramyāni viśokas tv abhijāyate dattvā ca vyañjanārthāya tathopakaraṇāni ca  Hbhv puṣpavṛkṣaṃ tathā dattvā deśasyādhipatir bhavet phalavṛkṣaṃ tathā nagarādhipatir bhavet  Hbhv tathāsugandhasādhanānīha paṭavāsāni yo naraḥ dadāti devadevasya so śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv kaṅkatasya pradānena viromas tv abhijāyate kūrcaprasādhanaṃ kṛtvā paraṃ maṅgalam aśnute  Hbhv vismāpanīyaṃ yat kiñcid dattvātyantaṃ sukhaṃ labhet  Hbhv vastrālaṅkaraṇādīnāṃ kṛṣṇārpaṇaphalaṃ ca yat upacāraprayoge prāk tatra tatra vyalekhi tat  Hbhv upacārāś ca vividhāḥ śrīmadbhagavadarcane śakyaśaktyādibhedena tāntrikair vaiṣṇavir matāḥ  Hbhv atha vividhopacārāḥāgameāsanasvāgate sārghye pādyam ācamanīyakam madhuparkācamasnānavasanābharaṇāni ca  Hbhv sugandhasumanodhūpadīpanaivedyavandanam prayojayed aracanājñām upacārāṃs tu ṣoḍaśa  Hbhv arghyaṃ ca pādyācamanamadhuparkācamāny api gandhādayo nivedyāntā upacārā daśa kramāt  Hbhv gandhādibhir nivedyāntaiḥ pūjā pañcopacārikī saparyās trividhāḥ proktās tāsām ekāṃ samācaret  Hbhv kvacic caāsanāvāhanaṃ caiva pādyārghyācamanīyakam snānaṃ vāso bhūṣaṇaṃ ca gandhaḥ puṣpaṃ ca dhūpakaḥ  Hbhv pradīpaś caiva naivedyaṃ puṣpāñjalir ataḥ param pradakṣiṇaṃ namaskāro visargaś caiva ṣoḍaśa  Hbhv kecic cāhuś catuḥṣaṣṭim upacārān mamārcane teṣv anekaprakāreṣu prakāraiko tra likhyate  Hbhv sukhasuptasya kṛṣṇasya prātar ādau prabodhanam vedaghoṣaṇavīṇāvivādyair vandistavair api  Hbhv jayaśabdā namaskārā maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ āsanaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca pādyārghyācamanāny api  Hbhv tataś ca madhuparkāḍhyācamanaṃ pādukārpaṇam aṅgamārjanam abhyaṅgodvartane snapanaṃ jalaḥ  Hbhv kṣīreṇa dadhnā haviṣā madhunā sitayā tathā mantrapūtaiḥ punar vārbhir aṅgavāso tha vāsasī  Hbhv upavītaṃ punaāc cācamanīyaṃ cānulepanam bhūṣaṇaṃ kusumaṃ dhūpo dīpo dṛṣṭyapasāraṇam  Hbhv naivedyaṃ mukhavāsas tu tāmbūlaṃ śayanottamam keśaprasādhanaṃ divyavastrāṇi mukuṭaṃ mahat  Hbhv divyagandhānulepaś ca kaustubhādivibhūṣaṇam vicitradivyapuṣpāṇi maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv ādarśaḥ sukhayānena maṇḍapāgamanotsavaḥ siṃhāsanopaveśaś ca pādyādyaiḥ punar arcanam  Hbhv punar dhūpādyarpaṇena prāgvan naivedyam uttamam tataś ca divyatāmbūlamahānīrājanaṃ punaḥ  Hbhv cāmaravyajanacchatraṃ gītaṃ vādyaṃ ca nartanam pradakṣiṇaṃ namaskāraḥ stutiḥ śrīcaraṇābjayoḥ  Hbhv tayoś ca sthāpanaṃ mūrdhni tīrthanirmālyadhāraṇam ucchiṣṭabhojanaṃ pādasevoddeśopaveśanam  Hbhv naktaṃ śayyāvinirmāṇaṃ divyair vividhasādhanaiḥ hastapradānaṃ śayanasthānāgamamahotsavaḥ  Hbhv śayyopaveśanaṃ śrīmatpādakṣālanapūrvakam gandhaprasūnatāmbūlārpaṇanīrājanotsavaḥ  Hbhv śeṣaparyaṅkaśayanapādasaṃvāhanādikam krameṇaite catuḥṣaṣṭhir upacārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  Hbhv sadācārānusāreṇa yad yad ācaryate svayam nityakarmādikaṃ tat tat śrīkṛṣṇasyāpi kārayet  Hbhv ato trālikhitaṃ yad yad upacārādikaṃ param sarvaṃ tat tac ca jānīyāl lokarītyanusārataḥ  Hbhv uktānāṃ copacārāṇām abhāve bhagavān sadā bhaktenārcyo yathālabdhais tair antarbhāvitair api  Hbhv athālabdhasamādhānamtantreupacāroktavastūnām upasaṅgrahaṇe vidhiḥ dravyāṇām apy abhāve tu puṣpākṣatayavaiḥ kriyāḥ  Hbhv arcopacāravastūnām abhāve samupasthite nirmalenodakenaiva dravyasampūrṇatā bhavet  Hbhv upacāreṣu dravyeṣu yat kiñcid duṣkaraṃ budhaḥ tat sarvaṃ manasā buddhyā puṣpakṣepeṇa kalpayet  Hbhv eteṣu copacāreṣu vittaśāṭhyavivarjitam yad asampannam eteṣāṃ manasā tu prakalpayet  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ śrītulasīmāhātmyeyad yan nyūnaṃ bhavaty eva rāmārādhanasādhanam tulasīdalamātreṇa yuktaṃ tat paripūryate  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde dravyaiḥ prasiddhair madyāgaḥ pratimādiṣv amāyinaḥ bhaktasya ca yathālabdhair hṛdi bhāvena caiva hi  Hbhv tato nujñāṃ prabhoḥ prārthya daṇḍavat taṃ praṇamya ca sāyaṃ bhuktvā yathānyāyaṃ sukhaṃ svapyāt prabhuṃ smaret  Hbhv atha śayanavidhiḥāgamenirguṇo niṣkalaś caiva viśvamūrtidharo vyayaḥ anādyante sadānante phaṇāmaṇiviśobhite kṣīrābdhimadhye yaḥ śete sa māṃ rakṣatu mādhavaḥ  Hbhv sabāhyābhyantaraṃ deham āpādatalamastakam sarvātmā sarvaśaktiś ca pātu māṃ garuḍadhvajaḥ  Hbhv iti rakṣāṃ puraskṛtya svaped viṣṇum anusmaran  Hbhv kiṃ cānyatraadbhiḥ śaucavidhiṃ vidhāya caraṇau prakṣāly copaspṛśeddviḥ saṃsmṛtya jagatpatiṃ vrajapatiṃ śrīvallabhīvallabham rādhāyāḥ suciraṃ pibantam amṛtāsārāyamāṇāṃ giraṃvastreṇāṅghriyugaṃ pramṛjyaa śayanaṃ tv āpādya sadyaḥ svapet  Hbhv kiṃ carāmaṃ skandaṃ hanumantaṃ vainateyaṃ vṛkodaram śayane yaḥ smaren nityaṃ duḥsvapnas tasya naśyati  Hbhv api ca skāndapādmayoḥ PadmaP ṛtukālābhigāmī yaḥ svadāranirataś ca yaḥ sarvadā brahmacārīha vijñeyaḥ sa gṛhāśramī  Hbhv ṛtuḥ ṣoḍaśayāminyaś catasras tāsu garhitāḥ putradās tāsu yā yugmā ayugmāḥ kanyakāpradāḥ  Hbhv tyaktvā candramasaṃ duṣṭaṃ maghāṃ mūlaṃ vihāya ca śuciḥ sannirviśet patnīṃ puṃnāmarkṣe viśeṣataḥ śuciṃ putraṃ prasūyeta puruṣārthaprasādhanam  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe aurvasagarasaṃvāde kṛtapādādiśaucaś ca bhuktvā sāyaṃ tato gṛhī gacchec chayyām asphuṭitām ekadārumayīṃ nṛpa  Hbhv nāviśālāṃ na vai bhagnāṃ nāsamāṃ malināṃ na ca na ca jantumayīṃ śayyām adhitiṣṭhed anāstṛtām  Hbhv prācyāṃ diśi śiraḥ śastaṃ yāmyāyām athavā nṛpa sadaiva svapataḥ puṃso viparītaṃ tu rogadam  Hbhv ṛtāv upagamaḥ śastaḥ svapatnyām avanīpate punnāmarkṣe śubhe kāle jyeṣṭhayugmāsu rātriṣu  Hbhv nāsnātāṃ tu striyaṃ gacchen nāturāṃ na rajasvalām nāniṣṭāṃ na prakupitāṃ nāpraśastāṃ na gurviṇīm  Hbhv nādakṣiṇāṃ nānyakāmāṃ nākāmāṃ nānyayoṣitam kṣutkṣāmām atibhuktāṃ vā svayaṃ caibhir guṇair yutaḥ  Hbhv snātaḥ sraggandhadhṛkprīto nādhyātaḥ kṣudhito pi vā sakāmaḥ sānurāgaś ca vyavāyaṃ puruṣo vrajet  Hbhv caturdaśyaṣṭamī caiva amāvasyātha pūrṇimā parvāṇy etāni rājendra ravisaṅkrāntir eva ca  Hbhv tailastrīmāṃsasambhogī parvasv eteṣu vai pumān viṇmūtrabhojanaṃ nāma prayāti narakaṃ nṛpa  Hbhv nānyayonāv ayonau vā nopayuktauṣadhas tathā devadvijagurūṇāṃ ca vyavāyī nāśramī bhavet  Hbhv caityacatvaratīrtheṣu naiva goṣṭhe catuṣpathe naiva śmaśānopavane salileṣu mahīpate  Hbhv proktaparvasvaśeṣeṣu naiva bhūpāla sandhyayoḥ gacched vyavāyaṃ matimān na mūtroccārapīḍitaḥ  Hbhv paradārān na gaccheta manasāpi kadācana kim u vācāsthibandho pi nāsti teṣu vyavāyinām  Hbhv mṛto narakam abhyeti hīyate cātra cāyuṣaḥ paradāraratiḥ puṃsām ubhayatrāpi bhītidā  Hbhv iti matvā svadāreṣu ṛtumatsu budho vrajet yathoktadoṣahīneṣu sakāmeṣv anṛtāv api  Hbhv iti teṣāṃ bhaktyupayogitvaṃ na syād yadyapi karmaṇām tathāpi kṛta ullekho gṛhiṣv āvaśyakaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv itthaṃ hi prātaru tthānāt pratyahaṃ śayanāvadhi śrīkṛṣṇaṃ pūjayan siddhasarvārtho sya priyo bhavet  Hbhv atha śrībhagavadarcanamāhātmyamśrīkūrmapurāṇena viṣṇvārādhanāt puṇyaṃ vidyate karma vaidikam tasmād anādimadhyāntaṃ nityam ārādhayed dharim  Hbhv tatraiva bhṛgvādīn prati sākṣāt śrībhagavaduktauyercayiṣyanti māṃ bhaktyā nityaṃ kaliyuge dvijāḥ vidhinā vedadṛṣṭena te gamiṣyanti tatpadam  Hbhv viṣṇurahasyeśrīviṣṇor arcanaṃ ye tu prakurvanti narā bhuvi te yānti śāśvataṃ viṣṇor ānandaṃ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv iti tatraiva śrībhagavaduktauna me dhyānaratāḥ samyagyoginaḥ parituṣṭaye tathā bhavanti devarṣe kriyāyogaratā yathā  Hbhv kriyāyogo hi mebhīṣṭaḥ parayogāt svanuṣṭhitāt tuṣṭir me sambhavet pumbhir bhaktimadbhir amatsaraiḥ  Hbhv yercayanti narā nityaṃ kriyāyogaratāḥ svayam dhyāyanti ye ca māṃ nityaṃ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ kriyā matāḥ  Hbhv kriyāhīnasya devarṣe tathā dhyānaṃ na muktidam na tathā māṃ vidur viprā dhyāninas tattvato vinā kriyāyogaratāḥ samyag labhante māṃ samādhinā  Hbhv yathā hi kāmadaṃ nṝṇāṃ mama tuṣṭikaraṃ param bhaktiyogaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ śubham  Hbhv saṃvatsareṇa yat puṇyaṃ labhante dhyānino mama prāpyante tad ihaikāhāt kriyāyogaparair naraiḥ  Hbhv ādipurāṇena karmasadṛśaṃ dhyānaṃ na karmasadṛśaṃ phalam na karmasadṛśas tyāgo na karmasadṛśaṃ tapaḥ na karmasadṛśaṃ puṇyaṃ na karmasadṛśī gatiḥ  Hbhv nāradīye NārP bhaktigrāhyo hṛṣīkeśo na dhanair dharaṇīdhara bhaktyā saṃpūjito viṣṇuḥ pradadāti manoratham  Hbhv tasmād viprāḥ sadā bhaktiḥ kartavyā cakrapāṇinaḥ janenāpi jagannāthaḥ pūjitaḥ kleśahā bhavet  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodaye kṛtāpi dambhahāsyārthe sevā tārayate janān viphalā nānyakarmeva kṛpāluḥ ko nv ataḥ paraḥ  Hbhv brahmavaivarte sa samārādhito devo muktikṛt syād yathā tathā anicchayāpi hutabhuk saṃspṛṣṭo dahati dvija  Hbhv dhanavān putravān bhogī yaśasvī bhayavarjitaḥ medhāvī matimān prājño bhavaty ārādhanād dhareḥ  Hbhv skānde sanatkumāramarkaṇḍeyasaṃvāde viśiṣṭaḥ sarvadharmāc ca dharmo viṣṇvarcanaṃ nṝṇām sarvayajñatapohomas tīrthasnānaiś ca yat phalam  Hbhv tat phalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ viṣṇuṃ sampūjya cāpnuyāt tasmāt sarvaprayatnena nārāyaṇam ihārcayet  Hbhv tatraiva śrīśivomāsaṃvāde yaḥ pradadyad dvijendraya sarvaṃ bhumiṃ sasagaram arcayed yaḥ sakṛd viṣṇuṃ tat phalaṃ labhate naraḥ  Hbhv masardham api yo viṣṇuṃ nairantaryena pūjayet puruṣottamaḥ sa vijñeyo viṣṇubhakto na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv madhyandinagate surye yo viṣṇuṃ paripūjayet vasupūrṇamahidatur yat punyaṃ tad avāpnuyāt  Hbhv prātar utthaya yo viṣṇuṃ satataṃ paripūjayet agnistomasahasrasya labhate phalam uttamam  Hbhv yo viṣṇuṃ prayato bhūtvā sayaṃkale samarcayet gavaṃ medhasya yajñasya phalam āpnoti durlabham  Hbhv evaṃ sarvāsu velāsu avelāsu ca keśavam sampūjayan naro bhaktyā sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv kiṃ punar yo rcayen nityaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam dhanyaḥ saḥ kṛtakṛtyaś ca viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv kiṃ ca dīkṣāmātreṇa kṛṣṇasya narā mokṣaṃ labhanti vai kiṃ punar ye sadā bhaktyā pūjayanty acyutaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrībrahmanaradasaṃvādesaṃsāresmin mahāghore janmamṛtyubhayākule pūjanaṃ vāsudevasya tārakaṃ vādibhiḥ smrtam  Hbhv sa nāma sukṛti loke kulaṃ tena hy alaṅkṛtam ādhāraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yena viṣṇuḥ prasaditaḥ  Hbhv yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva śubhānām api karmaṇām tad viśiṣṭaphalaṃ nṝṇāṃ sadaivārādhanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv kalau kalimalākrāntā na jānanti hariṃ param yercayanti tam īśānaṃ kṛtakṛtyas ta eva hi nāsti śreyottamaṃ nṝṇāṃ viṣṇor ārādhanat param  Hbhv yugesmin tamase tasmāt satataṃ harim arcayet arcite devadevese śaṅkhacakragadādhare  Hbhv arcitaḥ sarvadevāḥ syur yataḥ sarvagato hariḥ arcite sarvalokeśe surāsuranamaskṛte keśave keśikaṃsaghne na yāti narakaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv sakṛd abhyarcito yena helayāpi namaskṛtaḥ sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yat surair api pūjitam  Hbhv samastalokanāthasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ sākṣād bhagavato nityaṃ pūjanaṃ janmanaḥ phalam  Hbhv tatraivagre asāre khalu saṃsāre sāram etan nirūpitam samastalokanāthasya śraddhayārādhanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca yatra viṣṇukathā nityaṃ yatra tiṣṭhanti vaiṣṇavāḥ kalibāhyā narās te vai yercayanti sadā harim  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍeharer ārādhanaṃ puṃsāṃ kiṃ kiṃ na kurute bata putramitrakalatrārthaṃ rājyasvargāpavargadam  Hbhv haraty aghaṃ dhvamsayati vyādhīn ādhīn nirasyati dharmaṃ vivardhayet kṣipraṃ prayacchanti manoratham  Hbhv ata eva skānde dhruvaṃ prati markaṇḍeyasya vacanaṃ sakṛd abhyarcito yena devadevo janārdanaḥ sa prāpnoti paraṃ sthānaṃ satyam etan mayoditam  Hbhv tathāṅgīrasaḥ yasyāntaḥ sarvam evedaṃ yasya nānto mahātmanaḥ tam ārādhaya govindaṃ sthānam āgryaṃ yad icchasi  Hbhv pulastasya paraṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma yo sau sasvatapūruṣaḥ tam ārādhya hariṃ yāti muktim apy atidurlabham  Hbhv pulahasya aindram indraḥ paraṃ sthānaṃ yam ārādhya jagatpatim prāpa yajñapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ tam ārādhaya suvrata  Hbhv vasiṣṭhasya prāpnoty ārādhite viṣṇau manasā yad yad icchati trailokyāntargataṃ sthānaṃ kim u sarvottamottamam  Hbhv yan yan kāmayate kāmān nārī vā puruṣo pi vā tan samāpnoti vipulān samārādhya janārdanam  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ ārādhyaiva naro viṣṇuṃ manasā yad yad icchati phalaṃ prāpnoty avihataṃ bhūri svalpam athāpi vā  Hbhv idrsaṃ viṣṇupuranepi kiṃcid adhikaṃ cedaṃśrīmarīceḥanārādhitagovindair narair sthānaṃ nṛpātmaja na hi samprāpyate śreṣṭhaṃ tasmād ārādhayācyutam  Hbhv kiṃ ca tatraivabhaumān manorathān svargaṃ svargavandyaṃ tathāspadam prāpnoty ārādhite viṣṇau nirvāṇam api cottamam  Hbhv tathā brahmavaivarteyatpādodakam ādhāya śivaḥ śirasi nṛtyati yannābhinalinād āsīd brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ  Hbhv yadicchāśaktivikṣobhād brahmaṇḍodbhavasaṅkṣayau tam ārādhaya govindaṃ sthānam agryaṃ yadīcchasi  Hbhv nārasiṃhe markaṇḍeyasahasranikasaṃvādeyas tu sampūjayen nityaṃ narasiṃha nareśvara sa svargamokṣabhāgī syān nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv tasmād ekamanā bhūtvā yāvajjīvaṃ pratijñayā arcanān narasiṃhasya samprāpnoty abhivāñchitam  Hbhv tatraiva śrīvyāsaśukasaṃvāde śrīmārkaṇḍeyamṛtyuñjayasaṃvādānantaraṃnarake pacyamānas tu yamena paribhāṣitaḥ kiṃ tvayā nārcito devaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ  Hbhv udakenāpy alābhe tu dravyāṇāṃ pūjitaḥ prabhuḥ yo dadāti svakaṃ lokaṃ sa tvayā kiṃ na pūjitaḥ  Hbhv narasiṃho hṛṣīkeśaḥ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇaḥ smaranān muktido nṛṇāṃ sa tvayā kiṃ na pūjitaḥ  Hbhv bṛhannāradīyeditimāhātmye śrīsūtoktauyatra pūjāparo viṣṇos tatra vighno na bādhate rājā ca taskaraś cāpi vyādhayaś ca na santi hi  Hbhv pretāḥ piśācāḥ kuṣmāṇḍā grahā bālagrahās tathā ḍākinyo rākṣasāś caiva na bādhantecyutarcakam  Hbhv tatraiva yamabhagīrathasaṃvādepatraiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalair vārcya pūjārahitam acyutam sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ kulasaptatisaṃyutaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva dhvajāropaṇamāhātmye śrīviṣṇudūtānām uktauutkrāntikāle yannāma śrutavanto pi vai sakṛt labhante paramaṃ sthānaṃ kim u śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ  Hbhv muhūrtaṃ vā muhūrtārdhaṃ yas tiṣṭhed dharimandire sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ kim u śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ  Hbhv tatraiva vibhāṇḍakamuneḥ sumatinṛpaṃ prati avaśenāpi yat karma kṛtaṃ tu sumahat phalam dadāti nṝṇāṃ rājendra kiṃ punaḥ samyagarcanā  Hbhv prāyaścittaprakāraṇānte samparkād yadi vā mohād yas tu pūjayate harim sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramaṃ padam  Hbhv sarvāntarāyā naśyanti manaḥsuddhiś ca jāyate paraṃ mokṣaṃ labhec caiva pūjyamāne janārdane  Hbhv dharmārthakāmamokṣākhyā puruṣārthāḥ sanātanāḥ haripūjāparāṇāṃ tu sidhyante nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv sarvatīrthāni yajñāś ca sāṅgā vedāś ca sattamāḥ nārāyaṇarcanasyaite kālaṃ narhanti sodasim  Hbhv śrīviṣṇutoṣavidhipraśnottaresatyaṃ vacmi hitaṃ vacmi sāraṃ vacmi punaḥ punaḥ asārodagrasaṃsāre sāraṃ yad viṣṇupūjanam  Hbhv upalepanamāhātmyanteakāmād api ye viṣṇoḥ sakṛt pūjāṃ prakurvate na teṣām bhavabandhas tu kadācid api jāyate  Hbhv yajñadhvajopākhyānāntetasmāt śṛṇuta viprendra devo nārāyaṇo vyayaḥ jānato jānato vāpi pūjakānāṃ vimuktidaḥ  Hbhv te vandyās te prapūjyāś ca namaskāryā viśeṣataḥ yercayanti mahāviṣṇuṃ prapannārtipraṇāśanam  Hbhv ye yajanti spṛhāśūnyā hariṃ vā haram eva vā ta eva bhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ punanti vibudharṣabhāḥ  Hbhv pādme śrīnārāyaṇanāradasaṃvāde pūjavidhiprasaṅgemadbhakto yo madarcāṃ ca karoti vidhidṛṣṭaye tasyāntarāyaḥ svapnepi na bhavaty abhayo hi saḥ  Hbhv tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye nāradāmbarīṣasaṃvādeputrān kalatrān dīrghāyū rājyaṃ svargāpavargakam sa dadyād īpsitaṃ sarvaṃ bhaktyā sampūjito jitaḥ  Hbhv narakepi ciraṃ magnāḥ pūrvajā ye kuladvaye tatraiva yānti te svargaṃ yadārceta sūto harim  Hbhv tatraiva śrīyamabrahmasaṃvādeanārādhya hariṃ bhaktyā ko lokān prāpnuyād budhaḥ ārādhite harau kāmāḥ sarve karatalasthitāḥ  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare śrīkṛṣṇāmṛtastotreso pi dhanyatamo loke yo rcayed acutyaṃ sakṛt kiṃ punaḥ śraddhayā yuktaḥ sapuṣpaiḥ prativāsaram  Hbhv vaiṣṇavān api ye nityaṃ prapaśyanty arcayanti ca tepi viṣṇupadaṃ yānti kiṃ punar viṣṇusevakāḥ  Hbhv sa yogī sa viśuddhātmā sa śāntaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ sa śuddhaḥ sa ca sampūrṇaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ seveta yo naraḥ  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāmananyamanasaḥ śaśvad gaṇayanto kṣamālayā japanto rāmarāmeti sukhāmṛtanidhau manaḥ pravilāpyāmṛtībhūya sukhaṃ tiṣṭhanti kecana  Hbhv paricaryāparāḥ kecit prāsādādiṣu śerate manuṣyam iva taṃ draṣṭuṃ vyavahartuṃ ca bandhuvat  Hbhv kiṃ cayathā vidhiniṣedhau tu muktaṃ naviopasarpataḥ tathā na spṛśato rāmopāsakaṃ vidhipūrvakam  Hbhv śrībhagavadgītāsu evaṃ satatayuktā ye bhaktās tvāṃ paryupāsate ye cāpy akṣaram avyaktaṃ teṣāṃ ke yogavittamāḥ  Hbhv ity arjunena pṛṣṭaḥ śrībhagavān uvāca mayy āveśya mano ye māṃ nityayuktā upāsate śraddhayā parayopetās te me yuktatamā matāḥ  Hbhv caturthaskandhe BhP yatpādasevābhirucis tapasvināmaśeṣajanmopacitaṃ malaṃ dhiyaḥ sadyaḥ kṣiṇoty anvaham edhatī satīyathā padāṅguṣṭhaviniḥsṛtā sarit  Hbhv kiṃ ca nāradoktau BhP yathā taror mūlaniṣecanenatṛpyanti tatskandhabhujopaśākhāḥ prāṇopahārāc ca yathendriyāṇāṃtathaiva sarvārhaṇam acyutejyā  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe ca kaviyogeśvarasya vākyaṃ BhP manyekutaścidbhayam acyutasyapādāmbujopāsanam atra nityam udvignabuddher asadātmabhāvādviśvātmanā yatra nivartate bhīḥ  Hbhv śrībhagavataś ca BhP evaṃ kriyāyogapathaiḥ pumān vaidikatāntrikaiḥ arcann ubhayataḥ siddhiṃ matto vindaty abhīpsitām  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP mām eva nairapekṣyeṇa bhaktiyogena vindati bhaktiyogaṃ sa labhata evaṃ yaḥ pūjayeta mām  Hbhv gautamīyatantre śrīnāradasyatulasīdalamātreṇa jalasya culukena ca vikrīṇīte svam ātmānaṃ bhaktebhyo bhaktavatsalaḥ  Hbhv atha pūjānityatāmahābhāratemātṛvat parirakṣantaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakam yo nārcayati deveśaṃ taṃ vidyād brahmaghātakam  Hbhv ata evoktaṃ bṛhannāradīye pādodakamāhātmyākhyānārambheharipūjāvidhānaṃ tu yasya veśmani no dvijaḥ śmaśānasadṛśaṃ vidyān na kadāpi viśec ca tat  Hbhv ata evoktaṃ viṣṇudharmottare puṣpair vā yadi vā patraih phalair vā yadi vāmbubhiḥ yaṣṭavyaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣas tyaktvā kāryaśatāni ca  Hbhv kiṃ ca nāradīyenimitteṣu ca sarveṣu tattatkālaviśeṣataḥ pūjayed devadeveśaṃ dravyaṃ sampādya yatnataḥ  Hbhv ata evoktaṃ bhagavatā hāyagrīveṇa hāyaśīrṣapañcarātrepratiṣṭhitārcā na tyājyā yāvajjīvaṃ samarcayet varaṃ prāṇasya vā tyāgaḥ śiraso vāpi karttanam  Hbhv pūjayā nityatālekhi prāk ca naivedyabhakṣaṇe māhātmyaṃ ca paraṃ śālagrāmacakraprasaṅgataḥ  Hbhv pūjāṅgānāṃ ca māhātmyaṃ yad yad vilikhitaṃ purā tat sarvam iha pūjāyāṃ paryavasyati hi svataḥ  Hbhv pūjāmahimamattebhāh śāstrāraṇyavihāriṇaḥ kīṭena kati saṅgrāhyāḥ prabhāvam śrīharer vinā  Hbhv atha śrībhagavannāma sadā seveta sarvataḥ tanmāhātmyaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ saṅkṣepenātra likhyate  Hbhv atha śrībhagavannāmamāhātmyamtatra śrībhagavannāmaviśeṣasya ca sevanam ṛṣibhiḥ kṛpayādiṣṭaṃ tattatkāmahatātmanām  Hbhv atha kāmaviśeṣeṇa śrībhagavannāmaviśeṣasevāmāhātmyamtatra pāpakṣayārthaṃśrīkaurmeśrīśabdapūrvaṃ jayaśabdamadhyaṃjayadvayād uttaratas tathā hi triḥsaptakṛtvo narasiṃhanāmajaptaṃ nihanyād api viprahatyām  Hbhv mahābhayanivaranarthamtatraivaśrīpūrvo narasiṃho dvir jayād uttaratas tu saḥ triḥsaptakṛtvo japato mahābhayanivāraṇaḥ  Hbhv kālaviśeṣe tu maṅgalārthaṃviṣṇudharmottare mārkaṇḍeyavajrasaṃvādepuruṣaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca tathā saṅkarṣaṇaṃ vibhum pradyumnam aniruddhaṃ ca kramād abdeṣu kīrtayet  Hbhv balabhadraṃ tathā kṛṣṇaṃ kīrtayed ayanadvaye madhavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ tathā vai bhogasayinam  Hbhv padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ tathā devaṃ trivikramam kramena rajasardula vasantadisu kīrtayet  Hbhv viṣṇuṃ ca madhuhantāraṃ tathā devaṃ trivikramam vāmanaṃ śrīdharaṃ caiva hṛṣīkeśaṃ tathāiva ca  Hbhv dāmodaraṃ padmanābhaṃ keśavaṃ ca yadūttamam nārāyaṇaṃ mādhavaṃ ca govindaṃ ca tathā kramāt  Hbhv caitrādiṣu ca māseṣu devadevam anusmaret pradyumnam aniruddhaṃ ca pakṣayoḥ kṛṣṇaśuklayoḥ  Hbhv sarvaḥ śarvaḥ sivaḥ sthāṇur bhūtādir nidhir avyayaḥ adityādiṣu vareṣu kramād evam anusmaret  Hbhv viśvaṃ viṣṇur vaṣaṭkāro bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhuḥ bhūtabhṛd bhūtakṛd bhavo bhūtātmā bhūtabhavanaḥ  Hbhv avyaktaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo visvakarma sucisravaḥ sadbhavo bhavano bharta prabhavaḥ prabhur isvaraḥ  Hbhv aprameyo hṛṣīkeśah padmanabho maraprabhuḥ agrahyaḥ sasvato dhata kṛṣṇaś caitany anusmaret devadevasya nāmāni kṛttikadisu yadava  Hbhv brahmāṇaṃ śrīpatiṃ viṣṇuṃ kapilaṃ śrīdharaṃ prabhum dāmodaraṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ govindaṃ madhusūdanam  Hbhv bhūdharaṃ gadinaṃ devaṃ saṅkhinaṃ padminaṃ tathā cakriṇaṃ ca mahārāja prathamādiṣu saṃsmaret  Hbhv sarvaṃ vā sarvadā nāma devadevasya yādava  Hbhv nāmāni sarvāṇi janārdanasyakālaś ca sarvaḥ puruṣapravīrāḥ tasmāt sadā sarvagatasya nāmagrāhyaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ varadasya rājan  Hbhv vividhakāmasiddhaye capulastyoktaukāmaḥ kāmapradaḥ kāntaḥ kāmapālas tathā hariḥ ānando mādhavaś caiva kāmasaṃsiddhaye japet  Hbhv rāmaḥ paraśurāmaś ca nṛsiṃho viṣṇur eva ca vikramaś caivam ādīni japyāny arijigīṣubhiḥ  Hbhv vidyām abhyastatā nityaṃ japtavyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ dāmodaraṃ bandhagato nityam eva japen naraḥ  Hbhv keśavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam aniśaṃ hi tathā japet netrabādhāsu sarvāsu hṛṣīkeśaṃ bhayeṣu ca  Hbhv acyutaṃ cāmṛtaṃ caiva japed auṣadhakarmāṇi saṅgrāmābhimukho gacchan saṃsmared aparājitam  Hbhv cakriṇaṃ gadinaṃ caiva śārṅgiṇaṃ khaḍginaṃ tathā kṣemārthī pravasan nityaṃ dikṣu pracyādiṣu smaret  Hbhv ajitaṃ cādhipaṃ caiva sarvaṃ sarveśvaraṃ tathā saṃsmaret puruṣo bhaktyā vyavahāreṣu sarvadā  Hbhv nārāyaṇaṃ sarvakālaṃ kṣutapraskhalanādiṣu grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu devabādhāsu sarvataḥ  Hbhv dasyuvairinirodheṣu vyāghrasiṃhādisaṅkaṭe andhākāre tamastīvre narasiṃham anusmaret  Hbhv agnidāhe samutpanne saṃsmarej jalaśāyinam garuḍadhvajānusmaranād viṣavīryaṃ vyapohati  Hbhv snāne devārcane home praṇipāte pradakṣine kīrtayed bhagavannāma vāsudeveti tatparaḥ  Hbhv sthāpane vittadhānyāder apadhyāne ca duṣṭaje kurvīta tanmanā bhūtvā anantācyutakīrtanam  Hbhv nārāyaṇam śārṅgadharaṃ śrīdharaṃ puruṣottamam vāmanaṃ khaḍginaṃ caiva duṣṭasvapne sadā smaret  Hbhv mahārṇavādau paryaṅkaśāyinaṃ ca naraḥ smaret balabhadraṃ samṛddhyarthaṃ sarvakarmāṇi saṃsmaret  Hbhv jagatpatim apatyārthaṃ stuvān bhaktyā na sīdati śrīśaṃ sarvābhyudayike karmany āśu prakīrtayet  Hbhv ariṣṭeṣu hy aśeṣeṣu viśokaṃ ca sadā japet maruprapātāgnijalabandhanādiṣu mṛtyuṣu svatantraparatantreṣu vāsudevaṃ japed budhaḥ  Hbhv sarvārthaśaktiyuktasya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ yathābhirocate nāma tat sarvārtheṣu kīrtayet  Hbhv sarvārthasiddhim āpnoti nāmnām ekārthatā yathā sarvāṇy etāni nāmāni parasya brahmaṇo hareḥ  Hbhv evaṃ viṣṇudharmottare ca mārkaṇḍeyavajrasaṃvāde kiṃ cakūrmaṃ varāhaṃ matsyaṃ vā jalaprataraṇe smaret bhrājiṣṇum agnijanane japen nāma tv akhaṇḍitam  Hbhv garuḍadhvajānusmaraṇād āpado mucyate naraḥ jvarajuṣṭaśirorogaviṣavīryaṃ ca śamyati  Hbhv balabhadraṃ tu yuddhārthī kṛśyārambhe halāyudham uttarānāṃ vāṇijyārthī rāmam abhyudaye nṛpa  Hbhv maṅgalyaṃ maṅgalaṃ viṣṇum maṅgalyeṣu ca kīrtayet uttiṣṭhan kīrtayed viṣṇum prasvapan madhavaṃ naraḥ bhojane caiva govindaṃ sarvatra madhusūdanam  Hbhv tatraivānyatraauṣadhe cintayed viṣṇum bhojane ca janārdanam śayane padmanābhaṃ ca maithune ca prajāpatim  Hbhv saṅgrāme cakriṇaṃ kruddham sthānabhraṃśe trivikramam nārāyaṇaṃ vṛṣotsarge śrīdharaṃ priyasaṅgame jalamadhye ca vārāhaṃ pāvake jalaśāyinam  Hbhv kānane narasiṃhaṃ ca parvate raghunandanam duḥsvapne smara govindaṃ viśuddhau madhusūdanam māyāsu vāmanaṃ devaṃ sarvakāryeṣu mādhavam  Hbhv kiṃ cakīrtayed vāsudevaṃ ca anukteṣv api yādava kāryārambhe tathā rājan yatheṣṭaṃ nāma kīrtayet  Hbhv sarvāṇi nāmāni hi tasya rājansarvārthasiddhyai tu bhavanti pumsaḥ tasmād yatheṣṭaṃ khalu kṛṣṇanāmasarveṣu kāryeṣu japeta bhaktyā  Hbhv tatrākhilapāponmūlanatvamatha sāmānyataḥ śrībhagavannāmakīrtanamāhātmyamviṣṇudharme haribhaktisudhodaye coktaṃ nāradenaaho sunirmala yūyam rāgo hi harikīrtane avidhūya tamaḥ kṛtsnaṃ nṛṇām udeti sūryavat  Hbhv garudepāpānalasya dīptasya mā kurvantu bhayaṃ narāḥ govindanāmameghaughair naśyate nīrabindubhiḥ  Hbhv avaśenāpi yannāmni kīrtane sarvapātakaiḥ pumān vimucyate sadyaḥ siṃhatrastair mṛgair iva  Hbhv yannāmakīrtanaṃ bhaktyā vilāpanam anuttamam maitreyāśeṣapāpānāṃ dhātūnām iva pāvakaḥ  Hbhv yasmin nyastamatir na yāti narakaṃ svargo pi yaccintanevighno yatra niveśitātmamanaso brāhmo pi loko lpakaḥ muktiṃ cetasi yaḥ sthito maladhiyāṃ puṃsāṃ dadāty avyayaḥkiṃ citraṃ yadaghaṃ prayāti vilayaṃ tatrācyute kīrtite  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare sāyaṃ prātas tathā kṛtvā devadevasya kīrtanam sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate  Hbhv vāmanenārāyaṇo nāma naro narāṇāṃprasiddhacauraḥ kathitaḥ pṛthivyām anekajanmārjitapāpasañcayamharaty aśeṣaṃ śrutamātra eva  Hbhv skāndegovindeti tathā proktaṃ bhaktyā vā bhaktivarjitaiḥ dahate sarvapāpāni yugāntāgnir ivotthitaḥ  Hbhv govindanāmnā yaḥ kaścin naro bhavati bhūtale kīrtanād eva tasyāpi pāpaṃ yāti sahasradhā  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍepramādād api saṃspṛṣṭo yathānalakaṇo dahet tathauṣṭhapuṭasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ harināma dahed agham  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye lubdhakopakhyānāntenarāṇāṃ viṣayāndhānām mamatākulacetasām ekam eva harer nāma sarvapāpavināśanam  Hbhv ata eva tatraiva yamenoktamhari hari sakṛd uccāritamdasyucchalena yair manuṣyaiḥ jananījaṭharamārgaluptāna mama paṭalipiṃ viśanti martyāḥ  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye devaśarmopākhyānānte śrīnāradoktauhatyāyutaṃ pānasahasram ugramgurvaṅganākoṭiniṣevanaṃ ca steyāny anekāni haripriyeṇagovindanāmnā nihatāni sadyaḥ  Hbhv anicchayāpi dahati spṛṣṭo hutavaho yathā tathā dahati govindanāma vyājād apīritam  Hbhv tatraiva śrīyamabrāhmaṇasaṃvādekīrtanād eva kṛṣṇasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ duritāni vilīyante tamāṃsīva dinodaye  Hbhv nānyat paśyāmi jantūnām vihāya karikīrtanam sarvapāpapraśamanam prāyaścittam dvijottama  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP ayaṃ hi kṛtanirveśo janmakoṭyaṃhasām api yad vyājahāra vivaśo nāma svastyayanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv stenaḥ surāpo mitradhrug brahmahā gurutalpagaḥ strīrājapitṛgohantā ye ca pātakino pare  Hbhv sarveṣām apy aghavatām idam eva suniṣkṛtam nāmavyāharaṇaṃ viṣṇor yatas tadviṣayā matiḥ  Hbhv na niṣkṛtair uditair brahmavādibhistathā viśuddhyaty aghavān vratādibhiḥ yathā harer nāmapadair udāhṛtaistad uttamaślokaguṇopalambhakam  Hbhv BhP sāṅketyaṃ pārihāsyaṃ vā stobhaṃ helanam eva vā vaikuṇṭhanāmagrahaṇam aśeṣāghaharaṃ viduḥ  Hbhv patitaḥ skhalito bhagnaḥ sandaṣṭas tapta āhataḥ harir ity avaśenāha pumān nārhati yātanāḥ  Hbhv BhP ajñānād athavā jñānād uttamaślokanāma yat saṅkīrtitam aghaṃ puṃso dahed edho yathānalaḥ  Hbhv BhP brahmahā pitṛhā goghno mātṛhācāryahāghavān śvādaḥ pulkasako vāpi śuddhyeran yasya kīrtanāt  Hbhv laghubhāgavatevartamānaṃ tu yat pāpaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yad bhaviṣyati tat sarvaṃ nirdahaty āśu govindānalakīrtanāt  Hbhv sadā drohaparo yas tu sajjanānāṃ mahītale jāyate pāvano dhanyo harer nāmānukīrtanāt  Hbhv kaurmevasanti yāni koṭis tu pāvanāni mahītale na tāni tattulāṃ yānti kṛṣṇanāmānukīrtane  Hbhv bṛhadviṣṇupurāṇe nāmno sya yāvatī śaktiḥ pāpanirharaṇe hareḥ tāvat kartuṃ na śaknoti pātakaṃ pātakī janaḥ  Hbhv itihāsottamesvādo pi na hi śaknoti kartuṃ pāpāni yatnataḥ tāvantī yāvatī śaktir viṣṇor nāmno subhakṣaye  Hbhv viśeṣataḥ kalau skāndetan nāsti karmajaṃ loke vāgjaṃ mānasam eva vā yan na kṣapayate pāpaṃ kalau govindakīrtanam  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare śamāyālaṃ jalaṃ vahnes tamaso bhaskarodayaḥ śāntyai kaler aghaughasya nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv nāmnāṃ hareḥ kīrtanataḥ prayātisaṃsārapāraṃ duritaughamuktaḥ naraḥ sa satyaṃ kalidoṣajanmapāpaṃ nihaty āśu kim atra citram  Hbhv brahmāṇḍapurāṇevarākacāndrāyaṇataptakṛcchrairna dehiśuddhir bhavatīha tādṛk kalau sakṛn mādhavakīrtanenagovindanāmnā bhavatīha yādṛk  Hbhv kīrtanakartrkulasaṅgyādipavanatvaṃtatraivamahāpātakayukto pi kīrtayenn aniśaṃ harim śuddhāntaḥkaraṇo bhūtvā jāyate paṅktipāvanaḥ  Hbhv laghubhāgavategovindeti mudā yuktaḥ kīrtayed yas tv ananyadhīḥ pāvanena ca dhanyena teneyaṃ pṛthivī dhṛtā  Hbhv haribhaktisudhodayena caivam ekaṃ vaktāraṃ jihvā rakṣati vaiṣṇavī āśrāvya bhagavatkhyātiṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ punāti hi  Hbhv daśamaskandhe  yannāma gṛhṇann Hbhv dvādaśaskandhe BhP kṛte yad dhyāyato viṣṇuṃ tretāyāṃ yajato makhaiḥ dvāpare paricaryāyāṃ kalau tad dharikīrtanāt  Hbhv ekādaśe BhP kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ tviṣākṛṣṇaṃ sāṅgopāṅgāstrapārṣadam yajñaiḥ saṅkīrtanaprāyair yajanti hi sumedhasaḥ  Hbhv skānde camahābhāgavatā nityaṃ kalau kurvanti kīrtanam  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye  nāradoktaṃ harer nāmaiva nāmaiva nāmaiva mama jīvanam kalau nāsty eva nāsty eva nāsty eva gatir anyathā  Hbhv ataivoktamsakṛd uccārayanty eva harer nāma cidātmakam phalaṃ nāsya kṣamo vaktuṃ sahasravadano vidhiḥ  Hbhv pādmottarakhaṇḍe śrīrāmāṣṭottaraśatanāmastotre śrīśivenarakārādīni nāmāni śṛṇvato devi jāyate prītir me manaso nityaṃ rāmanāmaviśaṅkayā  Hbhv vaiṣṇavacintāmaṇauīśo haṃ sarvajagatāṃ nāmnāṃ viṣṇor hi jāpakaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmy eṣa harer nāma gatir nṝṇām  Hbhv ādipurāṇe ca śrīkṛṣṇārjunasaṃvādeśraddhayā helayā nāma raṭanti mama jantavaḥ teṣāṃ nāma sadā pārtha vartate hṛdaye mama  Hbhv na nāma sadṛśaṃ jñānaṃ na nāma sadṛśaṃ vratam na nāma sadṛśaṃ dhyānaṃ na nāma sadṛśaṃ phalam  Hbhv na nāma sadṛśas tyāgo na nāma sadṛśaḥ śamaḥ na nāma sadṛśaṃ puṇyaṃ na nāma sadṛśī gatiḥ  Hbhv kiṃ canāmaiva paramā muktir nāmaiva paramā gatiḥ nāmaiva paramā śāntir nāmaiva paramā sthitiḥ  Hbhv nāmaiva paramā bhaktir nāmaiva paramā matiḥ nāmaiva paramā prītir nāmaiva paramā smṛtiḥ  Hbhv nāmaiva kāraṇaṃ jantor nāmaiva prabhur eva ca nāmaiva paramārādhyo nāmaiva paramo guruḥ  Hbhv kiṃ canāmayuktān janān dṛṣṭvā snigdho bhavati yo naraḥ sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ viṣṇunā saha modate  Hbhv tasmān nāmāni kaunteya bhajasva dṛḍhamānasaḥ nāmayuktaḥ priyo smākaṃ nāmayukto bhavārjuna  Hbhv atha śrībhagavannāmajapasya smaraṇasya ca śravaṇasyāpi māhātmyam īṣad bhedād vilikhyate  Hbhv atha śrīmannāmajapamāhātmyamviṣṇurahasye śrībhagavaduktausatyaṃ bravīmi manujāḥ svayam ūrdvabāhuryo māṃ mukunda narasiṃha janārdaneti jīvan japaty anudinaṃ maraṇe ṛṇīvapāṣāṇakāṣṭhasadṛśāya dadāmy abhīṣṭam  Hbhv kāśīkāṇḍe agnibindustutaunārāyaṇeti narakārṇavatāraṇetidāmodareti madhuheti caturbhujeti viśvambhareti virajeti janārdanetikvāstīha janma japatāṃ kva kṛtāntabhītiḥ  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye  yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvādevāsudevajapāsaktān api pāpakṛto janān nopasarpanti tān vipra yamadūtāś ca dāruṇāḥ  Hbhv bṛhadviṣṇupurāṇekva nākapṛṣṭhagamanaṃ punarāvṛttilakṣaṇam kva japo vāsudeveti muktibījam anuttamam  Hbhv śrīmannāmasmaraṇamāhātmyamitihāsottamesvapnepi nāmasmṛtir ādipuṃsaḥkṣayaṃ karoty āhitapāparāśeḥ prayatnataḥ kiṃ punar ādipuṃsaḥprakīrtite nāgnir janārdanasya  Hbhv laghubhāgavatete sabhāgyā manuṣyeṣu kṛtārthā nṛpa niścitam smaranti ye smārayanti harer nāma kalau yuge  Hbhv pādme devahūtistutauprayāṇe cāprayāṇe ca yannāmasmaraṇān nṝṇām sadyo naśyati pāpaugho namas tasmai cidātmane  Hbhv tatraivottarakhaṇḍeyannāmasmaraṇād eva pāpinām api satvaram muktir bhavati jātūnāṃ brahmādīnāṃ sudurlabhā  Hbhv brahmavaivarteyadanudhyānadāvāgnidagdhakarmatṛṇaḥ pumān viśuddhaḥ paśyati vyaktam avyaktam api keśavam  Hbhv tad asya nāma jīvasya patitasya bhavāmbudhau hastāvalambadānāya pravīṇo nāparo hareḥ  Hbhv jāvālisaṃhitāyāmharer nāma paraṃ japyaṃ dhyeyaṃ geyaṃ nirantaram kīrtanīyaṃ ca bahudhā nirvṛtīr bahudhecchatā  Hbhv atha śrībhagavannāmamāhātmyambṛhannāradīye śrīnāradoktauyannāmaśravaṇenāpi mahāpātakino pi ye pāvanatvaṃ prapadyante kathaṃ stoṣyāmi khinnadhīḥ  Hbhv itihāsottameśrutaṃ saṅkīrtitaṃ vāpi harer āścaryakarmaṇaḥ dahaty enāṃsi sarvāṇi prasaṅgāt kim u bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  citraketūktau na hi bhagavann aghaṭitam idaṃtvaddarśanān nṛṇām akhilapāpakṣayaḥ yannāma sakṛc chravaṇātpukkaśo pi vimucyate saṃsārāt  Hbhv iti śrīmannāmnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ māhātmyeṣu sameṣv api kṛṣṇasyaivāvatāreṣu viśeṣaḥ ko pi kasyacit  Hbhv atha viśeṣataḥ śrīkṛṣṇāvatāramāhātmyambrahmāṇḍapurāṇe śrīkṛṣṇāṣṭottaraśatanāmamāhātmyesahasranāmnāṃ puṇyānāṃ trirāvṛttyā tu yat phalam ekāvṛttyā tu kṛṣṇasya nāmaikaṃ tat prayacchati  Hbhv idaṃ kirīṭī saṃjapya jayī pāśupatāstrabhāk kṛṣṇasya prāṇabhūtaḥ san kṛṣṇaṃ sārathim āptavān  Hbhv kim idaṃ bahunā śaṃsan mānuṣānandanirbharaḥ brahmānandam avāpyānte kṛṣṇasāyujyam āpnuyāt  Hbhv vārāhe ca śrīmāthuramāhātmyetatra guhyāni nāmāni bhaviṣyanti mama priye puṇyāni ca pavitrāṇi saṃsāracchedanāni ca  Hbhv tatraiva viśeṣataḥ śrīkṛṣṇeti nāmamāhātmyamdvārakāmāhātmye prahlādabalisaṃvādeatītāḥ puruṣāḥ sapta bhaviṣāś ca caturdaśa naras tārayate sarvān kalau kṛṣṇeti kīrtanāt  Hbhv kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti svapan jāgrad vrajaṃs tathā yo jalpati kalau nityaṃ kṛṣṇarūpī bhaved dhi saḥ  Hbhv brahmavaivartehanan brāhmaṇam atyantaṃ kāmato vā surāṃ piban kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇety ahorātraṃ saṅkīrtya śucitām iyāt  Hbhv viṣṇudharmekṛṣṇeti maṅgalaṃ nāma yasya vāci pravartate bhasmībhavanti rājendra mahāpātakakoṭayaḥ  Hbhv nārasiṃhe śrībhagavaduktaukṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti yo māṃ smarati nityaśaḥ jalaṃ bhittvā yathā padmaṃ narakād uddharāmy aham  Hbhv gāruḍe pādme casaṃsārasarpasaṃdaṣṭaṃ naṣṭaceṣṭaikabheṣajam kṛṣṇeti vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ śrutvā mukto bhaven naraḥ  Hbhv prabhāsapurāṇenāmnāṃ mukhyataraṃ nāma kṛṣṇākhyaṃ me parantapa prāyaścittam aśeṣāṇāṃ pāpānāṃ mocakaṃ param  Hbhv pādmeyatra yatra sthito vāpi kṛṣṇakṛṣṇeti kīrtayet sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā sa gacchet paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottare śrīkṛṣṇasahasranāmastotreballavīkānta kiṃ tais tair upāyaiḥ kṛṣṇanāma te kintu jihvāgragaṃ jāgran nirundhe hi mahābhayam  Hbhv tatraivānyatrasatyaṃ bravīmi te śambho gopanīyam idaṃ mama mṛtyusaṃjīvanīṃ nāma kṛṣṇākhyām avadhāraya  Hbhv bhāratavibhāgekṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇa ity antakālejalpan jantur jīvitaṃ yo jahāti ādyaḥ śabdaḥ kalpate tasya muktyaivrīḍānamrau tiṣṭhato nyāvṛṇasthau  Hbhv anyatrāpināma cintāmaṇiḥ kṛṣṇaś caitanyarasavigrahaḥ pūrṇaḥ śuddho nityamukto bhinnatvān nāmanāminoḥ  Hbhv ataivoktamtebhyo namo stu bhavavāridhijīrṇapaṅkasaṃmagnamokṣaṇavicakṣaṇapādukebhyaḥ kṛṣṇeti varṇayugalaṃ śravaṇena yeṣāṃānandathūrbhavati nartitaromavṛndaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ ca dvitīyaskandhe BhP  tad aśmasāraṃ hṛdayaṃ batedaṃyad gṛhyamāṇair harināmadheyaiḥ na vikriyetātha yadā vikāronetre jalaṃ gātraruheṣu harṣaḥ  Hbhv itihāsottame canāmni saṅkīrtite viṣṇor yasya puṃso na jāyate saromapulakaṃ gātraṃ sa bhavet kuliśopamaḥ  Hbhv kātyāyanasaṃhitāyāmnāmasaṅkīrtanāj jātaṃ puṇyaṃ nopacayanti ye nānāvyādhisamāyuktāḥ śatajanmasu te narāḥ  Hbhv sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sa mohaḥ sa ca vibhramaḥ yanmuhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvādeavamatya ca ye yānti bhagavatkīrtanaṃ narāḥ te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ tena pāpena karmaṇā  Hbhv śrutayaḥom āsya jānanto nāma cid viviktanmahas te viṣṇo sumatiṃ bhajāmahe  Hbhv oṃ tat sat oṃ padaṃ devasya namasāvyantaḥ śravasy avaśrava āpannaṃ ṛktam nāmāni cid dadhire yajñiyantibhadrāyānte raṇayantaḥ sandṛṣṭau  Hbhv oṃ tam u stotāraḥ pūrvaṃ yathāvidaṛtasya garbhaṃ januṣā pipartana āsya jānanto nāma cid viviktanmahas te viṣṇo sumatiṃ bhajāmahe  Hbhv ity ādyā iti īdṛśe nāmamāhātmye śrutismṛtiviniścite kalpayanty arthavādaṃ ye yānti ghorayātanām  Hbhv atha śrībhagavannāmārthavādakalpanādūṣaṇamśrīkātyāyanasaṃhitāyāmarthavādaṃ harer nāmni sambhāvayati yo naraḥ sa pāpiṣṭho manuṣyāṇāṃ niraye patanti sphuṭam  Hbhv brahmasaṃhitāyāṃ baudhāyanaṃ prati śrībhagavaduktauyannāmakīrtanaphalaṃ vividhaṃ niśamyana śraddadhāti manute yad utārthavādam yo mānuṣas tam iha duḥkhacaye kṣipāmisaṃsāraghoravividhārtinipīḍitāṅgam  Hbhv jaiminisaṃhitāyāṃ caśrutismṛtipurāṇeṣu nāmamāhātmyavāciṣu yerthavāda iti brūyur na teṣāṃ nirayakṣayaḥ  Hbhv tasmiṃś ca bhagavannāmni jagadekopakāriṇi viśvaikasevye matimān aparādhān vivarjayet  Hbhv yata uktaṃ pādme śrīnāradaṃ prati sanatkumāreṇa sarvāparādhakṛd api mucyate harisaṃśrayāt  Hbhv harer apy aparādhān yaḥ kuryād dvipadapāṃsavaḥ nāmāśrayaḥ kadācit syāt taraty eva sa nāmataḥ  Hbhv nāmno pi sarvasuhṛdo hy aparādhāt pataty adhaḥ  Hbhv atha nāmāparādhāḥtaṃ prati tenaivoktāḥ satāṃ nindā nāmnaḥ paramam aparādhaṃ vitanuteyataḥ khyātiṃ yātaṃ katham u sahate tadvigarhām śivasya śrīviṣṇor ya iha guṇanāmādisakalaṃdhiyā bhinnaṃ paśyet sa khalu harināmāhitakaraḥ  Hbhv guror avajñā śrutiśāstranindanaṃtathārthavādo harināmni kalpanam nāmno balād yasya hi pāpabuddhirna vidyate tasya yamair hi śuddhiḥ  Hbhv dharmavratatyāgahutādisarvaśubhakriyāsāmyam api pramādaḥ aśraddadhāne vimukhepy aśṛṇvatiyaś copadeśaḥ śivanāmāparādhaḥ  Hbhv śrutepi nāmamāhātmye yaḥ prītirahito dhamaḥ ahaṃmamādiparamo nāmni so py aparādhakṛt  Hbhv jāte nāmāparādhepi pramādena kathañcana sadā saṅkīrtayan nāma tadekaśaraṇo bhavet  Hbhv aparādhabhañjanaṃuktaṃ ca tenaiva tatra nāmāparādhayuktānāṃ nāmāny eva haranty agham aviśrāntaprayuktāni tāny evārthakarāṇi ca  Hbhv nāmaikaṃ yasya vāci smaraṇapathagataṃ śrotramūlaṃ gataṃ vāśuddhaṃ vāśuddhavarṇaṃ vyavahitarahitaṃ tārayaty eva satyam tac ced dehadraviṇajanatālobhapāṣaṇḍamadhyenikṣiptaṃ syān na phalajanakaṃ śīghram evātra vipra  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ śrīnāradena bṛhannāradīye mahminām api yannāmnaḥ pāraṃ gantum anīśvaraḥ manavo pi munīdrāś ca kathaṃ kṣuṇṇadhīr bhaje  Hbhv iti itthaṃ śrīkṛṣṇapādābje bhaktiḥ kāryā sadā budhaiḥ sā ca tasya prasādena mahāpuṇyāt prajāyate  Hbhv atha śrīmadbhakter durlabhatvamskānde śrīparāśaroktauna hy apuṇyavatāṃ loke mūḍhānāṃ kuṭilātmanām bhaktir bhavati govinde smaraṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ tathā  Hbhv tatraiva śrībrahmoktaunimiṣaṃ nimiṣārdhaṃ vā martyānām iha nārada nādagdhāśeṣapāpānāṃ bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv yogavāśiṣṭhejanmāntarasahasreṣu tapojñānasamādhibhiḥ narāṇāṃ kṣīṇapāpānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate  Hbhv ādivārāhejanmāntarasahasreṣu samārādhya vṛṣadhvajam vaiṣṇavatvaṃ labhed dhīmān sarvapāpakṣaye sati  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye  yajñadhvajanṛpopākhyānāntejanmakoṭisahasreṣu puṇyaṃ yaiḥ samupārjitam teṣāṃ bhaktir bhavec chuddhā devadeve janārdane  Hbhv sulabhaṃ jāhnavīsnānaṃ tathaivātithipūjanam sulabhāḥ sarvayajñāś ca viṣṇubhaktiḥ sudurlabhā  Hbhv itihāsasamuccaye śiloñchavṛttivākyegaṅgāyāṃ maraṇaṃ caiva dṛḍhā bhaktiś ca keśave brahmavidyāprabodhaś ca nālpasya tapasaḥ phalam  Hbhv agastyasaṃhitāyāmvratopavāsaniyamair janmakoṭyāpy aniṣṭhiteḥ yajñaiś ca vividhaiḥ samyag bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv viṣṇudharmottaredivasaṃ divasārdhaṃ vā muhūrtaṃ caikam eva vā nāśāc cāśeṣapāpasya bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv anekajanmasāhasrair nānāyonyantareṣu ca jantoḥ kaluṣahīnasya bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv daśamaskandhe gopīḥ prati uddhavoktau BhP dānavrātatapohoma japasvādhyāyasaṃyamaiḥ śreyobhir vividhaiś cānyaiḥ kṛṣṇe bhaktir hi sādhyate  Hbhv śrībhagavadgītāsu yeṣāṃ tv antagataṃ pāpaṃ janānāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām te dvandvamohanirmuktā bhajante māṃ dṛḍhavratāḥ  Hbhv pañcamaskandhe parīkṣitaṃ prati śrībādarāyaṇinā BhP rājan patir gurur alaṃ bhavatāṃ yadūnāṃdaivaṃ priyaḥ kulapatiḥ kva ca kiṅkaro vaḥ astv evam aṅga bhagavān bhajatāṃ mukundomuktiṃ dadāti karhicit sma na bhaktiyogam  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhaskandhe vṛtropākhyānānte BhP devānāṃ śuddhasattvānāṃ ṛṣīṇāṃ cāmalātmanām bhaktir mukundacaraṇe na prāyeṇopajāyate  Hbhv śrīmadbhaktyai namas tasyai yasyā māthāmtyamandaram yatprabhāveṇa lolo yaṃ kīṭo py uddhartum icchati  Hbhv atha śrībhagavadbhaktimāhātmyaṃtatrādau bhaktimataḥ kathañcid āpatitepi pāpe prāyaścittāntaranirasanatvam pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye nāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde PadmaP yathāgniḥ susamṛddhārciḥ karoty edhāṃsi bhasmasāt pāpāni bhagavadbhaktis tathā dahati tatkṣaṇāt  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhe ajāmilopākhyānārambhe BhP kecit kevalayā bhaktyā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ aghaṃ dhunvanti kārtsnyena nīhāram iva bhāskaraḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP yathāgniḥ susamṛddhārciḥ karoty edhāṃsi bhasmasāt tathā madviṣayā bhaktir uddhavaināṃsi kṛtsnaśaḥ  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ tatraiva śrīkarabhājanena BhP  svapādamūlaṃ bhajataḥ priyasyatyaktānyabhāvasya hariḥ pareśaḥ vikarma yac cotpatitaṃ kathañciddhunoti sarvaṃ hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ  Hbhv dvārakāmāhātmye candraśarmāṇaṃ prati śrībhagavatāmadbhaktiṃ vahatāṃ puṃsām iha loke parepi vā nāśubhaṃ vidyate kiñcit kulakoṭiṃ nayed ditam  Hbhv viṣayabhogepi taddoṣanirākaratvamekādaśaskandhe tatraiva BhP bādhyamāno pi madbhakto viṣayair ajitendriyaḥ prāyaḥ pragalbhayā bhaktyā viṣayair nābhibhūyate  Hbhv karmādhikāranirasanatvaṃtatraiva BhP tāvat karmāṇi kurvīta na nirvidyeta yāvatā matkathāśravaṇādau vā śraddhā yāvan na jāyate  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ prathamaskandhe BhP tyaktvā svadharmaṃ caraṇāmbujaṃ harerbhajann apakvo tha patet tato yadi yatra kva vābhadram abhūd amuṣya kiṃko vārtha āpto bhajatāṃ svadharmataḥ  Hbhv ekāntilakṣaṇe yac ca likhitaṃ śaraṇāgatau lekhyaṃ ca tattadvacanair etat sudṛḍhatām iyāt  Hbhv manaḥprasādakatvamprathamaskandhe BhP sa vai puṃsāṃ paro dharmo yato bhaktir adhokṣaje ahaituky apratihatā yayātmā suprasīdati  Hbhv ataivoktam ekādaśe BhP dharmaḥ satyadayopeto vidyā vā tapasānvitā madbhaktyāpetam ātmānaṃ na samyak prapunāti hi  Hbhv tatraiva BhP bhaktiḥ punāti manniṣṭhā śvapākān api sambhavāt  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhe BhP etāvān eva lokesmin puṃsāṃ dharmaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ bhaktiyogo bhagavati tannāmagrahaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ pādmekiṃ tasya bahubhiḥ mantraiḥ śāstraiḥ kiṃ bahuvistaraiḥ vājapeyasahasraiḥ kiṃ bhaktir yasya janārdane  Hbhv sarvaguṇādisevyatākāritvampañcamaskandhe prahlādoktau BhP yasyāsti bhaktir bhagavaty akiñcanāsarvair guṇais tatra samāsate surāḥ harāv abhaktasya kuto mahadguṇāmanorathenāsati dhāvato bahiḥ  Hbhv caturthe śrīdhruvaṃ prati manūtkau BhP tvaṃ pratyagātmani tadā bhagavaty anantaānandamātra upapannasamastaśaktau bhaktiṃ vidhāya paramāṃ śanakair avidyāgranthiṃ vibhetsyasi mamāham iti prarūḍham  Hbhv śrīpṛthuṃ prati śrīsanakādibhiḥ BhP yatpādapaṅkajapalāśavilāsabhaktyākarmāśayaṃ grathitam udgrathayanti santaḥ tadvan na riktamatayo yatayo pi ruddhasrotogaṇās tam araṇaṃ bhaja vāsudevam  Hbhv sarvamārgādhikatvamtṛtīye śrīkāpileye BhP na yujyamānayā bhaktyā bhagavaty akhilātmani sadṛśo sti śivaḥ panthā yogināṃ brahmasiddhaye  Hbhv ṣaṣṭhe ca BhP sadhrīcīno hy ayaṃ loke panthāḥ kṣemo kutobhayaḥ suśīlāḥ sādhavo yatra nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ dvitīye śrībādarāyaṇinā BhP na hy ato nyaḥ śivaḥ panthā viśataḥ saṃsṛtāv iha vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogo yato bhavet  Hbhv bhagavān brahma kārtsnyena trir anvīkṣya manīṣayā tad adhyavasyat kūṭastho ratir ātmany ato bhavet  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye śrīnāradoktaṃ  yathā samastalokānāṃ jīvanaṃ salilaṃ smṛtam tathā samastasiddhīnāṃ jīvanaṃ bhaktir iṣyate  Hbhv jīvanti jantavaḥ sarve yathā mātaramāśritāḥ tathā bhaktiṃ samāśritya sarve jīvanti dhārmikāḥ  Hbhv dhvajāropaṇamāhātmye śrīviṣṇudūtoktaumahāpātakayukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ īpsitāṃ bhagavadbhaktyā labhate paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvādeapatyaṃ draviṇaṃ dārā hārā harmyaṃ hayā gajāḥ sukhāni svargamokṣau ca na dūre haribhaktitaḥ  Hbhv prathamaskandhe BhP vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogaḥ prayojitaḥ janayaty āśu vairāgyaṃ jñānaṃ ca yad ahaitukam  Hbhv ekādaśe ca BhP yat karmabhir yat tapasā jñānavairāgyataś ca yat yogena dāmadharmeṇa śreyobhir itarair api  Hbhv sarvaṃ madbhaktiyogena madbhakto labhateñjasā svargāpavargaṃ maddhāma kathañcid yadi vāñchati  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ dvitīye BhP akāmaḥ sarvakāmo vā mokṣakāma udāradhīḥ tīvreṇa bhaktiyogena yajeta puruṣaṃ param  Hbhv mokṣādhikatvamtṛtīye kāpileye BhP animittā bhāgavatī bhaktiḥ siddher garīyasī jarayaty āśu yā koṣaṃ nigīrṇam analo yathā  Hbhv pañcame śrīṛṣabhadevacaritānte BhP yasyām eva kavaya ātmānam avirataṃ vividhavṛjinasaṃsāraparitāpopatapyamānam anusavanaṃsnāpayantas tayaiva parayā nirvṛtyā hy apavargam ātyantikaṃ paramapuruṣārtham apisvayam āsāditaṃ no evādriyante bhagavadīyatvenaiva parisamāptasarvārthāḥ  Hbhv dvādaśe ca śrīmārkaṇḍeyam uddiśya śrīśivoktau BhP naivecchaty āśiṣaḥ kvāpi brahmarṣir mokṣam apy uta bhaktiṃ parāṃ bhagavati labdhavān puruṣevyaye  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ pañcame śrībhagavantam uddiśya bādarāyaṇinā BhP yo dustyajān kṣitisutasvajanārthadārānprārthyāṃ śriyaṃ suravaraiḥ sadayāvalokām naicchan nṛpas taducitaṃ mahatāṃ madhudviṭsevānuraktamanasām abhavo pi phalguḥ  Hbhv ekādaśe ca bhagavatā BhP na pārameṣṭhyaṃ na mahendradhiṣṇyaṃna sārvabhaumaṃ na rasādhipatyam na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vāmayy arpitātmecchati mad vinānyat  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe śrīrudreṇa BhP vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktim udvahatāṃ nṝṇām jñānavairāgyavīryāṇāṃ neha kaścid vyapāśrayaḥ  Hbhv viṣṇupurāṇe ca śrīprahlādena ViP dharmārthakāmaiḥ kiṃ tasya muktis tasya kare sthitā samastajagatāṃ mūle yasya bhaktiḥ sthitā tvayi  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ nārasiṃhepatreṣu puṣpeṣu phaleṣu toyesvakrītalabhyeṣu sadaiva satsu bhaktyā sulabhye puruṣe purāṇemuktau kim arthaṃ kriyate prayatnaḥ  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ prathamaskandhe BhP ātmārāmāś ca munayo nirgranthā apy urukrame kurvanty ahaitukīṃ bhaktim itthambhūtaguṇo hariḥ  Hbhv śrīvaikuṇṭhalokaprāpakatvamvāmaneyeṣāṃ cakragadāpāṇau bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī te yānti niyataṃ sthānaṃ yatra yogeśvaro hariḥ  Hbhv skāndemunir jāpyaparo nityaṃ dṛḍhabhaktir jitendriyaḥ svagṛhepi vasan yāti tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe śrīvaikuṇṭhavarṇane BhP yac ca vrajanty animiṣāṃ ṛṣabhānuvṛttyādūre yamā hy upari naḥ spṛhaṇīyaśīlāḥ bhartur mithaḥ suyaśasaḥ kathanānurāgavaiklavyabāṣpakalayā pulakīkṛtāṅgāḥ  Hbhv daśame ca śrībrahmastutau BhP pureha bhūman bahavo pi yoginastvadarpitehā nijakarmalabdhayā vibudhya bhaktyaiva kathopanītayāprapedireñjo cyuta te gatiṃ parām  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye bhagavattoṣapraśnottare sarvadevamayo viṣṇuḥ śaraṇārtipranāśanaḥ svabhaktavatsalo devo bhaktyā tuṣyati nānyathā  Hbhv saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādasya bālopadeśe BhP nālaṃ dvijatvaṃ devatvaṃ ṛṣitvaṃ vāsurātmajāḥ prīṇanāya mukundasya na vṛttaṃ na bahujñatā  Hbhv na dānaṃ na tapo nejyā na śaucaṃ na vratāni ca prīyatemalayā bhaktyā harir anyad viḍambanam  Hbhv śrīnṛsiṃhastutau ca BhP manye dhanābhijanarūpatapaḥśrutaujastejaḥprabhāvabalapauruṣabuddhiyogāḥ nārādhanāya hi bhavanti parasya puṃsobhaktyā tutoṣa bhagavān gajayūthapāya  Hbhv anyatrāpi Padyāvalī vyādhasyācaraṇaṃ dhruvasya ca vayo vidyā gajendrasya kākubjāyāḥ kim u nāma rūpam adhikaṃ kiṃ tat sudāmno dhanam vaṃśaḥ ko vidurasya yādavapater ugrasya kiṃ pauruṣaṃbhaktyā tuṣyati kevalaṃ na ca guṇair bhaktipriyo mādhavaḥ  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ śrībhagavatā Gītā patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati tad ahaṃ bhaktyupahṛtam aśnāmi prayatātmanaḥ  Hbhv prathamaskandhe śrīhanumatoktamna janma nūnaṃ mahato na saubhagaṃna vāṅ na buddhir nākṛtis toṣahetuḥ tair yad visṛṣṭān api no vanaukasaścakāra sakhe bata lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ  Hbhv śrībhagavatsaṅgamakatvamśrībhagavadgītāsu bhaktyā tv ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidho rjuna jñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca tattvena praveṣṭuṃ ca paraṃtapa  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP yathāgninā hemamalaṃ jahātidhmātaṃ punaḥ svaṃ bhajate ca rūpam ātmā ca karmānuśayaṃ vidhūyamadbhaktiyogena bhajaty atho mām  Hbhv kiṃ ca BhP bhaktyoddhavānapāyinyā sarvalokamaheśvaram sarvotpattyapyayaṃ brahma kāraṇaṃ mopayāti saḥ  Hbhv śrībhagavadvaśīkāratvampādme kārttikamāhātmye śrīnāradaśaunakasaṃvādebhuktiṃ muktiṃ harir dadyāt arcito nyatra sevinām bhaktiṃ ca dadāty eṣa yato vaśyakarī hareḥ  Hbhv tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvādemāyājāniramāyo sau bhaktyā rājan na māyayā sādhyate sādhupuruṣaiḥ svayaṃ jānāti tad bhavān  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe ca tatraiva BhP na sādhayati māṃ yogo na sāṅkhyaṃ dharma uddhava na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo yathā bhaktir mamorjitā  Hbhv dharmaḥ satyadayopeto vidyā vā tapasānvitā madbhaktyāpetam ātmānaṃ na samyak prapunāti hi  Hbhv svataḥ paramapuruṣārthatātṛtīyaskandhe śrīkāpileye BhP sālokyasārṣṭisāmīpya sārūpyaikatvam apy uta dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā matsevanaṃ janāḥ  Hbhv navamaskandhe cāmbarīṣopākhyāne śrībhagavaduktau BhP matsevayā pratītaṃ te sālokyādicatuṣṭayam necchanti sevayā pūrṇāḥ kuto nyat kālaviplutam  Hbhv iti māhātmyaṃ yac ca bhagavadbhaktānāṃ likhitaṃ purā tadbhakter api vijñeyaṃ teṣāṃ bhaktyaiva tattvataḥ  Hbhv tathā pūjā tadaṅgānāṃ śrīmannāmno parasya ca draṣṭavyam iha māhātmyaṃ teṣāṃ bhaktyaṅgatā yataḥ  Hbhv atha śrīmadbhagavadbhaktinityatāyāvaj jano bhajati no bhuvi viṣṇubhaktivārtāsudhārasaviśeṣarasaikasāram tāvaj jarāmaraṇajanmaśatābhighātaduḥkhāni tāni labhate bahudehajāni  Hbhv daśame brahmastutau BhP śreyaḥsṛtiṃ bhaktim udasya te vibhokliśyanti ye kevelabodhalabdhaye teṣām asau kleśala eva śiṣyatenānyad yathā sthūlatuṣāvaghātinām  Hbhv ekādaśe BhP mukhabāhūrupādebhyaḥ puruṣasyāśramaiḥ saha catvāro jajñire varṇā guṇair viprādayaḥ pṛthak  Hbhv ya evaṃ puruṣaṃ sākṣād ātmaprabhavam īśvaram na bhajanty avajānanti sthānād bhraṣṭāḥ patanty adhaḥ  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ śrībhagavatā Gītā  na māṃ duṣkṛtino mūḍhāḥ prapadyante narādhamāḥ māyayāpahṛtajñānā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥ  Hbhv nityatvaṃ yad yad aṅgānāṃ bhakter vilikhitaṃ purā tena tenaiva nityatvam asyāṃ saṃsādhitaṃ param  Hbhv lakṣaṇāni ca tadbhakteḥ śrīmadbhāgavatādiṣu khyātāni śravaṇādīni likhyantethāpi kānicit  Hbhv atha śrīmadbhaktilakṣaṇānitatra sāmānyalakṣaṇamtṛtīyaskandhe śrīkāpileye BhP  devānāṃ guṇaliṅgānām ānuśravikakarmaṇām sattva evaikamanaso vṛttiḥ svābhāvikī tu yā animittā bhāgavatī bhaktiḥ siddher garīyasī  Hbhv atha viśeṣasādhanabhaktilakṣaṇānigautamīyatantre devatāyāṃ ca mantre ca tathā mantraprade gurau bhaktir aṣṭavidhā yasya tasya kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati  Hbhv tadbhaktajanavātsalyaṃ pūjāyāṃ cānumodanam sumanā arcayen nityaṃ tadarthe dambhavarjanam  Hbhv tatkathāśravaṇe rāgas tadarthe cāṅgavikriyā tadanusmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ yas tannāmopajīvati  Hbhv bhaktir aṣṭavidhā hy eṣā yasmin mlecchepi vartate sa muniḥ satyavādī ca kīrtimān sa bhaven naraḥ  Hbhv bhaktir aṣṭavidhā hy eṣā yasmin mlecchepi vartate sa muniḥ satyavādī ca kīrtimān sa bhaven naraḥ  Hbhv saptamaskandhe prahlādoktau BhP  śravaṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ viṣṇoḥ smaraṇaṃ pādasevanam arcanaṃ vandanaṃ dāsyaṃ sakhyam ātmanivedanam  Hbhv iti puṃsārpitā viṣṇau bhaktiś cen navalakṣaṇā kriyeta bhagavaty addhā tan manyedhītam uttamam  Hbhv tatraiva śrīnāradayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvāde BhP  śravaṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ cāsya smaraṇaṃ mahatāṃ gateḥ sevejyāvanatir dāsyaṃ sakhyam ātmasamarpaṇam  Hbhv pādme kārttikamāhātmye śrīyamadhūmraketusaṃvāde śravaṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ pūjā sarvakarmārpaṇaṃ smṛtiḥ paricaryā namaskāraḥ prema svātmārpaṇaṃ harau  Hbhv tatraivottarakhaṇḍe śrīśivapārvatīsaṃvāde PadmaP ādyaṃ tu vaiṣṇavaṃ proktaṃ śaṅkhacakrāṅkanaṃ hareḥ dhāraṇaṃ cordhvarpuṇḍrāṇāntanmantrāṇāṃ parigrahaḥ  Hbhv arcanaṃ ca japo dhyānaṃ tannāmasmaraṇaṃ tathā kīrtanaṃ śravaṇaṃ caiva vandanaṃ pādasevanam  Hbhv tatpādodakasevā ca tanniveditabhojanam tadīyānāṃ ca sevāṃ ca dvādaśīvrataniṣṭhitam  Hbhv tulasīropaṇaṃ viṣṇor devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ bhaktiḥ ṣoḍaśadhā proktā bhavabandhavimuktaye  Hbhv iti kiṃ ca darśanaṃ bhagavanmūrteḥ sparśanaṃ kṣetrasevanam āghrāṇaṃ dhūpaśeṣāder nirmālyasya ca dhāraṇam  Hbhv nṛtyaṃ bhagavadagre ca tathā vīṇādivādanam kṛṣṇalīlādyabhinayaḥ śrībhāgavatasevanam  Hbhv padmākṣamālāvidhṛtir ekādaśyādijāgaraḥ prāsādaracanādyanyaj jñeyaṃ śāstrānusārataḥ  Hbhv likhitā bhagavaddharmā bhaktānāṃ lakṣaṇāni ca tāni jñeyāni sarvāṇi bhakter vai lakṣaṇāṃ na hi  Hbhv teṣu jñeyāni gauṇāni mukhyāni ca vivekibhiḥ bahiraṅgāntaraṅgāṇi premasiddhau ca tāni yat  Hbhv bhedās tu vividhā bhakter bhaktabhāvādibhedataḥ muktāphalādigranthebhyo jñeyās tal likhanair alam  Hbhv premabhaktau ca siddhāyāṃ sarverthāḥ sevakāḥ svayam bhagavāṃś cātivaśyaḥ syāl likhyatesyāḥ sulakṣaṇam  Hbhv atha premabhaktilakṣaṇamnāradapañcarātreananyamamatā viṣṇau mamatā premasamplutā bhaktir ity ucyate bhīṣmaprahlādoddhavanāradaiḥ  Hbhv iti atha śrīmadbhakter durlabhatvampremabhakteś ca māhātmyaṃ bhakter māhātmyataḥ param siddham eva yato bhakteḥ phalaṃ premaiva niścitam  Hbhv cihnāni premasampatter bāhyāny abhyantarāṇi ca kiyanty ullikhatā tasyā mahimaiva vilikhyate  Hbhv saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādasya prahlādasya bālānuśāsane BhP niśamya karmāṇi guṇān atulyānvīryāṇi līlātanubhiḥ kṛtāni yadātiharṣotpulakāśrugadgadaṃprotkaṇṭha udgāyati rauti nṛtyati  Hbhv yadā grahagrasta iva kvacid dhasatyākrandate dhyāyati vandate janam muhuḥ śvasan vakti hare jagatpatenārāyaṇety ātmamatir gatatrapaḥ  Hbhv tadā pumān muktasamastabandhanastadbhāvabhāvānukṛtāśayākṛtiḥ nirdagdhabījānuśayo mahīyasābhaktiprayogeṇa samety adhokṣajam  Hbhv ekādaśe ca śrīkaviyogeśvarottare BhP śṛṇvan subhadrāṇi rathāṅgapāṇerjanmāni karmāṇi ca yāni loke gītāni nāmāni tadarthakānigāyan vilajjo vicared asaṅgaḥ  Hbhv evaṃvrataḥ svapriyanāmakīrtyājātānurāgo drutacitta uccaiḥ hasaty atho roditi rauti gāyatyunmādavan nṛtyati lokabāhyaḥ  Hbhv tatraiva śrīprabuddhayogeśvarottare BhP smarantaḥ smārayantaś ca mitho ghaughaharaṃ harim bhaktyā sañjātayā bhaktyā bibhraty utpulakāṃ tanum  Hbhv kvacid rudanty acyutacintayā kvaciddhasanti nandanti vadanty alaukikāḥ nṛtyanti gāyanty anuśīlayanty ajaṃbhavanti tūṣṇīṃ param etya nirvṛtāḥ  Hbhv śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde ca BhP kathaṃ vinā romaharṣaṃ dravatā cetasā vināvinānandāśrukalayā śudhyed bhaktyā vināśayaḥ  Hbhv vāg gadgadā dravate yasya cittaṃrudaty abhīkṣṇaṃ hasati kvacic ca vilajja udgāyati nṛtyate camadbhaktiyukto bhuvanaṃ punāti  Hbhv yathoktabhaktyaśaktau tu bhagavaccaraṇāmbujam śaraṇāgatabhāvena kṛtsnabhītighnam āśrayet  Hbhv atha śaraṇāpattiḥśrīmadbhagavadgītāsu sarvadharmān parityajya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ  Hbhv ekādaśaskandhe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP tasmāt tvam uddhavotsṛjya codanāṃ praticodanām pravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ ca śrotavyaṃ śrutam eva ca  Hbhv mām ekam eva śaraṇam ātmānaṃ sarvadehinām yāhi sarvātmabhāvena mayā syā hy akutobhayaḥ  Hbhv tannityatā cabrahmavaivarteprāpyāpi durlabhataraṃ mānuṣyaṃ vibudhepsitam yair āśrito na govindas tair ātmā vañcitaś ciram  Hbhv aśīticaturaś caiva lakṣāṃs tān jīvajātiṣu bhramadbhiḥ puruṣaiḥ prāpya mānuṣyaṃ janmaparyayāt  Hbhv tad apy aphalatāṃ jātaṃ teṣām ātmābhimāninām varākānām anāśritya govindacaraṇadvayam  Hbhv atha śaraṇāpattimāhātmyamuktaṃ ca rāmāyaṇe śrīraghunāthena vibhīṣaṇagamanaprasaṅgesakṛd eva prapanno yas tavāsmīti ca yācate abhayaṃ sarvadā tasmai dadāmy etad vrataṃ hareḥ  Hbhv nārasiṃhe vaikuṇṭhanāthenatvāṃ prapanno smi śaraṇaṃ devadevaṃ janārdanam iti yaḥ śaraṇaṃ prāptas taṃ kleśād uddharāmy aham  Hbhv nāmāparādhaprasaṅge pādme śrīnāradaṃ prati śrīsanatkumāreṇasarvācāravivarjitāḥ śaṭhadhiyo vrātyā jagadvañcakādambhāhaṅkṛtipānapaiśunaparāḥ pāpāntyajā niṣṭhurā ye cānye dhanadāraputraniratāḥ sarvādhamās tepi hiśrīgovindapadāravindaśaraṇā muktā bhavanti dvija  Hbhv brahmavaivartena hi nārāyaṇaṃ nāma narāḥ saṃśritya śaunaka prāpnuvanty aśubhaa satyam idam uktaṃ punaḥ punaḥ  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅgeparamārtham aśeṣasya jagatām ādikāraṇam śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāto govindaḥ nāvasīdati  Hbhv śāntiparvaṇi MBh  rājadharme bhīṣmayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvādesthitaḥ priyahite jiṣṇoḥ sa eva puruṣarṣabha rājaṃs tava ca durdharṣo vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ  Hbhv ya enaṃ saṃśrayantīha bhaktyā nārāyaṇaṃ harim te tarantīha durgāṇi na metrāsti vicāraṇā  Hbhv tṛtīyaskandhe viduramaitreyasaṃvāde BhP śārīrā mānasā divyā vaiyāse ye ca mānuṣāḥ bhautikāś ca kathaṃ kleśā bādhante harisaṃśrayam  Hbhv vāmane śrīprahlādabalisaṃvādeye saṃśritā harim anantam anādimadhyaṃnārāyaṇaṃ suraguruṃ śubhadaṃ vareṇyam śuddhaṃ khagendragamanaṃ kamalālayeśaṃte dharmarājakaraṇaṃ na viśanti dhīrāḥ  Hbhv ye śaṅkhacakrābjakaraṃ saśārṅgiṇaṃkhagendraketuṃ varadaṃ śriyaḥ patim samāśrayante bhavabhītināśaṃteṣāṃ bhayaṃ nāsti vimuktibhājām  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye prāyaścittaprakaraṇāntesaṃsāresmin mahāghore mohanidrāsamākule ye hariṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti te kṛtārthā na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv brahmapurāṇekarmaṇā manasā vācā yecyutaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ na samartho yamas teṣāṃ te muktiphalabhāginaḥ  Hbhv daśamaskandhe BhP samāśritā ye padapallavaplavaṃmahatpadaṃ puṇyayaśo murāreḥ bhavāmbudhir vatsapadaṃ paraṃ padaṃpadaṃ padaṃ yad vipadāṃ na teṣām  Hbhv prathame BhP yatpādasaṃśrayāḥ sūta munayaḥ praśamāyanāḥ sadyaḥ punanty upaspṛṣṭāḥ svardhunyāpo nusevayā  Hbhv dvitīye śrīśukoktau BhP kirātahūṇāndhrapulindapulkaśāābhīraśumbhā yavanāḥ khasādayaḥ yenye ca pāpā yadapāśrayāśrayāḥśudhyanti tasmai prabhaviṣṇave namaḥ  Hbhv tṛtīye maitreyoktau BhP kiṃ durāpādanaṃ teṣāṃ puṃsām uddāmacetasām yair āśritas tīrthapadaś caraṇo vyasanātyayaḥ  Hbhv daśame nāgapatnīstutau BhP na nākapṛṣṭhaṃ na ca pārameṣṭhyaṃna sārvabhaumaṃ na rasādhipatyam na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vāsamañjasa tvā virahayya kāṅkṣe  Hbhv ekādaśe ca śrīkarabhājanayogeśvarottare BhP devarṣibhūtāptanṝṇāṃ pitṝṇāṃnāyaṃ kiṅkaro nāyaṃ ṛṇī ca rājan sarvātmanā yaḥ śaraṇaṃ śaraṇyaṃgato mukundaṃ parihṛtya kartam  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ śrībhagavantaṃ prati uddhavena BhP tāpatrayeṇābhihatasya ghoresantapyamānasya bhavādhvanīśa paśyāmi nānyac charaṇaṃ tavāṅghridvandvātapatrād amṛtābhivarṣāt  Hbhv itthaṃ ca bodhyaṃ vidvadbhiḥ śaraṇāpattilakṣaṇam vācā hṛdā ca tanvāpi kṛṣṇaikāśrayaṇaṃ hi yat  Hbhv atha śaraṇāpattilakṣaṇamskandhegovindaṃ paramānandaṃ mukundaṃ madhusūdanam tyaktvānyaṃ vai na jānāmi na bhajāmi smarāmi na  Hbhv na namāmi na ca staumi na paśyāmi svacakṣuṣā na spṛhāmi na gāyāmi na vā yāmi hariṃ vinā  Hbhv iti kecid āhuś ca śaraṇāgatatvaṃ ṣaṭprakārakam prāyaḥ sakhyaprakāre tat paryavasyed vicārataḥ  Hbhv tac coktaṃ vaiṣṇavatantreānukūlyasya saṅkalpaḥ prātikūlyavivarjanam rakṣiṣyatīti viśvāso goptṛtve varaṇaṃ tathā ātmanikṣepakārpaṇye ṣaḍvidhā śaraṇāgatiḥ  Hbhv iti tavāsmīti vadan vācā tathaiva manasā vidan tatsthānam āśritas tanvā modate śaraṇāgataḥ  Hbhv ataivoktaṃ daśame śrībhagavantaṃ prati akrūreṇa BhP kaḥ paṇḍitas tvad aparaṃ śaraṇaṃ samīyādbhaktapriyād ṛtagiraḥ suhṛdaḥ kṛtajñāt sarvān dadāti suhṛdo bhajato bhikāmānātmanam apy upacayāpacayau na yasya  Hbhv tṛtīye śrīuddhavena BhP aho bakī yaṃ stanakālakūṭaṃjighāṃsayāpāyayad apy asādhvī lebhe gatiṃ dhātryucitāṃ tato nyaṃkaṃ vā dayāluṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajema  Hbhv iti athācārā bahuvidhāḥ śiṣṭācārānusārataḥ śrīvaiṣṇavānāṃ kartavyā likhyantetra samāsataḥ  Hbhv athācārāḥśrīviṣṇupurāṇe aurvasagarasaṃvāde gṛhasthācārakathanārambhe ViP devagobrāhmaṇān siddhān vṛddhācāryāṃs tathārcayet dvikālaṃ ca namet sandhyām agnīn upacaret tathā  Hbhv sadānupahate vastre praśastāṃ ca tathauṣadhīḥ gāruḍāni ca ratnāni vibhṛyāt prayato naraḥ  Hbhv prasnigdhāmalakeśaś ca sugandhaś cāruveśadhṛk kiṃcit parasvaṃ na haret nālpam apy apriyaṃ vadet  Hbhv priyaṃ ca nānṛtaṃ brūyān nānyadoṣān udīrayetnānyastriyaṃ tathā vairaṃ rocayet puruṣarṣabha  Hbhv na duṣṭaṃ yānam ārohet kulacchāyāṃ na saṃśrayet  Hbhv vidviṣṭapatitonmattabahuvairādikīṭakaiḥ bandhakī bandhakībhartuḥ kṣudrānṛtakathaiḥ saha  Hbhv tathātivyayaśīlaiś ca parivādarataiḥ śaṭhaiḥ budho maitrīṃ na kurvīta naikaḥ panthānam āśrayet  Hbhv nāvagāhej jalaughasya vegam agre nareśvara pradīptaṃ veśma na viśen nārohec chikharaṃ taroḥ  Hbhv na kuryād dantasaṅgharṣaṃ kuṣṇīyāc ca na nāsikām nāsaṃvṛtamukho jṛmbhec chvāsakāsau visarjayet  Hbhv noccair haset saśabdaṃ ca na muñcet pavanaṃ budhaḥ nakhān na khādayec chindyān na tṛṇaṃ na mahīṃ likhet  Hbhv na śmaśru bhakṣayel loṣṭaṃ na mūdnīyād vicakṣaṇaḥ  Hbhv jyotīṃṣy amedhyaśastāni nābhivīkṣeta ca prabho  Hbhv na huṅkuryāc chavaṃ gandhaṃ śavagandho hi somajaḥ  Hbhv catuṣpathaṃ ciatyataruṃ śmaśānopavanāni ca duṣṭastrīsannikarṣaṃ ca varjayen niśi sarvadā pūjyadevadvijajyotiśchāyāṃ nātikramed budhaḥ  Hbhv naikaḥ śūnyāṭavīṃ gacchet tathā śūnyagṛhe vaset  Hbhv keśāsthikaṇṭakāmedhyabalibhasmatuṣāṃs tathā snānārdradharaṇīṃ caiva dūrataḥ parivarjayet  Hbhv nānārthānāśrayet kāṃścin na jihmaṃ rocayed budhaḥ  Hbhv upasarpen na vai vyālaṃ ciraṃ tiṣṭhen na cotthitaḥ yatheṣṭabhojakāṃś caiva tathā devaparāṅmukhān varṇāśramakriyātītān dūrataḥ parivarjayet  Hbhv atīva jāgarasvapnau tadvat sthānāsane budhaḥ na seveta tathā śayyāṃ vyāyāmaṃ ca nareśvara  Hbhv daṃṣṭriṇaḥ śṛṅgiṇaś caiva prājño dūreṇa varjayet  Hbhv avaśyāyaṃ ca rājendra puro vātātapau tathā na snāyān na svapen nagno na caivopaspṛśed budhaḥ  Hbhv muktakacchaś ca nācāmed devādyarcāṃ ca varjayet naikavastraḥ pravartetaa dvijavācanike jape  Hbhv kiṃ ca ViP   na ca nirdhūnayet keśān nācāmec caiva cotthitaḥ pādena nākramet pādaṃ na pūjyābhimukhaṃ nayet  Hbhv apasavyaṃ na gacchec ca devāgāracatuṣpathān maṅgalyapūjyāṃś ca tathā viparītān na dakṣiṇām  Hbhv somārkāgnyambuvāyūnāṃ pūjyānāṃ ca na sammukham kuryān niṣṭhīvaviṇmūtrasamutsargaṃ ca paṇḍitaḥ  Hbhv tiṣṭhan na mūtrayet tadvat pathiṣv api na mūtrayet śleṣmaviṇmūtraraktāni sarvadaiva na laṅghayet  Hbhv śleṣmaṣṭīvanakotsargo nānnakāle praśasyate balimaṅgalajapyādau na home na mahājane  Hbhv yoṣito nāvamanyeta na cāsāṃ viśvased budhaḥ na caiverṣyur bhavet tāsu nādhikuryāt kadācana  Hbhv maṅgalyapuṣparatnājyapūjyānanabhivādya ca na niṣkrāmed gṛhāt prājñaḥ sadācāraparo naraḥ  Hbhv akālagarjitādau tu parvasvaśaucakādiṣu anadhyāyaṃ budhaḥ kuryād uparāgādike tathā  Hbhv varṣātapādike chatrī daṇḍī rātryaṭavīṣu ca śarīratrāṇakāmo vai sopānatkaḥ sadā vrajet  Hbhv nordhvaṃ na tiryagdūraṃ vā nirīkṣan paryaṭed budhaḥ yugamātraṃ mahīpṛṣṭhaṃ naro gacched vilokayan  Hbhv kiṃ ca ViP priyam uktaṃ hitaṃ naitad iti matvā na tad vadet śreyas tadrahitaṃ vācyaṃ yadyapy atyantavipriyam  Hbhv prāṇinām upakārāya yad eveha paratra ca karmaṇā manasā vācā tad eva matimān bhajet  Hbhv bṛhannāradīye sadācāraprasaṅge asāv aham iti brūyād dvijo vai hy abhivādane śrāddhaṃ vrataṃ tathā dānaṃ devatābhyarcanaṃ tathā yajñaṃ ca tarpaṇaṃ caiva kurvantaṃ nābhivādayet  Hbhv tathā snānaṃ prakurvantaṃ dhāvantam aśuciṃ tathā bhuñjānaṃ ca abhyaktaśirasaṃ tathā  Hbhv bhikṣānnadhāriṇaṃ caiva ramantaṃ jalamadhyagam kṛtebhivādane yas tu na kuryāt prativādanam nābhivādyaḥ sa vijñeyo yathā śūdras tathaiva saḥ  Hbhv mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇemadrālasālarkasaṃvādemārkaṇḍeyapurāṇemadrālasālarkasaṃvādeasatpralāpam anṛtaṃ vkpāruṣyaṃ ca varjayet asacchāstram asadvādam asatsevāṃ ca putraka  Hbhv keśaprasādhanādarśadarśanaṃ dantadhāvanam pūrvāhna eva kāryāṇi devatānāṃ ca tarpaṇam  Hbhv udakyā darśanaṃ sparśaṃ varjeta sambhāṣaṇaṃ tathā  Hbhv na cābhīkṣṇaṃ śiraḥsnānaṃ kuryān niṣkāraṇaṃ naraḥ śiraḥsnātaś ca tailena nāṅgaṃ kiṃcid api spṛśet  Hbhv panthā deyo brāhmaṇānāṃ rājo duḥkhāturasya ca vidyādhikasya gurviṇyā bhārārtasya mahīyasaḥ  Hbhv mūkāndhavadhirāṇāṃ ca mattasyonmattakasya ca puṃścalyāḥ kṛtavairasya bālasya patitasya ca  Hbhv upānadvastramālyāni dhṛtāny anyair na dhārayet upavītam alaṅkāraṃ kavalaṃ caiva varjayet  Hbhv na kṣiptabāhujaṅghaś ca prājñas tiṣṭhet kadācana na cāpi vikṣipet pādau vāsasā na ca dhūnayet  Hbhv mūrkhonmattavyasanino virūpān māyinas tathā nyūnāṅgānadhamāṃś caiva nopahāsen na dūṣayet  Hbhv parasya daṇḍaṃ nodyacchet śikṣārthaṃ putraśiṣyayoḥ nānulepanam ādadyād asnātaḥ snātakī kvacit  Hbhv na cāpi raktavāsāḥ syāc citravāsadharo pi vā kṣurakarmaṇi cānte ca strīsambhoge ca putraka snāyīta celavān prājñaḥ kaṭabhūmim upetya ca  Hbhv yugapaj jalam agniṃ ca bibhṛyān na vicakṣaṇaḥ nācakṣīta dhayantīṃ gāṃ jalaṃ nāñjalinā pibet  Hbhv śaucakāleṣu sarveṣu guruṣv alpeṣu vā punaḥ na vilambeta śaucārthaṃ na mukhenānalaṃ dhamet  Hbhv vipurṣo makṣikādyāś ca hastasaṅgād adoṣiṇaḥ ajāśvau muhato medhyau na gor vatsasya cānanam  Hbhv mātuḥ prasnavane medhyaṃ śakuniḥ phalapātane udakyāśaucinagnāṃś ca sūtikāntyācasāyinaḥ spṛṣṭvā snāyīta śaucārthaṃ tathaiva mṛtahāriṇaḥ  Hbhv nāraṃ spṛṣṭvāsthi sasnehaṃ snātaḥ śudhyati mānavaḥ ācamyaiva tu nisnehaṃ gām ālabhyārkam īkṣya vā  Hbhv na cālapej janaṃ dviṣṭaṃ vīrahīnāṃ tathā striyam devatātithisacchāstrayajñasiddhādinindakaiḥ  Hbhv kṛtvā tu sparśatālāpaṃ śudhyed arkāvalokanāt avalokya tathodakyām antyajān patitaṃ śaṭham vidharmisūtikāṣaṇḍavivastrānyāvasāyinaḥ  Hbhv mṛtaniryātakāś caiva paradāraratāś ca ye etad eva hi kartavyaṃ prājñaiḥ śodhanam ātmanaḥ  Hbhv kiṃ cayac cāpi kurvato nātmā jugupsām eti putraka tat kartavyam aśaṅkena yan na gopyaṃ mahājane  Hbhv bhaviṣyottare śrīkṛṣṇayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvādeupāsate na ye pūrvāṃ dvijāḥ sandhyāṃ na paścimām sarvāms tān dhārmiko rājā śūdrakarmaṇi yojayet  Hbhv dūrād āvasathān mūtraṃ dūrāt pādāvasecanam ucchiṣṭotsarjanaṃ bhūpa sadā kāryā hitaiṣiṇā  Hbhv ucchiṣṭau na spṛśec chīrṣaṃ sarve prāṇās tadāśrayāḥ keśagrāhān prahārāṃś ca śirasy etāni varjayet na pāṇibhyām ubhābhyāṃ tu kaṇḍūyāj jātu vai śiraḥ  Hbhv kiṃ casuvāsinīr gurviṇīś ca vṛddhaṃ bālāturau tathā bhojayet saṃskṛtānn eva prathamaṃ caramaṃ gṛhī  Hbhv aghaṃ sa kevalaṃ bhuṅkte vṛddhe govāhanādike yo bhuṅkte pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha prekṣatām apradāya ca  Hbhv varjayed dadhiśaktuṃ ca rātrau dhānāś ca vāsare  Hbhv kiṃ casrajaś ca nāvakarṣeta na bahir dhārayeta ca gṛhe pārāvatā dhanyāḥ śukāś ca sahasārikāḥ  Hbhv kaurme vyāsagītāyāmtṛṇaṃ vā yadi vā śākaṃ mūlaṃ vā jalam eva vā parasyāpaharan jantur narakaṃ pratipadyate  Hbhv na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇīyān na śūdrāt patitād api nānyasmād yācakatvaṃ ca ninditād varjayed budhaḥ  Hbhv nityaṃ yācanako na syāt punas tatraiva yācayet prāṇān apaharaty eṣa yācakas tasya durmatiḥ  Hbhv na devadravyahārī syād viśeṣeṇa dvijottamāḥ brahmasvaṃ ca nāpahared āpady api kadācana  Hbhv na viṣaṃ viṣam ity āhur brahmasvaṃ viṣam ucyate devasvaṃ vāpi yatnena sadā pariharet tataḥ  Hbhv na dharmasyāpadeśena pāpaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caret vratena pāpaṃ pracchādya kurvan strīśūdradambhanam pretyeha cedṛśo vipro garhyeta brahmavādibhiḥ  Hbhv devadrohād gurudrohaḥ koṭikoṭiguṇādhikaḥ jñānāpavāo nāstikyaṃ tasmād koṭiguṇādhikam  Hbhv kiṃ cahimavadvindhyayor madhye pūrvapaścimayoḥ śubham muktvā samudrayor deśaṃ nānyatra nivased dvijaḥ  Hbhv kṛṣṇo vā yatra carati mṛgo nityaṃ svabhāvataḥ puṇyāś ca viśrutā nadyas tatra vā nivased dvijaḥ ardhakrośān nadīkulaṃ varjayitvā dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv kiṃ caagninā bhasmanā caiva salilena viśeṣataḥ dvāreṇa stambhamārgeṇa padbhiḥ paṅktir vibhidyate parakṣetre carantīṃ gāṃ na cācakṣīta kasyacit  Hbhv naṣuryapariveśaṃ vā nendracāpaṃ na cāgnikam parasmai kathayed vidvān śaśinaṃ vā kathaṃcana tithiṃ pakṣasya na brūyān nakṣatrāṇi vinirdiśet  Hbhv na devaguruviprāṇāṃ dīyamānaṃ tu vārayet nindayed yo gurūn devān vedaṃ vā sopabṛṃhitam kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ raurave pacyate naraḥ  Hbhv tūṣṇīm āsīta nindāyāṃ na brūyāt kiṃcid uttaram karṇau pidhāya gantavyaṃ na cainam avalokayet  Hbhv varjayed rahasyaṃ ca pareṣāṃ gūhayed budhaḥ vivādaṃ svajanaiḥ sārdhaṃ na kuryād vai kadācana  Hbhv na pāpaṃ pāpinaṃ brūyād apāpaṃ vā dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv nekṣetodyantam ādityaṃ śaśinaṃ vā nimittataḥ  Hbhv āstaṃ yāntaṃ na vāristhaṃ nopasṛṣṭaṃ na madhyagam tirohitaṃ vāsasā vā na darśāntaragāminam  Hbhv nagnāṃ striyaṃ pumāṃsaṃ vā purīṣaṃ mūtram eva vā patitavyaṅgacāṇḍālān ucchiṣṭānucchiṣṭān nāvalokayet  Hbhv na muktabandhanāṃ gāṃ vā nonmattaṃ mattam eva vā spṛśen na bhojane patnīṃ nainām īkṣeta mehatīm  Hbhv kṣubantīṃ jṛmbhamāṇāṃ vā nāsanasthāṃ yathā sukham nodake cātmano rūpaṃ nakulaṃ śvabhram eva vā  Hbhv na śūdrāya matiṃ dadyāt kṛṣaraṃ pāyasaṃ dadhi nocchiṣṭaṃ vā ghṛtamadhu na ca kṛṣṇājinaṃ haviḥ  Hbhv na kuryāt kasyacit pīḍāṃ sutaṃ śiṣyaṃ ca tāḍayet nātmānam avamanyeta dainyaṃ yatnena varjayet na ca śiṣyānnaṃ satkuryān nātmānaṃ śaṃsayed budhaḥ  Hbhv na nadīṃ ca nadīṃ brūyāt parvateṣu na parvatam āvaset tena naivāpi yas tyajet sahavāsinam  Hbhv śiro bhyaṅgāvaśiṣṭena talenāṅgaṃ na lepayet romāṇi ca rahasyāni svāni khāni na ca spṛśet  Hbhv na pāṇipādavāṅnetracāpalāni samāśrayet nābhihanyāj jalaṃ padbhyāṃ pāṇinā na kadācana  Hbhv na ghātayed iṣṭakābhiḥ phalāni na phalena ca na mlecchabhāṣaṇaṃ śikṣen na karṣec ca padāsanam  Hbhv notsaṅge bhakṣayed bhakṣyān gāṃ ca saṃveśayen na hi nākṣaiḥ krīḍen na dhāveta strībhir vādaṃ ca cācaret  Hbhv na dantair nakhalomāni chindyāt suptaṃ na bodhayet na bālātapam āsevet pretadhūmaṃ vivarjayet  Hbhv naikaḥ supyāt śūnyagṛhe svayaṃ nopānahau haret nākāraṇād vā niṣṭhīven na bāhubhyāṃ nadīṃ taret  Hbhv na pādakṣālanaṃ kuryāt pādenaiva kadācana nāgnau pratāpayet pādau na kāṃsye dhārayed budhaḥ  Hbhv nābhipratārayed devān brāhmaṇān gām athāpi vā na spṛśet pāninocchiṣṭo viprā gobrāhmaṇānalān na caivānnaṃ padā vāpi na devapratimāṃ spṛśet  Hbhv nottared anupaspṛśya sravantīṃ no vyatikramet caityaṃ bṛhmaṃ naiva chindyān nāpsu ṣṭhīvanam utsṛjet na cāgniṃ laṅghayed dhīmān nopadadhyād adhaḥ kvacit  Hbhv na cainaṃ pādataḥ kuryāt tilabaddhaṃ niśi tyajet na kūpam avaroheta nācakṣītāśuciḥ kvacit  Hbhv agnau na prakṣiped agniṃ nādbhiḥ praśamayet tathā suhṛnmaraṇam ārtiṃ vā na svayaṃ śrāvayet parān apaṇyam atha paṇyaṃ vā vikrayaṃ na prayojayet  Hbhv puṇyasthānodakasthāne sīmāntaṃ vā kṛṣen na tu bhindyāt pūrvasamayaṃ satryopetaṃ kadācana  Hbhv parasparaṃ paśūn vyālān pakṣiṇo na ca yodhayet kārayitvā svakarmāṇi kārūn vidvān na vañcayet  Hbhv bahir gandhaṃ ca kudvārapraveśaṃ ca vivarjayet naikaś caret sabhāṃ vipraḥ samavāyaṃ ca varjayet  Hbhv na vījayed vā vastreṇa na devāyatane svapet nāgnigobrāhmaṇādīnām antareṇa vrajet kvacit  Hbhv nākrāmet kāmataś chāyāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ gavām api svāntu nākrāmayec chāyaṃ patitādyair na rogibhiḥ  Hbhv nāśnīyāt payasā takraṃ na bījāny upabījayet vivatsāyāś ca goḥ kṣīram auṣṭraṃ vā nirdaśasya ca āvikaṃ sandhinīkṣīram apeyaṃ manur abravīt  Hbhv hantakāram athāgryaṃ vā bhikṣāṃ vā śaktito dvijaḥ dadyād atithaye nityaṃ budhyeta parameśvaram  Hbhv bhikṣām āhur grāsamātram agryaṃ tasmāc caturguṇam puṣkalaṃ hantakāraṃ tu tac caturguṇam iṣyate  Hbhv mārkaṇḍeyebhojanaṃ hantakāraṃ vā agryaṃ bhikṣām athāpi vā adattvā tu na bhoktavyaṃ yathāvibhavam ātmanaḥ  Hbhv kāśīkhaṇḍenaivotkaṭāsaneśnīyān nāgnau vastv aśuci kṣipet śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā paraśrāddhe yo śnīyāj jñānavarjitaḥ dātuḥ śrāddhaphalaṃ nāsti bhoktā kilbiṣabhug bhavet  Hbhv notpāṭayel lomanakhaṃ daśanena kadācana karajaiḥ karajacchedaṃ kareṇaiva vivarjayet  Hbhv apadvāre na gantavyaṃ svaveśmaparaveśmanoḥ utkocadyutadautyārthadravyaṃ dūrāt parityajet  Hbhv niṣṭhīvanaṃ ca śleṣmāṇaṃ gṛhād dūre vinikṣipet uddhṛtya pañca mṛtpiṇḍān snāyāt parajalāśaye anuddhṛtya ca tatkartur enasaḥ syāt turīyabhāk  Hbhv brāhmeyas tu pāṇitale bhuṅkte yas tu phutkārasaṃyutam prasṛtāṅgulibhir yas tu tasya gomāṃsavac ca tat  Hbhv atrismṛtaunyūnādhikastanī yā gaur yāthavābhakṣyacāriṇī tayor dugdhaṃ na hotavyaṃ na pātavyaṃ kadācana  Hbhv ajā gāvo mahiṣyaś ca yāmedhyam api bhakṣayet havye kavye ca taddugdhaṃ gomayaṃ ca vivarjayet  Hbhv aṅgulyā dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ tathā mṛttikāprāśanaṃ caiva tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇaiḥ  Hbhv atrāpavādo manusmṛtausāmudraṃ saindhavaṃ caiva lavaṇe paramādbhute pratyakṣe api te grāhye niṣedhas tv anyagocaraḥ  Hbhv atrismṛtaudivā kapitthacchāyā ca niśāyāṃ dadhibhojanam kārpāsaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca śakrād api haret śriyam  Hbhv viṣṇusmṛtau cakapilāyāḥ payaḥ pītvā śūdras tu narakaṃ vrajet homaśeṣaṃ pibed vipro vipraḥ syād anyathā paśuḥ  Hbhv parihartuṃ punar lekhaṃ tattatśāstroktam anyathā yad atra likhitaṃ kiñcit tat kṣantavyaṃ mahātmabhiḥ  Hbhv ācārāś cedṛśāḥ santi parepi bahulāḥ satām te lokaśāstrato jñeyā apekṣyā yadi vaiṣṇavaiḥ  Hbhv nityatvam eṣāṃ māhātmyam apy atra likhitāt purā sadācārasya nityatvān māhātmyāc ca susidhyati  Hbhv iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāsenityakṛtyasamāpano nāmaekādaśo vilāsaḥ
